
-----title
将乐 (出生地)

蔡安礼同学于将乐县含云寺，受庆真禅师影响。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　居将乐。预乡荐。<br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　在将乐。读书于含云寺。作品：含云寺书事六绝句。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　讲学读书于含云寺。有文。作品：札记解义。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7f81324411854cbf9ba30fba9297cd44_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7f81324411854cbf9ba30fba9297cd44");'><span id='7f81324411854cbf9ba30fba9297cd44_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1080')">1077-1080年</a>，25-28岁</div><div id='7f81324411854cbf9ba30fba9297cd44' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　在将乐。授汀州司户参军，不赴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　居将乐。著《列子解》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　居将乐。作《虎头岩记》<div id='poem_1206834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206834?labeling=true' target='_blank'>虎头岩记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206834")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206834'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206834'>县城之东南有虎头岩者，昔显德间邑人设像于其中，冶金镂木为钟鼓以警朝昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206834_comment'></div>旁有隙地，可以种艺稼穑，僧之居此者，足以衣食焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206834_comment'></div>自熙宁以来，旁之地为渔利者所夺，而僧之居是岩者无以济朝夕，遂弃而之他，其后亦莫有守者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206834_comment'></div>故岩之左右前后，薪木者不禁，剪伐陵践，竹木无有遗蘖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206834_comment'></div>于是岩之丑形如张口待哺，耸据于东南之隅，邑人不暇求葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206834_comment'></div>熙宁丁巳，封内有警，市人惶骇之，无一日安其居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206834_comment'></div>县令吴侯来，始为之还定安集之，而民复得其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206834_comment'></div>及贼平，闾巷父老用昔者之言，以谓是祸也，斯岩实召之，遂闻于公，请县之僧可淳者使葺是堂，于岩腹刻木为像以镇之，所谓均庆禅祖是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206834_comment'></div>复作亭于岩股，以待往来之游观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206834_comment'></div>落成，而僧可淳者求予文以志之，乃为之言曰：物之废兴无巨细，皆有数焉，非人力之所能为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206834_comment'></div>穷山川，聚土石，顽然无关于利害，而谓能致祸福于百里之民，岂其然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206834_comment'></div>盖人之所欲完以葺于是者，数实然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206834_comment'></div>不然，则如之何而人乐为之也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206834_comment'></div>且盗贼之兴，其渐有故，非一日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206834_comment'></div>肆凶怙力之民，慢令侮禁，相视以成俗，其御之也，在得其术而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206834_comment'></div>使后之长是邑者，皆如吴侯，则彼之肆凶怙力者，方将遁形隐迹之不暇，尚安能病民哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206834_comment'></div>使后之人无术以御之，则盗贼之兴有在矣，斯岩者何与焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206834_comment'></div>以步仞之虚，而层轩叠径、云烟杳霭之间，幽崖塞蹬，乃若绘画，远至于井邑之繁，溪山之秀，环目而尽得之，则又足为游观之美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206834_comment'></div>故予因书其废兴之由，以示往来者，使观之无惑焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1206834_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　居将乐。作《杨母朱氏墓志》<div id='poem_1206848' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206848' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206848?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨母朱氏墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206848")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206848_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206848'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206848'>杨母朱氏，世家延平，居士讳某之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206848_comment'></div>杨父先娶萧氏，夫人乃继室也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206848_comment'></div>夫人之归，曾大父已没，独曾大母犹存，其为人严惮，不妄戏笑，躬以勤俭，畜子孙有节，专静而无嗜好，人莫测其欲，以故左右给使鲜有中其意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206848_comment'></div>夫人事之常得其欢心，治家事中外辑睦，配杨父无违德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206848_comment'></div>其岁时奉祀，割牲省器，必亲临之，未尝委诸妇，终其身不懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206848_comment'></div>生子二人，二妇皆少亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206848_comment'></div>诸孙幼失所恃，夫人朝夕抚养，必知其燠寒疾痛，缀完缉敝，悉躬为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206848_comment'></div>比其成人，教以义方，故诸孙卒得所恃为成人，夫人之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206848_comment'></div>其天资柔静婉淑，事无小大，喜怒未尝见于色，居常好善，唯恐有弗及，故卒受天祉，以康宁寿考终其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206848_comment'></div>逮诸孙有妇，犹执女功不替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206848_comment'></div>诸子孙或止之曰：「为母而年八十，亦可以已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206848_comment'></div>虽不躬为之，其忧无人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206848_comment'></div>何自苦如是耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206848_comment'></div>夫人从容言曰：「为妇而执女功，乃其常也，汝何异哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206848_comment'></div>且吾虽老矣，使吾明衰而视昏，则虽欲彊为，可得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206848_comment'></div>吾之所以不已者，第吾力之所能胜耳，汝何怪耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206848_comment'></div>其后子孙虽屡止之，其志终不可夺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206848_comment'></div>杨父讳明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206848_comment'></div>有子五人：曰某，曰某，夫人之出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206848_comment'></div>孙男六人：曰助，曰梦，曰时，曰度，曰州仆，曰二仆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206848_comment'></div>曾孙三人：曰迪，曰迥，曰遹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206848_comment'></div>女二人皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206848_comment'></div>享年八十有三，熙宁十年某月某日以疾终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206848_comment'></div>某年某月某日葬于白土之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206848_comment'></div>其仲孙时为之表而告其子孙曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1206848'>而子而孙，实繁其夥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206848_comment'></div>谁其育之，王母是妥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206848_comment'></div>迨其成人，弃汝而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206848_comment'></div>寸草有心，孰报春晖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206848_comment'></div>日往不复，形终此瘗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206848_comment'></div>刻石墓左，以示来裔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1206848_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　居将乐。春分寻医，不赴汀户任，杜门绩学。与邹夔交游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　居将乐。杜门绩学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>　居将乐。秋，离家赴调。有诗。作品：别西斋诸友。离家作（败叶辞故枝）离家作（胡雁依朔风）<br /></div><div class='label1' id='65c07983a2bc43038aa6759ccfe52961_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("65c07983a2bc43038aa6759ccfe52961");'><span id='65c07983a2bc43038aa6759ccfe52961_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>，30岁</div><div id='65c07983a2bc43038aa6759ccfe52961' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　居将乐。有诗寄游定夫。作品：寄游定夫（綘帷燕侍毎从容）寄游定夫（萧条清颍一茅庐）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年2月10日</a>　居将乐。长子迪生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　居将乐。冬，有诗。作品：元丰壬戌岁暮书事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　居将乐。有书寄程颢问《春秋》作品：寄明道先生书 其一。<div id='poem_1206512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄明道先生书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206512")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206512_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206512'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206512'>自奔走南归，不闻诲言久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206512_comment'></div>所居穷僻，贤士大夫不至其境，每学有所疑，则中怀罔然，思所以考正，徒北向瞻望而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206512_comment'></div>附语者以其视听不用耳目，故能传死者之事，有人所不知者，既已闻命矣，然其所以能视听不用耳目，则未闻其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206512_comment'></div>古者冠婚丧祭，必筮之吉，然后行事，则古之人，其动作未尝不择日也，其旨安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206512_comment'></div>《春秋》不书即位者四，隐、庄、闵、僖是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206512_comment'></div>诸儒之论纷然不知所从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206512_comment'></div>左氏谓隐公为摄，以经考之，则隐非摄明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206512_comment'></div>然三《传》皆谓有让桓之志，其果何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206512_comment'></div>先王之时，诸侯疑无相盟之事，然考之《周官》司盟之职曰：「掌盟载之法，凡邦国有疑会同，则掌其盟约之载」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206512_comment'></div>《觐礼》朝诸侯于坛讫，乃加方明于坛而祀之，列诸侯于庭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206512_comment'></div>《玉府》「共珠盘玉敦」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206512_comment'></div>《戎右》「以玉敦辟盟，遂役之，赞牛耳<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1206512", 1206512, "Clauses/40/Comments/1")'>桃茢</span>」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206512_comment'></div>《司盟》北面诏告明神，诸侯以次歃血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206512_comment'></div>则诸侯相盟，礼所有也，不识二《礼》之说果可以为据耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206512_comment'></div>抑亦附会之说耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206512_comment'></div>《春秋》之凡书盟者，又何谓也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206512_comment'></div>「秋七月，天王使宰咺来归惠公仲子之赗」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206512_comment'></div>以传考之，则仲子者惠公之妾，桓公之母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206512_comment'></div>从之说者皆以为惠公之母，其曰惠公仲子者，以别惠公之母耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206512_comment'></div>其不同若此，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206512_comment'></div>《春秋》之学不传久矣，每以不得从容左右，亲受指诲为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206512_comment'></div>鄙心所疑，非止一二，但未敢缕陈，恐烦听览耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206512_comment'></div>惟先生不以愚鄙见弃，一一见教，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1206512_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　居将乐。有诗。作品：酬林志宁。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d07583008d4d46d0a66ee82a13659b2e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d07583008d4d46d0a66ee82a13659b2e");'><span id='d07583008d4d46d0a66ee82a13659b2e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>，31岁</div><div id='d07583008d4d46d0a66ee82a13659b2e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年1月</a>　居将乐。正月，赴徐州司法任。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d622b33b069043a7a4f2ac39400e6b31_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d622b33b069043a7a4f2ac39400e6b31");'><span id='d622b33b069043a7a4f2ac39400e6b31_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1087')">1085-1087年</a>，33-35岁</div><div id='d622b33b069043a7a4f2ac39400e6b31' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年7月</a>　在将乐。丁继母忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　在将乐。有文。作品：与陈传道序。<div id='poem_1206641' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206641' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206641?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与陈传道序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206641")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206641_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206641'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206641'>予尝谓学者视圣人，其犹射之于正鹄乎，虽巧力所及，有中否远近之不齐，然未有不志乎正鹄而可以言射者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206641_comment'></div>士之去圣人或相倍蓰，或相什佰，所造固不同，然未有不志乎圣人而可以言学者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206641_comment'></div>自孔子没，更战国至秦，遂焚书、坑儒士，六经中绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206641_comment'></div>汉兴，虽稍稍复出，然圣学之失，其传尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206641_comment'></div>由汉至唐千馀岁，士之博闻强识者，世岂无其人耶，而卒未有能窥圣学之堂奥者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206641_comment'></div>岂当时之士卒无志于圣人耶，而卓然自立者何其少也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206641_comment'></div>若唐之韩愈，盖尝谓「世无仲尼，不当在弟子之列」，则亦不可谓无其志也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206641_comment'></div>及观其所学，则不过乎欲雕章镂句，取名誉而止耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206641_comment'></div>然则士固不患不知有志乎圣人，而特患乎不知圣人之所以学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206641_comment'></div>且古之圣人固宜莫如舜也，舜之在侧微，与木石居、鹿豕游，固无异于深山之野人也，是岂以文采过人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206641_comment'></div>伏羲画八卦，书断自《尧典》，当是时，六经盖未有也，而舜之所以圣者，果何自哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206641_comment'></div>夫舜，圣人也，生而知之，无事乎学可也，自圣人而下，则未有可以不学者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206641_comment'></div>舜之臣二十有二人，相与共成帝业者，是果皆生知耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206641_comment'></div>不然，其何以学也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206641_comment'></div>由是观之，六经虽圣人微言，而道之所存，盖有言不能传者，则经虽具，犹不能谕人之弗达也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206641_comment'></div>然则圣之所以为圣，贤之所以为贤，其必有在矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206641_comment'></div>虽然，士之去圣远矣，舍六经亦何以求圣人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206641_comment'></div>要当精思之，力行之，超然默会于言意之表，则庶乎有得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206641_comment'></div>若夫过其藩篱，望其门墙，足未踰阈，而辄妄意其室中之藏，则幸其中也，难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206641_comment'></div>呜呼，今之士未尝以此学也，类皆分文析字，屑屑于章句之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206641_comment'></div>甚者广记问、工言辞，欲誇多斗靡而已，是乌用学为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206641_comment'></div>彭城陈君传道，志学之士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206641_comment'></div>其将之官也，求予言，故因为发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206641_comment'></div>然未知陈君果以吾言为然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206641_comment'></div>其未以为然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206641_comment'></div>幸明告我，庶几其有警也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1206641_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年9月20日</a>　在将乐。程颐有《答杨时慰书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　在将乐。有文。作品：寄翁好德书 其二。邓文伯字序。杨仲远字序。与杨仲远书。与杨君玉书。与邹尧叟书。<div id='poem_1206822' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206822' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206822?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邓文伯字序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206822")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206822_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206822'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206822'>武阳邓平更其名曰洵武，间而语予曰：「平之名久矣，未有知其为倒士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206822_comment'></div>梦有神人告我曰：『子之名平，其字倒士，使子之困穷也，殆以是夫』！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206822_comment'></div>予觉而异之，徐而思之，意者殆天将启予乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206822_comment'></div>吾困穷之病，将由此有瘳乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206822_comment'></div>不然，何神之告我详而警我之至也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206822_comment'></div>越明，乃以洵武易之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206822_comment'></div>吾子姑为我字之，以相神之惠，斯亦故旧之义也，子其无辞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206822_comment'></div>予闻而诺之，为之言曰：夫一体之盈虚消息通乎天地，应于物类，则祸福之来，兆于彼而此应之，亦其理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206822_comment'></div>然天棐谌，命靡常，而古之人所以应天者，亦求诸己而已，君宜勉之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206822_comment'></div>夫有武必济之以文，请字曰文伯，并为说以纪其事云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1206822_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206821' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206821' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206821?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨仲远字序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206821")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206821_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206821'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206821'>杨君敦仁以其名求字于予曰：「愿闻一言以进其不及」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206821_comment'></div>自惟不肖，何足以副其求？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206821_comment'></div>然义不敢默，乃告之曰：仁之道，其至矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206821_comment'></div>虽孔子犹罕言也，况馀人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206821_comment'></div>然试尝语子以吾所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206821_comment'></div>夫忠恕者，仁之方也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206821_comment'></div>宽裕温柔者，仁之质也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206821_comment'></div>齐庄中正者，仁之守也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206821_comment'></div>发强刚毅者，仁之用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206821_comment'></div>无迷其方，无毁其质，慎守之，力行之，则仁其庶几乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206821_comment'></div>曾子曰：「士不可以不弘毅，任重而道远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206821_comment'></div>仁以为己任，不亦重乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206821_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1206821", 1206821, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>死而后已</span>，不亦远乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206821_comment'></div>今吾子以敦仁自名，可谓知任重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206821_comment'></div>予愿以仲远配子之名，益将期子于远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206821_comment'></div>夫任重而不期于致远，中必自画而已，其于仁乎何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206821_comment'></div>然古之为此道者，果何求哉，亦曰无迷其方，无毁其质，慎守之，力行之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206821_comment'></div>反是而求所谓仁其庶几者，非吾所敢知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206821_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206821_comment'></div>有名而不孚其实者，古人耻之，而今人不以为耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206821_comment'></div>吾子将有志乎古人，而求免于今人，则宜勉之无忽云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1206821_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206516' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206516' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206516?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与杨仲远书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206516")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206516_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206516'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206516'>得所惠书，谓能不变于俗，此固区区所望，而吾子所当勉也，甚慰甚慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206516_comment'></div>道废千年，学士大夫溺于异端之习久矣，天下靡然成风，莫知以为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206516_comment'></div>士志于道者，非见善明、用心刚，往往受变而不自知，此俗习之移人，甚可畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206516_comment'></div>若夫外势利声色，不为流俗诡谲之行，以是为不变于俗，则于学者未足道也，吾子勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206516_comment'></div>先帝睿圣，方将大有为，而遽有凶变如此，固天下所同戚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206516_comment'></div>今天子即位，务在宽民，一时聚歛之臣迁谪殆尽，东州民吏如释重负，息阴休迹而遇清风也，幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206516_comment'></div>不知吾乡亦觉如此否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206516_comment'></div>司马君实已作两府，甚慰民望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206516_comment'></div>伯淳先生近自汝召作宗丞，想已在京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206516_comment'></div>君玉或未归，计早晚当勉之令就学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206516_comment'></div>某苟禄如常，贱吏冗职，无补于万分，而旧学日废，以此易彼，孰得孰失？</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1206516_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206517?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206517'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206517'>近日不审为学何地？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206517_comment'></div>向者欲往定夫处，今果然否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206517_comment'></div>夫为己之学，正犹饥渴之于饮食，非有悦乎外也，以为弗饮弗食，则饥渴之病必至于致死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206517_comment'></div>人而不学，则失其本心，不足以为人，其病盖无异于饥渴者，此固学之不可已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206517_comment'></div>然古之善学者，必先知所止，知所止然后可以渐进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206517_comment'></div>伥伥然莫知所之，而欲望圣贤之域，多见其难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206517_comment'></div>此理宜切求之，不可忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206517_comment'></div>某迂拙之学无以希世，而望古不及，又不自量力之不足也，犹孜孜不已，宜为后生豪俊之所悯笑，而乃过为吾弟之所取信，故尤区区不敢嘿也，惟亮之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206517_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206518' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206518' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206518?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206518_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206518'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206518'>辱示高文，用意精深，益见好学之笃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206518_comment'></div>夫养气之道如治苗然，舍之而不耘，则有稂莠之伤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206518_comment'></div>助之长，则揠之而槁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206518_comment'></div>其说是也，然将不舍而耘之，则宜奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206518_comment'></div>与夫助之长者又何辨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206518_comment'></div>此近似之际，体之者尤当慎择也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206518_comment'></div>夫以天废人，以人灭天，固不可也，然养气者不废人，不灭天，则天人犹两立矣，乌睹所谓合一者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206518_comment'></div>反身者，反求诸身也，盖万物皆备于我，非自外得，反诸身而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206518_comment'></div>反身而至于诚，则利人者不足道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206518_comment'></div>伯夷求仁而得仁，子贡以是知孔子不为卫君，其言正为让国而发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206518_comment'></div>至于天下视之为去就，则夷齐非求为此也，乌得以此为求仁之效哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206518_comment'></div>是犹未免以迹论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206518_comment'></div>生之谓性，未有过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206518_comment'></div>告子论生之所以谓之性，则失之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206518_comment'></div>老氏之有无，佛氏之色空，盖将明天下而赜，非有人物之异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206518_comment'></div>老子以有生于无，又曰有无之相生，是不知有无一致矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206518_comment'></div>《正蒙》谓万象为太虚中所见物，则物与虚不相资，卒陷于浮图以山河大地为见病之说，山河大地正指物言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206518_comment'></div>若谓指物言之可也，则浮图见病之说不足非矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206518_comment'></div>此与佛氏以心法起灭天地，更当究观，所谓心法起灭天地之旨，未易以一言攻之也，更详味之如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206518_comment'></div>或有未尽，无惜疏示。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1206518_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206519' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206519?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206519_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206519'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206519'>寄示杂论，用意精确，益见好学之笃也，甚慰甚慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206519_comment'></div>夫克己者，扬雄所谓胜己之私是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206519_comment'></div>反身而诚，则常体而足，无所克也，故前书论反身与克己异意耳，更详考之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206519_comment'></div>告子知生之谓性，而不知生之所以谓之性，故失之，非生之谓性有二说也，特告子未达耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206519_comment'></div>《乾》之六爻有臣位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206519_comment'></div>而坤之六爻无君位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206519_comment'></div>夫《乾》之九二虽曰有臣位，然君德也，故曰「学以聚之，问以辨之，宽以居之，仁以行之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206519_comment'></div>《易》曰「见龙在田」、「利见大人」，君德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206519_comment'></div>汤之于伊尹，学焉而后臣之，其此之谓乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206519_comment'></div>用是求之，则乾坤君臣之位可推而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206519_comment'></div>某在此虽多事，亦时得开卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206519_comment'></div>闻于经史颇有论著，并所讲《乾》、《坤》义，无惜录示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206519_comment'></div>冗迫，书不能究。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206519_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206520?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206520'>世之学者皆言穷达有命，特信之未笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206520_comment'></div>某窃谓其知之未至也，知之斯信之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206520_comment'></div>今告人曰水火不可蹈，人必信之，以其知之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206520_comment'></div>告人曰富贵在天不可求，亦必曰然，而未有信而不求者，以其知之不若蹈水火之著明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206520_comment'></div>孟子曰：「莫之为而为者，天也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206520_comment'></div>莫之致而致者，命也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206520_comment'></div>又曰：「得之不得为有命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206520_comment'></div>世之后生晚学读《孟子》者，皆知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206520_comment'></div>孔子曰：「五十而知天命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206520_comment'></div>岂今之后学者皆能如孔子，必至五十而后知耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206520_comment'></div>盖孔子之所知殆不止此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206520_comment'></div>宦学之馀，试一思之如何？</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1206520_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206521' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206521' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206521?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206521_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206521'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206521'>诸子之学，折诸圣人，犹望洋向若，其辨自屈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206521_comment'></div>儒佛之论，造其极致，则所差𦕈忽耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206521_comment'></div>其义难知，而又其辞善遁，非操戈入室未易攻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206521_comment'></div>虽横渠之博辨精深，犹未能屈之为城下之盟，况馀人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206521_comment'></div>置而勿论可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206521_comment'></div>要当深造而自得之，则其辨自见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206521_comment'></div>近日治经读史如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206521_comment'></div>家居既不为外事湮汩，谅须精到也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206521_comment'></div>或有论议，寄示为幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206521_comment'></div>先生书录去，某到此未暇开卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206521_comment'></div>西厅稍宽旷，有园亭，足以自适，旬日事渐定，计可温寻旧学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206521_comment'></div>冗迫，不能尽万一。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1206521_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206524' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206524' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206524?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与杨君玉书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206524")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206524_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206524'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206524'>久别，不审为况何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206524_comment'></div>比得足下书，辞旨超迈，慨然似有志者，甚慰甚慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206524_comment'></div>夫君子之学，求仁而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206524_comment'></div>孔子之徒，自子贡以下，其说有未闻者，而吾子自谓知之，其所造远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206524_comment'></div>然知之者不如好之者，愿加好焉，则异日所进未易量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206524_comment'></div>某诸况如昨，无足念者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206524_comment'></div>未间，千万加爱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206524_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206526' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206526' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206526?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与邹尧叟书<span class='inlineComment2'>（尧叟名夔，刘执中婿。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206526")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206526_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206526'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206526'>递中伏辱赐教，并以诗见酬，辞精旨远，深用钦服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206526_comment'></div>非君子笃于故旧，何以及此，幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206526_comment'></div>仍审秋凉起居万福，又良慰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206526_comment'></div>某穷居下邑，与世不相闻，出无所之，行无所从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206526_comment'></div>闭门一室，聊以自娱，俯仰几席之间，游泳乎诗书之渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206526_comment'></div>虽鄙钝无所得，然与世之竞纷华，冒声色，以昏聋其耳目者较之，其亦足乐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206526_comment'></div>惟是不亲师友之训，于中不无歉然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206526_comment'></div>未涯趋会，切希为国自寿。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1206526'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206526_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　在将乐。有文与吴国华论王安石。作品：与吴国华书。答吴国华书。<div id='poem_1206528' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206528' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206528?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答吴国华书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206528")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206528_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206528'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206528'>辱赐教，伏审夏热起居平宁，甚慰怀仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206528_comment'></div>仍蒙谆复诲谕，开其所未悟，幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206528_comment'></div>然其间似有未相悉者，义不可苟止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206528_comment'></div>且某于程氏之门，所谓过其藩未入其域者也，安敢自附为党与，以攻王氏之学？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206528_comment'></div>夫王氏之学，其失在人耳目，诚不待攻，而攻之者亦何罪耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206528_comment'></div>昔人有为神农之言者，其徒自以为圣，而孟子鄙之曰「鴃舌之人」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206528_comment'></div>仲子之廉，孟子则曰「蚓而后可」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206528_comment'></div>伯夷，柳下惠皆圣人也，至其隘与不恭，孟子则曰「君子不由」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206528_comment'></div>仲尼之门，三尺童子羞称管晏，人有毁仲尼者，其门弟子皆称誉以为不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206528_comment'></div>若孟子者，岂喜攻人之恶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206528_comment'></div>而为孔氏徒者，率皆不顾于义，立党尚气相攻耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206528_comment'></div>不然，何为其亦纷纷譊譊也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206528_comment'></div>盖不直则道不见，我且直之，孟子所不得已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206528_comment'></div>孟子时去孔子未远，其徒相与传守，故其流风馀韵，犹有存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206528_comment'></div>当是时，杨墨肆行，孟子且不能默而拒之，至不知者以为好辩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206528_comment'></div>况今去孟子千有馀岁，圣学失传，异端竞起，其害有过于杨墨者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206528_comment'></div>幸而有得圣人之道者，则曰：「吾不敢攻人之恶，姑自守而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206528_comment'></div>为其徒者又畏天下指为党人，遂皆胶口闭舌，不敢别白是非，则世之人亦何赖乎知道者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206528_comment'></div>某以为如是，恐非圣贤之用心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206528_comment'></div>某自惟浅陋，不足取合于世，故未尝敢辄出所有告语于人，以取讥讪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206528_comment'></div>窃谓于国华忝为同道，故妄肆狂瞽，渎闻乎左右，非敢攻人之恶，盖欲审其是非，以观朋友之合否耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206528_comment'></div>然前书所论谓王氏不知道而已，语人不知道，即谓之攻人之恶，是必誉天下之人为圣贤，然后可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206528_comment'></div>自守所学以排异端，即谓之立党，尚气相攻，是必无择是非，一切雷同，然后可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206528_comment'></div>国华谓王氏固多不中理之言，言有不中理，皆不知道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206528_comment'></div>由汉而来，为传注者多矣，其言之合道者亦自过半，然不可果谓之知道者，以不中理者多故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206528_comment'></div>古之言知味者称易牙，夫岂以辛咸酸苦，人皆不能知耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206528_comment'></div>然必以易牙为知味者，谓淄渑之合而不失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206528_comment'></div>如易牙亦时有中否焉，即谓之知味，则天下皆易牙也，何足相过哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206528_comment'></div>国华谓知道与尽道者固异，又曰知道而未尽，则不能无惑，故王氏末年溺于释老，又为《字说》，此为大戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206528_comment'></div>夫知道者，果且有大戾乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206528_comment'></div>且王氏奉佛，至舍其所居以为佛寺，其徒有为僧者，则作诗以奖就其志，若有美而不及者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206528_comment'></div>夫儒佛不两立久矣，此是则彼非，此非则彼是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206528_comment'></div>又佛之去中国不知其几千万里，正孟子所谓鴃舌之人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206528_comment'></div>王氏乃不会其是非邪正，尊其人，师其道，是与陈良之徒无以异也，而谓知道者为之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206528_comment'></div>夫所贵乎知道者，谓其能别是非，审邪正也，如是非邪正无所分辨，则亦乌在其知道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206528_comment'></div>然以其博极群书，某故谓其力学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206528_comment'></div>溺于异端，以从夷狄，某故谓其不知道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206528_comment'></div>国华毋谓某何以见其如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206528_comment'></div>且古人之于道，盖有知之未尽，行之未至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206528_comment'></div>如燕人适越，至吴而止，则可谓行之而未至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206528_comment'></div>观越之都，望其郛郭城社，而未能究知宗庙之美，则可谓知越而未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206528_comment'></div>若夫将适越而北其辕，则不可谓行之未至也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206528_comment'></div>指吴为越，则不可谓知之未尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206528_comment'></div>今王氏所行皆北其辕者也，尊佛老为圣人，是指吴为越也，乌得谓知之未尽，行之未至耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206528_comment'></div>昔者管仲以区区之齐，乃能九合诸侯，一匡天下，曾西犹谓其功烈如彼其卑也，而羞比之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206528_comment'></div>王氏擅天下利势，其功烈无足称者，非特卑而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206528_comment'></div>然则知道者固无补于治乱也，而士亦乌用知道为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206528_comment'></div>以王氏之博物洽闻，某虽穷日夜之力以终身焉，不敢望其至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206528_comment'></div>若以知道如王氏而止，则某不敢与闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206528_comment'></div>国华所论孔子之徒，皆未可以一言断其终身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206528_comment'></div>子贡曰「性与天道，不可得而闻」，则其始之未闻，何足怪哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206528_comment'></div>然其后之所进者远矣，但学者未之考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206528_comment'></div>国华谓诏书无废王学之命，某观王氏之学，其精微要妙之义多在《字说》，既已禁之，则名虽未废而实废之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206528_comment'></div>虽然废不废，君子何容心哉，谨守其是者而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206528_comment'></div>前书所以及之者，为应科举者言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206528_comment'></div>人行急，辞不逮意，国华诚思之如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206528_comment'></div>如未中理，愿更疏示，当谨承教也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1206528_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年10月</a>　在将乐。服除。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='88690da44bd84265aeb33dbd985aae0d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("88690da44bd84265aeb33dbd985aae0d");'><span id='88690da44bd84265aeb33dbd985aae0d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>，36岁</div><div id='88690da44bd84265aeb33dbd985aae0d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年7月</a>　在将乐。有文。作品：求仁斋记。<div id='poem_1206827' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206827' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206827?labeling=true' target='_blank'>求仁斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206827")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206827_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206827'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206827'>元祐戊辰秋七月，予至自京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206827_comment'></div>友人黄君过予，问劳苦之暇，因谓予曰：「吾于县北墉之隅，西山之麓得废址焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206827_comment'></div>薙草辇石，辟地为黉舍，有讲诵之堂，燕休寝息之庐，宾客之位，无一不完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206827_comment'></div>将聚族亲子弟教之，虽乡人愿至者不拒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206827_comment'></div>子盍为我名之，尽其义以告」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206827_comment'></div>居数日，予相与一临之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206827_comment'></div>其地高明亢爽，下临康庄之衢，负城西南诸峰，首尾盘厉，联亘十馀里，皆隐然得之几席之上，而俯仰之际，如在深山大泽，丘荒之间，埃𡏖之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206827_comment'></div>此真学者之所居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206827_comment'></div>予徘徊久之，乃昌言诵之曰：「吾邑距中州数千里之远，舟车不通，缙绅先生与一时怀德秉义之士，足以表世范俗者，皆无自而至，士之欲为君子者何所取资耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206827_comment'></div>故后生晚学无所窥观，游谈戏豫，不闻箴规切磨之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206827_comment'></div>同则嬉狎，异则相訾，至悖义踰礼而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206827_comment'></div>虽英材异禀间时有之，亦不过诵六艺之文，百家之编，为章句之儒，钓声利而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206827_comment'></div>一日衒鬻而不售，则反视平昔所有，皆陈腐剽剥，无所用之，往往转而易业者，十尝六七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206827_comment'></div>此与廛夫贩父积百货，坐市区，逐什一之利，流徙无常者何异耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206827_comment'></div>予尝悼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206827_comment'></div>又窃自悲其力之不足，欲逃此而未能，思得吾党之士，柔不溺于随，刚不愤于欲者，相进于道，庶几少激颓俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206827_comment'></div>今吾子乃能经营于此，以教学为事，是真有志者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206827_comment'></div>然予尝谓古之学者求仁而已矣，《传》曰：「放于利而行多怨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206827_comment'></div>又曰：「求仁而得仁，又何怨」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206827_comment'></div>夫衒鬻而不售，转而易业者，皆放于利而怨者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206827_comment'></div>吾愿以「求仁」名子之斋，庶乎求之必得而无怨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206827_comment'></div>虽然，古之人所以求仁者，不亦难乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206827_comment'></div>夫孔子之徒问仁者多矣，而孔子所以告之者岂一二言欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206827_comment'></div>然而犹曰「罕言」，岂不以仁之道至矣，而言之不能尽欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206827_comment'></div>故凡孔子之所言者，皆求仁之方也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206827_comment'></div>若夫仁则盖未之尝言，是故其徒如由、赐者，虽曰升堂之士，至于仁，则终身莫之许也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206827_comment'></div>然则所谓求之难，不其然欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206827_comment'></div>学者试以吾言思之，以究观古之人所以求之之方，将必有得矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1206827_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4a929fcd5b2848dc9d756b36240b6b1a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4a929fcd5b2848dc9d756b36240b6b1a");'><span id='4a929fcd5b2848dc9d756b36240b6b1a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1093')">1090-1093年</a>，38-41岁</div><div id='4a929fcd5b2848dc9d756b36240b6b1a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年10月2日</a>　在虔州。父埴卒，解官居制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年12月</a>　贺铸有《寄墨代书赠杨时》诗寄杨时。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　居将乐，在丧制。有文。作品：先君行状。<div id='poem_1206845' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206845' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206845?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先君行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1091年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206845")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206845_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206845'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206845'>先君讳某，南剑州将乐县人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206845_comment'></div>祖讳某，父讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206845_comment'></div>先君为人质直而信厚，其遇事接物初若不可忤，而胸中洞然，无含怒宿怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206845_comment'></div>其治家勤约有节，虽一介不妄以与人，亦不妄取人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206845_comment'></div>自皇祖而上，世为农家，至先君始励其子以学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206845_comment'></div>熙宁中，某以进士出身，而先君喜不形于言色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206845_comment'></div>其后虽屏居不仕殆十年，而先君亦莫之问也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206845_comment'></div>及闻其从师友之贤，磨切以德义，则充然厌其欲，其恬于荣利而乐于义方如此，盖天性也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206845_comment'></div>元祐五年十月戊戌以疾终于家，享年六十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206845_comment'></div>先君娶陈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206845_comment'></div>再娶廖氏，六年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206845_comment'></div>有子二人：曰某，曰某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206845_comment'></div>将以某年某月某日葬于石龟山之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206845_comment'></div>呜呼，吾先君平生为善，惟日不足，不幸少不从宦学，不得与当世贤士大夫游，故隐行弗彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206845_comment'></div>而其嗣孤某幼不肖，惧终无以成亲之名，以昭示后世子孙，乃泣而书之，求铭于有道君子，藏诸幽宫，庶足为亡者之慰云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1206845_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年4月</a>　在丧制。夏四月，与二三昆弟至杨道真君洞，作记。作品：杨道真君洞记。<div id='poem_1206832' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206832' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206832?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨道真君洞记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206832")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206832_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206832'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206832'>县城之北隅，封山之麓有洞焉，闻之长老言，以为杨道真君之所居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206832_comment'></div>杨道真君于传记无传，而其洞于图经弗载，是非真伪莫得而考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206832_comment'></div>元祐五年岁大旱，乡人诣真君祷雨辄应，予窃异之，欲往游焉而未暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206832_comment'></div>越二年壬申夏四月，因与二三昆弟蹑履担簦，翛然而往，行近五里馀，而颓崖断堑，荒翳险绝，初若不可投步，扪萝引蔓，仅能至其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206832_comment'></div>而呀然一室，如神刓鬼刻，其中窈然，莫能窥其远近也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206832_comment'></div>洞之北户有泉，汪洋汗漫，意其能宅灵气而兴云雨者有在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206832_comment'></div>予彷佛久之，喟然叹曰：今夫通邑大都，当舟舆之会，达官显人缨绂相属于其间，一有异境，则登览赋咏，朝出乎笔舌之端，而暮传四方矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206832_comment'></div>过情之文，雕绘百态，诡异而浮实者十常六七，故闻风者每以未至为恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206832_comment'></div>至于穷山绝俗，僻陋之邦，缙绅游士之所不至，虽有瑰奇绝特之观，往往为幽潜之士遁世而弗耀者擅而有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206832_comment'></div>是人也，虽欲窥寻其声光且不可得，尚能显其所寓哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206832_comment'></div>于戏，物之显晦，其不在人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206832_comment'></div>虽然，显晦者诚在人也，而天地之美，隐秀含媚于荒丘榛莽之间常自如也，夫岂有加损哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206832_comment'></div>然则斯洞之无闻，未足以慨吾心也，姑书其岁月以为记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206832_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年1月</a>　在将乐，丁忧服除，赴调。有诗送蔡安礼。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='af560b92a22247b2a3b04a71b131e159_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("af560b92a22247b2a3b04a71b131e159");'><span id='af560b92a22247b2a3b04a71b131e159_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>，42岁</div><div id='af560b92a22247b2a3b04a71b131e159' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　或在将乐。有文。作品：与游定夫书 其三。与游定夫书 其四。<div id='poem_1206551' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206551' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206551?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与游定夫书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206551")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206551_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206551'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206551'>某穷居习閒久矣，乍尔莅事，不无应接之烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206551_comment'></div>然义所当勉，亦不敢苟且自堕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206551_comment'></div>事有间即读《易》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206551_comment'></div>然无朋游共学相与讲明，每有所疑，徒切瞻企耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206551_comment'></div>去年相别时定夫亦读《易》，计须精到，有便愿以所得见教，不宜有吝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206551_comment'></div>盖吾侪所学，既与世背驰，朋友数人又各南北，切磋之益，以待面求亦无及矣，公宜亮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206551_comment'></div>固不敢嘿嘿，亦当有浼问以取质左右也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206551_comment'></div>吾友閒居，从游者必多，所得有人否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206551_comment'></div>其质有可进者，宜切诱掖之，不当以彊聒为耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206551_comment'></div>敝乡二杨与舍弟欲亲炙席下，果然否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206551_comment'></div>幸加驱策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206551_comment'></div>区区非纸可尽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1206551_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206552?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206552'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206552'>主上睿圣，方进退大臣，以兴复太平之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206552_comment'></div>元丰丕绩，计指日可望，政令一新，但恐疏愚无以奉承耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206552_comment'></div>学中长贰为谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206552_comment'></div>近不闻报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206552_comment'></div>苏季明向除博士，曾到任否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206552_comment'></div>京师非食贫之地，公聚口颇众，度其势能久居否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206552_comment'></div>趋舍之方，宜审处也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206552_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　或在将乐。有诗寄游酢。作品：归雁。感事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年2月2日</a>　居将乐。二月二日，离家赴浏阳任。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='5f35945f750d45fcbb20575b87200d3f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5f35945f750d45fcbb20575b87200d3f");'><span id='5f35945f750d45fcbb20575b87200d3f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>，46岁</div><div id='5f35945f750d45fcbb20575b87200d3f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年7月</a>　自浏阳归，七月，著《周易解义》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年7月</a>　居将乐，有文。作品：蔡奉议墓志铭。<div id='poem_1206850' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206850' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206850?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蔡奉议墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206850")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206850_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206850'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206850'>安礼既没之明年，其族兄某以其弟亢踵门而告曰：「先兄疾大渐，顾而谓亢曰：『吾不幸至于不讳，宜以铭属公』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206850_comment'></div>今葬有期，敢以请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206850_comment'></div>予曰：「吾于安礼有平生之旧，朋友之恩，非一朝燕游好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206850_comment'></div>自幼学以至成人十馀年间，出处语默，无一不同者，而以铭属予，予虽不能文，其何可辞」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206850_comment'></div>乃叙其世族历官行事始终之大节，而铭之曰：君姓蔡，讳元方，安礼其字也，南剑州将乐人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206850_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，祖讳某，父讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206850_comment'></div>君世富赀，诸父皆浮侈妄费殆尽，独君之皇考能自力，不计有无，资君以学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206850_comment'></div>君亦感激奋励，焚膏继晷，不少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206850_comment'></div>穷探博取，发为辞章，卒以名闻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206850_comment'></div>熙宁九年同进士出身，主饶州鄱阳簿，移福州怀安、惠州博罗县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206850_comment'></div>因荐改宣德郎、知建昌军南丰县，以年劳改奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206850_comment'></div>绍圣四年某月某日以疾卒于官，享年四十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206850_comment'></div>君为人果毅明达，与朋友信，不诡合而妄随，遇事立断，不可回挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206850_comment'></div>初为怀安，代有日，会更役法，君亲为按籍，一日而差毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206850_comment'></div>吏不得摇手为奸利用，以为怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206850_comment'></div>君去，旁邑吏舞籍为隐漏，以赃败，陷重辟，无一免者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206850_comment'></div>吏始相庆，德君曰：「微令严而明，吾属无类矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206850_comment'></div>异时君过境上，故吏逆君拜庭下，以是为谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206850_comment'></div>其在南丰，岁适大饥，流亡莩踣者相枕籍，君为法赈之，赖以全活者不可胜纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206850_comment'></div>君之为政彊敏，与民为条约而不可犯，然简节而疏目明，亦易避也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206850_comment'></div>其破奸剔蠹，必锄尽根穴乃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206850_comment'></div>故所至有风绩，吏畏其威，而民安乐之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206850_comment'></div>某年某月某日葬于卞山之麓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206850_comment'></div>君娶郑氏，生女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206850_comment'></div>再娶黄氏，无男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206850_comment'></div>以其弟之子某为后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206850_comment'></div>昔君每以书抵予，未尝不以是为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206850_comment'></div>今其已矣，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206850_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1206850'>谓天尔啬兮胡德之纯，谓天尔厚兮后胡不蕃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206850_comment'></div>凭大灵兮骑云，款天阍而上诉兮邈乎不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206850_comment'></div>惟有德为不朽兮长存，后欲有考兮视此铭文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1206850_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年8月</a>　八月，启程前往开封。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ffb16bdea1e741478905a4c8c7a616e1_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>，47岁</div><div id='ffb16bdea1e741478905a4c8c7a616e1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: /></div><div class='label1' id='8d04e7cced32482cbe4e7dea0e73f0ad_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8d04e7cced32482cbe4e7dea0e73f0ad");'><span id='8d04e7cced32482cbe4e7dea0e73f0ad_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1100')">1099-1100年</a>，47-48岁</div><div id='8d04e7cced32482cbe4e7dea0e73f0ad' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　公自长沙还，植兰竹、猫头竹于东西轩。后调官京师，逾年而归，兰竹皆衰悴，感而成诗。作品：公自长沙还，植兰竹、猫头竹于东西轩。调官京师，逾年而归，兰竹皆衰悴，感而成诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　居将乐。讲学于含云寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　居将乐。作勉学歌示诸生。作品：此日不再得示同学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年4月15日</a>　居将乐。四子适生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年11月</a>　因伯母病，归家看望。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在将乐，有诗。作品：题吴国华钓台。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>，50岁</div><div id='1bcb197bea3445f4918cfa6ec230fb31' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　在将乐。作墓表。作品：居士余君墓表。<div id='poem_1206878' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206878' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206878?labeling=true' target='_blank'>居士余君墓表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206878")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206878_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206878'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206878'>居士余君讳适，字永叔，南剑州将乐人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206878_comment'></div>祖讳可，父讳思，世为田家，以赀自雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206878_comment'></div>至君始业儒，为乡进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206878_comment'></div>其为人倜傥，喜任侠，赴人之急，惟恐不及，虽陷宪网，滨死地，弗顾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206878_comment'></div>四方君子过吾邑者，必归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206878_comment'></div>有无共之，虽倒廪倾囷弗吝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206878_comment'></div>晚益豪放，以诗酒自娱，尤喜读《列子》之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206878_comment'></div>家无留藏，悉以资宴游之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206878_comment'></div>歌呼谈笑，至淋漓颠倒而不厌，其自视了然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206878_comment'></div>尝曰：「人生适意耳，何苦以废虐之生自刑也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206878_comment'></div>其为诗初若不用意，而语辄奇丽，至今侪类犹能道之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206878_comment'></div>熙宁九年五月己巳以疾终于尤川之漆坑，其弟节以君之丧归葬于邑之西山，是年六月壬子也，享年四十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206878_comment'></div>君娶廖氏，后君百有二日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206878_comment'></div>无子，女一人，予之室也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206878_comment'></div>是时予方举进士，窃名仕籍，而君之葬不得临穴视窆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206878_comment'></div>已游宦四方，必数年乃一归，而君之墓有宿草矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206878_comment'></div>荒丘之间，马鬣鳞比，几不可识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206878_comment'></div>予窃悲君之无后，而岁时展省独恃吾子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206878_comment'></div>今其若此，可不为之表识乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206878_comment'></div>故特叙其为人大略，揭之墓上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206878_comment'></div>虽予言不足以重君，尚庶吾后世子孙知其为君之墓而不忘也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1206878_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年9月</a>　在将乐。为伯母俞氏作墓志铭。作品：俞氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1206851' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206851' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206851?labeling=true' target='_blank'>俞氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁元年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206851")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206851_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206851'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206851'>夫人俞氏，予伯父讳某之继室也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206851_comment'></div>曾祖讳英，祖讳怀选，父讳守琼，世为南剑州人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206851_comment'></div>自皇考而上，隐德不仕，以赀杰其乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206851_comment'></div>子弟始皆业儒，为名进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206851_comment'></div>夫人端静严饬，不妄笑语，虽遇子弟，未尝有戏慢之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206851_comment'></div>治家勤约有节，中馈之事，必身亲之，至老不懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206851_comment'></div>初，伯父亡，子尚幼，夫人以孀稚自营，攻苦食淡，仰取俛拾，卒克有家，子孙赖之不坠先业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206851_comment'></div>元符三年十有一月甲戌以疾终，享年七十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206851_comment'></div>伯父有子五人，其二夫人出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206851_comment'></div>曰炳，曰允蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206851_comment'></div>崇宁元年九月丙申葬于龟山之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206851_comment'></div>始夫人疾革，予方以漕檄窃食清流，北归省之床下，已不能言，犹颔之，若有嘱予者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206851_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206851_comment'></div>意欲何言耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206851_comment'></div>于其葬，乃泣而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206851_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1206851'>阴静而啬，兹理之常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206851_comment'></div>无非无仪，妇德乃光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206851_comment'></div>渊哉夫人，展也其臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206851_comment'></div>刻铭幽宫，以示不忘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1206851_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年9月</a>　九月，公赴荆州教授。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9030cb55694e4afa98e711c8b8bb28f4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9030cb55694e4afa98e711c8b8bb28f4");'><span id='9030cb55694e4afa98e711c8b8bb28f4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>，63岁</div><div id='9030cb55694e4afa98e711c8b8bb28f4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　自毗陵单骑还乡。有文。作品：资圣院记。<div id='poem_1206840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>资圣院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206840")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206840'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206840'>将溪据闽之上游，地险而隘，以崇山大陵为郭郛，惊湍激流为沟池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206840_comment'></div>鱼稻果蔬与凡资身之具，无所仰而足，故五季之乱，人乐居焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206840_comment'></div>负城之北有寺曰桥庵者，伪唐保大初僧师诘避地结茅之所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206840_comment'></div>乾祐三年始以资圣名之，迄今百六十有六年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206840_comment'></div>皇祐庚辰，僧无我东徙不百步，面东衢，以便往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206840_comment'></div>未克完而无我卒，更五十馀年无继之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206840_comment'></div>上漏旁穿，风雨弗庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206840_comment'></div>崇宁四年，始命僧永璘尸之，用日者之言复其故址。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206840_comment'></div>既成，不远千里以书求文为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206840_comment'></div>政和乙未，予还自毗陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206840_comment'></div>居数日，过其门而寝庑殿宇皆完洁，无一不可喜者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206840_comment'></div>又作弥陀、观音、势至像而严饰之，望之晬然，金碧焜耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206840_comment'></div>乃喟然叹曰：天下之事，废兴岂不以人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206840_comment'></div>此有国有家者之所同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206840_comment'></div>予去松楸十有四年始一归，而昔之蘖者今拱矣，牛羊斧斤相寻于其上，而折泄者不可胜计，闾巷亦萧然非昔日也，为之怆然不能自释者累日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206840_comment'></div>独是寺焕然一新，岂非居得其人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206840_comment'></div>私自念丘墓之寄，舍此人其谁宜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206840_comment'></div>故于其堂之西偏治一室焉，寘先人之遗像以为岁时展省之地，而璘师不予御也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206840_comment'></div>异时松楸折泄之患，庶几其免乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206840_comment'></div>甚矣夫，吾衰久矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206840_comment'></div>周流四方，欲营菟裘而无易于吾之故丘者，岂特昔人乐居之哉，行当庇身先人之庐而归老焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206840_comment'></div>幅巾杖屦，徜徉龟山之阴，与田夫野老相从于此，枕石漱流，窃自比于舞雩之下，将有日矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1206840_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　居将乐，有文。作品：白云庵记。含云寺真祠遗像记。<div id='poem_1206838' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206838?labeling=true' target='_blank'>白云庵记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206838")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206838'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206838'>廖君无隅一日过余而告曰：「先君得吉卜于孔山之阳，即其兆域之隅结屋数楹，杂莳松桂，间以奇花异卉，以为岁时展省少休之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206838_comment'></div>未几而先君殁，既襄事，乃因其旧而广之，作慕堂以奉其像，寘佛其旁，命僧正持居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206838_comment'></div>又以春晖名其轩，清风名其亭，以示报亲诒谋之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206838_comment'></div>而总名之曰白云庵，盖取狄梁公望云思亲之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206838_comment'></div>愿得一言识之，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206838_comment'></div>予告之曰：君方筮仕之初，而预有去亲之忧，用狄梁公之言名其庵，其志远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206838_comment'></div>然狄公当嬖臣孽后穷凶之时，罗织之狱起而毒流天下，亡身赤族者背项相望矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206838_comment'></div>乃欲以一苇之微，障江河之流，鲁缟之薄，当燕弧朔干之劲，岂易胜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206838_comment'></div>公独见义必为，挺然不可回挠，其忠义贯白日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206838_comment'></div>故虽一言之善，亦足以垂无穷，盖其始终大节有以耸动观听故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206838_comment'></div>使公之坚白不足，而淄磷于世变，则虽顷步不忘其亲，累千百言，亦恶足以示后世哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206838_comment'></div>君能追用其言而思其人，慕其大节以自立，则异时有望云而思亲，将必犹今之视昔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206838_comment'></div>君其勉之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206838_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>含云寺真祠遗像记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206839")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206839'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206839'>师讳庆真，姓萧氏，顺兴大干人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206839_comment'></div>年十四弃家为浮屠，十九受具戒，游江西，得法于泐潭月禅师，已而遍参诸方而后归老焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206839_comment'></div>建中靖国元年秋七月晦，晨兴，以偈示众，更衣坐逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206839_comment'></div>越翼日，用荼毗法，得五色舍利，以其骨葬于其寺之东南隅北庵之原，以所得舍利为塑像奉事之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206839_comment'></div>政和乙未，予适自毗陵归故丘，其徒惟觉诣予求文为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206839_comment'></div>予与真师游非一日矣，是时予尚幼，方肄业为科举之文，挟策读书，穷日夜之力为进取计，盖未知有亡羊之忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206839_comment'></div>师每曳锡过堂下，释椎凿而议之数矣，予亦莫之省也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206839_comment'></div>然见其神宇泰定，不以世累撄其心，虽未能尽知其所有，亦窃意其非凡僧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206839_comment'></div>比予年加渐长，知为学之方，听其言，考其所知，益信其贤，而予已出仕矣，始恨不得相从复如昔日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206839_comment'></div>今其已矣，过其庐，升其堂，萧然无复有斯人也，怆然兴叹者久之，乃为之书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1206839_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4b95d8abfa2741589b758b7b18aa62d0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4b95d8abfa2741589b758b7b18aa62d0");'><span id='4b95d8abfa2741589b758b7b18aa62d0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1135')">1128-1135年</a>，76-83岁</div><div id='4b95d8abfa2741589b758b7b18aa62d0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年11月</a>　自毗陵还南剑之将乐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年12月</a>　在将乐，有文。作品：枢密曹公墓志铭。周宪之墓志铭。<div id='poem_1206876' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206876' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206876?labeling=true' target='_blank'>枢密曹公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206876")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206876_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206876'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206876'>宋兴，臣一海内，养息天下几二百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206876_comment'></div>民生戴白不见兵革，自三代而下，承平之久，未有如是之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206876_comment'></div>崇宁以来，大臣肆为蔽欺，盘游无度，侈汰日滋，谀言盈庭，而法家拂士不容于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206876_comment'></div>故上下俱溺于燕安鸩毒，而瞑眩之药弗进，天下病之，无敢言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206876_comment'></div>是时枢密曹公为秘书省正字，献书尽言，犯而无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206876_comment'></div>上皇优容之，初不加怒，有旨赴都堂问状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206876_comment'></div>宰臣王黼诘之，意有在焉，而公语不酬，黼怒，翌日编管柳州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206876_comment'></div>人皆为公危之，公独怡然自若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206876_comment'></div>虽名隶罪籍，而清议翕然归之，以为公辅器也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206876_comment'></div>渊圣嗣位，召为御史，自御史六迁为延康殿学士、签书枢密院事，从人望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206876_comment'></div>公讳辅，字戴德，南剑州沙县人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206876_comment'></div>曾祖逞，赠正奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206876_comment'></div>曾祖妣邓氏，咸安郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206876_comment'></div>林氏，齐安郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206876_comment'></div>祖宝臣，宣德郎致仕，赠正奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206876_comment'></div>祖妣邓氏，高平郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206876_comment'></div>考孚，赠宣奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206876_comment'></div>妣罗氏，咸宁郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206876_comment'></div>公幼颖悟绝人，大父常奇之，谓「异日大吾门者，必此儿也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206876_comment'></div>元符三年中进士第，调福州宁德县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206876_comment'></div>以宣奉公卧病，乞侍养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206876_comment'></div>丁母夫人忧，未除，丁宣奉公忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206876_comment'></div>服除，调寿州安丰县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206876_comment'></div>改通仕郎，试中词学兼茂科，特转文林郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206876_comment'></div>未一月，除敕令所删定官，改宣教郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206876_comment'></div>乞补外，通判安肃军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206876_comment'></div>用年劳转奉议郎，除主管南外宗室财用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206876_comment'></div>未一月，除秘书省正字，磨勘转承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206876_comment'></div>上书，编管柳州，坐废六年，量移袁州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206876_comment'></div>初在安肃，兼榷场事，得旨市北珠，公奏疏，其略曰：「以彼锱铢之物，易吾亿万之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206876_comment'></div>彼诚以此养士则士勇，以此赏战则战胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206876_comment'></div>是借寇兵，资盗粮也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206876_comment'></div>上悟而罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206876_comment'></div>靖康初召还，被旨引对，论事毕，上曰：「朕所虑为无将也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206876_comment'></div>公曰：「昔汉高祖得萧何为丞相，何进韩信为大将军，属以兵柄，卒成帝业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206876_comment'></div>相得人，则韩信出矣，无将亦非所虑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206876_comment'></div>他日又论：「汉用萧何而得韩信，汉王失军亡众，跳身遁者数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206876_comment'></div>何尝从关中遣军补其处，非上所诏令召，而数万之众会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206876_comment'></div>与楚相守荥阳数年，军无见粮，何尝转漕关中，给食不乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206876_comment'></div>夫将与兵、食，当是时无急于此三者，而何独办之，则天下大计在得一相而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206876_comment'></div>今宰相纵不能如何所为，盍亦各输所长，兼采众论，夙夜勤畏，协心戮力，共济艰难，以成中兴之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206876_comment'></div>乃因循苟且，日复一日，无肯以身任责者，遂至缓于事机，误国大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206876_comment'></div>此而不惩，后将何悔？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206876_comment'></div>愿正其因循苟且之罪，而罢黜之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206876_comment'></div>因而奏曰：「陛下用此数人于艰难之际，败事必矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206876_comment'></div>上曰：「卿姑待之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206876_comment'></div>公曰：「国家存亡在此一举，不容犹豫」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206876_comment'></div>上曰：「朕已有处置」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206876_comment'></div>次日奏事罢，徐进曰：「臣前论宰执，陛下语臣已有处置，未见行遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206876_comment'></div>臣言官，论列大臣，势不两立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206876_comment'></div>以臣言为是，乞早施行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206876_comment'></div>不然，臣且有罪，不复居此职」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206876_comment'></div>退而居家待罪，上手诏褒谕，遣中使押令供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206876_comment'></div>又乞以河北、河东、陕西三路有习知山川险易出入向背，绘为三图以进，摽揭控扼形势之地，以究知分屯战守制敌之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206876_comment'></div>遣将出师，则按图指纵，而庙算决矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206876_comment'></div>又言：「王云出使，遣人回奏，大金意欲得十六字故号，及玉辂衮冕仪物之类，且云不复索三镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206876_comment'></div>朝廷释然解忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206876_comment'></div>欲推尊僭大，为不可加之语以崇奉之，乘舆上服径推挽出境，以为屈己爱民，社稷大计当如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206876_comment'></div>臣窃以为社稷大计在此一举，诚不可忽，然或者宽忧于一时，而不知移祸于异日，将使天地易位，神民失归，逆行倒置，有不忍言者，为患为辱，古未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206876_comment'></div>何以言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206876_comment'></div>既与之以如是之名，彼将缘名而责实；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206876_comment'></div>既与之以如是之器，彼将缘器而致用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206876_comment'></div>一二年间，或以观兵较猎，或以省方巡狩为名，悉其国众进压我境，侈辞大意以号令我，自谓据域中最大，臣妾海宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206876_comment'></div>当是时，俛首而听之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206876_comment'></div>抑犹有以却之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206876_comment'></div>却之则强弱不敌，祸且甚于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206876_comment'></div>俛首听从，则天地安得不易位，神民安得不失归乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206876_comment'></div>又引鲁仲连却帝秦之说以为證，累千馀言，曲折详尽，此其大略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206876_comment'></div>公在试院中，闻诸奉使计议人并改为和议，左右一二辅臣议不协，遽图引去，公奏疏曰：「今之议者一于和，非也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206876_comment'></div>一于战，亦非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206876_comment'></div>一于和，则敌势凭陵，国威沮折，三镇之复，寻背前约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206876_comment'></div>一于战，则堂堂二百年基业决成败于交锋之间，其危甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206876_comment'></div>臣愿以和为名，以战为实，二者不可一废，惟吾先后用之耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206876_comment'></div>上深然之，即试院中除谏议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206876_comment'></div>及出院，又言：「金使王汭以和为名，朝夕到阙，恐谋国之臣便以甘言软语为敌实情，或至缓备，堕黠计中，则前日之祸踵而至矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206876_comment'></div>因论朝廷宜急而缓者五事以献，如邢、洺、磁、相当寇南冲，而不命将分兵，团集民伍，置屯列寨之类是也，皆一时要务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206876_comment'></div>未几迁给事中，公言：「臣章叠叠至数百纸，其间施行十未二三，陛下虽虚心听纳，而人臣置而不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206876_comment'></div>谏臣失职，负不知去之罪，敢复冒荣而进乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206876_comment'></div>恳辞不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206876_comment'></div>左右或为上言：「擢曹辅寘谏垣令论事，忽有移命，得无以为厌听纳乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206876_comment'></div>上曰：「曹辅遇事辄发，敛怨多矣，姑令就閒耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1206876_comment'></div>不旬浃，除御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1206876_comment'></div>是时何㮚罢中书侍郎，兼领开封府事，眷遇犹厚，公称谢中即奏㮚轻儇不可任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1206876_comment'></div>及金人渡河，公即奏曰：「去岁贼寨城外西北，地势卑下，不知决水灌，最为失策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1206876_comment'></div>今分城中兵数万出据东南，劄连珠寨以接外援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1206876_comment'></div>贼营西北，引水灌之，必得其利」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1206876_comment'></div>上以为然，宰相唐恪曰：「水可决，城中兵留为根本，不可出」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1206876_comment'></div>公曰：「兵留城中，用兵之死法」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1206876_comment'></div>恪坚持不出兵，先决水浸西北，东南无兵，为金所据，遂绝外援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1206876_comment'></div>及除佥书枢密院，而金人犯城已三日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1206876_comment'></div>何㮚以宰相领守御，公副之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1206876_comment'></div>㮚忌公，奏遣报谢金营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1206876_comment'></div>公留营七日而归，㮚方信妖人郭景，用六甲兵，募市井无赖数千，坚将出战，公曰：「自古用兵，未有以妖术成功者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1206876_comment'></div>力争不从，以病乞解机务，凡三章，未报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1206876_comment'></div>京城已失守，金人以今上领大元帅，握重兵在外，不自安，欲令迎还京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1206876_comment'></div>朝廷不得已，遣公往兴仁府迎之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1206876_comment'></div>公密启上曰：「方今外援独康王耳，不若留在外，使贼犹有所惮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1206876_comment'></div>上曰：「卿言极是，但得一公文回报足矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1206876_comment'></div>公至兴仁，以其情语守，遂收公文以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1206876_comment'></div>金人欲邀銮舆出郊，议未决，何㮚奏事出，云：「车驾翌日出郊」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1206876_comment'></div>公遽云：「贼意殆不可测，此行恐与前日不同」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1206876_comment'></div>㮚厉声诋公，公又率冯澥共说之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1206876_comment'></div>澥与㮚同乡，齿长，冀幸一听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1206876_comment'></div>㮚不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1206876_comment'></div>及出幸，至北狩，皆如公所料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1206876_comment'></div>金将北去，遣使押公还，时张邦昌僭立已二十馀日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1206876_comment'></div>既归私室，卧病不出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1206876_comment'></div>邦昌屡胁公视事，卒辞之，以死自誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1206876_comment'></div>潜以书遣太学生杨愿、陈抃献今上，会上遣宣赞舍人黄永锡至京师，公因具述围城及遭变始末附以进，遂奔济州迎驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1206876_comment'></div>从至南京，首陈五事：一曰分屯要害，以整兵伍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1206876_comment'></div>二曰疆理新都，以便公私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1206876_comment'></div>三曰甄收人材，驾驭用之，共图勋烈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1206876_comment'></div>四曰恩威并行，叛而讨之，服而舍之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1206876_comment'></div>五曰裂近边之地为数镇，以谨防狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1206876_comment'></div>上嘉纳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1206876_comment'></div>及上即位，赴召，立行事毕，即奏言：「臣比备位枢府，以至宗社失守，乞赐诛殛」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1206876_comment'></div>不许，差内侍押赴都堂依旧供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1206876_comment'></div>是日得伤暑病告假，因上章待罪，明日宣对，面谕曰：「前执政独留卿，又以疾辞，何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1206876_comment'></div>特给假宣医，早晚内侍存问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1206876_comment'></div>连上三章乞致仕，未允，以五月丙申薨于位，享年五十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1206876_comment'></div>讣闻，上为之震悼，赐水银龙脑以敛，仍赙恤其家，许陈乞恩例外特与长子改京秩，敕有司择日临奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1206876_comment'></div>夫人张氏，一再辞免，从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1206876_comment'></div>建炎二年十二月丙辰葬于□□县治东崇安洲先茔之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1206876_comment'></div>初娶郑氏，先公二十四年卒，追封和义郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1206876_comment'></div>再娶张氏，封永嘉郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1206876_comment'></div>长子绅，承事郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1206876_comment'></div>次纶、绂、总，补承奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1206876_comment'></div>女适承事郎罗永，次适将仕郎林次膺，次适进士邓士饶，季未笄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1206876_comment'></div>公天资孝谨，仁施宗族，而义著朋友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1206876_comment'></div>弟轵幼鞠于季父，后复归，公尽以所得赀产与之，不少留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1206876_comment'></div>士贫归之，解衣推食无吝色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1206876_comment'></div>自少刻意力学，知名于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1206876_comment'></div>涖官临政，所至有能称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1206876_comment'></div>更历县道，救荒赈饥，民赖其力多矣，然在公为不足道，故不复缕载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1206876_comment'></div>有《籁鸣集》十五卷，《南行集》十卷，奏议十卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1206876_comment'></div>既葬，其孤不远数舍来请铭，乃为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_135_1206876'>曹氏之先，仍世不逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1206876_comment'></div>潜光于幽，公奋自躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1206876_comment'></div>位卑志豪，言人所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1206876_comment'></div>负罪南迁，随遇而安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1206876_comment'></div>靖康之初，方时多虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1206876_comment'></div>寇骑凭陵，庭论纷如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1206876_comment'></div>天子念公，邦之遗直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1206876_comment'></div>亟命赐还，荐膺显秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1206876_comment'></div>进居宥密，知无不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1206876_comment'></div>奉辞狡窟，全璧而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1206876_comment'></div>天地易位，挺然一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1206876_comment'></div>济流贯河，在污而洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1206876_comment'></div>公之清名，宜载鼎彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1206876_comment'></div>作此铭诗，用广厥垂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1206876_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_149_1206876'>「曹」下原无「公」字，据正文及下篇文例补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_149_1206876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1206876'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_148_1206876_0'>⑴ 《杨龟山先生集》卷三七。又见同治《沙县志》卷七。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1206876_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1206874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206874?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周宪之墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206874")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206874'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206874'>公讳某，字宪之，姓周氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206874_comment'></div>其先本周苗裔，平王东迁，次子烈封汝坟，秦灭周，以汝坟为郡，子孙因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206874_comment'></div>至十八世孙仁为汉太中大夫，徙家阳陵，子孙咸至大官，自汉历唐，世有显人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206874_comment'></div>其后绵远，族众散适他郡，有居处之遂昌者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206874_comment'></div>公之远祖避唐乱，自遂昌徙之浦城，故今为浦城人。<div class='inline'
