id='poem_sentence_62_1206572_comment'></div>王师所过，民被其毒有甚于盗贼，百姓至相谓曰：「宁被盗贼，不愿王师入境」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206572_comment'></div>军无律一至于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206572_comment'></div>此二事最今日之急务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206572_comment'></div>自蔡京用事，王黼、李邦彦继之，祖宗之法扫荡殆尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206572_comment'></div>如尚书省戾祖宗之法者非一二事，冗官之未澄汰，与役法之弊所当损益，未易缕数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206572_comment'></div>然今日二事，在《易》盖《蛊》之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206572_comment'></div>《蛊》之成卦，刚上而柔下，刚柔不交，上下不相与，不足与有为，巽而上无刚健之才，不能以有为，此事之所以蛊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206572_comment'></div>《左传》「皿虫为蛊」，蛊者败坏之象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206572_comment'></div>先王之治蛊也，如治陋室然，欂栌扂楔，各安所施，不易其处，则庶几其苟完矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206572_comment'></div>物物而纷更之，腐者败，倾者不可复支矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206572_comment'></div>夫通变之谓事，因其财而通变之，则蛊元亨而天下治矣，此治蛊之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206572_comment'></div>此二事其大略如此，其委曲措画，在执国柄者详视而审处之，非毫楮可尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206572_comment'></div>夫执中不可以无权，执中无权，犹执一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206572_comment'></div>圣人所谓权者，犹权衡之权，量轻重而取中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206572_comment'></div>用之无铢两之差，则物得其平矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206572_comment'></div>今物有首重而末轻者，执其中而不知权，则物失其平，非所以用中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206572_comment'></div>世人以用智为知权，误矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206572_comment'></div>孟子曰：「所恶于智者，为其凿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1206572_comment'></div>如智若禹之行水，则无恶于智也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1206572_comment'></div>盖禹之行水，循固然之理，行其所无事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1206572_comment'></div>若用智以为权，则皆智之凿，孟子之所恶也，可不慎欤！</div><div id='poem_sentence_83_1206572_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1133')">1132-1133年</a>　在将乐。有文。作品：忠毅向公墓志铭。跋诸公与徐仲车诗册。送严尉。三经义辩。日录辩。字说辩。<div id='poem_1206873' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206873' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206873?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忠毅向公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206873")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206873'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206873'>某年月日，北寇袭陈，余时在行朝，得报，谓同列曰：「陈守向公必死矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206873_comment'></div>为之废寝食者累日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206873_comment'></div>未几讣至，人或问曰：「方今雄藩巨镇拥重兵弃城而遁者踵交于道，陈无高城深池以为阻固，以千百惰羸之卒，当天骄屡胜之兵，虽庸人知其不敌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206873_comment'></div>避其锋而去，宜无不可者，何自而知其必死也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206873_comment'></div>余曰：「公之忠贯白日，非死生祸福能易其操者，其素行然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206873_comment'></div>余以是知之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206873_comment'></div>闻者莫不钦叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206873_comment'></div>其孤将以某年月日葬公于某所某原，以通判潼川府朱震之状来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206873_comment'></div>余告之曰：公之仗节死义有谏臣之章，议行易名有太常之诔，褒赠之典，布在天下，其勋烈不待余言而传也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206873_comment'></div>然公自筮仕以来，所至皆有风绩可书，世人或未知之也，亦不可湮没而无传，乃叙而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206873_comment'></div>公讳子韶，字和卿，故相文简公之曾孙，钦圣宪肃皇太后之再从侄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206873_comment'></div>世为开封人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206873_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，故任国子博士，赠开府仪同三司、守太尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206873_comment'></div>曾祖妣李氏，封太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206873_comment'></div>祖讳某，故任西京左藏库副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206873_comment'></div>祖妣王氏，封太原县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206873_comment'></div>考讳某，故任太中大夫致仕，赠通奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206873_comment'></div>妣夏侯氏，封硕人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206873_comment'></div>公生而有异禀，不妄嬉戏，庄重如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206873_comment'></div>比志学，即游贤关，清约如寒士，人不知其为相门后族之子侄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206873_comment'></div>其强学自励，至焚膏继晷不少懈，同舍相与语曰：「君子之于学也，息焉而后能安其学，君何自苦如是」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206873_comment'></div>公愀然对曰：「家门衰替，敢不彊勉，而自惰乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206873_comment'></div>如永嘉刘安节辈，皆伊川先生之门人，有识致，讶其语，因问之曰：「公家富贵闻天下，二郡王日奉朝请，仕于中外，以材望显者甚众，何谓家门衰替也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206873_comment'></div>公曰：「先丞相事业寂寥久矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206873_comment'></div>安节壮其言，引为忘年交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206873_comment'></div>元符二年，与国学荐，钦圣闻之喜甚，补假承奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206873_comment'></div>三年擢进士第，唱名集英殿，钦圣登紫云楼，密令宦者引公至楼下视之，翌日赐赉有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206873_comment'></div>注保州司法参军，有旨改承事郎，皆特恩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206873_comment'></div>差监在京炭场，会有族人除太府卿，以亲嫌罢，改授签书荆南府节度判官厅公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206873_comment'></div>是时公方冠，初未更事，而练达政体如素官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206873_comment'></div>知荆南马瑊器其才，府事多赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206873_comment'></div>瑊去，董必代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206873_comment'></div>公尝具袍笏，而必以短帽束带见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206873_comment'></div>必为人简严，属吏无敢忤其意者，公移书责之，不少屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206873_comment'></div>秩满，知苏州吴江县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206873_comment'></div>苏人私铸黄钱，流布一路，诸邑听民自便，郡守是之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206873_comment'></div>公独以为不可，为书极言其害，下令禁切之，一县无敢犯者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206873_comment'></div>中司论其事，诏置狱绳故纵之吏，诸邑皆曰：「太守之命也，吴江令尝力争以为不可，书具在」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206873_comment'></div>公闻制使来，自谓理须被逮，即具舟束装以俟，吏及门即行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206873_comment'></div>初，太守意公以抗论不从为功，比公至，卒无一言及太守者，守甚德之，而后信其为仁人君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206873_comment'></div>狱成，自太守而下皆贬秩，公独赏一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206873_comment'></div>其后太守孙公杰召诸邑会议，欲一大保置一鼓楼，保丁五人，以备巡警，盗发则鸣鼓以相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206873_comment'></div>公曰：「一大保二十五家而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206873_comment'></div>如吴江外镇有合境不过五里者，无虑数百家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206873_comment'></div>若二十五家置一楼，则不可胜计矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206873_comment'></div>又以数十人持梃更巡，则其间不无彊悍不逞者递相侵陵，则斗争自兹始矣，不可为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206873_comment'></div>郡守意欲必行之，不从，公持之益坚，逾月不能决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206873_comment'></div>同列厌苦之，谓公曰：「不若禀令而归，到县则措置在我矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206873_comment'></div>公曰：「不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206873_comment'></div>禀令归而不行，则有司得以慢令罪我矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206873_comment'></div>久之，卒如公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206873_comment'></div>大观二年，除开封府右曹参军，明年，转朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206873_comment'></div>李彪欲言蔡京擅权误国，书草具未上，有告其事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206873_comment'></div>丞相何公取旨下彪开封狱，有司谓彪谤讪大臣，欲置之重典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206873_comment'></div>公方初来，力争之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206873_comment'></div>李孝寿尹开封，依违不断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206873_comment'></div>丞相张公用公议，薄彪罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206873_comment'></div>已而京复相，御史论彪狱不当，乃流彪海岛，李孝寿已死，追所赠五官，更追三官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206873_comment'></div>公时已去职监在京进奏院，追三官，停任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206873_comment'></div>四年，叙朝散郎、监保州盐酒税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206873_comment'></div>五年，以建储赦，复朝散大夫、提点信州太霞宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206873_comment'></div>未几除知虢州，不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206873_comment'></div>六年，差主管西京外宗室财用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206873_comment'></div>外宗室之法，未出仕者计口给食，至是有养子以增数者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206873_comment'></div>公与同官高大中论曰：「财用不足，患之细也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206873_comment'></div>蓄养他人子，则本支乱矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206873_comment'></div>公乃建议为之措画，以去其弊，宗室财用以黄河退滩地、淮浙围田及常平赡学所不取者充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206873_comment'></div>案牍隔远，吏缘为奸，隐漏不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206873_comment'></div>公手自翻阅，尽得其情，量入为出，无匮乏之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206873_comment'></div>判外宗正赵士暕常患不及，公笑而不答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206873_comment'></div>他日出其大数，沛然有馀，士暕服其明焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206873_comment'></div>七年移管南京外宗室财用，俄复还旧任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206873_comment'></div>宣和元年，除知虔州，又除知建昌军，未赴，除夔州路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206873_comment'></div>朝廷议罢新开边郡，公条陈利害，请罢溱、播、思、珍四州，反其县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206873_comment'></div>同官谓珍不可废，公争之不能得，乃罢三州，而珍州至今以为不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206873_comment'></div>久之，泸南帅刘亚夫复用夷冉万耍议，请开溪州路南通辰沅，西抵泸戎，置一州二县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206873_comment'></div>诏发潼川府及夔州两路兵输钱粮，辟官属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206873_comment'></div>泸南遣南骑兵至涪州，责钱绢甚急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206873_comment'></div>公率同官王蕃论奏其事，蕃意难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206873_comment'></div>公曰：「若有疑，某自具奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206873_comment'></div>蕃乃同上疏曰：「顷年庞寅孙守夔，创开边隙，是时欲建溪州，冉万耍曰险阻深僻，不可为郡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1206873_comment'></div>今万耍与冉蛮老以仇怨相攻，乃更建议开路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1206873_comment'></div>且路之所经者十有一族，而七族被诱，四族不出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1206873_comment'></div>四族者，蛮老在其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1206873_comment'></div>又有蛮由册一族，以人为粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1206873_comment'></div>彼万耍意在报仇，假官军以杀蛮老耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1206873_comment'></div>且自昔蛮人纳土请置州郡，必先通路创屋，以俟王人官司遣人相视，然后调兵储粮，经理其地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1206873_comment'></div>今请吏者未集，山溪未通，遽遣王师深入不测，是委肉于饿虎之蹊也，事大不便」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1206873_comment'></div>奏方上，而大役已兴矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1206873_comment'></div>郡邑骚动，萧然烦费，人心震恐，识者危之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1206873_comment'></div>公又为书上二府、申御史台，极陈开边徼置州县以蛮夷弊中国之害，争论甚力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1206873_comment'></div>俄得可报，亚夫削官，其役遂罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1206873_comment'></div>夔路廉访使者曹东请筑瞿唐关，乃唐夔州故基也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1206873_comment'></div>山岭越溪谷，楼橹城壁费甚广，请置兵三千屯守，公申尚书省曰：「世乱则守险，世治则去险而居平陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1206873_comment'></div>守险者所以固强圉，居平陆者所以杜觊觎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1206873_comment'></div>故前代割据夔州，附瞿唐关，本朝削平僭乱，丁谓、薛颜乃移夔居鱼腹以就平土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1206873_comment'></div>今无故劳民费财，而起战争，又屯兵于外，太阿倒持，若一夫开关奋臂，则夔州无兵可抗，非久长之利」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1206873_comment'></div>东怒，欲以他事中公，竟不能，而瞿唐关止因其旧而增葺之，卒如公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1206873_comment'></div>六年，使还，入对延和殿，首荐寒士，上皇颔之，曰：「进贤受上赏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1206873_comment'></div>当路阻格之，不报，除知蔡州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1206873_comment'></div>下车，去贪暴，屏巨猾，宽逋负，举下吏可任以事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1206873_comment'></div>然后兴学校，延见儒士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1206873_comment'></div>有县令狃旧例献遗利以入公帑，公判其状付州学养士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1206873_comment'></div>前守计份议开小河泄积水，功大不能就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1206873_comment'></div>公论其非于部使者，曰：「小河浅狭，不足容诸水之入，徒费财力，有害而无利」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1206873_comment'></div>乃罢其役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1206873_comment'></div>八年，主管亳州明道宫，除知徐州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1206873_comment'></div>靖康元年，近臣荐公材堪出使，除京东转运副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1206873_comment'></div>户部尚书聂昌以国用不足，讽诸路进羡馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1206873_comment'></div>知密州郭奉世与昌有旧，进万缗，昌荐诸朝，请赏之，以劝天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1206873_comment'></div>公劾奉世曰：「一路财用，有馀不足相补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1206873_comment'></div>设使密有馀财，当具数闻，部使者通融计会，资兵吏之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1206873_comment'></div>安可不恤大计，不顾他州，进通用之财，徼非道之宠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1206873_comment'></div>不罚奉世，无以惩奸，而主计近臣首开聚敛之端，浸不可长」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1206873_comment'></div>士论韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1206873_comment'></div>于是有旨下京东治其事，会昌入副西枢，故事不竟，奉世罚金而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1206873_comment'></div>山东久苦李彦暴虐，朝廷初罢梁山泺税、燕山夫钱，黜兴利之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1206873_comment'></div>民凋瘵未复，盗贼相煽野聚，公条具民间利病十馀事上之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1206873_comment'></div>丁通奉忧，解官，与诸弟居淮宁府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1206873_comment'></div>会蔡州缺守，州人邀使者马首，愿得公三年，使者上其事，而蔡已除新守矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1206873_comment'></div>乃起复就除知淮宁府，公三拜章乞终丧，不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1206873_comment'></div>公视事六月，寇兵至陈，公率诸弟城守，励战士，开谕百姓，曰：「汝等坟墓之国，去此何之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1206873_comment'></div>吾与汝当以死守之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1206873_comment'></div>城昼夜攻急，公亲擐甲胄，冒矢石，遣其弟子率赴东京留守司乞援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1206873_comment'></div>兵未至，寇益众，城陷，公犹率众巷战，力屈被执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1206873_comment'></div>渠帅坐城，欲降之，酌酒于前，左右按令屈膝，公植立不动，戟手骂之，遂见害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1206873_comment'></div>时年五十，实二年二月二十二日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1206873_comment'></div>有陈掞默记其处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1206873_comment'></div>公弟中奉大夫、新知唐州事子褒，朝请郎子衮，迪功郎子某，皆见害，家已破散，掞入其府，取公诰敕藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1206873_comment'></div>季子鸿六岁，乳母抱去，遇寇兵，夺其母，弃儿井中，有出之者，兵又击之，一夕复活，他日过，复抱藏民家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1206873_comment'></div>后公子沈奔丧，乃得公遗骸并诰敕及鸿以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1206873_comment'></div>后二年，子率守仪真，遣人至淮宁访寻得公季女于民家，时年十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1206873_comment'></div>娶夏侯氏，封令人，先公八年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1206873_comment'></div>男十人，女五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1206873_comment'></div>让，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1206873_comment'></div>混、汋及三女早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1206873_comment'></div>护，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1206873_comment'></div>溥，通仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1206873_comment'></div>涖、溥、瀚及洛、汝为寇骑所掠，未知所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1206873_comment'></div>沈，登仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1206873_comment'></div>鸿以褒典补将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1206873_comment'></div>孙女一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1206873_comment'></div>谏官上疏曰：「臣伏闻去冬夷人入寇，诸路守臣或望风逃遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1206873_comment'></div>杰然以忠义自奋，誓以死守者，陈州之向子韶是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1206873_comment'></div>至城陷，犹率众巷战，与介胄之士同毙于兵革之下，行道之人称颂咨嗟，忠义之士愤发激昂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1206873_comment'></div>愿下明诏褒子韶忠义之节，优加爵秩以旌显之，搜求其后而锡赉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1206873_comment'></div>天下闻风，孰不踊跃奋厉，为陛下尽死节乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1206873_comment'></div>五月二十七日，有旨赠三官四资，本宗有服亲将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1206873_comment'></div>时秀州兵乱，害武功郎、江东西路经制司书写机宜文字辛安宗，有旨赠五官，与六资恩泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1206873_comment'></div>谏官再上疏曰：「今戎事未息，一赏之行，万众观听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1206873_comment'></div>朝廷出于无心，而见闻者妄意轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1206873_comment'></div>又向迩来守土之臣，望风奔避者不可一二数，如子韶城陷犹能身率馀兵巷战致死，诚可载之信史，无愧古人，以励臣节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1206873_comment'></div>一时恩赠，所宜特厚，岂当更居安宗之下」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1206873_comment'></div>于是诏增二资恩泽，特赠通议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1206873_comment'></div>久之，有言「用兵以来，仗节死义者甚少，朝廷所以风励之有未至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1206873_comment'></div>望明诏礼官，凡临难不屈死节昭著者，特赐之谥，使得垂名不朽，亦风励节义之一端也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1206873_comment'></div>太常以公名闻，有旨赐谥「忠毅」，闻者耸然以为效忠义之劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1206873_comment'></div>公为人端悫夷易，不事表暴，一言之出，洞见心膂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1206873_comment'></div>通奉公笃于惇族，公承其志，率诸弟分俸以均给本房之未仕及待阙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1206873_comment'></div>远方珍异，必以时至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1206873_comment'></div>通奉有疾，衣不解带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1206873_comment'></div>与人交，主于忠信，不为浮文末礼，以投众人耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1206873_comment'></div>书尺不过一幅，语严而意尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1206873_comment'></div>所至必与君子长者游，暇则观书，门无杂宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1206873_comment'></div>与人议论匪一，然必反复曲折归于至当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1206873_comment'></div>发为辞章，典雅温厚，有唐词人之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1206873_comment'></div>自始仕，由幕职至县令，退为筦库，进而处刺史二千石，一以诚意为主，不以色辞假人，故居官可纪，去必见思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1206873_comment'></div>至其陷大难，临大节而不可夺，非苟然者，盖其胸中素定也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1206873_comment'></div>高才远识，未究其用，而遽至此，呜呼，命矣夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1206873_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_169_1206873'>狄人侵疆，横流稽天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1206873_comment'></div>取义舍生，维公则然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1206873_comment'></div>秉节不渝，几至覆宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1206873_comment'></div>昊天不闻，罹此鞠凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1206873_comment'></div>季子之幼，亡而复存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1206873_comment'></div>神实相之，将大其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1206873_comment'></div>褒赠之荣，永光窀穸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1206873_comment'></div>忠毅之名，千古无斁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_176_1206873_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋诸公与徐仲车诗册</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206673")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206673'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206673'>余昔过山阳，尝一见先生，侍坐终日，得所未闻多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206673_comment'></div>迨今三十馀年，追念不能忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206673_comment'></div>绍兴二年，其子安道来尉吾邑，一日踵吾门，出诸公与先生往还诗书示余，求言以刻诸石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206673_comment'></div>余谓先生之节义如大圭，不琢而其美自见，非雕绘所能增饰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206673_comment'></div>然诸公皆一时名世之士，其言足以信今传后，而歆慕如此，镂之金石，使百世而下见之，必有闻而兴起者，亦非小补也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1206673_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　在将乐。章才邵来问学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年10月</a>　在将乐。尚书廖刚来问学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　居将乐。胡安国（文定）借公所著书及质正《春秋传》作品：答胡康侯（其五）<div id='poem_1206569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206569?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答胡康侯书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206569")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206569_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206569'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206569'>承示及《春秋事实》，鄙意犹有疑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206569_comment'></div>所论虞氏之史，直书其君之名而不避，载其父母昆弟之恶而不隐，某窃谓四岳称舜之父顽、母嚚、象傲，乃舜在侧微未登庸之时言之，宜若无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206569_comment'></div>周人虽以讳事神而有谥法，然且名之曰幽厉，孝子慈孙百世不能改，则虽有谥，其恶犹不隐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206569_comment'></div>《礼》曰「临文不讳」，故文王名昌，而《雍》之诗曰「克昌厥后」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206569_comment'></div>武王名发，而《小宛》之诗曰「明发不寐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206569_comment'></div>若此类，皆临文不讳也，虽周亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206569_comment'></div>庄公名同，而书「同盟」，僖公名申，而书「戊申」，不可谓从虞史之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206569_comment'></div>「将仲子」、「叔于田」皆刺庄公也，「清人」刺文公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206569_comment'></div>不胜其母而害其弟，诗人以刺庄公，而不及段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206569_comment'></div>使高克将兵久而不召，众散而归，诗人以刺文公而不及克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206569_comment'></div>以庄、文之罪著矣，不待《春秋》书之而后见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206569_comment'></div>鄙意如此，更思之如何。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1206569_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　居将乐。有复文定《春秋》正朔书。作品：答胡康侯（其六）答胡康侯（其七）<div id='poem_1206570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206570?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答胡康侯书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206570")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206570_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206570'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206570'>刘质夫受经于明道、伊川之门积有年矣，其论元年之义详甚，某故未敢轻议其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206570_comment'></div>蒙录示第一段，义非高明不见鄙外，何以得此，幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206570_comment'></div>公之用意精深，非浅陋所能窥其阃奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206570_comment'></div>然意有所疑，义不敢默，姑试言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206570_comment'></div>所谓元者，仁也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206570_comment'></div>仁者，心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206570_comment'></div>《春秋》深明其义，当自贵者始，故治国先正其心，其说似太支离矣，恐改元初无此意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206570_comment'></div>三代正朔如忠、质、文之尚，循环无端，不可增损也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206570_comment'></div>秦以亥为正，失其旨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206570_comment'></div>斗纲之端连贯营室，织女之纪指牵牛之初，以纪日月，故曰星纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206570_comment'></div>五星起其初，日月起其中，其时为冬至，其辰为丑，三代各据一统，明三统常合而迭为首，周环五行之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206570_comment'></div>周据天统，以时言也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206570_comment'></div>商据地统，以辰言也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206570_comment'></div>夏据人统，以人事言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206570_comment'></div>故三代之时，惟夏为正，谓春秋以周正纪事是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206570_comment'></div>正朔必自天子出，改正朔恐圣人不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206570_comment'></div>若谓以夏时冠月，如定公元年冬十月陨霜杀菽，若以夏时言之，则十月陨霜，乃其时也，不足为灾异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206570_comment'></div>周十月乃夏之八月，若以夏时冠月，当曰秋十月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206570_comment'></div>正朔如建子丑是也，虽用夏时月，不可谓改正朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206570_comment'></div>鄙意如此，公试思之如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206570_comment'></div>如未中理，更希疏示，以开未悟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1206570_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206571' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206571?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206571_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206571'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206571'>圣学不明，士志于道者往往汩于世习而不知，虽英才异禀，卒能自拔于流俗者无几也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206571_comment'></div>某尝私窃谓学者之视圣人，其犹射者之于正鹄乎，虽巧力所及，有远近中否之不齐，未有不至于正鹄而可以言射也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206571_comment'></div>士之去圣人或相倍蓰，或相什百，所造固不同，未有不同乎圣人而可以言学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206571_comment'></div>譬之升堂奥者，必得其门而入乃可至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206571_comment'></div>过其藩，望望然去之，则终身不能至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206571_comment'></div>然则至学非难，知所以学为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206571_comment'></div>某愚不自量力之不足也，妄有意焉，思得朋游共学，左右提掖，觊获一游其藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206571_comment'></div>乃今得康侯，盖知衰老之有望也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206571_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　居将乐。有复文定嘱编集《二程先生语录》书。作品：答胡康侯（其八）答胡康侯（其九）答胡康侯（其十）<div id='poem_1206572' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206572' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206572?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答胡康侯书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206572")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206572_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206572'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206572'>承示问政事先后缓急之序，与夫要领所在，某自视昏耄，何足以知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206572_comment'></div>以公积学之久，经纶之业皆素所餍饫者，乃下询于陈腐陋儒，非公不以贤自挟，乐取诸人以为善，何以有此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206572_comment'></div>三复来贶，钦叹无已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206572_comment'></div>然厚意不可以虚辱，试诵其所闻，惟宽明不以僭渎为罪，则万万幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206572_comment'></div>某切观自金人渝盟，河北、淮南诸郡皆非吾有，民物凋弊，赋入无几，军储资用十百于前日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206572_comment'></div>天时地利在今日皆不可恃也，所恃者人和而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206572_comment'></div>方时艰难，不早为之经画，一日有不足，不免暴取于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206572_comment'></div>一失民心，其患有不可胜言者，不得不虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206572_comment'></div>某窃谓当今政事惟理财最为急务，考之先王所谓理财者，非尽笼天下之利而有之也，取之有道，用之有节，各当于义之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206572_comment'></div>取之不以其道，用之不以其节，而不当于义，则非理矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206572_comment'></div>故《周官》以九职任之，而后以九赋歛之，其取之可谓有道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206572_comment'></div>九赋之入，各有所待，如关市之赋以待王之膳服，邦中之赋以待宾客之类是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206572_comment'></div>邦之大用，内府受之，邦之小用，外府受焉，有不可得而侵紊之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206572_comment'></div>冢宰以九式均节之，下至工事刍秣之微，匪颁好用，皆有式焉，虽人主不得而渝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206572_comment'></div>所谓惟王及后、世子不会，特膳服之类而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206572_comment'></div>有不如式，虽有司不会，冢宰得以式论之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206572_comment'></div>世儒以谓至尊不可以法数制之，非正论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206572_comment'></div>夫天之所生，地之所藏，今犹昔也，昔常有馀而今不足，其弊必有在矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206572_comment'></div>朝廷盖未之究也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206572_comment'></div>建隆之初，荆湖、江浙、河东、川、广、福建皆非朝廷有也，所有者惟南京东西数郡而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206572_comment'></div>当五季之乱，干戈日寻，然未尝以用不足为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206572_comment'></div>崇宁以来，承祖宗积累之厚，尺地莫非其有也，一民莫非其臣也，而日以不足为忧，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206572_comment'></div>处之不得其道故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206572_comment'></div>国家景德、皇祐尝为《会计录》以总核天下财赋之出入，百官饩廪之奉、军储边计，凡邦国之经用，皆有常数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206572_comment'></div>如内府所藏以待军兴郊赏之费，茶盐之入以待边储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206572_comment'></div>元丰之《备对》，元祐之《会计》皆放此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206572_comment'></div>此祖宗之遗法，盖得《周官》待用之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206572_comment'></div>今宜为《绍兴会计录》，取祖宗三书参较之，凡吏员之增减，兵旅之多寡，户口之登耗，赋入之盈虚，皆可考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206572_comment'></div>知有馀不足之弊根，可以究见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206572_comment'></div>然后量入以为出而均节之，残破州县使有无相补，庶无阙事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206572_comment'></div>祖宗设制置发运司，盖始于王朴之议，其措画可谓详尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206572_comment'></div>朝廷捐数百万缗以为籴本，使总六路之计，通融移用，与三司相为表里，以给中都之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206572_comment'></div>六路丰凶更有不常，一路岁稔则增籴以充漕计，饥凶去处则罢籴，使输折斛钱而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206572_comment'></div>故上下俱宽，而中都不乏，最为良法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206572_comment'></div>自胡师文以籴本为羡馀以献，发运司拱手无可为者，此直达之议所从起也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206572_comment'></div>既行直达，而盐法随变，其患有不可胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206572_comment'></div>盖转搬与盐法相因以为利，不可偏举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206572_comment'></div>祖宗时荆湖南北、江东西漕米至真阳下卸，即载盐以归，诸路每岁所得盐课无虑数十万缗以充经费，故漕计不乏，则横歛不加于民，而上下裕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206572_comment'></div>自钞盐之法行，盐课悉归榷货，诸路一无所得，故漕计日以不给，而经用不可阙，非出于漕臣之家，亦取诸民而已，此上下所以俱受其弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206572_comment'></div>闽中旧官卖盐每觔二十七文，今民间每觔至百二三十文，细民均被其害，而盗贩所以公行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206572_comment'></div>所谓制置发运与三司相为表里者，盖发运通融六路之计，钱谷银绢之类，视三司所阙者为之应辨，故中都常不阙也，其为利多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206572_comment'></div>自黄帝立丘乘之法以寓军政，历世因之，未之有改也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206572_comment'></div>至周为尤详，居则为比闾族党州乡，出则为五两军师之制，使之相保相受，刑罚庆赏相及，用一律也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206572_comment'></div>天子无事，岁三田以供祭祀宾客，充君之庖而已，其事宜若缓而不切也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206572_comment'></div>而王执路鼓亲临之，教以坐作进退，有不用命者，则刑戮随之，其教习之严如此，故六乡之兵出则无不胜，以其威令素行故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206572_comment'></div>丘井之废久矣，兵农不可以复合，而伍两军师之制不可不讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206572_comment'></div>无事之时使之相保相受，刑罚庆赏相及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206572_comment'></div>用之于有事之际，则申之以束伍之令，督之旌旗指挥之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206572_comment'></div>临难而不相救，见敌而不用命，必戮无赦，使士卒畏我而不畏敌，然后可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206572_comment'></div>若夫伍法不修，虽有百万之师，如养骄子，不可用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206572_comment'></div>《传》曰：「秦之善士不可当齐、晋之节制，齐、晋之节制不可以当汤、武之仁义」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206572_comment'></div>某窃谓虽有仁义之兵，苟无节制，亦不可以取胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206572_comment'></div>《甘誓》曰：「左不攻于左，汝不恭命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206572_comment'></div>右不攻于右，汝不恭命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206572_comment'></div>弗用命则孥戮女」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206572_comment'></div>《牧誓》曰：「不愆于六步七步，乃止，齐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206572_comment'></div>不愆于四伐五伐，乃止，齐焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206572_comment'></div>其节制之严盖如此，故圣人著之于经，以为后世法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206572_comment'></div>故诸葛孔明曰：「有制之兵，无能之将，不可以败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206572_comment'></div>无制之兵，有能之将，不可以胜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206572_comment'></div>此之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206572_comment'></div>夫军政不修无甚于今日，闽中盗贼初啸聚不过数百而已，其后猖獗如此，盖王师养成其祸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206572_comment'></div>贼在建安几二年，无一人一骑至贼境者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206572_comment'></div>王师所过，民被其毒有甚于盗贼，百姓至相谓曰：「宁被盗贼，不愿王师入境」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206572_comment'></div>军无律一至于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206572_comment'></div>此二事最今日之急务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206572_comment'></div>自蔡京用事，王黼、李邦彦继之，祖宗之法扫荡殆尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206572_comment'></div>如尚书省戾祖宗之法者非一二事，冗官之未澄汰，与役法之弊所当损益，未易缕数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206572_comment'></div>然今日二事，在《易》盖《蛊》之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206572_comment'></div>《蛊》之成卦，刚上而柔下，刚柔不交，上下不相与，不足与有为，巽而上无刚健之才，不能以有为，此事之所以蛊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206572_comment'></div>《左传》「皿虫为蛊」，蛊者败坏之象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206572_comment'></div>先王之治蛊也，如治陋室然，欂栌扂楔，各安所施，不易其处，则庶几其苟完矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206572_comment'></div>物物而纷更之，腐者败，倾者不可复支矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206572_comment'></div>夫通变之谓事，因其财而通变之，则蛊元亨而天下治矣，此治蛊之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206572_comment'></div>此二事其大略如此，其委曲措画，在执国柄者详视而审处之，非毫楮可尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206572_comment'></div>夫执中不可以无权，执中无权，犹执一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206572_comment'></div>圣人所谓权者，犹权衡之权，量轻重而取中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206572_comment'></div>用之无铢两之差，则物得其平矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206572_comment'></div>今物有首重而末轻者，执其中而不知权，则物失其平，非所以用中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206572_comment'></div>世人以用智为知权，误矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206572_comment'></div>孟子曰：「所恶于智者，为其凿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1206572_comment'></div>如智若禹之行水，则无恶于智也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1206572_comment'></div>盖禹之行水，循固然之理，行其所无事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1206572_comment'></div>若用智以为权，则皆智之凿，孟子之所恶也，可不慎欤！</div><div id='poem_sentence_83_1206572_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206573' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206573' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206573?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206573_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206573'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206573'>伊川先生语录，在念未尝忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206573_comment'></div>但以兵火散失，收拾未聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206573_comment'></div>旧日惟罗仲素编集备甚，今仲素已死于道途，行李亦遭贼火，已托人于其家寻访，若得五六，亦便下手矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206573_comment'></div>和卿志文深愧鄙拙，不足以发扬其美，蒙公见与，可以塞责矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206573_comment'></div>《三经义辨》已成书，俟脱藁即附去，以求参订也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206573_comment'></div>近因伤冷，嗽大作，累日不能兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206573_comment'></div>昨日方稍平，然饮食犹未复常，倦甚，作书不及一一。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206573_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206574' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206574' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206574?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206574_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206574'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206574'>荆公黜王爵，罢配享，谓其所论多邪说，取怨于其徒多矣，此《三经义辨》盖不得已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206574_comment'></div>如《日录》、《字说》亦有少论著，然此事不易为，更须朋友参订之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206574_comment'></div>今粗已成书，更俟审详脱稿，即缮写附去也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1206574_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　居将乐。作文。作品：与李丞相书（其一）与李丞相书（其二）邹公侍郎奏议序。与邹德久书（其一）与邹德久书（其二）答曾元忠书（其一）答曾元忠书（其二）答曾元忠书（其三）枢密郑公墓志铭。曾文昭公行述。南剑州陈谏议祠堂记。<div id='poem_1206613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206613?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与李丞相书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206613")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206613_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206613'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206613'>两日前得胡康侯书，备闻湖湘事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206613_comment'></div>自马友等四寇继至，截留税数，不以上供，又重加裒刻，剥民肤髓，官吏残贼布满州县，皆欲变为盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206613_comment'></div>及公到部，按治大奸赃数辈，稍选令佐，严禁科歛，奉行朝廷法令，遵守不违，百姓始知上有天台之尊，下有州郡之体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206613_comment'></div>初抚三路，檄鼎帅进兵讨杨么，潭兵先入，已破数寨，吕宪书云「有破竹之势」矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206613_comment'></div>后闻有旨，鼎不受节制，贼复炽，湖湘之民深以为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206613_comment'></div>钧旆既东还，去思日甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206613_comment'></div>功名之会，自古所难，在公为不足道，重为朝廷惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206613_comment'></div>相望数舍，无由面对，区区书不能究。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206613_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206614?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206614'>昔公在朝，威望隐然如长城，民恃以无恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206614_comment'></div>比年以来，世路日艰棘，毒流四方，淮浙为甚，延及吾闽，盗贼蜂起，无得宁息者，良可骇叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206614_comment'></div>钧旆南还，士论以为天意必有在，宇内共庆，非特小邑之私喜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206614_comment'></div>行遂参觐，他须面承乃究。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206614_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206649?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邹公侍郎奏议序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206649")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206649'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206649'>道乡邹公自少以道学行义知名于时，其为人也，和顺积中，而英华发外，望之睟然见于颜面，不问知其为仁人君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206649_comment'></div>其遇事接物犹虚舟，然而坚挺之姿如精金良玉，不可磨磷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206649_comment'></div>元符中，用侍臣之荐擢居谏垣，从人望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206649_comment'></div>是时哲宗皇帝厉精求治，用贤如不及，一见即以公辅期之，嘉言入告，无不从者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206649_comment'></div>适中宫虚位之久，大臣欲自结于嬖昵之私，为保位之谋，迎意媚合，不以正，公力言之，以为公议不允，忤上旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206649_comment'></div>奸谀之徒恶其害己，相与协力挤之于陷阱之中，又下石焉，皆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206649_comment'></div>公之章留中不下，乃伪为之，加以诋诬不实之语<span class='inlineComment2'>（如取他人之子而杀其母之类。）</span>，流布中外，欲天下闻之，真若有罪者，其为谋深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206649_comment'></div>虽有端人正士，无敢为公辩明者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206649_comment'></div>公既殁迨今二十馀年，昔之奸朋凋丧略尽，而正论行焉，真伪是非始有在矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206649_comment'></div>绍兴三年，其子柄集公之奏议一编，属余为叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206649_comment'></div>余于公非一朝燕游之好也，知公为尤详，其事之本末皆余所亲闻见者，故详著之，以昭示来世，庶乎使小人知君子之为善，终不可诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206649_comment'></div>公之将亡，余适还自京师，闻公疾革，未及弛担即驰往省之，见其薾然仅存馀息，然语不及私，犹以国事为问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206649_comment'></div>盖其平生以天下之重为己任，至垂绝而不忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206649_comment'></div>每追念及之，怆然不能释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206649_comment'></div>呜呼，世道凋丧久矣，不复有斯人也！</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1206649_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206594?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与邹德久书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206594")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206594'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206594'>先公奏议序纳去，鄙拙不足以发扬盛德，负愧多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206594_comment'></div>闻令弟欲令福唐镂板传之久远，甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206594_comment'></div>然其间有弹击权要，今子孙恐有当路者，见之遂为世仇，不可不虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206594_comment'></div>如欧公有从谏，正谓此耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206594_comment'></div>若镂板可节去弹击之章，未须传也，公更思之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1206594_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206595?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206595'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206595'>相别之久，特蒙枉顾，殊慰倾企。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206595_comment'></div>非笃于情义，何以有此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206595_comment'></div>间违忽复累月，比日不审为况何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206595_comment'></div>伏惟燕休，德履佳胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206595_comment'></div>江北虽屡有捷报，而所传不一，殊令人忧疑不解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206595_comment'></div>向承欲还毗陵，果成行否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206595_comment'></div>近得小子适十月书云：城中人皆窜伏乡下，北寇犹未退，听天兵往来，六飞亲行，恐常、润之人未得奠枕而居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206595_comment'></div>世事如此，奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206595_comment'></div>末由会集，切冀以时保啬。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1206595_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206582' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206582' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206582?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答曾元忠书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206582")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206582_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206582'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206582'>先公道学行义，为世儒宗，嘉言谠议，著在天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206582_comment'></div>过蒙以行述见属，文鄙意陋，不足以发扬盛美，方自愧恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206582_comment'></div>复承赐翰，重加奖与，伏读汗颜，无所容措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206582_comment'></div>相望南北，无由展奉区区，书不能究。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206582_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206583' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206583' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206583?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206583_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206583'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206583'>自还乡，盗贼蜂起，两年避地奔窜，未尝一日安居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206583_comment'></div>敝乡今岁方稍宁息，江西山党未有悛心，时有窃发者出没境上，居民不无惊扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206583_comment'></div>虔寇未平，而此月初间建昌复兵叛，闭城焚劫南丰，县官骨肉与邑人多遁至建宁县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206583_comment'></div>昨日或传已就招安，未知是否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206583_comment'></div>敝邑已遣人往探问，更数日必有的耗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206583_comment'></div>此曹非剿灭之，无以惩后，若只招安，如养骄子，少不如意，则复思乱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206583_comment'></div>世路如此，奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206583_comment'></div>秋暑尚炽，更切对时珍啬，前膺召擢，慰此颂望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206583_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206584' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206584' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206584?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206584_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206584'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206584'>先公行述，寡陋不足以发扬德美，负愧多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206584_comment'></div>遗稿为诸子收去，今皆不在家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206584_comment'></div>示谕有脱漏处，公可自以意添入；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206584_comment'></div>或他有未安处，亦当以意损益之，无害，吾徒不必为形迹之嫌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206584_comment'></div>此文欲传远，不可草草，幸照亮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1206584_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206877' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206877' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206877?labeling=true' target='_blank'>枢密郑公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206877")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206877_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206877'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206877'>建炎三年七月戊子，枢密郑公薨于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206877_comment'></div>其子玙将以绍兴三年十一月乙巳葬公于建州城卫紫芝山，以书属予铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206877_comment'></div>予与公昆弟游非一日也，义不得辞，乃序而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206877_comment'></div>公讳瑴，字致刚，姓郑氏，其先光州固始人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206877_comment'></div>唐僖宗时避乱从王潮入闽，居建城南乡之龙池，故今为建州人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206877_comment'></div>其上世皆晦迹不仕，至公之皇考宣奉公始以词学擅名乡邦，励诸子以学，相继登科，皆有闻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206877_comment'></div>公其季子也，政和八年以贡士第，除安陆教官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206877_comment'></div>待次权尉于信阳，用捕盗功改承务郎、监南康酒税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206877_comment'></div>中司陆德先、侍御史郑滋荐为御史台主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206877_comment'></div>金人入寇，中都失守，上以元帅总戎于济濮，公挺身归之，从至南都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206877_comment'></div>上即位除监察御史，明年被上旨，治嘉兴狱回，称旨，迁司谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206877_comment'></div>累章乞移跸金陵，控大江以为阻，因忤大臣意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206877_comment'></div>事虽不行，上深知之，迁谏议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206877_comment'></div>明年，金人复犯维扬，公扈从渡江，上面谕曰：「不用卿言，以至此」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206877_comment'></div>及驻跸钱塘，苗傅、刘正彦逆乱，以上为睿圣皇帝，册皇太子即位，公庭立面折之，不能夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206877_comment'></div>私窃谓逆贼凶焰炽甚，非结外援无可为者，乃上章待罪求去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206877_comment'></div>将北走平江、金陵，与吕颐浩等议兴复计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206877_comment'></div>太后降诏不允，迁中司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206877_comment'></div>二凶窃威福之柄，肆行杀戮，日至都堂侵秉机政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206877_comment'></div>公谓，便宜军法，行之所部士卒可也，馀当闻诸朝廷，付之有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206877_comment'></div>都堂国论所从出，非外迁之臣可得而与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206877_comment'></div>抗章力言之，乞告示傅等宜一遵典法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206877_comment'></div>章留中不下，公对，恳请降付三省施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206877_comment'></div>「乱臣虽以横逆加，臣死职，不当避也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206877_comment'></div>章下，傅等果出怨言，然亦少戢矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206877_comment'></div>又闻以佥书枢密召吕颐浩，以礼部尚书召张浚，分张浚兵，令以五百人归陕西，而浚不受尚书之召，亦不肯分所部兵，遂谪浚以散官居郴州，擢俊以节度知凤翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206877_comment'></div>公知出傅等奸谋，假朝命使外无彊兵谋臣，内生变乱，得以自肆，遂具章乞留吕颐浩知金陵，浚不当谪降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206877_comment'></div>即遣官更姓名微服为贾人，徒步如平江见张浚等，具言城中事，合严设兵备，张声势，持重缓进，使其自遁，无致城中之变，惊动三宫，此为上策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206877_comment'></div>浚等闻知，皆感激奋励，为赴难计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206877_comment'></div>又忽宣诏以上为皇太弟、天下兵马大元帅，幼主为皇太侄监国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206877_comment'></div>公震恐不知所为，即与大臣进议，以为：「在廷公卿百司郡吏皆昔之臣属也，今则与之比肩事主矣，稽之于古则无所取法，行之于今则实逆天道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206877_comment'></div>或者谓为大元帅可以任军旅之大事，臣窃以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206877_comment'></div>昔舜之禅禹也，犹命禹徂征有苗，则禹虽受禅，而征伐之事舜犹亲之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206877_comment'></div>唐之睿宗传位皇太子以听小事，自尊为太上皇以听大事，如是无不可者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206877_comment'></div>则稽之于古为有法，行之于今为得宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206877_comment'></div>太后依旧垂帘同听政，以安人心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206877_comment'></div>其命遂已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206877_comment'></div>既而义师西向，上复位，公之力为多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206877_comment'></div>遂除佥书枢密院事，上降御笔手诏奖谕，有「景想节义」之言，其事可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206877_comment'></div>车驾既还建康，留公弹压，谓左右曰：「郑某兵民所信爱，故令护太后驾，须其至，将国任焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206877_comment'></div>其忠义结二圣之知盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206877_comment'></div>公自春徂夏，夙夜尽瘁，至忘寝食，因感暑湿，得腹疾四日，上犹令赴省议事，疾甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206877_comment'></div>有旨宣医，不效，遂不起，享年五十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206877_comment'></div>讣闻，上嗟惜久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206877_comment'></div>前一日皇太子薨，上顾谓大臣曰：「朕丧元子犹能自排遣，郑某讣至，殆不能释也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206877_comment'></div>褒赠之典皆度越夷等，特赐田十顷，居室五十间，以抚其孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206877_comment'></div>曾大父讳仁顺，大父讳嵩，以公贵，赠正奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206877_comment'></div>父镇，故任登仕郎，赠宣奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206877_comment'></div>母游氏，赠普安郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206877_comment'></div>娶张氏，朝奉大夫微之女，封齐安郡夫人，有贤行，配公无违德，闺阁之内雍如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206877_comment'></div>公将葬，夫人以九月丁卯卒于建安之私第，享年五十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206877_comment'></div>男二人：长曰玙，承务郎、佥书邵武军判官厅公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206877_comment'></div>次曰琪，承奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206877_comment'></div>孙曰继祖，承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206877_comment'></div>皆尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206877_comment'></div>公于艰危中，荐历台谏，章数十上，皆人所难言者，非安危所系，皆略而不言，著其大节而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206877_comment'></div>事之本末，于公自叙之章可以槩见，有旨章告中外，不可诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206877_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1206877'>烈烈郑公，逢时多艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206877_comment'></div>徇国忘身，为世大闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206877_comment'></div>抗言于庭，妖凶屏息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206877_comment'></div>天位复常，繄公之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206877_comment'></div>守节不渝，载之宸翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206877_comment'></div>大哉王言，炳若星焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206877_comment'></div>弗磨弗切，惟石之坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206877_comment'></div>刻铭幽宫，万世之传。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1206877_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206846?labeling=true' target='_blank'>曾文昭公行述</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206846")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206846_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206846'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206846'>公讳肇，字子开，建昌军南丰县人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206846_comment'></div>曾氏系出于鄫，少康之子曲列之始封也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206846_comment'></div>更夏、商、周千有馀岁，微不见于经传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206846_comment'></div>春秋之际，为莒所灭，其太子巫仕鲁，乃去邑为曾氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206846_comment'></div>巫生阜，阜生晰，晰生参，参生元、西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206846_comment'></div>父子俱为孔门高弟，曾氏遂有闻于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206846_comment'></div>自是复晦而不显，又千有馀岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206846_comment'></div>至宋兴，公之皇祖密公始以文学仕太宗、真宗为名臣，于时荐登膴仕者，代不乏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206846_comment'></div>至公又以文学登进士第，调台州黄岩县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206846_comment'></div>邵安简公闻其贤，请为州学教授，四方之士盖有闻风重道接踵至者，蹐门授经无虚席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206846_comment'></div>是时上方向用儒臣，欲以经术造士，近臣言公经行宜居首善之地，不宜淹留一郡，有旨延和殿赐对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206846_comment'></div>公所陈皆上所欲闻者，酬问久之，殆将更仆矣，除崇文校书兼国子直讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206846_comment'></div>未几迁馆阁校勘，删定《九域志》，改大理寺丞，同知太常礼院，权判太仆寺、殿中省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206846_comment'></div>元丰元年，除集贤校理，转殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206846_comment'></div>久之，上读公所撰《曾鲁公行状》，称善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206846_comment'></div>会修仁宗、英宗两朝正史，乃以公为国史院编修官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206846_comment'></div>中书公巩入判太常，以亲嫌罢礼官，判登闻鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206846_comment'></div>自秦以来，礼文残缺，先儒各以臆说，无所稽据，公在职多所釐正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206846_comment'></div>亲祠皇地祇于北郊，盖自公发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206846_comment'></div>虽众议不同，而公独引经辨析，词旨精悫，故异论莫能夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206846_comment'></div>其议明堂配享遍及五帝，初虽不合，后亦卒见施用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206846_comment'></div>官制行，除吏部郎中，每便殿引选人，上常目送之出殿门乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206846_comment'></div>再迁朝奉郎，与修两朝宝训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206846_comment'></div>国史成，锡宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206846_comment'></div>故事，非侍从官不坐殿上，特命进公，其眷遇之厚，盖示将用公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206846_comment'></div>未几，丁太夫人忧，居丧哀毁瘠甚，年未四十，髭发尽变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206846_comment'></div>服除，入为户部郎中，复还吏部，迁右司郎中，覃恩赐绯衣银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206846_comment'></div>哲宗嗣位，宣仁太后垂帘听政，用司马温公、吕申公为宰相，士多傅时自效，公独挺然不为世变所移，由是诸公益贤之，知其有常德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206846_comment'></div>以公先帝史官，故命公充《神宗实录》检讨官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206846_comment'></div>擢起居舍人兼权中书舍人，数月，召试即真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206846_comment'></div>迁实录修撰，赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206846_comment'></div>初除未拜命书，会除叶康直直龙图阁、知秦州，公即上疏论康直素不闻有可用之材，昨在陕西，随军失亡为多，先帝常命械系，欲诛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206846_comment'></div>康直谄事李宪，卒赖以免，其人可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206846_comment'></div>正当黜退，以章先帝之明，岂可更加奖擢？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206846_comment'></div>执政讶不先白，言者承望协力攻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206846_comment'></div>范公纯仁在枢府，语人曰：「善人不见容，则纯仁辈不可居此矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206846_comment'></div>诸公知公议所与，咸为之言，章请外，五上不听，乃出视事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206846_comment'></div>门下侍郎韩公维面奏范百禄所为不正，及有非理事十馀件，帘中怒甚，以为辅臣奏劾臣僚，当公行具章疏明论曲直，既无明文，何异谗毁，黜知邓州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206846_comment'></div>公不草制，两上章论之，曰：「维执政，为朝廷别白邪正是非，真得大臣体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206846_comment'></div>虽案牍不具，出于口奏，岂可便谓之欺君？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206846_comment'></div>大臣参与国论，臧否人物，不必一切须形文字，顾所言当与不当，行之人心服与不服耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206846_comment'></div>今陛下责维徒口奏而已，遂谓有欺君之意，臣恐命下之日，人心眩惑，谓陛下以疑似之罪逐大臣，恐于陛下盛德不为无损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206846_comment'></div>执政大臣自此以维为戒，无敢开口论议臧否人物，君臣上下更为形迹，恐非陛下推赤心待大臣之谊，亦非大臣展布四体以事陛下之道也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206846_comment'></div>竟以他舍人行下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206846_comment'></div>事虽不从，士论韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206846_comment'></div>谏官王觌言执政，忤旨，落职知润州，公封还词头，言：「觌之一身出入内外，不足为重轻，而陛下寄腹心于大臣，寄耳目于台谏，二者相须，不可阙一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206846_comment'></div>今觌一言论及执政，即日去之，是何异爱腹心，涂耳目，岂不殆哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206846_comment'></div>上悟，加觌直龙图阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206846_comment'></div>三省议更科举，公独建议，以谓：「三代两汉人材之盛，风俗之美，后世莫能及者，取士以行，不专以言故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206846_comment'></div>今虽诏内外官举经明行脩之士，中第之日优其恩典，不独取之以言，又本其行，庶乎近古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206846_comment'></div>然徒使举之，而不由乡里之选，又无考察之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206846_comment'></div>与斯举者随众牒试于有司，糊名誊录，校一日之长，不惟士失自重之义，且于课试之际，无以别异于众人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206846_comment'></div>则所谓本其行者，亦徒虚文而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206846_comment'></div>谓宜别立一科，稍仿三代两汉取士官人之法，因今之宜，斟酌损益，要之无失古意而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206846_comment'></div>至于投牒乞试、糊名誊录之数，非古制者，一切罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206846_comment'></div>待遇恩数，尽居词赋经义等科之上，庶使学者尊经术，惇行义，人人笃于自修，则人材不盛，风俗不美，未之有也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206846_comment'></div>太皇太后受册，有司检用章献明肃太后故事，当御文德殿，奏疏曰：「伏见太皇太后听政以来，止于延和殿垂帘视事，受契丹人使朝见，亦止御崇政殿，未尝出践外朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206846_comment'></div>盖外朝天子之正宁，太皇太后崇执谦德，不欲临御，以为天下后世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206846_comment'></div>推此言之，受册外朝，殆非太皇太后之意，特以故事当然耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206846_comment'></div>窃详故事，天圣二年两制定皇太后受册于崇仁殿，仁宗自出圣意，特诏有司改文德殿，此盖人主一时之制，非典法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206846_comment'></div>愿下明诏，屈从天圣二年两制之议，受册于崇政殿，仰称太皇太后克己复礼、谦恭抑损之盛德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206846_comment'></div>中批令学士院降诏，如公所请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206846_comment'></div>是岁坤成节，礼官建议于崇政殿上寿，其升殿赐酒并文武百官拜表班次，并用天圣三年故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206846_comment'></div>三省枢密院时降朝旨，不全用天圣三年故事及有司之议，乃引九年会庆殿上寿如乾元节之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206846_comment'></div>公奏疏曰：「太皇太后昨降诏书，以谓不敢自同章献太后，今此举似与前后本末不相称，殆非太皇太后之意，特执政大臣出于不思耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206846_comment'></div>疏入，从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206846_comment'></div>公之画规，太母之听言，前古靡俪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206846_comment'></div>非主圣臣直，宁有是夫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206846_comment'></div>皇太妃亲属有韦城县民侯称者，负官钱，内批特与宽展纳钱年限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206846_comment'></div>公言：「此在县官事至微末，恐不足以上烦诏旨，以启倖门」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206846_comment'></div>又言：「近日颇有干求内降特与差遣者，此虽未足仰累二圣大公至正之德，窃恐侥倖之人转相扳援，烦渎圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206846_comment'></div>杜渐防微，宜自今日」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206846_comment'></div>仍录仁宗戒敕内降入条以进，乞置之座右，少助省览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206846_comment'></div>奉使契丹回，道过雄、瀛二州，百姓各经国信使副陈述役法不便事，公言：「臣于役法本不详知，乞明诏有司，更加考察，不惮增改，归于便民而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206846_comment'></div>昔在熙宁中，更定役法，臣兄布实与其事，臣今言之，不为无嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206846_comment'></div>但承乏从官将出使，亲见二州之民有所陈述，不敢顾避隐默为自全计也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206846_comment'></div>又言：「臣以使事还至河北，闻朝廷命王孝先开孙村口，回河东流，复故道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206846_comment'></div>及见运使谢卿材言河流稍入地中，无可回之理，但当闭塞支流，纵之北去，正是行其所无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206846_comment'></div>卿材尝画八事闻于朝，简易明白，似有可采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206846_comment'></div>乞下水官及河北监司公共讲求，及卿材所陈利害，孰为得失，具奏朝廷，择其善者断而行之，庶使论议早定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206846_comment'></div>继闻召都水使者王孝先、河北转运使谢卿材、判官张景先赴三省询究利害，而三人所论不同，朝廷未敢臆决，遣官行视，然诏书但令相度孙村口有无未及利害，如孙村口不可修，即于不近界河踏逐一处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1206846_comment'></div>则是虽曰遣官行视，而必欲回河之意已先定于庙堂之上矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1206846_comment'></div>然则遣二近臣，从数十官吏衔命而出，不知果何为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1206846_comment'></div>及二近臣还奏，如卿材说，遂出孝先知曹州，徙景先陕西路，公力疏其罪，执政不得已，为之改命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1206846_comment'></div>至绍圣初，时论益主东流，而河回辄决，公私受弊，卒如公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1206846_comment'></div>秦王后止袭公爵，诏有司议所当立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1206846_comment'></div>公言：「诸侯有国，子孙以嫡相承，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1206846_comment'></div>况承亮先朝所立，传国再世，可复议移夺乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1206846_comment'></div>四年春，旱甚，中丞李公常请罢春宴，执政难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1206846_comment'></div>公率彭公汝砺上疏曰：「天灾方作，民食未充，正君臣侧身畏惧忧恤百姓之时，乃相与饮食燕乐，恐无以消复天变，导迎和气」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1206846_comment'></div>翼日有旨罢宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1206846_comment'></div>二公在朝，论事数与时忤，至是浸不容矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1206846_comment'></div>当是时，丞相范公纯仁、左丞王公存论议多是与二公合，异意者欲尽去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1206846_comment'></div>会有以蔡丞相确安州诗上者，谏官交章以为谤讪，谪新州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1206846_comment'></div>范、王二公争之不能得，同时罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1206846_comment'></div>先是，公与彭公约，当制者必极论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1206846_comment'></div>会公除给事中，未拜，彭公当制，言甚力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1206846_comment'></div>谏官多前日与公论异者，言彭公实公使之，诬以卖友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1206846_comment'></div>公不自辨，固辞新命请外，章四上，除宝文阁待制、知颍州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1206846_comment'></div>明年徙齐州，未至，改陈州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1206846_comment'></div>在颍，浚清河百馀里，以通东南物货，人至今赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1206846_comment'></div>部使者议开八丈沟，疏陈、蔡积水，颍人素以为患，公拒其议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1206846_comment'></div>使者以语訹公，公复移书折之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1206846_comment'></div>及徙陈，执论益坚，人于是知公非私于一州也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1206846_comment'></div>越明年，移知应天府兼南京留守司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1206846_comment'></div>守当东南孔道，士大夫舟车衔尾，结辙而至，平时宴劳无虚日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1206846_comment'></div>公曰：「饰厨传以邀往来之誉，吾不为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1206846_comment'></div>乃积公帑之馀，大兴学校，亲加训导，养成人材为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1206846_comment'></div>居数月，除中书舍人，命格不下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1206846_comment'></div>七年秋还朝，守尚书礼部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1206846_comment'></div>是岁哲宗初祀南郊，有诏合祭天地，如祖宗故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1206846_comment'></div>公守前议论之，语甚厉，不报，乃拜章自劾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1206846_comment'></div>徙刑部，不拜，请去不已，降知徐州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1206846_comment'></div>在徐数月，徙知江宁府兼江南东路兵马钤辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1206846_comment'></div>绍圣初徙知瀛州，充高阳关路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1206846_comment'></div>哲宗既亲政，追用旧臣，尽复熙丰之法，数称公议礼有守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1206846_comment'></div>及公入对，口不及垂帘事，所陈皆国家大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1206846_comment'></div>尝谓：「人主虽有自然之圣质，必赖左右前后皆得其人，以为立政之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1206846_comment'></div>唐太宗平定四方，有志治道，时引虞世南等聚于禁中，号十八学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1206846_comment'></div>退朝之暇，从容燕见，咨询无倦，或至夜分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1206846_comment'></div>是以后世言治独称贞观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1206846_comment'></div>臣谓宜于此时慎选忠信端良博古多闻之士，置诸左右，以参谋议，以备顾问，与夫深处法宫之中，亲近亵狎之徒，其损益相去万万矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1206846_comment'></div>忤贵近意，故不得留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1206846_comment'></div>是时，元祐诸公皆流窜岭表，最后谪前史官范祖禹等，以实录讥讪为罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1206846_comment'></div>初，实录成，公与陆佃、林希以尝在属，例转一官，公奏「臣不逮成书，不可因人之功以叨赏典」，累辞不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1206846_comment'></div>至是，希为中书舍人，纳所迁官，在职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1206846_comment'></div>公耻自陈以觊幸免，遂与佃俱夺一官，降小郡，以公知滁州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1206846_comment'></div>御史言希不当与公异，佃与奏书，不当与公同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1206846_comment'></div>仍削佃职，除公集贤殿修撰，守滁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1206846_comment'></div>岁满，除知泰州，又二年徙海州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1206846_comment'></div>元符三年，上皇即位，钦圣太后权同听断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1206846_comment'></div>一日，二府奏事，帘中宣谕曰：「先帝在宫中，尝称曾某可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1206846_comment'></div>鲁公为枢密，实与闻之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1206846_comment'></div>先帝谓神宗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1206846_comment'></div>召还，除中书舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1206846_comment'></div>即日请对，言：「治道在广言路而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1206846_comment'></div>祖宗以来，数诏百官，使以次对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1206846_comment'></div>神宗举而行之，于熙宁之初，以兴起事功，为后世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1206846_comment'></div>愿陛下迹神考之故事，修转对之制，下不讳之令，明诏百官，下及民庶，得极言时政，无有所隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1206846_comment'></div>然后择其善者而行之，且报之以赏，大则加以爵秩，小则锡之金帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1206846_comment'></div>其言不足采，若狂妄牴牾者，一切置之，不以为罪，庶以鼓动天下敢言之气」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1206846_comment'></div>会日蚀四月朔，故事当降诏求直言，特命公草诏，因具著所以言于上者，敷告中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1206846_comment'></div>于是投匦者日以千数，故上得尽闻天下事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1206846_comment'></div>大臣有欲害公者，未有以发，乃改公所撰孔平仲复官制词，著平仲讥讪先烈之罪，激之使自辨，因以挤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1206846_comment'></div>公录二词白上，言：「陛下既赦其罪，俱当明著圣恩叙复之意，不必更载前来贬谪之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1206846_comment'></div>万一可用用之，如不可用，则臣为不称职，即乞罢中书舍人职事，以允公议」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1206846_comment'></div>上察其非罪，促令赴省供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1206846_comment'></div>及对，慰谕久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1206846_comment'></div>元祐士大夫再以赦甄叙，或复旧职，典方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1206846_comment'></div>公奏：「生者蒙恩已厚矣，唯是游魂枯骴未蒙圣泽，死而有知，岂得无望？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1206846_comment'></div>请如寇准、曹利用故事，检会臣寮昨已死被追贬，或贬死未经叙复者，还其所夺官职及本蒙恩泽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1206846_comment'></div>又乞如祖宗朝，每大赦后置看详编配罪人一司，命官典领，使流窜废锢之人均被恩施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1206846_comment'></div>皆见纳用，由是上恩溥及存没矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1206846_comment'></div>累迁朝请大夫，擢翰林学士、知制诰，又数月，兼侍读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1206846_comment'></div>上尝从容谓公曰：「卿学术在廷无过之者，非玉堂之上不可以处卿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1206846_comment'></div>公顿首谢，因言：「近世帝王善为治者，莫如唐太宗，善言治者莫如唐陆贽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1206846_comment'></div>太宗贞观之治，论者谓庶几成、康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1206846_comment'></div>史官掇其大者，别为一书，谓之《贞观政要》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1206846_comment'></div>陆贽事唐德宗，知无不言，言无不尽，要其归必本于帝王之道，必稽于六艺之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1206846_comment'></div>此二书，一代之文章，实百王之龟鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1206846_comment'></div>伏愿陛下退朝之暇，䌷绎经史之馀，取此二书置之坐右，留神省览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1206846_comment'></div>发言行事，以此为准，庶于盛德有补万一」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1206846_comment'></div>又言：「伏睹诏书，知州军辞见与文臣带一路兵钤及监司职任者，并须上殿指挥，皆罢而不见，愚窃所未谕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1206846_comment'></div>今陛下初即尊位，方当厉精为治，日接群臣，以广聪明，以通众志之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1206846_comment'></div>而遽有此变更，窃恐四方闻之，或意陛下倦于咨询，或意陛下略于待士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1206846_comment'></div>而为一监司长吏者，亦将苟且因循，无自励之志，非所以崇德美、兴治功也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1206846_comment'></div>给事中二人相继封驳除目，三省进呈，令中书舍人书读行下，公言：「三省各有职守，不相侵踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1206846_comment'></div>门下所以驳正中书违失，故中书舍人不兼给事中职事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1206846_comment'></div>恐因此隳坏官制，有损治体」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1206846_comment'></div>谏官陈瓘以言及东朝与政事被谪，公适馆伴虏使，事毕还家，即奏书两宫曰：「瓘昨日所论，臣虽不知其详，以诏旨观之，瓘言虽狂，其意则忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1206846_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1206846_comment'></div>瓘以疏远小臣，妄意宫闱之事，披写腹心，无所顾避，此臣所谓狂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1206846_comment'></div>皇太后有援立明圣不世之大功，有前期归政过人之盛德，万一有纤毫可以指议，则于清躬不为无累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1206846_comment'></div>瓘以爱君之诚，陈预防之戒，欲以开悟圣心，保全盛美，忘身为国，臣子所难，此臣所谓忠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1206846_comment'></div>昔东汉明德马皇后常谓章帝曰：『吾但含饴弄孙，不复关政』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1206846_comment'></div>章帝亦能不顾所生，极其尊事之礼，故一时母子之贤，著之史册，为后世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1206846_comment'></div>本朝慈圣光献皇后归政之后，游心物外，历英宗、神宗两朝，功隆德盛，称美至今」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1206846_comment'></div>公所以处上母子之间，委曲详尽，有人所难言者，不可缕载也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1206846_comment'></div>初，瓘得罪，左右无敢言者，公独尽言，请复瓘旧职，其犯颜婴锋率此类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1206846_comment'></div>先是，礼部议哲宗升祔，宜于太庙殿增一室，公献议称：「《书》、《礼记》皆云七庙，国朝自僖祖而下至仁宗，始备七世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1206846_comment'></div>故英宗祔庙则迁顺祖，神宗祔庙则迁翼祖，三昭三穆，合于典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1206846_comment'></div>今大行皇帝祔庙，当与神宗为昭穆，上迁宣祖，以合礼文七世三昭三穆之谊」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1206846_comment'></div>时为礼部者方执政，故公议见绌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1206846_comment'></div>时议者又言上当为哲宗服期从兄弟之服，公在迩英读《史记》，至「尧崩，三年之丧」毕，因言：「尧、舜同出黄帝，舜且为尧丧三年者，舜尝臣尧故也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1206846_comment'></div>侍读温益进言曰：「《史记》世次不足信，若尧、舜同出，则舜娶尧女为娶从祖姑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1206846_comment'></div>公以《史记》世次、《礼记·祭法》、《大传》之说质于上前，益语塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1206846_comment'></div>时有陈大中至正之论者，以元祐、绍圣均为有失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1206846_comment'></div>鲁公称上命，命公推此意为诏，明谕天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1206846_comment'></div>公见上言：「陛下欲建皇极，以消弭朋党，须先分君子小人，赏善罚恶，不可偏废」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1206846_comment'></div>开说甚至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1206846_comment'></div>已而诏自中出，上命鲁公适视草禁中，因举数事为戒，所谓休息百姓，总核庶工，甄叙材良，敦奖正直，澄清风俗，振肃纪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1206846_comment'></div>退与鲁公言，未尝不丁宁反复以此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1206846_comment'></div>本朝学士弟草兄制惟韩氏与公，无他比也，士论荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1206846_comment'></div>而公独以满盈为惧，力祈补外，章三上，三请对，引祖宗朝学士许避亲嫌故事，期于必得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1206846_comment'></div>上面谕曰：「朕初即位，首召用卿，岂可遽求出也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1206846_comment'></div>除龙图阁学士、提举中太一宫兼集禧观公事，修撰《哲宗实录》，仍侍读如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1206846_comment'></div>恳辞逾月，不受命，请郡益确。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1206846_comment'></div>上封还乞外奏，乃出称谢，然犹申前请，上固彊之，故退而奏诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1206846_comment'></div>朝廷更茶法，内侍阎守勤主之，公谓与民争利，不可为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1206846_comment'></div>是时守勤方用事，势倾中外，非守义弗渝，无敢忤其意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1206846_comment'></div>元年，太史复奏，四月朔太阳当蚀，公请对，言：「今连年日蚀，皆在正月岁旦之夕，赤气亘天，变不虚生，必有所自」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1206846_comment'></div>因陈天人精祲之说，至诚恳激，言发涕下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1206846_comment'></div>退，力请外，得知陈州，徙知太原府、充河东路经略安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1206846_comment'></div>公奏：「西事素非所习，且臣兄布尝与措置，议论之际不无妨嫌」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1206846_comment'></div>力辞不赴，改知南京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1206846_comment'></div>公前自陈徙宋，遗爱未远，是行，稚耋送迎交于境上，宋人闻公再来，欢动城邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1206846_comment'></div>徙知扬州兼淮南东路兵马钤辖，到官一日，徙知定州路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1206846_comment'></div>会元祐士大夫再被降黜，公义不独全，请与俱贬，言者继之，落龙图阁学士，谪知和州，道除舒州灵仙观，时崇宁元年七月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1206846_comment'></div>鲁公已罢政，言路率公素所不合者，未敢诵言排公，乃言元符末有外臣上书议及宫禁，因疏大臣数人尝有是议，而窜公名其间，坐夺两官，徙居岳州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1206846_comment'></div>明年秋，治上封事异趣者千馀人，因追咎公草求言诏，贬濮州团练副使，汀州安置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1206846_comment'></div>在汀二年，杜门不与人接，日阅书数卷而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1206846_comment'></div>室内仅容一榻，坐卧其中，若将终身焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1206846_comment'></div>人不堪其忧，而公处之裕如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1206846_comment'></div>手诏左迁官例许内徙，移公台州，鲁公亦自衡徙舒，会于途中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1206846_comment'></div>未及徙所，又例还爵秩，授公散郎，与鲁公还居润州里第，戴白相从，人所歆慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1206846_comment'></div>岁馀，二公同时寝疾，公遽命诸子以生不及养太师，殁必返葬其墓下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1206846_comment'></div>自是旬日，语不及家事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1206846_comment'></div>鲁公薨，翼日公亦不起，实大观元年八月丙辰，享年六十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1206846_comment'></div>累勋上护军，封曲阜县开国子，食邑五百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1206846_comment'></div>八宝恩追复朝请郎，后再以恩复朝请大夫、集贤殿修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1206846_comment'></div>公天资仁厚，而刚大之气睟然见于颜面，望之若不可犯，而即之则温然可亲，不问知其为盛德君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1206846_comment'></div>与人交，无远近疏戚之间，不为虚词饰貌，一以诚意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1206846_comment'></div>引掖后进惟恐不及，一经品目，人人自好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1206846_comment'></div>自少力学，于六经百氏之书无所不究，含英茹实，以畜其德，非如世儒徒摭其华，雕绘组织，为辞章而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1206846_comment'></div>经纶之业，盖其素所蕴积也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1206846_comment'></div>故其在朝，则以论思之责为己任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1206846_comment'></div>出藩于外，则所至有成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1206846_comment'></div>瀛州救荒之政，全活者不可以数计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1206846_comment'></div>至其受代，则民挽留之，圮道阖门而不得去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1206846_comment'></div>更十一州，若此类不可悉数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1206846_comment'></div>然在公为不足道，故略而不载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1206846_comment'></div>平居于物无所嗜，惟藏书万馀卷，手自雠校，终老不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1206846_comment'></div>穷探博取，无所遗忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1206846_comment'></div>虽外国山川道里远近夷险，无不洞悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1206846_comment'></div>与辽使语，道其委曲，皆大惊服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1206846_comment'></div>及自朐山还朝，某官某送伴辽使，使者语某曰：「昨朝会日执某事者，非曾舍人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1206846_comment'></div>吾闻其名久矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1206846_comment'></div>其为夷狄钦慕如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1206846_comment'></div>家素贫，未尝屑意有无，而以字孤振乏为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1206846_comment'></div>由布衣以至处显，视其居处被服饮食无少异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1206846_comment'></div>殁之日，陈无新衣，荐无完衾帷，器用敝恶，阖门千指无所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1206846_comment'></div>闻其风者，虽庸夫贱隶，皆叹息为之泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1206846_comment'></div>诸孤卜以二年十一月葬公于南丰县世贤乡梅潭之原，遵治命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1206846_comment'></div>曾祖讳仁旺，累赠太师、沂国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1206846_comment'></div>曾祖妣陈氏，楚国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1206846_comment'></div>祖讳致尧，尚书户部郎中、直史馆，赠太师、密国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1206846_comment'></div>祖妣黄氏，赵国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1206846_comment'></div>考讳易占，太常博士，赠太师、鲁国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1206846_comment'></div>妣周氏，周国太夫人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1206846_comment'></div>吴氏，吴国太夫人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1206846_comment'></div>朱氏，鲁国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1206846_comment'></div>娶强氏，累封和义郡君，尚书祠部郎中、三司户部判官讳至之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1206846_comment'></div>有贤行，能宜家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1206846_comment'></div>有子八人：长曰绲，通直郎、知扬州天长县丞事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1206846_comment'></div>次曰纵，承事郎、监太平州芜湖县酒税务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1206846_comment'></div>绚，宣义郎、监兖州东岳庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1206846_comment'></div>统，将仕郎、监应天府柘城县税务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1206846_comment'></div>緎，将仕郎、监睦州酒税务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1206846_comment'></div>纬，承务郎、权知泗州招信县丞事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1206846_comment'></div>续、纁，举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1206846_comment'></div>女四人：长适宣德郎王律，次适宣义郎刘𫢝，二尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1206846_comment'></div>孙男二十人：悰、恪、慥、悦、怀、悟、愔、悌、恂、愖、怡、恢、旨、恽、惠、忳、惔、懔、懙、憺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1206846_comment'></div>孙女六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1206846_comment'></div>公以文学擅名，自结主知，朝廷每脩一书，必以公为选首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1206846_comment'></div>自仁宗至哲宗四朝大典，公悉与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1206846_comment'></div>有《曲阜集》四十卷、外集十卷、奏议十二卷、《迩英殿故事》一卷、《元祐外制集》十二卷《、庚辰外制集》三卷、《内制集》五卷、《尚书讲议》八卷、《曾氏谱图》一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1206846_comment'></div>公殁逾二十年，今天子即位，尽还元祐贬死人官职，复公龙图阁学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1206846_comment'></div>绍兴二年，赐谥文昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1206846_comment'></div>公久在论思之职，参订国论，献替为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1206846_comment'></div>兵火之馀，朝廷载籍焚灭殆尽，虽至言显行著在天下，然日月逝矣，恐浸久或失其传，故掇其大节而详著之，以备异日史氏采录焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_269_1206846_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206830' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206830' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206830?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南剑州陈谏议祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206830")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206830_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206830'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206830'>延平旧有学，负城之隅，抗西山之巅，士之肄业于其中者无虚室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206830_comment'></div>建炎四年为贼所焚，知州事刘侯子翼视旧址险而隘，故迁之城南，就夷旷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206830_comment'></div>方经始，未及成而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206830_comment'></div>今太守周侯绾之来也，市材鸠工，以终其事，教授石君公彻实董其役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206830_comment'></div>二人相与协力成之，又即其西偏立谏议陈公莹中之祠，岁时从祀焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206830_comment'></div>堂成，属予为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206830_comment'></div>余谓周侯之政知所先务矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206830_comment'></div>谨庠序之教，追祀前哲，以矜式士类，非有尊德乐义之诚心，无以及此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206830_comment'></div>世之为吏者，举以治文书、理民讼为急，而不知使无讼者有在于是也，可无述乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206830_comment'></div>乃究其本而为之言曰：自孟子没，圣学失传，六经微言晦蚀于异论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206830_comment'></div>宋兴，锄颣夷荒，养息百有馀年，名儒继出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206830_comment'></div>至嘉祐、治平间，文物之盛，未有前比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206830_comment'></div>熙宁更新法度，以经术造士，世儒妄以私智之凿，分文析字，而枝辞蔓说乱经矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206830_comment'></div>假六艺之文以济其申、商之术，一有戾己，则流放窜殛之刑随其后，虽世臣元老，槩以四凶之罪目之，天下靡然无敢忤其意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206830_comment'></div>故佞谀成风，而正论熄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206830_comment'></div>士气不振，积至于崇、宣述其事，而流毒滋甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206830_comment'></div>当是时，横流稽天，而莹中以身捍之，几灭顶而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206830_comment'></div>刚大之气，充塞宇宙，先知之明，为时蓍龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206830_comment'></div>非命世之才而能自拔于流俗者，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206830_comment'></div>寘之学校，使后生晚进目睹其遗像，宜有向风而兴起者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206830_comment'></div>异时羽仪天朝，使奸谀屏息，将必有人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206830_comment'></div>至是，邦人思咏周侯之遗德无穷已也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1206830_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　在将乐。胡安国自衡阳寄《伊川语录》写本二册。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　居将乐。胡安国（文定）自衡阳寄《伊川语录》写本二册，公答书。作品：答胡康侯（十一）<div id='poem_1206575' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206575' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206575?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答胡康侯书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206575")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206575_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206575'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206575'>某衰朽，杜门待尽，平时亲故凋丧略尽，绝无过从者，惟时亲书册以自适耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206575_comment'></div>家所藏书为贼弃毁，仅存一二语录常在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206575_comment'></div>念先生之门馀无人，某当任其责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206575_comment'></div>蒙寄示二册，尤荷留念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206575_comment'></div>然兹事体大，虽寡陋不敢不勉，近因阅《三经义》，见有害义理处，略为之著论，以正王氏之失。<div class='inline'
