id='poem_sentence_4_1206575_comment'></div>盖尝论之于朝，去其王爵，罢配享，后生晚学未必知其非也，姑欲终此一事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206575_comment'></div>书成，未脱稿，款曲当录以纳去取正左右，庶可传远也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206575_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　居将乐。有答胡安国书。作品：答胡康侯（十二）答胡康侯（十三）答胡康侯（十四）答胡康侯（十五）答胡康侯（十六）答胡康侯（十七）<div id='poem_1206576' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206576' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206576?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答胡康侯书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206576")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206576_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206576'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206576'>承谕及江西宣谕使风采可仰，吾乡使者甚不挠，但未见惠泽及民，污吏革面者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206576_comment'></div>盗贼得韩、申二将平之，今已无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206576_comment'></div>敝乡去岁大疫，恶少旧常作过者死亡略尽，自此可无盗贼之虞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206576_comment'></div>近见报襄阳镇抚檄诸郡领兵收复中都，屡捷，洋州亦有报杀获金寇千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206576_comment'></div>所至有捷报，中兴可指日望也，可喜可喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206576_comment'></div>和卿平生相知，第鄙文不足以发盛美为愧耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206576_comment'></div>浙中数事与初授恩命，皆其亲闻见者，故不敢专用行状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206576_comment'></div>其他皆无更易，如宗室养他人子，初云财用不足，患之细也，养他人子，则宗枝乱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206576_comment'></div>其建议乃云「有父兄在，同居者减半，而养母勿给」，于是其弊渐去，则只是以财不足为忧，凡宗室例皆裁减，与所谓乱宗枝之意不相应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206576_comment'></div>公更问其详，为增损之，乃善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206576_comment'></div>伊川先生语录昔尝集诸门人所问，以类相从，编录成帙，今皆失之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206576_comment'></div>罗仲素旧有一本，今仲素已死，著其婿寻之未到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206576_comment'></div>近宣干喻子才云有本甚多，计到浙中便付来。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206576_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206577' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206577?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206577_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206577'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206577'>便中辱赐教，伏审迩辰燕休，台候万福，欣慰欣慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206577_comment'></div>某衰朽杜门粗适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206577_comment'></div>闲中自去岁来稍安静，而汀、邵与江西邻，虔州时有窃发者侵逼境上，王师往来恟恟，不能治安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206577_comment'></div>昨日又闻建安有此警，帅司遣兵会合，未知如何也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206577_comment'></div>江北虽屡有捷报，而所传不一，闻之忧喜相半，未能释然不以为虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206577_comment'></div>世事如此，奈何奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206577_comment'></div>示谕湖湘州县皆帖然，人已归业，殊可喜，此岳将之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206577_comment'></div>然屯戍之多，所至艰窘，非特长沙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206577_comment'></div>闽中素贫，近降祠部一万道，已敷配在民间，贫家所敷已二百千，未知所从出，细民可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206577_comment'></div>不知湖湘有此否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206577_comment'></div>事之可忧者非毫楮可尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206577_comment'></div>馀寒未解，惟冀为道保重，副此颂祝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1206577_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206578?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206578'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206578'>语录子才所寄已到，方编集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206578_comment'></div>诸公所录，以类相从，有异同当一一考正，然后可以渐次删润，非旬月可了也，俟书成即纳去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206578_comment'></div>某近著《三经义辨》，正王氏之学缪戾处方就，俟脱藁纳去取正左右，庶可传后学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206578_comment'></div>曾吉甫顷在维扬，亦尝相聚，但初未尝讲学耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206578_comment'></div>公既称其如此，士大夫间岂易得哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206578_comment'></div>若得其来时，亲其绪论，固所幸愿也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1206578_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206579?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206579_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206579'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206579'>久不闻问，方深驰企。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206579_comment'></div>辱书，伏审旅寓台候万福，欣慰欣慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206579_comment'></div>某老拙如常，去冬松溪贼范忠大作，武尉被害，焚劫县道略尽，首领已为申将擒获，残党出境，势无能为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206579_comment'></div>又传虔寇陈颙犯漳、汀，朝廷已遣申将往讨捕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206579_comment'></div>敝邑相去差远，民间不甚惊扰，稍得安居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206579_comment'></div>时亲书册，聊用自适耳，馀无足道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206579_comment'></div>正远瞻晤，惟冀对时为道自重。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206579_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206580' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206580' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206580?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206580_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206580'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206580'>知令似龙图先往湖外，得近信否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206580_comment'></div>长沙方易帅，势未可往，更俟浙帅来如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206580_comment'></div>徐行未晚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206580_comment'></div>伯纪言章丑诋之，以为有跋扈之渐，天下知有宣抚，不知有朝廷，赖君相眷知，犹得宫祠而罢，甚幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206580_comment'></div>浙帅尚在岭表，不知何时可来湖中？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206580_comment'></div>么贼未殄，伯纪已有罢命，新帅未到，人情不无向背，万一有警，为之奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206580_comment'></div>在伯纪尤可虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206580_comment'></div>梁参议闻已归，未到乡里，云径往福唐搬家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206580_comment'></div>得渠来，则湖外事可尽知也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1206580_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206581?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206581_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206581'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206581'>某窃谓「令出惟行，弗惟反」，欲令之不反，当慎其始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206581_comment'></div>始之不慎，虽欲不反，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206581_comment'></div>闽中二三年来盗贼群起，在四川军被害为甚，夷伤之馀，民力凋敝极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206581_comment'></div>蒙恩放免绍兴二年秋夏二税，及役钱一料，非朝廷勤恤民隐，何以得此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206581_comment'></div>既而漕司检准绍兴令，诸赦降放及倚阁税租者，各不得过三分，行下州县，依旧催纳七分，急于星火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206581_comment'></div>民被其泽，方欢欣鼓舞，未逾月遂转而为怨咨，良可惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206581_comment'></div>朝廷既有著令不得过三分，赦书不应全放，是徒为文具罔民耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206581_comment'></div>后虽有德意，人谁信之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206581_comment'></div>恐自是民不立矣，其患有不可胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206581_comment'></div>赦书既已尽放，有司亦不宜沮格，二者胥失矣，皆不慎令之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206581_comment'></div>放税租出于一时之异恩，自当量灾伤，分数减放，使民受实惠，何必著为令格？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206581_comment'></div>不得过三分是豫为罔民之具，以资裒刻之吏耳，非令之善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206581_comment'></div>某衰朽杜门，不欲闻外事，因催税者及门，见邑中行移如此，恐远方利病公所欲知，故辄及之，愿勿以语人，恐贻不恤纬之谤，至祷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206581_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　居将乐。有答萧子庄书。作品：答萧子庄书（其一）答萧子庄书（其二）答萧子庄书（其三）<div id='poem_1206603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206603?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答萧子庄书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206603")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206603_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206603'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206603'>老朽文思衰落，重蒙以殿记见属，不欲固违厚意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206603_comment'></div>辞鄙意陋，不足以传远，徒负愧耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206603_comment'></div>向在谏垣，尝论王氏之失，太学诸生安于所习，鬨然群起而非之，赖君相之明，卒从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206603_comment'></div>今虽有定论，学者真知其非者或寡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206603_comment'></div>屏居投闲，因摭《三经义》，辨有害理处是正之，以示后学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206603_comment'></div>文字多，未暇录去，俟小子早晚带行过仙邑，可一览也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1206603_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1135')">1134-1135年</a>　居将乐。作文。作品：跋了翁责沈侍。跋温公与刘侍郎御帖。跋邹公送子诗。浦城县学重修文宣王殿记。答萧子庄。<div id='poem_1206683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋温公与刘侍郎帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206683")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206683'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206683'>熙宁之初，吴兴刘公位台端，论事忤大臣意，谪知江州，一时清议冤之，无敢言者，独文正温公抗章于廷诤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206683_comment'></div>事之本末，安抚参政张公论之详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206683_comment'></div>公将行，文正造门叙别，又以手翰问行期，有「道胜名立」之言，其相与之意厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206683_comment'></div>夫天下之善士斯友天下之善士，二公终始一节，不约而同，其取友可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206683_comment'></div>览是遗墨，三复兴叹，乃附其说于后。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1206683'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1206683_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋邹公送子诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206674")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206674_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206674'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206674'>君子之泽，五世而斩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206674_comment'></div>盖人之于亲，四世而缌服穷，六世而亲属竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206674_comment'></div>服穷则遗泽浸微矣，故五世而斩，此古今之常理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206674_comment'></div>舍人邹公于其子筮仕之初，以诗赆行，其丁宁训饬，不以宠禄为荣，而以阴骘苍生为念，则其垂裕之意岂浅哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206674_comment'></div>积至于道乡，缌服已穷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206674_comment'></div>今其元孙出其诗示余，余得而伏读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206674_comment'></div>观公所以训迪其子孙与道乡所以奉承之志，则邹氏之流泽岂常理之足云，虽亘古百世而益光矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206674_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206603?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答萧子庄书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206603")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206603_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206603'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206603'>老朽文思衰落，重蒙以殿记见属，不欲固违厚意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206603_comment'></div>辞鄙意陋，不足以传远，徒负愧耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206603_comment'></div>向在谏垣，尝论王氏之失，太学诸生安于所习，鬨然群起而非之，赖君相之明，卒从之。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年1月</a>　在开封师，有文。作品：题萧欲仁大学篇后。<div id='poem_1206659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题萧欲仁大学篇后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206659")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206659'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206659'>学始于致知，终于知止而止焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206659_comment'></div>致知在格物，物固不可胜穷也，反身而诚，则举天下之物在我矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206659_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「天生蒸民，有物有则」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206659_comment'></div>凡形色之具于吾身，无非物也，而各有则焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206659_comment'></div>目之于色，耳之于声，口鼻之于臭味，接乎外而不得遁焉者，其必有以也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206659_comment'></div>知其体物而不可遗，则天下之理得矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206659_comment'></div>天下之理得，则物与吾一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206659_comment'></div>无有能乱吾之知，思而意其有不诚乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206659_comment'></div>由是而通天下之志，类万物之情，赞天地之化，其则不远矣，则其知可不谓之至矣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206659_comment'></div>知至矣，则宜有止也，譬之四方万里之远，苟无止焉，则将焉归乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206659_comment'></div>故见其进未见其止，孔子之所惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206659_comment'></div>古之圣人，自诚意正心至于平天下，其理一而已，所以合内外之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206659_comment'></div>世儒之论以高明处己，中庸处人，离内外，判心迹，其失是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206659_comment'></div>故余窃谓《大学》者，其学者之门乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206659_comment'></div>不由其门而欲望其堂奥，非余所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206659_comment'></div>萧君欲仁，志学之士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206659_comment'></div>录示《大学》一篇，求余言以题其后，其意盖非苟然者，故聊为发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206659_comment'></div>苟于是尽心焉，则圣人之庭户可策而进矣，欲仁其勉之哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1206659_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年1月23日</a>　出京师。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='34b3808b97ef4b1c94b6ddcac9a98c0a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("34b3808b97ef4b1c94b6ddcac9a98c0a");'><span id='34b3808b97ef4b1c94b6ddcac9a98c0a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>，62岁</div><div id='34b3808b97ef4b1c94b6ddcac9a98c0a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年4月</a>　离萧山赴开封。磨勘转朝奉郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年6月</a>　在开封。差提点均州（湖北均县）明道观。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='592e3169bd834d23b8c862d055e48842_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("592e3169bd834d23b8c862d055e48842");'><span id='592e3169bd834d23b8c862d055e48842_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1126')">1124-1126年</a>，72-74岁</div><div id='592e3169bd834d23b8c862d055e48842' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年12月</a>　以秘书郎召，至开封。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年2月</a>　在开封，迁著作郎。有文。作品：面对上徽宗疏。<div id='poem_1206491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>面对上徽宗疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206491")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206491'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206491'>尧舜曰「允执厥中」，孟子曰「汤执中」，《洪范》曰「皇建其有极」，历世圣人由斯道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206491_comment'></div>熙宁之初，大臣文六艺之言以行其私，祖宗之法纷更殆尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206491_comment'></div>元祐继之，尽复祖宗之旧，熙宁之法一切废革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206491_comment'></div>至绍圣、崇宁抑又甚焉，凡元祐之政事著在令甲，皆焚之以灭其迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206491_comment'></div>自是分为二党，缙绅之祸至今未殄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206491_comment'></div>臣愿明诏有司，条具祖宗之法，著为纲目，有宜于今者举而行之，当损益者损益之，元祐、熙、丰姑置勿问，一趋于中而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1206491_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年3月</a>　在开封，有与执政札子。作品：论时事札子。<div id='poem_1206497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论时事劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和七年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206497")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206497_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206497'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206497'>衰晚退伏田庐，杜门待尽，无复馀念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206497_comment'></div>今兹误辱世论，被旨召对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206497_comment'></div>疏远贱吏，得一见君父，臣子之荣愿毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206497_comment'></div>而到阙累月，未得对班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206497_comment'></div>私自念言，陋儒陈腐之业，不得为世用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206497_comment'></div>加之衰病薾然，无以自效，日想东归，为首丘计，惟是忧国爱君之心不能忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206497_comment'></div>今士大夫不敢尽言天下之事，不过为保身之谋耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206497_comment'></div>不知所以谋国乃所以谋身，天下不宁而保其身者，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206497_comment'></div>某以疏远，虽欲有言，无由上达，辄条具十数事，皆今日之急务，傥可少裨国论，望阁下为朝廷留念，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1206497_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论时事劄子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>一、慎令</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206498")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206498'>《书》曰：「令出惟行，弗惟反」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206498_comment'></div>欲令之不反，当慎其始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206498_comment'></div>始之不慎，而轻以示人，虽欲不反，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206498_comment'></div>近睹榜示：宣和六年未纳税赋、租赋、沿纳、和买，预买并放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206498_comment'></div>又曰：「今年放免租税等，尚虑监司州县别作名目科纳，致民人不被实惠，仰所属监司具放免过实数闻奏，当议朝廷支降钱物应副」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206498_comment'></div>即不声说只为流移及盗贼人户方免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206498_comment'></div>今广济军以放税降官冲替，则前日诏令皆为虚文耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206498_comment'></div>夫安土服业之民不为盗贼，皆不被惠泽，惟流亡转为盗贼者独免租赋，则百姓何惮不流亡而为盗贼乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206498_comment'></div>是朝廷以诏令诱致之也，其为患岂小哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206498_comment'></div>孔子曰：「自古皆有死，民无信不立」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206498_comment'></div>以今日之事视之，兵与食皆不可去，犹以信为可去，不亦异乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206498_comment'></div>以孔子言为不可用则已，如以为可用，则存信尤当谨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206498_comment'></div>今抚谕之使方行，而失信如此，虽有至意，人谁信之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206498_comment'></div>则使者徒为此行耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206498_comment'></div>某窃谓其失未远，尚可追改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206498_comment'></div>宜如前诏，一切放免，竭取中都所有支降应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206498_comment'></div>庶几民信而从之，则流亡盗贼亦有衰息之期矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206498_comment'></div>不尔，恐四方闻之，冀免租赋，皆相率为盗贼，不可不虑也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1206498_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206499' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206499' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206499?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>二、茶法</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206499_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206499'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206499'>榷茶自唐末始有，祖宗盖尝行之矣，而官自鬻之，积年之久，流弊滋甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206499_comment'></div>仁祖令有司会榷茶净利，均为茶租而户输之，弛其禁，使自兴贩，县官坐收榷茶之利，而民得自便，无冒禁之患，可谓公私两利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206499_comment'></div>故当时诏书有曰：「民被诛求之困，日惟咨嗟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206499_comment'></div>官受滥恶之入，岁以陈腐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206499_comment'></div>私藏盗贩，犯者实繁，严刑重诛，情所不忍，是于江湖数千里设陷阱以害吾民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206499_comment'></div>间遣使者往就问之，而皆欢然，愿弛榷法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206499_comment'></div>岁入之课，少时上官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206499_comment'></div>历世之弊，一旦以除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206499_comment'></div>著为经常，不复更制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206499_comment'></div>尚虑喜于立异之人，缘而为奸之党，妄陈奏议，以惑官司，必寘明刑，以戒狂谬」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206499_comment'></div>其训告可谓至矣，后世所宜守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206499_comment'></div>今茶租钱输之如故，而榷法愈密，是榷之又榷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206499_comment'></div>趋今之变，若未能尽弛其禁，犹当少宽之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206499_comment'></div>二浙穷荒之民，有经岁不食盐者，茶则不可一日无也，一日无之则病矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206499_comment'></div>昔时晚春采造，谓之黄茶，每觔不过三二十钱，故细民得以厌食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206499_comment'></div>今买引之直已过数倍矣，未有茶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206499_comment'></div>民间例食贵茶，而细民均受其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206499_comment'></div>行法之初，裒刻之吏以配买引数多为功，苟冒恩赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206499_comment'></div>今以岁课最高为额，上户有敷及十数引者，一引陪费无虑十数千，则人不易供矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206499_comment'></div>诸犯榷货不得根究来历，违者以故入人罪论，自祖宗至于熙丰，未之有改也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206499_comment'></div>今茶法独许根究来历，盗贩者皆无赖小民，一为捕获，则妄引来历，以报私怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206499_comment'></div>官司不敢沮抑，追呼蔓延，狴犴充斥，经时不能决，良可悯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206499_comment'></div>某窃谓宜革去根究来历之法，无追呼之扰，蠲最高之额，以平岁课，罢增羡之赏，惩贪吏希功厉民之虐，庶乎民少安其生矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1206499_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206500?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>三、盐法</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206500_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206500'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206500'>榷盐自汉有之，非一日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206500_comment'></div>周世宗征河东，河朔之民遮道诉盐法之不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206500_comment'></div>世宗会所得盐法息，均之人户岁输之，从民愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206500_comment'></div>熙宁间有献议再榷者，方神考大有为之时，凡可以益国而利民者，知无不为，以是为不可，沮其议而不行，是终不可行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206500_comment'></div>河朔与辽为邻，祖宗优恤之，特异于他路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206500_comment'></div>盖养之于无事之时，以备缓急也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206500_comment'></div>困之于无事之时，则于有事之际何赖焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206500_comment'></div>今日之寇盗是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206500_comment'></div>盐息之敷在人户者，亦输之如故，而又设官置司与他路等，恐非祖宗优恤之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206500_comment'></div>江浙蚕盐，于春初均与之，为蚕缫之用，蚕熟，以绢偿之，不为厉民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206500_comment'></div>今蚕盐不立，而蚕绢不免，则盐之利入官已多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206500_comment'></div>山谷之民，食盐之家十无二三，而州县均敷盐钞，民间陪费与茶引等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206500_comment'></div>迫于殿最之严，往往计口授之，以充岁额，人何以堪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206500_comment'></div>今朝廷不立岁额，免比较，其裕民之意厚矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206500_comment'></div>然不比较，使民得自便，则盐课必亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206500_comment'></div>朝廷不资盐息之用则可，若犹未免，则盐事司安得坐视其亏欠而恬不加察乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206500_comment'></div>前此方贼之后，二浙盖尝不立额比较矣，而岁额大亏，盐事司切责州县不觉察私贩，致有亏欠，州县苟逭谴责，亦不免敷派取办，虽名不比较，而比较之实仍在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206500_comment'></div>某窃谓宜酌中立额，使州县易办，则民亦少纾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206500_comment'></div>若不立额，则盐司督责必以旧额为责，裒刻之吏务以应办为功，则所取无有限度，其为害益深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206500_comment'></div>征入之课，以五年酌中数为额，祖宗以来，自有常法，不可改也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1206500_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206501?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>四、转般</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206501'>转般盖得刘晏之遗意，朝廷捐数百缗与为籴本，使总六路之计，通融移用，以给中都之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206501_comment'></div>六路丰凶更有不常，一路丰稔则增籴以充漕计，饥凶去处则使之输折斛钱而已，故公私俱宽，而中都不乏，最为良法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206501_comment'></div>自胡师文以籴本为羡馀以献，而制置司拱手无可为者，直达之议所从起也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206501_comment'></div>今欲复转般而籴本取之诸路，漕计犹且不足，而又歛取之，非天降地出，又非出于漕臣之家，取于民而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206501_comment'></div>二浙兵火夷伤之馀，疮痍未合，民穷无告，则其患有不可测者，前日之事是也，安可不为之虑哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206501_comment'></div>欲复转般，宜遵旧制，捐数百万缗与为籴本，则其事济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206501_comment'></div>不然，徒为纷纷，无益于国也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206501_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206502?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>五、籴买</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206502'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206502'>籴买之名不一、非特均籴、结籴之类而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206502_comment'></div>取之虽多，而州郡无一月之积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206502_comment'></div>祖宗时，预买䌷绢，每疋支钱一千，限正月十五日以前支讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206502_comment'></div>方春匮乏时，民间得钱，颇以为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206502_comment'></div>是时浙绢至中都，每疋之直千二三百钱，预支一千于人户，无所亏损矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206502_comment'></div>今江浙虽云预买，而钱不时得，郡县盖有白取之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206502_comment'></div>产绢县分每疋不下二千三四百足钱，而上户有敷及百馀疋者，民力固未易办矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206502_comment'></div>又有非时抛买，如燕山丝绢之类，所须不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206502_comment'></div>秋成，谷未上场，而催科之吏已及门矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206502_comment'></div>力耕之民日食糠秕，而输官常恐不足，欲民之不流亡，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206502_comment'></div>昔熙宁中，三司与发运司相为表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206502_comment'></div>三司有馀粟，则以粟转为钱、为银绢以充上供之数，他物亦然，故有无相资，无偏重之弊，而发运司常为邦用之根本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206502_comment'></div>今预买实得一千，民间陪费已多，况又未必得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206502_comment'></div>若今发运司通融六路之计，有无相补，于出绢州郡用常法，依在市中价于人户量行折科，减预买之数，亦足以少宽民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206502_comment'></div>寻常折变，多为民害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206502_comment'></div>盖州郡不依时值，高估常赋合纳之物，低估绢价，故受其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206502_comment'></div>若严约束，谷价虽依发运司和籴之利，不得故为低昂，比之预买一千，又未必得钱，则利害亦相远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206502_comment'></div>今浙绢两贯三四百足钱一疋方可，中官纵胥吏为奸，只与时直之半，所省亦多矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1206502_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206503?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>六、坑冶</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206503_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206503'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206503'>坑冶，利之所在，有矿苗去处，不待劝率而人自寻逐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206503_comment'></div>凡坑户皆四方游手，未有赍钱本而往者，全藉官中应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206503_comment'></div>令烹鍊到银铜入官，而钱不时得，则坑户无以自给，散而之他，此岁课所从耗失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206503_comment'></div>取矿皆穴地而入，有深及五七里处仅能容身，一有摧陷，则无遗类矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206503_comment'></div>非有厚利，人谁为之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206503_comment'></div>纵大兴发，亦民间私自货易，官中亦无所得，虽有重法，不能禁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206503_comment'></div>若以数千万缗分在诸场中，使以时给与，则坑冶自兴，不须他求也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206503_comment'></div>泉布所以权物重轻，通有无，其利柄当操之在上，禁私铸非以取利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206503_comment'></div>今钱一千重六觔，铜每觔官买其直百钱，又须白蜡和之，乃能成钱，除火耗剉磨损折，须六七觔物料乃得一千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206503_comment'></div>铜自涔水、永兴数千里运致，其脚乘又在百钱之外，薪炭之费、官兵廪给、工匠率分，其支用不赀，一二细计，千四五百钱本方得一千，何利之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206503_comment'></div>方财用匮乏之时，欲兴鼓铸取利，以纾目前之急，非长策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206503_comment'></div>然比年鼓铸，岁额不敷，非特官吏弛慢所致，无铜故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206503_comment'></div>但取会诸监亏欠因依，其说自见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206503_comment'></div>今遣使诸路未必有新坑可采，鼓铸亦未必有铜，使者持节而往，必不肯坐视，不为之计也，不过督责州县，认定岁额，取诸民而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206503_comment'></div>一不应办，则以不职罢之，谁敢不从？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206503_comment'></div>铜非民间所有，督迫之严，不免毁钱为铜以输官，更旧为新，徒费工力，所损多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206503_comment'></div>元符中亦尝遣使踏逐坑冶，奸吏诡妄百出，乃以新坑铜量增价市之，岁终与旧坑铜通融以充岁额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206503_comment'></div>监官无亏课之责，不复检束；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206503_comment'></div>而坑户得以自便，以旧为新，冒取善价，而新坑实无有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206503_comment'></div>其欺罔莫此为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206503_comment'></div>或恐诸路引此例施行，不可不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206503_comment'></div>宜令诸路如坑冶不至兴发，或无铜鼓铸，不得令诸郡虚认岁额，州郡亦不得依随虚认数目，庶几不至大段搔扰，而民不受弊矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1206503_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206504' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206504' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206504?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>七、边事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206504_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206504'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206504'>今日之事无急于边事、盗贼者，然二者盖相因而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206504_comment'></div>居者困于调歛，壮者疲于馈挽，财力俱弊，则流亡转而盗贼，理势然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206504_comment'></div>既往无可咎，而来者犹可图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206504_comment'></div>窃谓燕云之师宜退守内地，以受馈饷之入，使燕军更番请给于此，庶几出纳自我，无大入折欠之虞，征夫免称贷备偿之扰，则民力不至大困矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206504_comment'></div>今云中得百里之地，则增百里转输之费，徒敝吾民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206504_comment'></div>出倍称之息以资黠寇，其害非小也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206504_comment'></div>夫军以常胜名之，则骄其心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206504_comment'></div>粮以计口授之，则滋其欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206504_comment'></div>狄人何厌之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206504_comment'></div>比闻道路言云：朝廷授与之田鲜有肯耕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206504_comment'></div>虽流言未尽可信，以理推之，恐或有之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206504_comment'></div>夫力田与安坐而食，其劳佚相反矣，其不耕固不足怪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206504_comment'></div>纵能使之力耕，不知遂能罢计口之食乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206504_comment'></div>若未能罢，是徒富之资其桀骜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206504_comment'></div>如闻燕地尚多閒田，不若募边民为弓箭手，如陕西例，蠲其租赋，使习骑射，亦足杀常胜军之势，仍立定额，无使增置，不三五年可渐消矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206504_comment'></div>近见端门外优戏百技，率多燕人异时归附在州郡者，皆讥察其出入，自有常法，其周防非无为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206504_comment'></div>不知今燕人在中都知其数否，宁知无奸细混处其中乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206504_comment'></div>讥察之法，不可废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206504_comment'></div>戎狄豺狼之心，未可尽信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206504_comment'></div>昔唐太宗从温彦博之议处降寇于河南，魏郑公以为不可，力争之不能得，不二三年卒为乱，如郑公之议，此前事可监也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1206504_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206505' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206505' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206505?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span>八、盗贼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206505_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206505'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206505'>闻楚、泗有兵为东寇捍御，然淮南州郡如通、泰、涟水之类皆与东州邻，宜皆有备，不独楚、泗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206505_comment'></div>若通、泰有警，则维扬逼矣，扬、楚、泗皆当湖南北、江东西、二浙饷道之冲，中都所仰，一犯其境，则饷道难矣，不可不为之深虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206505_comment'></div>如闻东寇数万欲就降者，古之受降如受敌，未可轻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206505_comment'></div>不知数万之众，欲处之何地？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206505_comment'></div>必使之有可归之业，得以温饱，然后无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206505_comment'></div>处之失当，则其患有甚于不降矣，此尤当审处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206505_comment'></div>今山东之兵不立统帅，讨荡与招安者各自为计，盗贼安所适从乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206505_comment'></div>昔唐以九节度之师，不立统帅，虽李、郭之善兵，犹不免败衄，况馀人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206505_comment'></div>某窃谓宜立统帅，使一路之兵咸受节制，可招则招，可讨则讨，庶乎措置归一，则事克有济矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1206505_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206506?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span>九、择将</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206506'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206506'>将帅犹难其人，本兵之地，当预养之，非一旦仓卒可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206506_comment'></div>昔侯君集学兵于李靖，靖曰：「中原无事，吾教君集御戎狄而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206506_comment'></div>则用兵中原与御戎狄异矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206506_comment'></div>今东北之寇用兵于中原也，燕云之帅御戎狄者，不识知其说者今有其人否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206506_comment'></div>宜令两制而上各举所知堪为将帅者，有智勇足以敌忾待暴、久沉下僚未为世用者，令监司郡守皆得以名闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206506_comment'></div>或自负材武不为人知者，亦使得自陈，询事考言，有可采者，不次用之，则鼓刀贩缯之杰必有为时而出者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206506_comment'></div>未尝求之，不可谓天下之广咸无其人焉，此尤宜留意也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206506_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206507?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span>十、军制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206507'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206507'>都城居四达之冲，无高山巨浸以为阻固，所恃者兵而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206507_comment'></div>凡卫士皆天子之爪牙，不宜有间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206507_comment'></div>近见驾前有常入祗候者，巾服稍异，又闻有御前备缓急者，是卫士分为二三矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206507_comment'></div>名号既殊，则待之必异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206507_comment'></div>待之有异，则人怀异心，不可用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206507_comment'></div>承平之久，亦何缓急之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206507_comment'></div>而兵之彊弱在统之得其人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206507_comment'></div>昔李光弼于军中无所更置，一号令之，气色为之精明，则兵之彊弱，岂不以其人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206507_comment'></div>祖宗以来，军制最为详密，不可增损也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1206507_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年7月12日</a>　在开封。上疏乞为《宣和会计录》，除迩英殿说书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　在开封。有辞状。作品：辞免除迩英殿说书状。<div id='poem_1206449' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206449' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206449?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免迩英殿说书状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206449")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206449_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206449'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206449'>右，臣伏蒙圣恩，除臣充迩英殿说书者，闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206449_comment'></div>切惟陛下圣学高明，劝讲之官宜得深于经术之士以充其选，如臣浅陋，其敢冒居？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206449_comment'></div>伏望圣慈追还成命，以安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206449_comment'></div>所有敕命未敢祗受，已送秘书寄纳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206449_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年7月12日</a>　在开封。有文。作品：谢除迩英殿说书表。<div id='poem_1206476' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206476' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206476?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除迩英殿说书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年7月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206476")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206476_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206476'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206476'>臣某言：伏蒙圣恩，除臣充迩英殿说书，寻具状辞免，奉圣旨不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206476_comment'></div>备员东观，曾未逾时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206476_comment'></div>讲经宸庭，荐膺异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206476_comment'></div>恳辞上渎，成命弗渝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206476_comment'></div>省分非宜，以荣为惧<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206476_comment'></div>伏念臣仕惟为禄，学不知方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206476_comment'></div>自怜挟筴以亡羊，奚殊博簺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206476_comment'></div>几类画墁而志食，有愧轮舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206476_comment'></div>拓落一官，践更三世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206476_comment'></div>偶以桑榆之晚景，亲逢睿圣之误知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206476_comment'></div>擢寘书林，复陪经幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206476_comment'></div>嗟伏生之已老，徒诵遗编；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206476_comment'></div>顾申公之无文，宁堪待问？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206476_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下至仁天覆，盛德日新，虽小善而不遗，无一夫之弗获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206476_comment'></div>致兹庸陋，亦预甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206476_comment'></div>非尧舜之道不陈，敢忘训奖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206476_comment'></div>惟虞夏之书具在，益懋前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206476_comment'></div>期自竭于埃涓，庶或逃于尸素。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1206476_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年8月</a>　在开封。八月，赐祭器、谱牒、金盆花。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年12月26日</a>　闻金人之寇，有札子。作品：论金人入寇札子（其一）<div id='poem_1206508' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206508' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206508?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论金人入寇劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　十二月二十六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年12月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206508")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206508_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206508'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206508'>切谓今日事势如卧之积薪之上，火已燃矣，安危之机间不容发，度事之可为者，宜速为之，不可缓也，缓之则必有后时之悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206508_comment'></div>时方艰危，当自奋励，进贤退奸，竦动观听，庶或可为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206508_comment'></div>若示之以怯惧之形，委靡不振，则事去矣，不可不勉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206508_comment'></div>山有虎，藜藿为之不采，故汲黯在朝，淮南寝谋，视公孙弘辈如发蒙耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206508_comment'></div>论黯经世之才，未必能过弘辈也，特其直气足以镇压奸雄之心耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206508_comment'></div>朝廷威望弗振，使奸雄一以弘辈视之，则无复可为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206508_comment'></div>如某人某人若置之言路必有可观，如某人某人虽一时忤旨得罪，而节义素为中外所瞩，召还则足以收人望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206508_comment'></div>天下有道，守在四夷，今纵未能如是，当于要害处严为守备，比至都城之下，尚何及哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206508_comment'></div>无徒纷纷动摇人心，无益于事也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1206508_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　在开封，任迩英殿说书，作文。作品：陆少卿墓志铭。钱忠定公墓志铭。陆少卿墓志铭。<div id='poem_1206868' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206868' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陆少卿墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和七年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206868")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206868'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206868'>公讳恺，字疆仲，姓陆氏，其先吴郡人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206868_comment'></div>六世祖权，唐末为建安县丞，值中原乱，不克归，因家福州之侯官，故今为侯官人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206868_comment'></div>曾祖中和，赠职方员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206868_comment'></div>祖廙仕左侍禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206868_comment'></div>父长宾，任大理寺丞，累赠通议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206868_comment'></div>母吴氏，赠太硕人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206868_comment'></div>公自幼颖拔不群，博览强记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206868_comment'></div>元丰初，未冠，游太学，标望绝人，一时名儒往往忘辈行蹐门愿交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206868_comment'></div>元祐更新学校，祭酒孔公武仲得其文，奇之，称誉不离口，学者益歆慕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206868_comment'></div>元符三年登进士第，调庐州司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206868_comment'></div>太守龚公原一见待以殊礼，侍御史彭公汝霖、祭酒今丞相白公时中俱荐试学官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206868_comment'></div>召檄至，公曰：「吾困科举二十馀年，晚得一官，朝廷不吾知，欲使之裹饭复入场屋，吾不能也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206868_comment'></div>卒辞不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206868_comment'></div>崇宁大兴学校，郡以公兼掌钱谷，士不之教官之庐，而公之户外屦常满矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206868_comment'></div>执经考疑，虚往实归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206868_comment'></div>秩满，用荐者迁通仕郎，丞相刘公正夫以给事中兼领外诸司，辟公管勾文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206868_comment'></div>阅半岁，改宣教郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206868_comment'></div>外诸司罢，公之子调官济南，怜其少，求与之近，乞监密州板桥镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206868_comment'></div>镇濒海，舶至多异国珍货，吏习为奸欺以渔取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206868_comment'></div>公以身先之，一毫不少黩，海商便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206868_comment'></div>以外诸司赏典转奉议郎，又以八宝恩转承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206868_comment'></div>逾年，御史中丞石公公弼辟为检法官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206868_comment'></div>已而石公以罪去，坐是二岁不迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206868_comment'></div>吴公执中复以儒学荐，召至政事堂，除太府寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206868_comment'></div>明年迁司农寺丞，磨勘转朝奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206868_comment'></div>上方搜访人才，刘公以中书侍郎有异眷，荐士三人，以公为称首，赐对称旨，擢司勋员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206868_comment'></div>车驾幸尚书省，转朝散郎，迁光禄少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206868_comment'></div>刘公既相，除宗正少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206868_comment'></div>方将力荐，引以自助，刘公遽以病去，故弗克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206868_comment'></div>时修玉牒，公纂缉上临御以来政事之大者，十年为一书，上之，转朝请郎，磨勘转朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206868_comment'></div>太常少卿缺员，有旨遴柬，丞相郑公居中、余公深以公启，拟命下之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206868_comment'></div>数日，侍御史张朴进对，论事毕，上忽谓朴曰：「朕用陆某奉常，识其人否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206868_comment'></div>朴对陆某老于儒学，有士望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206868_comment'></div>上深然之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206868_comment'></div>崇宁置议礼局，至是并归礼寺，公于拟议参订为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206868_comment'></div>又修《因革礼》一百卷，上览嘉之，转朝散大夫，磨勘转朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206868_comment'></div>补外，乃以直徽猷阁知均州，关决庶务，无钜细剧易皆亲之，吏敛手不敢为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206868_comment'></div>先是，人惰农，不知灌溉之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206868_comment'></div>公出郊为之劝相，人始尽力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206868_comment'></div>岁大稔，父老勒石道傍，为耕者之劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206868_comment'></div>公之爱民，出于诚心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206868_comment'></div>因旱祷龙祠，三日不雨，公对神自咎曰：「守土之不职，宜菑其身，民何辜，将不粒食矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206868_comment'></div>因泫然，左右为感动，未旋车，大雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206868_comment'></div>邻郡飞蝗蔽地千里，过境弗下，父老候公出，迎拜，以手加额曰：「微公德化所感，民其饿殍矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206868_comment'></div>襄邓大饥，仰粟于我郡，人请闭籴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206868_comment'></div>公曰：「今天下一家，非秦晋比，奚此疆彼界之异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206868_comment'></div>晋之不义，《春秋》犹讥焉，吾不忍为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206868_comment'></div>于是转输相属于道，饥民赖之以济，其为德厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206868_comment'></div>三舍之法罢，士不知所归，公至，聚生徒，择属吏之有学行者为之师，讲肄课试，悉视成均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206868_comment'></div>郡人争遣子弟，献腴田以资其费，唯恐后，士风复振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206868_comment'></div>于暇日又时往临之，申之以孝弟之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206868_comment'></div>郡大治，士民咏歌之，为《均阳乐》十篇以颂其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206868_comment'></div>未几受代到阙，除知泉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206868_comment'></div>未行得疾，终于京师，实宣和六年四月辛酉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206868_comment'></div>享年六十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206868_comment'></div>娶黄氏，有贤行，配公无违德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206868_comment'></div>子男五人：曰震，承议郎、太学博士，以学行知名于时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206868_comment'></div>曰涣，宣教郎、开封府刑曹掾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206868_comment'></div>曰鼎，以疾废不仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206868_comment'></div>曰巽，曰需，皆将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206868_comment'></div>诸子俱好学有立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206868_comment'></div>女适从政郎、汀州司仪曹事薛锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206868_comment'></div>孙男六人，女二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206868_comment'></div>公少孤，事母以孝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206868_comment'></div>其为人敦厚笃实，一言之出，终身可复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206868_comment'></div>遇人以礼，无贵贱贤愚之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206868_comment'></div>平居恂恂，似不能言者，徐而叩之，亹亹无倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206868_comment'></div>其文纯深，析理论事，足见其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206868_comment'></div>其为诗平淡清远，有晋人之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206868_comment'></div>虽应用辞章，咸有典则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206868_comment'></div>践更省事殆十年，同进者衮衮登禁从，公回翔不出故列，无滞淹之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206868_comment'></div>尝谓人曰：「吾学古入官，期以报国利民，顾天下事非辅相大臣不得行，非谏官御史不得言，非侍从之臣不得与国论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206868_comment'></div>今久处朝行，无一毫补，殆非素志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206868_comment'></div>吾老矣，得一郡为朝廷布宣德意，牧养小民，其可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206868_comment'></div>遂抗章力请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206868_comment'></div>既得郡，治有成绩，如其言，士论韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206868_comment'></div>公在均阳，岁荐丰，筑亭临汉上，时从僚吏往游焉，与民同乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206868_comment'></div>又赋诗以广其意，郡人悉播之乐章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206868_comment'></div>至是闻公之亡，登是亭者皆为之感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206868_comment'></div>诸孤将以七年十二月辛酉葬公于怀安县之马鞍山，以毗陵守何公衮之状来请铭，余未暇作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206868_comment'></div>葬有期，又不远千里走仆致书速余铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1206868_comment'></div>昔余在熙宁中，与其兄忱相友善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1206868_comment'></div>是时公尚少，颉颃诸兄间，眉宇秀发，意其必为令器，以诗见贻，有成人风度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1206868_comment'></div>已而学益进，行益修，挺然为时闻人，则余之知公，盖在诸公之先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1206868_comment'></div>虽位不称德，而见于事业者，亦足以垂世传后矣，乃为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_1206868'>昔公兄弟，联车至止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1206868_comment'></div>公方妙龄，鸾鹄停峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1206868_comment'></div>问学日滋，浸以文鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1206868_comment'></div>旋登于朝，为时名卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1206868_comment'></div>出藩于外，蔚有成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1206868_comment'></div>飞蝗不下，神监其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1206868_comment'></div>邦人之思，形于咏歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1206868_comment'></div>勒铭幽宫，百世不磨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_91_1206868_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206867?labeling=true' target='_blank'>钱忠定公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和七年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206867")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206867_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206867'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206867'>宣和六年三月五日，龙图阁学士、正奉大夫致仕钱公以疾薨于毗陵私第之正寝，享年七十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206867_comment'></div>讣闻，天子诏特赠光禄大夫，赙赐加等，下所属郡佽助其葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206867_comment'></div>其家上公行事于朝，考六家书，谥曰忠定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206867_comment'></div>越明年正月壬寅，诸孤护其丧归葬杭州大慈山之原，既乃诣予泣而言曰：「先公勋德载史氏，易名议行，著于太常，褒赠崇恤，具存恩典，终始光荣，昭于一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206867_comment'></div>惟是幽堂之刻，发扬其亲同为不朽者，宜有以称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206867_comment'></div>大惧陨越，弗克以承子责，敢以是请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206867_comment'></div>予与公有同年之旧，义不得辞，乃叙而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206867_comment'></div>公讳即，字中道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206867_comment'></div>其先出于颛帝之后，曰陆终，封于彭城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206867_comment'></div>至子孚仕周为钱府上士，遂以官命氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206867_comment'></div>子孙稍迁居下邳，至汉末逊公避乱，徙乌程，又徙钱塘之临安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206867_comment'></div>忠懿以吴越入觐，公之高祖以宗属锡官，遂居京师，为开封人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206867_comment'></div>曾大父子节，故任右班殿直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206867_comment'></div>祖昌济，故赠朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206867_comment'></div>父垂范，故任朝散郎、知太平州，致仕，赠银青光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206867_comment'></div>自皇考占籍宜兴，今遂为毗陵人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206867_comment'></div>公天资隽茂，稚齿已如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206867_comment'></div>年十三，居母丧，哀慕毁瘠，见者感动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206867_comment'></div>既冠，游太学，以文行知名于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206867_comment'></div>熙宁九年中进士第，授安州司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206867_comment'></div>吏有诬服自盗抵死，属邑具狱上于郡，公明其冤状，守将喜而谓曰：「劾县狱当得赏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206867_comment'></div>答曰：「治狱得情乃其职，挤人以论功，非吾志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206867_comment'></div>闻者叹服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206867_comment'></div>章敏滕公甫力荐之，称有气节，异时必为名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206867_comment'></div>移博州防御推官，知杭州临安县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206867_comment'></div>异时县民转徙，豪右冒垦其田，官不能直者悉夺还之，流冗复业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206867_comment'></div>又除二税积弊以蠲民瘼，至今邑人颂其遗爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206867_comment'></div>调福州观察推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206867_comment'></div>福唐为七闽都会，狱讼繁夥，连帅悉以付公，府无留事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206867_comment'></div>丁银青忧，服除，调睦州军事推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206867_comment'></div>三衢有冤狱，久不决，属部使者以闾里宿怨，檄往按治，挟荐牍动公，风欲鍜鍊以快其私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206867_comment'></div>至则折狱平允，所全活者二十三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206867_comment'></div>或问之，对曰：「吾宁老冗选中，岂忍以数十人觅一荐哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206867_comment'></div>未几改宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206867_comment'></div>丁文安郡夫人忧，服除，知颍昌府郾城县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206867_comment'></div>修奉泰陵，期会严促，乃躬自监督，役均费省，人乐趋事，先期告具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206867_comment'></div>会氾水霖潦败桥，府亟以属公，三日桥成，人服其敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206867_comment'></div>继奉二后园陵，辟为京西转运司属官，有不下司体究采石事，事领于内侍，使者惮不敢，乃请代往，按治不挠，收罪之尤者寘于理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206867_comment'></div>王博文帅鄜延，荐为经抚司官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206867_comment'></div>夏人有来归者，当命以官，公察其言色有异，诘问屈服，果所遣牒者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206867_comment'></div>崇宁中，朝廷欲抚纳西羌，久而不至，主帅忧之，檄巡行塞下，宣谕德意，旬日，监军贵酋款塞降附者至数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206867_comment'></div>代还，赐对称旨，除提举鄜延路弓箭手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206867_comment'></div>蒐简精密，占籍者皆为战士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206867_comment'></div>尽括闲田为将吏冒占者，以广招募。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206867_comment'></div>初，塞上给田，人一顷，马半之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206867_comment'></div>牧者不足供刍秣，畜马日久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206867_comment'></div>至是始增之，槩给一顷，人获其利，而边骑益众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206867_comment'></div>就除陕西路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206867_comment'></div>王师收复银州，被旨专董刍粮，飞挽夙办，第功居最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206867_comment'></div>延帅经制五路边事，除鄜延路经略安抚判官兼总管勾，权帅事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206867_comment'></div>久之，经制罢帅，复领旧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206867_comment'></div>泾原兵失利，渭帅与总管争诉于上，论者请付狱以正军法，数遣官按治，观望奏报不直，特旨命公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206867_comment'></div>遂驰至泾原，具得其实以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206867_comment'></div>且言：「刘安、种师中有功边陲，愿少宽假，以责来效」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206867_comment'></div>上从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206867_comment'></div>刘安止降秩，士论大惬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206867_comment'></div>崇宁中，陕西铁币日轻，视铜钱不能十一，而官俸独给铁钱，在职者不能赡，官旷不补，事有浸废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206867_comment'></div>因建言倍给选人之俸，凡摄事者理任受举，许同正员，人乐就职，百废具举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206867_comment'></div>公自为幕府，以方略闻，后稍权帅事，将使指，望实益孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206867_comment'></div>上深知其才，驿召赴阙，亟命入对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206867_comment'></div>上问西人兵力，公曰：「夏国本数州之地，盗据灵夏，浸以彊大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206867_comment'></div>元丰中兵临其城下，羌戎壅河决水，士马几歼，遂无成功」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206867_comment'></div>上曰：「灵武终不可取耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206867_comment'></div>公曰：「戎狄之民皆兵也，居不糜廪食，动不劳转输，故便于用众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206867_comment'></div>虽兵之去来，飘忽如风雨，而不能持久，又其所短也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206867_comment'></div>愿申戒边臣，严饬武备，蒐练戎士，积粟坚垒，先为不可胜之计，以观其衅，屈其所长，而乘其所短，则可以得志矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206867_comment'></div>上又问大寨泉可取否，奏曰：「臣闻其地逼近灵武，曩时进取，号为得策，计虑不审，亟筑亟退，反为夏人所有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206867_comment'></div>距汉界百馀里地，皆潟卤无水泉，古所谓瀚海也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206867_comment'></div>间有之，不可饮，马口鼻皆裂，大兵不可往」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206867_comment'></div>审问边将，皆以为然，上首肯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206867_comment'></div>翼日除直龙图阁、知庆州兼环庆路经略安抚使、马步军都总管，再入谢，上宣谕曰：「屡诏环庆进筑，久而无功，今当属卿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206867_comment'></div>乃谢而言曰：「陛下过听以任臣，顾虽绵薄，敢不罄竭，仰承睿训」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206867_comment'></div>旬日凡三进对，所陈边防利害、攻守计策甚众，上深嘉纳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206867_comment'></div>事多施行，削稿不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206867_comment'></div>陛辞，乃赐三品服以宠其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206867_comment'></div>诏趣之镇，即日就道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206867_comment'></div>初，绍圣中城清平关，关之左右皆沃壤，地旷绝无捍蔽，人莫敢耕牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206867_comment'></div>乃即关之东西筑徐丁台、韦章埧，赐名曰安边城，曰归德堡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206867_comment'></div>东西相望，控制要害，包地万馀顷，人得以纵耕其中，岁收以数万计，公私利之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206867_comment'></div>初城徐丁也，一日下令遣发，诸将愕眙，不知所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206867_comment'></div>公曰：「亟往即事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1206867_comment'></div>比及境上，大兵已集，刍粟版筑之物，无一不具，三日而城毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1206867_comment'></div>夏人骇叹，服其神速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1206867_comment'></div>环庆自大寨泉退衄之后，士气沮伤，至是复大振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1206867_comment'></div>踰年移知延安府兼鄜延路经略安抚使、马步军都总管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1206867_comment'></div>河东、陕西皆边夏国，人使文檄往来，独由鄜延，号为西边门户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1206867_comment'></div>凡中国移檄与诸路理办疆事，率由延帅刊定，以付边吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1206867_comment'></div>夏人书檄至密，阅其当受与否，诸边皆禀覆行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1206867_comment'></div>自公至鄜延，每屈之以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1206867_comment'></div>朝廷初用八宝，夏人以所赐御宝大于曩时，言于边，公令边吏谕以御宝度数非臣下所当议，拒却不受，自是西人畏服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1206867_comment'></div>使人入境，所举小不如式，劾引伴者坐之，移檄夏国，责其失礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1206867_comment'></div>其后至者皆惕息惟谨，无敢纵以生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1206867_comment'></div>初，羌人久拒命，上许其纳款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1206867_comment'></div>谍者数言将进誓表，而累岁不效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1206867_comment'></div>公策知敌情，言羌必不来，然至与不至不足问，当严备以待之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1206867_comment'></div>因条上备御之策，上以为然，除集贤殿修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1206867_comment'></div>乃城清远、镇边二寨以遏贼冲，增筑龙泉、御谋二城保聚边民，吾圉益固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1206867_comment'></div>大观初，关辅饥民流至边，因上言：「常平官失职，使流冗就食塞下，则边粟益贵，且非所以示夷狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1206867_comment'></div>宜令所在资送还乡，以振给之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1206867_comment'></div>诏从其请，民得复业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1206867_comment'></div>秋大霖雨，传言敌闻城坏，将大入寇，诸将请起卒之践更者以益兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1206867_comment'></div>朝廷下走马章，敕诸道增严备御，他路调兵骚然，独鄜延按堵如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1206867_comment'></div>因上言：「臣审料夏人决不寇边」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1206867_comment'></div>迄冬果无警，诸老将皆服公料敌精审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1206867_comment'></div>诏以公守边镇静，备御有伦，除徽猷阁待制，仍再任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1206867_comment'></div>西边恃蕃兵弓箭手为用，异时患蕃官侵扰，莫敢绳治，乃悉为约束，犯者无贷，自是皆获安业，人心感服，战守赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1206867_comment'></div>鄜延边袤千里，而诸城疏逖，敌易乘间，乃增置杏子镇、青卢，移万世、屈丁堡，东接河东，西连环庆，声援相属，弥缝边隙，敌不得间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1206867_comment'></div>除显谟阁直学士，复再任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1206867_comment'></div>再上章恳辞，不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1206867_comment'></div>政和初，内侍童贯宣抚陕西，法有弛张可从宜者得罢行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1206867_comment'></div>长安万物腾跃，众货益轻，乃严设科条，欲力平之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1206867_comment'></div>计司承望风旨，取市价率减什四，违者重寘于法，民至罢市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1206867_comment'></div>又行均籴法，贱入民粟，增估金帛以偿之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1206867_comment'></div>下至蕃兵射士之授田者，咸被抑配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1206867_comment'></div>全陕骚然，几至生变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1206867_comment'></div>帅臣诸司不视利病，奉承推行惟恐后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1206867_comment'></div>公独以为不可，极陈其害，章上不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1206867_comment'></div>时贯方用事，权倾中外，人皆为之危慄，而抗章继上，言益切至，士大夫闻章中诋贯论事多质直语，往往争传诵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1206867_comment'></div>坐是贬永州团练副使，永州安置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1206867_comment'></div>然平物价、均籴亦为之罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1206867_comment'></div>在永数月，上念其忠，亟复徽猷阁待制，除永兴军路安抚使、马步军都总管、兼知永兴军府，在道改知兴仁府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1206867_comment'></div>朝廷复行夹锡钱，乃申敕公移一准铜钱，槩用无偏，府中帖然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1206867_comment'></div>旁郡官私与民出纳，自为轻重，民疑以挠，交易不通，始大愧服，乃视兴仁为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1206867_comment'></div>寻移知青州，兼京东东路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1206867_comment'></div>至镇，改充河东路经略安抚使、马步军都总管、兼知太原府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1206867_comment'></div>以童贯领宣抚使，奏乞辞避，玺书褒答不允，河东诸司与被边属郡如代、岚、石、麟、府，咸许以事宜闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1206867_comment'></div>时传虚声，以勤忧顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1206867_comment'></div>公曰阃寄当以静胜，乃严戒边吏，凡制事必慎择可信者，重以赏罚御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1206867_comment'></div>自是警奏不妄，边邮晏如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1206867_comment'></div>政和五年春，以足疾乞领宫祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1206867_comment'></div>章五上，乃得请，提举杭州洞霄宫，复徽猷阁直学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1206867_comment'></div>盗发帮原，声震东南，起知宣州，捍蔽江左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1206867_comment'></div>或告公曰：「宣、歙俱邻于贼，歙破，即宣危矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1206867_comment'></div>公感久疾，可以力辞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1206867_comment'></div>公曰：「方急难中，岂人臣爱身时也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1206867_comment'></div>乃扶疾就任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1206867_comment'></div>时寇兵逼属邑，民大振扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1206867_comment'></div>公之威名凛然，人恃以安，郡境赖之，迄用保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1206867_comment'></div>上心嘉赏，除龙图阁学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1206867_comment'></div>贼平，以疾乞致仕，章三上，未报，特召赴阙，除河东宣抚司参谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1206867_comment'></div>乃力陈老疾，不足备驱策，词意恳至，遂得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1206867_comment'></div>特授正奉大夫致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1206867_comment'></div>家居三年，以疾薨，薨之夕，有星陨于寝室之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1206867_comment'></div>公刚毅方正，见义敢为，不可回夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1206867_comment'></div>虽犯权要，蹈患难，不顾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1206867_comment'></div>胸中无城府，推诚待人，洞见腹心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1206867_comment'></div>持己甚严，而遇下明恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1206867_comment'></div>临政恺悌，人不忍欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1206867_comment'></div>久任帅阃，不为贵倨阔略细务，听讼折狱，纤悉得情，而归于宽厚，民尤感服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1206867_comment'></div>雅以清约自将，一介不妄以取与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1206867_comment'></div>延帅圭田，皆在极边，将吏役所部为之耕种，岁入千计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1206867_comment'></div>公至是乃捐其地募弓箭手，丝毫无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1206867_comment'></div>更两镇凡十馀年，量敌制胜，动中机会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1206867_comment'></div>每以疆吏生事为戒，乃语人曰：「为国守边，安危所系，但当宣国威灵，严于自治，使夷狄不敢侵侮，边邮得以晏然，是为称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1206867_comment'></div>若亲小利，召戎起衅，图尺寸功，冀幸宠荣，吾不忍为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1206867_comment'></div>识者以为至论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1206867_comment'></div>凡所辟荐，不假人以私，必视其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1206867_comment'></div>拔自部曲，多为一时名将，号为知人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1206867_comment'></div>性诚孝，每以褒赠不逮其祖为恨，遂以所得官奏乞回授，特旨从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1206867_comment'></div>敦穆宗族，恩意满至，常遇郊恩，舍其子孙，先官犹子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1206867_comment'></div>斥俸馀置义田宅，近族子孙聚而居之，养生之用，皆取具焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1206867_comment'></div>有文集三十卷，提奏议七十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1206867_comment'></div>娶同郡胡宗说之女，封硕人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1206867_comment'></div>先公十二年卒，赠淑人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1206867_comment'></div>子男二人：长曰耦，承议郎、真州排岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1206867_comment'></div>次曰耚，朝奉郎、通判亳州军州事，以学行吏能见称于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1206867_comment'></div>一女，适从政郎、江宁府溧阳县丞胡朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1206867_comment'></div>孙男九人：曰徽言，登仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1206867_comment'></div>曰太冲，曰如愚，曰康锡，皆承务郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1206867_comment'></div>曰保衡，通仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1206867_comment'></div>馀四人并女尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1206867_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_171_1206867'>烈烈我公，惟时干城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1206867_comment'></div>威加羌戎，一尘不惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1206867_comment'></div>嬖倖恃权，狂澜稽天<span class='inlineComment2'>（缺）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_173_1206867_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　在开封，任迩英殿说书，有经筵讲义十三则。作品：吉人为善节。<div id='poem_1206686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书经筵讲义<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>吉人为善节</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206686")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206686'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206686'>「德惟一，动罔不吉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206686_comment'></div>德二三，动罔不凶」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206686_comment'></div>所谓吉人者，以其德惟一也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206686_comment'></div>所谓凶人者，以其德二三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206686_comment'></div>盖诚则一，不诚则矫诬妄作，故二三，此吉凶所由分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206686_comment'></div>舜鸡鸣而起，禹思日孜孜，寸阴是惜，为善惟日不足也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206686_comment'></div>丹朱惟慢游是好，傲虐是作，罔昼夜，额额为不善，惟日不足也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206686_comment'></div>舜为法于天下，可传于后世，孔子于禹无间然，人君所当法者，舜、禹而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206686_comment'></div>夫世之乱亡之君，非尽无欲善之心，而天下卒至于不治者，以其见善不明，而所谓善者，未必善故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206686_comment'></div>古之欲明明德于天下者，必先于致知，致知所以明善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206686_comment'></div>欲致其知，非学不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206686_comment'></div>故傅说之告其君曰「念终始典于学」以此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1206686_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年1月</a>　在开封，任迩英殿说书，乞罢阉寺防城。作品：上钦宗论不可复近奄人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在开封，任迩英殿说书，作文。作品：上钦宗论不可复近奄人（第二状）论金人入寇札子（其二）乞上殿奏状。上钦宗皇帝（其一）<div id='poem_1206509' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206509' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206509?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论金人入寇劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（二）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206509")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206509_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206509'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206509'>某切计金人倏往倏来，如禽兽然，必不能具糗粮，越数千里而窥我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206509_comment'></div>近边州军宜坚壁清野，勿与之战，使抄略无所得，则当自困矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206509_comment'></div>若攻城略地，本路帅司当遣援兵策应，必未能朝夕下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206509_comment'></div>若彼不为攻城之计，俟其过则附近城寨连兵以蹑其后，如中山、真定之类，有坚城重兵然后出与之战，使之腹背受敌，则可以制胜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206509_comment'></div>要之，彼必不能持久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206509_comment'></div>然今日之事当以收人心为先，人心不附，虽有高城深池，坚甲利兵，不足恃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206509_comment'></div>边事之兴，免夫之役均被海内，人怨神怒，驯致今日，误国之罪宜有归矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206509_comment'></div>小人剥民希宠，其事不一，而西城聚歛，东南花石，其害尤甚，闻有旨一切罢去，此甚盛举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206509_comment'></div>然前此盖尝罢之，诏墨未乾，而花石应奉之舟已衔尾至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206509_comment'></div>今虽复申前令，而祸根不去，人谁信之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206509_comment'></div>欲去祸根，恐大臣难言，但言路得人，必有为朝廷出力者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206509_comment'></div>宿奸巨蠹，借应奉之名豪夺民财，盖不可以数计，天下之人含怒积忿，郁而不得发几二十年矣，欲致人和，去此三者正今日之先务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206509_comment'></div>夫天地之藏取之不竭，实在山泽，摘山煮海之利，天下财计所从出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206509_comment'></div>今榷货所入岁以千万计，皆诸路昔日之经费也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206509_comment'></div>收之中都，诸路一毫不可得，则岁用安得不窘耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206509_comment'></div>凡上供之所须与一路之经费，非出于漕臣之家，取诸民而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206509_comment'></div>此民力所由弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206509_comment'></div>今虽蠲免岁额，罢比较，漕计无与焉，终无益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206509_comment'></div>不若一循旧制，归之漕司，则岁用足而民力自纾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206509_comment'></div>论者必谓舍此朝廷必至于乏用，某切以谓不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206509_comment'></div>若台谏有人，必能为朝廷谋之，则财货可不求而自足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206509_comment'></div>然此事须得人而后见，非毫楮可以预言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206509_comment'></div>祖宗之时，转般与盐法相因以为利，若尽复祖宗之法，则天下事思过半矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206509_comment'></div>今河北山东民之凋弊已甚，虽欲取之，无所取也，所仰者东南而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206509_comment'></div>二浙夷伤之馀，疮痍未合，更诛求不已，则前日方腊之事可以为监者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206509_comment'></div>昔唐方用兵之时，裴度复相，则先以延见士夫为急，故能有成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206509_comment'></div>夫稽于众，舍己从人，舜之为舜，以此而已，况其下者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206509_comment'></div>盖天下之事，非庙堂之心可以独运，合天下之智，则事无不济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206509_comment'></div>唐元和以后数用兵，宰相不休沐，或继火乃得罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206509_comment'></div>李德裕在位，虽遽书警奏，皆从容裁决，率午漏下还第，休沐如平时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206509_comment'></div>德裕宁任独智自运，恝然不以军务为念哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206509_comment'></div>盖镇安人心，不得不如是耳，此皆前事可验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206509_comment'></div>今一有警，则修城池，试挂搭，得无动摇人心乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206509_comment'></div>兼燕人之走中都者填溢衢巷，漫不知其数，虽夷夏有异，而念坟墓，怀庐井，其心则同也，岂无奸细伺隙于其间乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206509_comment'></div>人心一摇，则其祸有不可测者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206509_comment'></div>昔唐太宗寘降寇于内地，仍择酋长备官京师，正与今日之事类，不数年卒为乱，然后驱之塞外，则已晚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206509_comment'></div>此已事之验，不可不监也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206509_comment'></div>当今则不可遽为之，当徐为之，谋庶无后患也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1206509_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206450' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206450' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206450?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞上殿状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年1月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206450")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206450_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206450'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206450'>右，臣伏睹陛下即政之初，适当国家多事之际，凡在臣子，苟有见闻，咸宜自竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206450_comment'></div>况臣备员劝讲，义岂敢默，辄有所见利害，欲面奏陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206450_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降睿旨，令臣上殿敷奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1206450_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206442' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206442' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206442?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上钦宗皇帝疏<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>乞谨号令</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年1月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206442")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206442_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206442'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206442'>《书》曰：「慎乃出令，令出惟行，弗惟反」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206442_comment'></div>欲令之不反，当谨其始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206442_comment'></div>始之不谨，而轻以示人，虽欲不反，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206442_comment'></div>比见敕榜，索金银于士庶之家，不纳者许人告诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206442_comment'></div>既而不行，未一二日又复前诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206442_comment'></div>崇宁以来，令有朝下而夕改者，故宽恤之诏，年一举之，徒挂墙壁而已，而民不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206442_comment'></div>今陛下即位之初，一言之出，臣下禀令，四海观听，尤不可不谨，不宜复蹈前辙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206442_comment'></div>其言有曰「庶免吾民肝脑涂地」，何遽至是耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206442_comment'></div>虽事出仓卒，犹当婉其辞，少存国体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206442_comment'></div>示之以怯惧之形，使狄人轻侮中国，无复忌惮，其失言甚矣，皆不谨令之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206442_comment'></div>孔子曰：「自古皆有死，民无信不立」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206442_comment'></div>夫兵食可去，而信不可去，圣人之垂戒深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206442_comment'></div>臣愿陛下凡诏告中外，当详议而后行，稽孔子无信不立之言，谨乃出令，以一民听，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206442_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年2月8日</a>　在开封。除右谏议大夫兼侍讲，公具辞免，不允。作品：辞免谏议大夫奏状。<div id='poem_1206451' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206451' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206451?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免谏议大夫状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206451")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206451_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206451'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206451'>右，臣二月初八日准尚书省劄子，三省枢密院同奉圣旨，除臣右谏议大夫，日下供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206451_comment'></div>闻命震恐，不知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206451_comment'></div>切惟谏诤之臣以绳愆纠缪为职，宜得刚明之才以充其选，顾臣何人，其敢冒处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206451_comment'></div>伏望圣慈追还成命，以允公议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206451_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在开封。有上表。作品：举吕好问自代。谢除谏议大夫兼侍讲。上钦宗皇帝（其二）上钦宗皇帝（其三）上钦宗皇帝（其四）<div id='poem_1206452' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206452' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206452?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举吕好问自代</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206452")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206452_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206452'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206452'>右，臣伏见朝奉大夫吕好问，勋德之后，蔚有典刑，笃实而多闻，疏通而守正，论议气节，凛然有古诤臣之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206452_comment'></div>非特臣所不如，亦当代难得之士，举以代臣，实允公议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1206452_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206477' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206477' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206477?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除谏议大夫兼侍讲表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206477")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206477_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206477'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206477'>臣某言：伏奉制命，除臣试右谏议大夫兼侍讲，仍赐紫章服者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206477_comment'></div>擢居谏省，叨被误恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206477_comment'></div>进侍经筵，尤惭非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206477_comment'></div>宠荣过分，循省若惊<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206477_comment'></div>窃以怀经世之忠者常患无其时，有适时之才者常患无其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206477_comment'></div>况值离明之继照，仍丁泰吉之大来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206477_comment'></div>周道砥平，舜聪四达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206477_comment'></div>寘在七人之列，是为千载之逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206477_comment'></div>如臣者识昧趋今，学惟泥古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206477_comment'></div>獐头鼠目，何意求官？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206477_comment'></div>马渤牛溲，宁堪待用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206477_comment'></div>顾天下之事，惟谏臣得以尽言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206477_comment'></div>遭圣人之时，非贤者曷胜其任？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206477_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下涓流必受，大壑益深，端一德以当天，奉三无而抚世，故兹庸妄，获与选抡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206477_comment'></div>敢不勉励前修，仰酬洪造？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206477_comment'></div>居官任职，自知无以踰人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206477_comment'></div>补过尽忠，庶勉全于晚节。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1206477_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206443' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206443?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上钦宗皇帝疏<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206443")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206443_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206443'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206443'>臣昨蒙赐对，妄以狂瞽之言上论宰相，陛下不加斧钺之诛，寘之言路，臣虽糜捐无以报称。<div class='inline'
