id='poem_sentence_0_1206443_comment'></div>比闻士民伏阙以数万计，诟詈大臣，发其隐慝，无所不至，盖国人之所共弃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206443_comment'></div>夫爵刑，天之所以命有德，讨有罪，虽人君不得而私焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206443_comment'></div>《书》曰：「天聪明自我民聪明，天明畏自我民明畏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206443_comment'></div>则人君所以奉天者，亦因诸民而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206443_comment'></div>民之所弃，天实讨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206443_comment'></div>方陛下临御之初，适当艰难之际，宰相尤宜考择，内修政事，外攘夷狄，非得真贤不足胜其任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206443_comment'></div>惟陛下早留意焉，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206443_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206444' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206444?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月18日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206444_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206444'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206444'>臣窃惟河朔为朝廷重地，三镇又为河朔之要藩，自周世宗迄于艺祖、太宗，百战而后得之，其艰难甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206444_comment'></div>一旦弃之，姑以舒目前之急则可，以为经远之计则未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206444_comment'></div>方寇骑之来，士不素养，欲战则无其人，艛橹未修，欲守则无其具，割地赐金，势有不得已者，臣故曰以纾目前之急则可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206444_comment'></div>河朔郡县犬牙相错，今以三镇二十州之地与之，贯吾腹中，则一方边面裂而三矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206444_comment'></div>建城壁，备器械，练兵积谷，未易以岁月计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206444_comment'></div>其距京城无藩篱之固，寇骑疾驱不数日而至，又非前日之比，岂不殆哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206444_comment'></div>臣故曰以为经远之计则未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206444_comment'></div>四方勤王之师逾月而后集，使之无功而去，厚赐之则无名，不与则生怨，后有缓急，召之宜有不受命者，不可不虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206444_comment'></div>姚平仲之出，杀伤相当，未为大衄，胜负兵家之常数，未足为深戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206444_comment'></div>传闻三镇之民欲以死拒之，万一不守，则数州之众肝脑涂地矣，朝廷宁忍坐视而不救乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206444_comment'></div>臣窃谓三镇拒其前，吾以重兵蹑其后，使之腹背受敌，宜若可为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206444_comment'></div>臣本书生，军旅之事未之学也，不敢自信其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206444_comment'></div>有如种师中、刘光世之徒，皆一时名将，始至而未用，臣欲乞陛下召至榻前，问以方略可否，必有定论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206444_comment'></div>苟有万全之计，不可失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206444_comment'></div>朝廷欲专守和议，以契丹百年之好犹不能保，宁能保此强寇乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206444_comment'></div>然朝廷许与金银以千万计，秋高马肥，乘间而来，责其偿者，彼不为无辞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206444_comment'></div>当是时，金银不可复取之于民，援兵不可以卒致，其患有不可胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206444_comment'></div>孔子与蒲人盟曰「要盟」，神不听，卒渝之，不以为不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206444_comment'></div>今良将劲卒，咸欲自效，失此不为，则后将噬脐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206444_comment'></div>惟陛下留神而审处之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1206444_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206445' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206445' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206445?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月18日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206445_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206445'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206445'>臣窃观自汉迄唐，待戎狄之道无如祖宗之时，百年之间，民生戴白，不见兵革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206445_comment'></div>奸臣要功，为国生事，与恶而弃好，驯致今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206445_comment'></div>方寇骑逼城，备御无素，卑辞厚礼以纾目前之急，盖势有不得已而然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206445_comment'></div>割要害之地以为盟好，则非经远之计也，臣固尝论矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206445_comment'></div>比闻金人驻兵磁、相，劫掳无有纪极，破大名成安一县，驱掠子女二千馀人，杀令佐二人而去，誓书之墨未乾，而背不旋踵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206445_comment'></div>吾虽欲专守和议，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206445_comment'></div>昔赵割六县之地使赵郝约事于秦，虞卿谓赵王曰：「秦之攻王也，倦而归乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206445_comment'></div>王以其力尚能进，爱王而不攻乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206445_comment'></div>王曰：「秦不遗馀力矣，必以倦而归也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206445_comment'></div>虞卿曰：「秦以其力攻其所不能取，倦而归，王又以其力之所不能取以送之，是助秦自攻也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206445_comment'></div>今日之事正类于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206445_comment'></div>夫去其巢穴，越数千里之远而犯人之国都，盖危道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206445_comment'></div>使其力能攻之，则城中之物皆其有也，尚何事求哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206445_comment'></div>彼见吾高城深池，未易轻犯，勤王之师四面而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206445_comment'></div>姚平仲固尝与之交兵矣，忍而不敢怒，请和而去，则其情可见，盖亦惧而归，非爱我而不攻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206445_comment'></div>朝廷割三镇二十州之地与之，是亦助寇而自攻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206445_comment'></div>闻肃王初与约，及河而返，今挟之而往，此败盟之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206445_comment'></div>臣窃谓朝廷宜以肃王为问，责其败盟，必得肃王后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206445_comment'></div>三镇之民以死拒之于前，而吾以重兵拥其后，势必得所欲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206445_comment'></div>若犹未从，则声言其罪而讨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206445_comment'></div>夫师以直为壮，是举直在我矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206445_comment'></div>三镇闻之，士气必振，此万全之计，不可失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206445_comment'></div>若三镇穷蹙而王师不救，则其民必谓朝廷视其涂炭而莫之恤，则戴后之心懈，而大事去矣，不可不虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206445_comment'></div>窃闻出师之令，庙算不一，屡行而屡反，如是则士气必懈惰，欲其成功，难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206445_comment'></div>唐宪宗平淮西，韩愈谓凡此蔡功惟断乃成，未有举大事不断而能成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206445_comment'></div>伏望断自宸衷，无惑于浮议，则天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1206445_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在开封。有奏文。作品：上钦宗论父子天性宜一于诚。上钦宗论宣仁诬谤未明瑶华位号未复。上钦宗乞分别邪正消除党与。上钦宗乞罢茶盐榷法。诏以右谏议大夫兼国子祭酒。上钦宗论用人太易。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年3月</a>　在开封。转朝奉大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年4月</a>　在开封。有奏乞诛姚古。作品：上钦宗皇帝（其五）<div id='poem_1206446' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206446' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206446?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上钦宗皇帝疏<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206446")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206446_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206446'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206446'>臣窃惟太原，天下之根本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206446_comment'></div>唐高祖起晋阳，后唐庄宗、石晋、刘智远辈皆据有太原而取天下，自古以来未有不以为重地也，罕一举而取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206446_comment'></div>契丹，剧贼也，今围太原累月，顿兵不移，包藏祸心，岂易量哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206446_comment'></div>姚古拥重兵为援，逗留不进，万一太原不守，其祸有不可测者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206446_comment'></div>军政如此，何以用人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206446_comment'></div>昔周世宗伐李筠，诸将望风而奔，世宗自力战，大败归，卧帐中不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206446_comment'></div>太祖曰：「何不尽诛大将，以偏裨代之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206446_comment'></div>世宗大喜，起坐曰：「正合朕意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206446_comment'></div>于是斩樊爱能以下数十人，一举而取高平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206446_comment'></div>自是兵威震天下，遂以平诸国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206446_comment'></div>今姚古坐视太原危急而不救，死有馀辜，释而不诛，则无以振国威矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206446_comment'></div>臣愿陛下用太祖之言，法世宗之断，诛姚古以肃军政，拔偏裨之可将者代之，明示赏罚，使士各用命，庶乎太原可全也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1206446_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在开封。上书论姚古不救太原。作品：上钦宗皇帝（其六）<div id='poem_1206447' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206447' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206447?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上钦宗皇帝疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（六　靖康元年四月）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206447")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206447_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206447'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206447'>臣比闻粘罕三月中自太原分兵入汾州界，至四月复还太原，往来二州之间，如在无人之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206447_comment'></div>所经县镇焚劫屠戮，殆无孑遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206447_comment'></div>王师坐视不救，若非己事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206447_comment'></div>至四月半，贼离汾州还太原，统制林良器等四人方至汾州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206447_comment'></div>入城十馀日，坐糜廪粟，无敢向敌者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206447_comment'></div>姚古节制诸将，拥重兵，躬自逗留不进，宜诸将皆无肯用命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206447_comment'></div>臣尝论姚古逗留，当以军法从事，久未蒙施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206447_comment'></div>今太原围闭累月，危急甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206447_comment'></div>访闻大兵尚在威胜军，无一人一骑入太原境者，惟范琼不受姚古节制，独能引兵稍进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206447_comment'></div>诸将逗留，古实为之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206447_comment'></div>奈何惜一姚古不诛，坐视要害之地而不救乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206447_comment'></div>万一太原之民以王师不救，必谓朝廷弃之，别生异心，则祸起肘腋，非金人之比，不可不虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206447_comment'></div>自金人残灭契丹，人人知其必有南窥之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206447_comment'></div>郭药师，逆贼也，包藏祸心，亦人人知其必反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206447_comment'></div>王安中见祸乱已形，觊幸脱归，不复以告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206447_comment'></div>蔡靖抗章论奏，而白时中、李邦彦、蔡攸、蔡懋等蔽蒙苟安，恬不加恺，浸成大患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206447_comment'></div>今太原危急如此，朝廷当以前事为监，不可缓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206447_comment'></div>一失太原，则大事去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206447_comment'></div>臣愿陛下明诏大臣悉力措画，速正姚古逗留之罪，诛之以肃军政，遴柬有武略可任者代之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206447_comment'></div>偏裨犹有不用命者，一以军法从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206447_comment'></div>庶几士气稍振，使敌人有所忌惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206447_comment'></div>若朝廷未欲遽诛大将，姑用唐故事尽行削夺，使白衣从军，以责后效，犹之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206447_comment'></div>不尔，则秋冬之交，风劲草衰，强寇长驱而南，益无忌惮，悔无及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206447_comment'></div>惟陛下留神而幸听之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1206447_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年5月</a>　在开封。上书乞追夺王安石爵，毁去孔庙配享之像。准奏。谏官冯獬上疏诋公，公亦罢祭酒。作品：上钦宗皇帝（其七）<div id='poem_1206448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上钦宗皇帝疏<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206448")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206448'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206448'>臣伏见蔡京用事二十馀年，蠹国害民，几危宗社，人所切齿，而论其罪者曾莫知其所本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206448_comment'></div>盖京以继述神宗皇帝为名，实挟王安石以图身利，故推尊安石，加以王爵，配享孔子庙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206448_comment'></div>而京所为自谓得安石之意，使无得而议，其小有异者，则以不忠不孝之名目之，痛加窜黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206448_comment'></div>人皆结舌莫敢为言，而京得以肆意妄为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206448_comment'></div>则致今日之祸者，实安石有以启之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206448_comment'></div>臣谨按，安石挟管商之术，饰六艺以文奸言，变乱祖宗法度，当时司马光已言其为害当见于数十年之后，今日之事，若合符契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206448_comment'></div>其著为邪说以涂学者耳目，败坏其心术者，不可缕数，姑即其为今日之害尤甚者一二事以明之，则其为邪说可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206448_comment'></div>昔神宗皇帝尝称美汉文惜百金以罢露台，曰：「朕为天下守财耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206448_comment'></div>此谨乃俭德，惟怀永图，正宜将顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206448_comment'></div>安石乃言：「陛下若能以尧舜之道治天下，虽竭天下以自奉不为过，守财之言非正理」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206448_comment'></div>曾不知尧舜茅茨土阶，未尝竭天下以自奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206448_comment'></div>其称禹曰「克俭于家」，则竭天下以自奉者，必非尧舜之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206448_comment'></div>其后王黼以应奉花石之事，竭天下之力，号为享上，实安石竭天下自奉之说有以倡之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206448_comment'></div>其释《凫鹥》守成之诗，于末章则谓：「以道守成者，役使群众，泰而不为骄，宰制万物，费而不为侈，孰敝敝然以爱为事」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206448_comment'></div>夫《凫鹥》之五章特曰：「凫鹥在亹，公尸来止熏熏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206448_comment'></div>旨酒欣欣，燔炙芬芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206448_comment'></div>公尸燕饮，无有后艰」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206448_comment'></div>诗之所言，正谓能持盈，则神祇祖考安乐之而无后艰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206448_comment'></div>自古释之者，未有为泰而不为骄，费而不为侈之说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206448_comment'></div>安石独倡为此说，以启人主之侈心，其后蔡京辈轻费妄用，专以侈靡为事，盖祖此说耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206448_comment'></div>则安石邪说之害，岂不甚哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206448_comment'></div>臣伏望睿断正安石学术之缪，追夺王爵，明诏中外，毁去配享之像，使淫辞不为学者之惑，实天下万世之幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1206448_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　又乞追还元佑诸公旧职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　公屡上章乞罢谏省，不允。作品：辞免谏议侍讲奏状（其一）辞免谏议侍讲奏状（其二）辞免谏议侍讲奏状（其三）辞免谏议侍讲奏状（其四）<div id='poem_1206453' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206453' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206453?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免谏议侍讲状<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　五月初十日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年5月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206453")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206453_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206453'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206453'>右，臣准开封府告示，奉圣旨，学官等并罢，臣自罢权祭酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206453_comment'></div>切念臣退伏田庐，杜门待尽十有馀年，误蒙上皇召自閒废之中，寘之馆阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206453_comment'></div>陛下即位，复被眷知，擢居谏省，仍侍经幄，兼权祭酒，顾虽糜捐，无以报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206453_comment'></div>而臣自供职以来，论事无补，人微望重，学术谬愆，无以镇服士心，自取悔吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206453_comment'></div>尚赖天度包荒，未加窜殛，私自省循，无所容措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206453_comment'></div>所有谏垣经筵之任，尤难冒居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206453_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐罢免，除臣福建路合入差遣或宫祠，任便居住，以安愚分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206453_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206454' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206454' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206454?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免谏议侍讲状<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　五月十四日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年5月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206454")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206454_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206454'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206454'>右，臣误蒙陛下擢寘谏垣，仍兼劝讲，皆朝廷高选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206454_comment'></div>顾臣庸虚，不足任职，加以老病交侵，目视昏眊，两胫痹弱，行立俱艰，虽欲贪荣冒居，力所不逮，已尝具状乞赐罢免，除臣福建路合入差遣或宫祠，任便居住，以安愚分，未蒙指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206454_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐矜悯，检会前奏施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1206454_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206455' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206455' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206455?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免谏议侍讲状<span class='inlineComment2'>（三　十六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年5月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206455")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206455_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206455'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206455'>右，臣伏蒙陛下以臣奏乞福建路差遣或宫观，任便居住，赐诏不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206455_comment'></div>特恩曲被，感激涕零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206455_comment'></div>切念臣年逾七十，疾病交侵，目昏不能远视，足弱难于久立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206455_comment'></div>近有章疏，皆封以入，不请对，亦常冒闻天听，陛下所知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206455_comment'></div>实恐因此旷败，旁招人言，陛下迫于公议，虽欲终始保全，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206455_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐矜悯，检会前奏施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1206455_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206456' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206456' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206456?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免谏议侍讲状<span class='inlineComment2'>（四　二十四日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年5月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206456")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206456_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206456'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206456'>右，臣准尚书省今月二十四日劄子，以臣累奏乞福建路差遣或宫观，任便居住，奉圣旨不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206456_comment'></div>臣不避严诛，再沥血诚，上干天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206456_comment'></div>伏念臣陋学浅闻，论事无补，不惟德薄望轻，不足任职，而犬马之齿已逾七十，加以疾病交攻，日虞颠仆，虽欲贪荣冒居，实所不逮，伏望圣慈检会前奏施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1206456_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年6月4日</a>　乞致仕。作品：乞致仕奏状。<div id='poem_1206457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206457?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞致仕状<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月四日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年6月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206457")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206457'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206457'>右，臣累上封章乞福建路合入差遣或宫祠，任便居住，伏蒙圣慈未赐俞允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206457_comment'></div>切念臣犬马之齿已逾七十，礼律皆当引年辞禄，陛下圣度优容，未加废斥，天地之恩无以论报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206457_comment'></div>近日疾病交攻，腰膝痹疼，乘骑不便，日有颠仆之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206457_comment'></div>在告几月，久废职事，坐糜饩廪，义实难安，不敢再有陈请，乞守本官致仕，以安愚分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206457_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　除给事中，具奉辞免，降诏不允。作品：辞免给事中奏状（其一）辞免给事中奏状（其二）辞免给事中奏状（其三）<div id='poem_1206458' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206458' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206458?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免给事中状<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　六月九日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年6月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206458")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206458_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206458'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206458'>右，臣准尚书省劄子，伏蒙圣恩除臣给事中者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206458_comment'></div>闻命震惊，无所容措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206458_comment'></div>伏念臣老病交侵，不任朝谒，方乞解官致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206458_comment'></div>求去而获迁，是美官要职可以要致也，岂惟于臣私义不安，实恐上累朝廷名器有滥授之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206458_comment'></div>伏望睿慈追还成命，检会前奏施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1206458_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206459' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206459' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206459?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免给事中状<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　十八日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年6月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206459")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206459'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206459'>右，臣准尚书省劄子，以臣辞免给事中恩命，奉圣旨不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206459_comment'></div>闻命惶惧，罔知攸措，不敢苟避烦渎之诛，须至再竭悃诚，上干天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206459_comment'></div>伏念臣年逾七十，已上封章乞解官致仕，误蒙睿恩除臣前件差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206459_comment'></div>臣虽至愚，岂不知贪恋圣明，进居要职，足为荣耀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206459_comment'></div>实以衰病交侵，不任朝谒，老不知止，贻笑缙绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206459_comment'></div>伏望圣慈追还成命，令臣致仕，以安愚分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1206459_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206460' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206460?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免给事中状<span class='inlineComment2'>（三　二十八日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年6月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206460")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206460_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206460'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206460'>右，臣伏蒙圣慈以臣辞免给事中，乞解官致仕，赐诏不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206460_comment'></div>睿恩误被，蔀屋生光，宠逾分涯，但深感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206460_comment'></div>切惟七十致仕，著在礼律，士夫所宜循守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206460_comment'></div>而臣犬马之齿七十有四，背经违律，负罪多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206460_comment'></div>岂不知退伏田庐，躬耕食力，孰若日近清光，坐享厚禄之为安荣也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206460_comment'></div>实以衰病，筋力不支，兼臣方引年辞位，遂蒙迁擢，使臣黾勉扶病就职，必致人言，冒宠之诛，无以自逭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206460_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣诚恳，特降睿旨，令臣致仕，以安愚分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206460_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年6月</a>　乞致仕，不允，有谢表。作品：谢赐诏乞致仕不允表。<div id='poem_1206478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐诏乞致仕不允表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206478")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206478'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206478'>臣某言：伏蒙圣慈，以臣辞免给事中、乞致仕，赐诏不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206478_comment'></div>异恩俯及，省分非宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206478_comment'></div>祗服训辞，惟知感涕<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206478_comment'></div>伏念臣赋材谫薄，禀命奇穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206478_comment'></div>遭时清明，误被抡选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206478_comment'></div>空坐糜于饩廪，讫无补于丝毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206478_comment'></div>老病交侵，神志俱耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206478_comment'></div>筋骸痹弱，屣履如遗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206478_comment'></div>头目眩昏，看朱成碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206478_comment'></div>日怀丘首之念，亟图曳尾之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206478_comment'></div>屡竭悃诚，未回天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206478_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下举无弃物，常善救人，凡在钧陶之中，不遗瓦甓之贱，致兹庸陋，亦未弃捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206478_comment'></div>虽老马已疲，尚羁于伏枥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206478_comment'></div>而敝帷之赐，终冀于深仁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1206478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　乞宫观。作品：乞宫观札子。<div id='poem_1206510' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206510' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206510?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞宫观劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206510")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206510_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206510'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206510'>某叨被诏恩，擢侍经幄，遂获切近清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206510_comment'></div>某虽至愚，岂不知幸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206510_comment'></div>特以衰病侵凌，两胫痹弱，跪拜俱艰，不任朝谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206510_comment'></div>年逾七十，旦暮人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206510_comment'></div>食贫累重，未能引年辞位，忍耻侥求，冀得宫祠之禄，尽此馀年，负罪多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206510_comment'></div>伏望钧慈察其诚恳，特为奏除一宫观差遣，任便居住，使垂尽之年，不至失所，不胜幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1206510_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年7月4日</a>　在开封，除徽猷阁直学士，提举西京嵩山崇福宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在开封，辞免徽猷阁直学士，降诏不允。作品：辞免徽猷阁直学士奏状（其一）辞免徽猷阁直学士奏状（其二）辞免徽猷阁直学士奏状（其三）<div id='poem_1206461' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206461' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206461?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免徽猷阁直学士状<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　七月五日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年7月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206461")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206461_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206461'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206461'>右，臣准尚书省劄子，七月四日三省同奉圣旨，除臣徽猷阁直学士，差提举西京嵩山崇福宫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206461_comment'></div>叨被圣恩，荣愧交集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206461_comment'></div>伏念臣以衰病乞骸，特蒙睿慈，曲垂矜悯，未即弃捐，尚畀宫祠之禄，天地生成之恩，无以论报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206461_comment'></div>所有直学士之职，非臣凉薄所堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206461_comment'></div>伏望陛下追寝成命，乞守本官提举崇福宫，以安愚分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1206461_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206462?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免徽猷阁直学士状<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　十七日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年7月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206462")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206462_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206462'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206462'>右，臣伏蒙圣慈以臣辞免徽猷阁直学士恩命，赐诏不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206462_comment'></div>祗奉宸纶，益深震惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206462_comment'></div>切惟直学士之职，自祖宗以来，未有自谏省躐等而授者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206462_comment'></div>臣虽蒙除给事中，即未曾供职，资浅望轻，义难冒处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206462_comment'></div>伏望陛下特降睿旨，追寝成命，庶协公议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1206462_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206463' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206463' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206463?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免徽猷阁直学士状<span class='inlineComment2'>（三　二十六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年7月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206463")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206463_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206463'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206463'>右，臣伏蒙圣慈以臣辞免徽猷阁直学士，赐诏不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206463_comment'></div>臣愚屡竭悃诚，上干天听，烦渎之罪，宜无所逃，夙夜忧惶，罔知攸措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206463_comment'></div>然臣义有未安，不敢苟止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206463_comment'></div>切惟延阁之命，尤为华选，祖宗以来，未尝轻授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206463_comment'></div>方朝廷修明百度，一循旧制，裁抑侥倖，理宜谨始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206463_comment'></div>臣岂敢以蝼蚁之微，首犯名分，贪荣冒居，上紊典宪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206463_comment'></div>伏望陛下特降睿旨，追还成命，以实公议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206463_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年7月</a>　在开封，钦宗察杨时恳辞，改除徽猷阁待制，提举崇福宫。有谢表。作品：谢除待制表。<div id='poem_1206479' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206479' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206479?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除待制表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206479")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206479_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206479'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206479'>效职无闻，自宜力去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206479_comment'></div>锡恩甚宠，尤在牢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206479_comment'></div>尚叨延阁之华，仍窃直祠之廪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206479_comment'></div>拊存备至，感激难言<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206479_comment'></div>伏念臣材不适时，学惟泥古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206479_comment'></div>久安朴野，已难彊于筋骸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206479_comment'></div>晚际休明，固愿张其肝胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206479_comment'></div>既不能媚俗以同众，又无以扬己而取名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206479_comment'></div>顾蒲柳之已衰，亦风波之足畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206479_comment'></div>加之疾疢，重积凌兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206479_comment'></div>念公朝当责实之时，而谏省非养閒之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206479_comment'></div>粗知出处进退之节，敢不乞身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206479_comment'></div>岂图终始悯怜之私，未令失禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206479_comment'></div>暨丐还于秘职，遂冒贡以忱辞，虽尽力于循墙，犹忝荣于持橐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206479_comment'></div>向非全度，何以曲成？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206479_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下盛德溥临，大明旁烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206479_comment'></div>欲招徕于忠直，庶兴起于治功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206479_comment'></div>故于谏诤之官，务尽优容之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206479_comment'></div>倘不能而知止，亦终惠之有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206479_comment'></div>致此摧颓，荐膺眷渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206479_comment'></div>臣谨当祗承大赐，钦颂至言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206479_comment'></div>景迫桑榆，勉报丘山之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206479_comment'></div>心倾葵藿，敢忘雨露之施！</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1206479_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年7月</a>　在开封。徽猷阁待制，提举崇福宫。作品：向太中墓志铭。<div id='poem_1206870' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206870' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206870?labeling=true' target='_blank'>向太中墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（靖康元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206870")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206870_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206870'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206870'>向氏自微子封于宋，左师戌始见于《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206870_comment'></div>秦汉而下无显者，至文简公起布衣，相真宗，勋名载国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206870_comment'></div>继以钦圣宪肃皇后配神宗，以盛德母仪天下，向氏遂为著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206870_comment'></div>公讳某，字某，文简之曾孙，钦圣宪肃之从弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206870_comment'></div>生而有异禀，自幼不戏弄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206870_comment'></div>八岁而孤，哀毁如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206870_comment'></div>及长，挺然有立，为众所钦惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206870_comment'></div>用宪肃恩补右班殿直，调曹州定陶尉，监秦州酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206870_comment'></div>用荐者移伏羌城兵马监押，又用荐者移通远军管界巡检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206870_comment'></div>特旨差熙河路计置物货局，陕西转运使奏辟催促钱纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206870_comment'></div>四迁至西头供奉官，遂以太子右司御率府率致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206870_comment'></div>以子封迁太子右卫率，又四迁为右骁卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206870_comment'></div>官制行，四迁为武功大夫，莱州团练使，荣州防御使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206870_comment'></div>换文资，两迁至太中大夫致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206870_comment'></div>靖康元年六月七日，以疾终于正寝，享年六十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206870_comment'></div>公虽出于贵胄，而清约如寒儒，啬于自奉，而亲族之有匮急者则周之，不为有无计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206870_comment'></div>字兄之孤与己子，人不见其异也，中外辑睦无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206870_comment'></div>诸子游仕四方，有以鲜衣献者，辄藏之不服，曰：「昔吾父母未尝有也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206870_comment'></div>于人无德不酬，而有负于己者，未尝形言色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206870_comment'></div>尝寓居棣州之七里镇，清河水暴泛，居人危惧，公身率千馀人负土筑堤为捍蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206870_comment'></div>堤成，水至不为患，镇人德之，至今不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206870_comment'></div>定陶素多盗，公为尉，威望隐然，盗潜伏出境，无敢犯者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206870_comment'></div>涖事所至有能称，年未及奉身而归，用不究其才，论者惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206870_comment'></div>然居都城几三十年，优游卒岁，视天下无一物足以撄其心者，其所得多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206870_comment'></div>祖讳某，故任国子博士，赠开府仪同三司、守太尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206870_comment'></div>祖母二李氏，皆累封太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206870_comment'></div>父讳某，故任西京左藏库副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206870_comment'></div>母王氏，封太康县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206870_comment'></div>娶夏侯氏，朝奉郎某之女，有贤行，配公无违德，累封令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206870_comment'></div>子男十二人：曰某，中奉大夫、权发遣京东路计度转运副使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206870_comment'></div>某，武经郎、河间府路安抚司准备将领，为国死事，赠武功郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206870_comment'></div>某，中奉大夫、河北东路宣抚司勾当公事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206870_comment'></div>某，朝请郎、知虢州卢氏县事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206870_comment'></div>某，儒林郎、知太原府平晋县事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206870_comment'></div>某，通直郎、新中山府司录事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206870_comment'></div>某，忠翊郎、监通天门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206870_comment'></div>某，迪功郎、新渭川白马县丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206870_comment'></div>馀皆早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206870_comment'></div>女九人：长适宗室右班殿直令钟，幼适文林郎吴并，馀皆先公卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206870_comment'></div>孙男二十七人，女十六人：某女，长适进士王叔夏，馀并幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206870_comment'></div>诸孤将以是年七月某日葬公于丰台村，状公之行，请铭于余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206870_comment'></div>余虽未及识公，而与其子游，习闻其风旧矣，乃为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206870_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1206870'>公于轩裳，脱若蝉蜕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206870_comment'></div>清约自将，其德靡悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206870_comment'></div>有子之贤，庆流必长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206870_comment'></div>将大厥声，公为不亡。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1206870_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　将离开封。上奏乞选将练兵，乞为《靖康会计录》作品：上渊圣皇帝。<div id='poem_1206437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上渊圣皇帝疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206437")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206437'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206437'>臣以凡庸之才叨被误恩，擢寘谏垣，仍侍经幄，丝毫未有所补，而迫以桑榆晚暮，衰病日侵，不足以任职，引年之请，屡渎天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206437_comment'></div>伏蒙陛下眷怜，未忍摈弃，授以宫祠之禄，使毕此馀生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206437_comment'></div>天地之恩，无以报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206437_comment'></div>念将去国，恐自此遂填沟壑，无复再瞻清光，犬马之情，不能自已，谨竭所闻以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206437_comment'></div>伏望陛下清閒之燕，俯赐览观，庶或补于万分，臣不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206437_comment'></div>臣闻古之欲明明德于天下者先治其国，欲治其国者先齐其家，欲齐其家者先修其身，欲修其身者先正其心，欲正其心者先诚其意，欲诚其意者先致其知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206437_comment'></div>致知在格物，物格而后知至，知至而后意诚，意诚而后心正，心正而后身修，身修而后家齐，家齐而后国治，国治而后天下平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206437_comment'></div>自一身之修，推而至于天下，无二道也，本诸诚意而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206437_comment'></div>臣窃观陛下育德东宫十有馀年，惟诗书是习，玩好声色之奉不接于耳目，虽名实未加于上下，而恭俭之德天下已孚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206437_comment'></div>临御之初，东寇未平，北骑寻至，城无楼橹，士不素练，守御之具阙如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206437_comment'></div>城中之民安恃而无恐者，惟陛下盛德耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206437_comment'></div>未平之寇，皆投戈负耒，复为力耕之农，岂一人一日之力所能胜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206437_comment'></div>诚意感通，而人自服从，其效可见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206437_comment'></div>自古愿治之君，惟在慎一相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206437_comment'></div>盖宰相人主之心膂也，台谏耳目也，百执事股肱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206437_comment'></div>心膂之谋虑不深，耳目之视听不明，股肱之宣力不彊，而能安其身者未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206437_comment'></div>臣窃谓君臣相与之际，尤当以诚意为主，一有不诚，则任贤不能勿贰，去邪不能勿疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206437_comment'></div>忠邪不分，鲜克以济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206437_comment'></div>昔在仁祖时，韩琦为谏官，论四执政，一日而尽去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206437_comment'></div>有唐陈师合言人主不可假宰相以事权，太宗曰：「是欲间吾君臣也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206437_comment'></div>遂逐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206437_comment'></div>故贞观、嘉祐之治几至三代，此任贤去邪之效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206437_comment'></div>若仁祖而不明，则必以韩琦之言为已甚，太宗而怀贰，则必以师合之言为忠，岂不殆哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206437_comment'></div>近见台谏有言宰相者，陛下两置而不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206437_comment'></div>使言之无实而不罪，则谗邪谮愬者得以肆其奸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206437_comment'></div>言之有实而不行，则鄙夫患失者得以安其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206437_comment'></div>如是而求治，臣知其难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206437_comment'></div>唐中宗时，崔琬对仗弹宗楚客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206437_comment'></div>故事，大臣被弹则俯伏趋出，立朝堂待罪，楚客更愤怒自陈忠鲠为琬所诬，中宗不穷问，命琬与楚客结为兄弟以和解之，故中宗卒有和事之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206437_comment'></div>和事非人主之美称也，可不监之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206437_comment'></div>臣愿陛下明是非，辨邪正，有罪则去，妄言必诛，则小大之臣有所惩戒，咸怀忠良矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206437_comment'></div>如是而天下不治，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206437_comment'></div>夫舜之命禹征苗也，禹以益赞之言而班师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206437_comment'></div>二臣未尝禀命也，而安行之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206437_comment'></div>舜亦诞敷文德，而莫之问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206437_comment'></div>以后世言之，二臣遂事之诛，宜无所逃也，非君臣相与以诚，绝无间言，乌有是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206437_comment'></div>人君之任臣，当慎其始而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206437_comment'></div>苟非其人，虽一日居其位不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206437_comment'></div>疑而用之，其弊有不可胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206437_comment'></div>初，德宗在藩邸，亲见代宗为政之弊，嬖溺奄宦，为缙绅祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206437_comment'></div>及其即位，痛惩之，省四方不急之贡，罢梨园乐工及献珍禽奇兽怪草异木，纵驯象四十有二于荆山之阳，又出宫女数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206437_comment'></div>中外耸观，谓太平可以立致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206437_comment'></div>淄青军士至投戈相顾曰：「明主出矣，吾属犹反乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206437_comment'></div>疏斥宦官，亲任朝士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206437_comment'></div>张涉、薛邕之徒，俱以儒雅入侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206437_comment'></div>已而二人继以赃败，于是始疑在庭之臣无可倚信者，而宦官因得藉口，故近习用而朝士疏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206437_comment'></div>盖其任臣，其始不慎择故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206437_comment'></div>夫南北司相为轻重，此重则彼轻，此轻则彼重，理之必至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206437_comment'></div>其后歛天下之财，归之大盈，以为私藏，借商除陌税间架之令行，而天下骚然矣，其弊益甚于代宗之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206437_comment'></div>奄人用事，至持天下之柄授之，卒有门生国老之称，可胜痛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206437_comment'></div>盖其初出于一时之锐，无至诚不已之心以持之，未有终不变者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206437_comment'></div>此前世覆车之辙，可以为监矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206437_comment'></div>近闻百工技巧虽尽废罢，犹私畜于宦臣之家，觊幸异时投间而入，不可不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206437_comment'></div>窃闻道路之言顿异前日，虽细民无知，亦朝廷有以召之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206437_comment'></div>自正月以来，屡降德音，尽复祖宗之旧赋外，征歛并行蠲除，闾巷欢忻鼓舞，日需膏泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206437_comment'></div>今既数月矣，未有一事如祖宗之时者，赋外征歛，率由旧贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206437_comment'></div>自崇宁迄于宣和，宽恤之诏，岁一举之，宣之通衢而人不听，挂之墙壁而人不睹，以其文具而实不至故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206437_comment'></div>陛下嗣守神器，尤宜慎始，诏令如此，是亦文具而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206437_comment'></div>后虽有德意，人谁信之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206437_comment'></div>孟子曰：「得天下有道，得其民，斯得天下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206437_comment'></div>得其民有道，得其心，斯得民矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206437_comment'></div>夫民者，邦本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206437_comment'></div>一失其心，则邦本摇矣，不可不虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206437_comment'></div>然边陲未宁，勤王之师无虑数十万计，萃于朔方，日费不赀，而边郡残破，十无一二，涓流积之而尾闾泄之，臣知其不易供也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206437_comment'></div>朝廷未能一如诏旨不取于民者，亦事有不可得已耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206437_comment'></div>而远方百姓，盖未之知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206437_comment'></div>人君高拱于一堂之上，而四方万里之远，欲上之德户知之，臣恐非智力所及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206437_comment'></div>《周官》掸人「掌诵王志，道国之政事，巡天下邦国而语之」，正为此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206437_comment'></div>臣愿陛下修掸人之官，每路遣使一员，慎简忠信可任者，使诵上志，道国之政事，遍历所部而语之，候边事稍宁，兵革衰息，则赋外蠲除悉如前诏，不为虚文，使百姓晓然知息肩之有期，则人将和悦而正王面矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206437_comment'></div>此今日之急务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206437_comment'></div>仍令询究民之利病可以兴除者，吏之能否可以升黜者，弊政良法可以罢行者，条具以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206437_comment'></div>方嬖倖持权，官吏出其门者日求珍货以媚悦之，奸赃狼籍，无敢谁何者，上下相蒙，贿以成俗，污染之久，未易遽革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206437_comment'></div>臣尝论其一二，虽蒙施行，不过放罢而已，未尝究治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206437_comment'></div>昔成王以商之顽民封康叔，则告之曰：「敬明乃罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206437_comment'></div>人有小罪，非眚，乃惟终，自作不典，式尔，有厥罪小，乃不可不杀」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206437_comment'></div>圣人岂乐于杀人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206437_comment'></div>道之弗从，令之不服，非有严刑重诛不能禁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206437_comment'></div>既历三纪，世变风移，而后康王以成周之众命毕公，则告之曰：「惟德惟义，时乃大训」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206437_comment'></div>先王之施德刑非有异也，因时而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206437_comment'></div>凡诸路奸赃之吏，当究见情实，稽成王告康叔之意，甚者肆诸市朝，投之岭海，庶乎人怨少伸，和气充塞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206437_comment'></div>自崇宁以来，为害之甚无如茶盐二法，臣尝论之详矣，今复转般而钞法不变，未见其利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1206437_comment'></div>祖宗设置发运司，盖得刘晏之遗意，朝廷捐数百万缗与为籴本，使总六路之计，通融移用，以给中都之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1206437_comment'></div>六路丰凶更有不常，一路丰稔则增籴以充漕计，饥凶去处则罢籴，使输折斛钱而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1206437_comment'></div>故上下俱宽，而中都不乏，最为良法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1206437_comment'></div>自胡师文以籴本为羡馀以献，而制置、发运司拱手无可为者，此直达之议所从起也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1206437_comment'></div>今复转般，而籴本乃取之诸路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1206437_comment'></div>昔在诸路，每岁一路所得盐课无虑数十万缗，自钞法行，盐课悉归榷货务，诸路一无所得，漕计日已不给；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1206437_comment'></div>今又歛取之，非出于漕臣之家，亦取诸民而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1206437_comment'></div>民力困敝，徒为纷纷，无补于事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1206437_comment'></div>臣近询之民间，谓朝廷虽有复转般之名，而直达之实犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1206437_comment'></div>诸路米至真、扬、楚、泗，未尝入敖，徒于文历内为收支文具而已，此尤非更法之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1206437_comment'></div>臣窃谓盐法与转般相因以为利，自行直达，而盐法随变，所谓相因为利者两失之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1206437_comment'></div>祖宗时，荆湖南北、江东西漕米至真、扬下卸，即载盐以归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1206437_comment'></div>交纳有剩数，则官以时直售之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1206437_comment'></div>舟人皆私市附载而行，阴取厚利，故以船为家，一有罅漏则随补葺之，为经远计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1206437_comment'></div>太宗尝谓侍臣曰：「倖门如鼠穴，不可塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1206437_comment'></div>篙工、柁师有少贩鬻，但无妨公，不必究问」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1206437_comment'></div>非洞见民隐，何以及此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1206437_comment'></div>自直达钞盐之法行，而回纲无所得，沿江州县亦无批请，故毁舟盗卖以充日食，而败舟亡卒处处有之，转为贼盗，不可胜计，其为害非细也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1206437_comment'></div>臣窃谓转般、盐法为发运司职事之根本，二者不可偏举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1206437_comment'></div>不捐数百万以为籴本，无回运以养舟人，则虽复转般，无异直达矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1206437_comment'></div>近见发运司漕米至汴中，损失者十几五六，盖人船皆处之非其道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1206437_comment'></div>昔刘晏于扬子置十场造船，每船给钱千缗，或言所用实不及半，虚费太多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1206437_comment'></div>晏曰：「不然，论大计不计小费，凡事必为永久之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1206437_comment'></div>今始置船场，执事者至多，当使之私用无穷，则官物坚好矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1206437_comment'></div>异时有患吾给钱多，减之过半，则不能运矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1206437_comment'></div>至咸通中，有司计费而给，无羡馀，船益脆薄易坏，漕运遂废矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1206437_comment'></div>闻真、扬起纲，凡治舟所须之物、调夫庸直皆不以例给，篙工、挽卒逃亡四出，沿汴以清河兵递行牵挽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1206437_comment'></div>清河兵素非纲官所辖，肆行盗窃，不可禁止；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1206437_comment'></div>加之上漏下湿，非沈溺则腐败而不可食，其损失多矣，皆惜小费不论大计之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1206437_comment'></div>臣欲乞朝廷严立法制，船场不得减尅工料，优给支费，庶得坚实，无疏漏之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1206437_comment'></div>复运盐之利，使篙工、柁师以船为家，则官物自无损折矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1206437_comment'></div>自汉唐以来，善治财赋者必以刘晏为称首，晏之言曰：「理财当以养民为先，户口众多，赋税自广」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1206437_comment'></div>此至论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1206437_comment'></div>然晏专用盐利以充军国之用，其为法止于出盐乡置官，收买盐户所煮之盐转鬻商人，任其所之，无馀事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1206437_comment'></div>其始，江淮盐课岁不过四十万缗，季年乃至六百馀万缗，不啻相什百也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1206437_comment'></div>岂当时可行，而今不可行耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1206437_comment'></div>臣尝任越州萧山县令，境内有钱清盐场，亭户多窜亡，至追捕拘系之，乃肯就役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1206437_comment'></div>尝究问其故，盖盐之入官一觔不过四五钱，积盐之久，必有耗折，官吏任责，则入盐加耗，理所不免，计其工力之费不偿其二三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1206437_comment'></div>又所至匮乏，钱不时得，此亭户所以多窜亡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1206437_comment'></div>饥寒所迫，非私鬻之无以自给，故盗贩十百为群，被甲荷戈名裹送者不下数十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1206437_comment'></div>官司畏其生事，护送出境，得无侵扰已倖矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1206437_comment'></div>夫深山穷谷有经年不食盐者，至附郭之民不可一日无也，钞盐之价高而私贩贱，故食私盐多而岁课所以不敷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1206437_comment'></div>非抑配编户，则盐钞无肯售者，此其弊根也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1206437_comment'></div>朝廷若于出盐乡增价售之，使其私用无窘，则亭户孰肯冒禁与盐贩者私市哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1206437_comment'></div>弊根既去，则岁课自敷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1206437_comment'></div>夫天之所生，地之所藏，昔常有馀而今不足，其弊必有自矣，朝廷盖未之究也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1206437_comment'></div>建隆之初，荆湖、江浙、河东、川、广、福建皆非朝廷有也，所有者淮南、京东西数郡而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1206437_comment'></div>承五季之乱，干戈日寻，然未尝以用不足为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1206437_comment'></div>今尺地莫非其有也，一民莫非其臣也，贡赋之入十倍于前时，而日以不足为忧，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1206437_comment'></div>处之未得其道故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1206437_comment'></div>昔皇祐尝为《会计录》以总核天下财赋之出入，百官饩廪之俸、军储边计，凡邦国之经用，皆有常数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1206437_comment'></div>元丰之《备对》，元祐之《会计》，皆放此为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1206437_comment'></div>臣伏望陛下明诏大臣为《靖康会计录》，取皇祐、元丰、元祐三书以为式，吏员之增减，兵旅之多寡，户口之登耗，赋入之盈虚，与凡经用之数，以三书参较之，有馀不足之本，可以究见矣，然后从而救治之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1206437_comment'></div>宰相岁终制国用，量入以为出，而忧国用之不足，非臣所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1206437_comment'></div>臣在阙门之外，庙堂之论，臣不得而与闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1206437_comment'></div>然得之于道路之言，以为执政大臣治文书，究细务，日不暇给，其如天下之大计何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1206437_comment'></div>臣窃谓今日之急务惟政事之未修，边陲战守之未备，皆阙然不讲，此臣之所深忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1206437_comment'></div>臣愿陛下敦谕大臣，阔略细务付之有司，专务修政事，振军律，练兵选将，为战守之备，庶乎纲举而万目自张矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1206437_comment'></div>臣不胜幸望之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_139_1206437_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　疑在开封。有文。作品：曹子华墓志铭。跋江民表与赵表之帖。祭刘器之。<div id='poem_1206869' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206869' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206869?labeling=true' target='_blank'>曹子华墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（靖康元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206869")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206869_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206869'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206869'>君讳璪，字子华，其先金陵人，避李氏之乱，徙居江阴，故今为江阴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206869_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，祖讳某，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206869_comment'></div>父讳某，故赠朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206869_comment'></div>母朱氏，赠恭人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206869_comment'></div>曹氏自高祖以来无显者，至君之世父确始以文行知名于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206869_comment'></div>熙宁更新学校，遴柬天下名儒，训迪多士，公时在选中，擢为国子直讲，学者翕然师尊之，曹氏遂有闻于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206869_comment'></div>君之昆弟幼从直讲公为学，得其绪言，䌷绎不懈，故皆屹然有立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206869_comment'></div>初，朝议公场屋不偶，退屏世累，从桑门之徒游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206869_comment'></div>比其亡也，清窭滋甚，君亦以累举不售，相其兄力治生，不计有无，资其弟以学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206869_comment'></div>其后家日益富，而弟琏卒以名进士登科，通金闺籍，君与有力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206869_comment'></div>其为子而孝于亲，为弟而恭其兄，为兄而友其弟，笃于爱钦，中外无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206869_comment'></div>性夷易，不为畦畛，与人言，洞见心膂，故人有过，虽面折之，而人亦莫之憾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206869_comment'></div>遇人不以贵贱贫富为厚薄，一于诚而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206869_comment'></div>晚益闲放，以诗酒自娱，杜门索居，终日兀如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206869_comment'></div>靖康元年四月癸亥，以疾终于家，享年五十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206869_comment'></div>娶赵氏，有贤行，配君无违德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206869_comment'></div>子男一人，曰峤，举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206869_comment'></div>女一人，适登仕郎慕容邦弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206869_comment'></div>有孙一人，未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206869_comment'></div>以是年某月壬辰葬于县之顺化乡黄山之原，其孤娶余之女孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206869_comment'></div>以其叔朝请公之状来请铭，乃为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1206869'>积善在躬，寿胡不多？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206869_comment'></div>天实为之，命也奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206869_comment'></div>瘗铭新阡，其永不磨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1206869_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋江民表与赵表之帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206678")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206678'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206678'>民表将之官，以书抵予，告行期，未及修报而凶讣至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206678_comment'></div>人生如朝露，岂不信然欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206678_comment'></div>今见其手泽，惘然不觉为之流涕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206678_comment'></div>民表不妄许可，表之虽未及识，观民表所与如此，则其人亦可知矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206678_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206890' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206890' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206890?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭刘器之文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206890")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206890_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206890'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206890'>呜呼我公，惟德是仔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206890_comment'></div>秉义直行，与天为徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206890_comment'></div>元祐之初，圣贤相逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206890_comment'></div>位冠七人，为时宗工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206890_comment'></div>道大不容，迁于南服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206890_comment'></div>劫火洞然，不烬惟玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206890_comment'></div>时方清明，仁贤汇征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206890_comment'></div>昊天弗吊，丧我正臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206890_comment'></div>衔觞一恸，匪以其私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206890_comment'></div>侑食以文，其知我悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206890_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1206890_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
许昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='158d2f1b37aa47ee9e50be3c0593b425_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("158d2f1b37aa47ee9e50be3c0593b425");'><span id='158d2f1b37aa47ee9e50be3c0593b425_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年</a>，29岁</div><div id='158d2f1b37aa47ee9e50be3c0593b425' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>与游酢自京师绕道颍昌，以师礼见明道先生（程颢）。有文。<div id='poem_1206511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206511' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206511?labeling=true' target='_blank'>见明道先生书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1081年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206511")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206511_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206511'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206511'>某鄙朴无知，不量力之不足也，窃慕古人之学，诵其书，论其世，想见其为人而师之有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206511_comment'></div>然以浅闻卑见，未能灼知古人大体，故刻意虽坚，终未有得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206511_comment'></div>尝观古之为士者，所至远近虽不同，其秉节励行，皆有以自立于世，岂其材悉能过人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206511_comment'></div>特以先王教学之道明，而士于此时无私习之蔽故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206511_comment'></div>周道衰，庠序之法废，故家遗俗随以熄灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206511_comment'></div>幸而有孔子出焉，振先王已坠之教，驾说于当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206511_comment'></div>而从之游者若参之鲁，师之辟，由之谚，师之过，商之不及，其材固非有大过人也，然其闻所未闻，见所未见，而馀言遗行有后世宿儒皓首而不能穷者，则士之得所依归，岂曰小补之哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206511_comment'></div>自秦汉迄于魏、晋、隋、唐之间，明知之士见于其时，不无人矣，间有一节一义可称于世者，槩以圣人中道，非过则不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206511_comment'></div>岂其材皆不逮古耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206511_comment'></div>徒以学无师承，不知所以裁之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206511_comment'></div>以今较古，则学之难易又可知已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206511_comment'></div>且三代而上，道德明而异端熄，邪说诐行不作于下，士之朝夕蹈袭者，无非礼乐之间，则其学岂不易致耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206511_comment'></div>末世以来，诸子百家，异端并起，是非纷错，无所考正，士之始学者如适九达之衢，从横曲折，眩然莫知所之，非有导其前，则终身未见其至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206511_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206511_comment'></div>师道废久矣，后世之士不能望见古人之万一者，岂不以此欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206511_comment'></div>某尝悲夫世之人自蔽曲学，不求有道者正之，而又自悲其欲求有道者而未之得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206511_comment'></div>调官至京师，于朋游间获闻先生之绪言，鄙俗之心固以潜择，于是慨然兴起曰：古之人其相去甚远矣，尚或诵其诗，读其书，论其世，想见其为人而师之，又况亲逢其人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206511_comment'></div>其往不可复矣，此区区所以有今日之请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206511_comment'></div>先生其将哀其愚，悯其志，而进之使供洒扫于门下，则千万幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1206511_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在颍昌。有诗。作品：颍昌西湖泛舟（其一）颍昌西湖泛舟（其二）别游定夫。送吴子正序。<div id='poem_1206640' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206640' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206640?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送吴子正序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1081年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206640")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206640_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206640'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206640'>六经，先圣所以明天道，正人伦，致治之成法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206640_comment'></div>其文自尧舜历夏周之季，兴衰治乱成败之迹，救敝通变因时损益之理，皆焕然可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206640_comment'></div>网罗天地之大文理，象器幽明之故，死生终始之变，莫不详谕曲譬，较然如数一二，宜乎后世高明超卓之士，一抚卷而尽得之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206640_comment'></div>予窃怪唐虞之世，六籍未具，士于斯时非有诵记操笔缀文，然后为学也，而其蕴道怀德，优入圣贤之域者何多耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206640_comment'></div>其达而位乎上，则昌言嘉谟足以亮天工而成大业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206640_comment'></div>虽困穷在下，而潜德隐行犹足以经世励俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206640_comment'></div>其芳猷美绩又何其章章也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206640_comment'></div>自秦焚诗书、坑术士，六艺残缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206640_comment'></div>汉儒收拾补缀，至建元之间，文辞粲如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206640_comment'></div>若贾谊、董仲舒、司马迁、相如、扬雄之徒继武而出，雄文大笔，驰骋古今，沛然如决江汉，浩无津涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206640_comment'></div>后虽有作者，未有能涉其波流也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206640_comment'></div>然贾谊明申韩，仲舒陈灾异，马迁之多爱，相如之浮侈，皆未足与议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206640_comment'></div>惟扬雄为庶几于道，然尚恨其有未尽者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206640_comment'></div>积至于唐，文籍之备，盖十百前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206640_comment'></div>元和之间，韩柳辈出，咸以古文名天下，然其论著不诡于圣人盖寡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206640_comment'></div>自汉迄唐千馀岁，而士之名能文者无过是数人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206640_comment'></div>及考其所至，卒未有能倡明道学，窥圣人阃奥如古人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206640_comment'></div>然则古之时六籍未具，不害其善学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206640_comment'></div>后世文籍虽多，亡益于得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206640_comment'></div>孔子曰：「予非多学而识之，予一以贯之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206640_comment'></div>岂不信矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206640_comment'></div>武阳吴子正，余之畏友也，博闻强识，于诸子百氏之书无所不究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206640_comment'></div>循是而进，益求古人所谓卓约者而守之，庶乎其至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206640_comment'></div>区区于汉唐之士以多文自富，务为辞章以惊眩末俗，非善学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206640_comment'></div>夫赠言为别，以相规切，盖古朋友之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206640_comment'></div>故于子正之行，辄书以为赠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1206640_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
建瓯
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='55a6b2a9a6084481b4970b532f0fa861_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("55a6b2a9a6084481b4970b532f0fa861");'><span id='55a6b2a9a6084481b4970b532f0fa861_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>，31岁</div><div id='55a6b2a9a6084481b4970b532f0fa861' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年1月</a>　赴徐州司法任，春初至建安，托林志宁附书与游酢。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c03f7a42d9e948d9a9c06f21d042fc36_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c03f7a42d9e948d9a9c06f21d042fc36");'><span id='c03f7a42d9e948d9a9c06f21d042fc36_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，49岁</div><div id='c03f7a42d9e948d9a9c06f21d042fc36' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年11月</a>　建瓯。自建阳县丞任罢归，过瓯宁乾明寺，作志。作品：乾明寺修造记。<div id='poem_1206837' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206837' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206837?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乾明寺修造记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206837")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206837_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206837'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206837'>建中靖国元年岁在辛巳，余以漕檄二令于东阳，有大比丘惠康以书抵余曰：「乾明之为禅寺，更四代而康始继之，栖佛之庐未完者十二，雨濡风剥，二阁蔽其前，尤如悬疣之在肤，而翳之在目也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206837_comment'></div>欲完而迁之久矣，计其瑰材坚甓之用费累钜万，殆非毫聚铢积所能为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206837_comment'></div>郡人吴某乃捐金千缗助成吾志，窃谓用力之勤，而施财之厚，皆不可以无述也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206837_comment'></div>公盍为我记之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206837_comment'></div>是年冬，余在东阳罢归，过其门，而环庑翼然，丹楹曲槛，雕栾镂磶，渥彩焜耀，如入化人之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206837_comment'></div>峙二阁于东西序，虚明深靓，豁如疣抉而翳去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206837_comment'></div>乃喟然叹曰：吾州当水陆之冲，舟舆之会，四方游士道闽中而过者，盖舻相衔而辐相轹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206837_comment'></div>而又山水之胜，清明伟丽，为东南之最，宜有台池园囿魁殊诡异，以供宾客燕嬉之好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206837_comment'></div>然而地瘠而贫，故其民勤约而敦本，啬用而寡求，凡居室服器，趋完而已，皆不足为美观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206837_comment'></div>比年以来，岁屡不登，编户齐民方且以艰食为虞，而康师乃能于荐饥之时导勤约之俗，厚施以成其事，其中必有足以感于人者，是可叹也已，乃为之书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1206837_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
衢州
