-----title
徐州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2ea24a62d2ba46daa5ccd8c4baa75d01_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2ea24a62d2ba46daa5ccd8c4baa75d01");'><span id='2ea24a62d2ba46daa5ccd8c4baa75d01_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1085')">1083-1085年</a>，31-33岁</div><div id='2ea24a62d2ba46daa5ccd8c4baa75d01' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年4月2日</a>　过吕梁百步，到徐州官舍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　在徐州任。有文。作品：寄明道先生书 其二。<div id='poem_1206513' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206513' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206513?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄明道先生书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206513")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206513_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206513'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206513'>某尝欲治《春秋》，读之数卷，浅识未能窥见其门户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206513_comment'></div>远去师席，疑无质问，中欲辍之，又惜其初心之勤，惓惓不能自已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206513_comment'></div>诵习之馀，每妄有所亿，然未知圣人之旨果可以如此求否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206513_comment'></div>谨录之以质诸左右，傥因暇时一赐观览，正其非谬，以开导之，则幸甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206513_comment'></div>隐元年：「郑伯克段于鄢」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206513_comment'></div>段以不义得众，公弗能制，终欲制之，畏人之多言，则克段者郑伯而已，非国人所欲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206513_comment'></div>故不称国讨而书曰「郑伯」，盖交讥之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206513_comment'></div>夫仁人之亲爱其弟，非徒富贵之而已，亦必为之节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206513_comment'></div>富贵而不为之节，使之骄慢陵僭，以速祸败，则其亲爱之也，适所以害之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206513_comment'></div>故《诗》称郑伯不胜其母，以害其弟，而《春秋》书曰「郑伯克段」，正谓是欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206513_comment'></div>夫克者，胜敌之辞，以胜敌之辞加之，则段之强可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206513_comment'></div>段之强，由辨之不早辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206513_comment'></div>「日有食之」，《谷梁》曰：「吐者外壤，食者内壤，阙然不见其壤，有食之者，言有物食之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206513_comment'></div>夫日月之变有常数焉，此巧历所能穷也，而《春秋》记以为异者，盖先王克谨天戒，因以正厥事，则日之有变岂徒然哉，必有以也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206513_comment'></div>故书曰「日有食之」，而其辞若有食之者，盖所以归咎于人事，而不以常数为不足畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206513_comment'></div>桓元年三月，「公会郑伯于垂，郑伯以壁假许田」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206513_comment'></div>二年三月，「公会齐侯、陈侯、郑伯于稷，以成宋乱」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206513_comment'></div>夏四月，「取郜大鼎于宋」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206513_comment'></div>夫宋督杀其君而公成其乱，取郜大鼎以归，公弑隐公而郑伯会公于垂，以壁假许田，则鲁之乱，郑伯成之也，不书，为内讳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206513_comment'></div>夫郑伯之假田与公之取鼎，其求赂一也，而书之异辞，内外之分然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206513_comment'></div>三年夏，「齐侯、卫侯胥命于蒲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206513_comment'></div>胥命盖若葵丘之会，束牲载书而不歃血，有五命之类是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206513_comment'></div>齐、卫敌国，莫为命主，故曰胥命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206513_comment'></div>至治之时，诸侯述职以听天子之命而已，何胥命之有哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206513_comment'></div>然葵丘之会不书命，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206513_comment'></div>盖五霸桓公为盛，葵丘之会实为盟主，故不书命，盖不与其擅命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206513_comment'></div>其他若及宋之类，义例甚众，并前书所问，皆未能晓，略赐疏示，乃至愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206513_comment'></div>浼渎左右，徒用愧畏，惟先生诲人不倦，未拒绝之，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1206513_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年5月</a>　在徐州任。有书寄程二十三。作品：寄程二十三书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（程二十二，指明道先生程颢子汝阳簿。）</span><div id='poem_1206522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206522?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄程二十三书<span class='inlineComment2'>（明道先生子，汝阳簿。）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206522")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206522_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206522'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206522'>自去年夏，曾奉问并颍川书一角，及得吾友递中附到八月书，乃知未达，不审此书竟能达否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206522_comment'></div>某正月尽离乡，四月初方到官所，敝司事稍简，不至废学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206522_comment'></div>然彭城士类凋落，友朋绝少，索居终日，无过门者，不闻道义之益，恐遂默默，浸为庸人，深可忧畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206522_comment'></div>追思在颍之乐，进趋文席，退讲所闻，邈不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206522_comment'></div>汝阳迩日所游，从者何人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206522_comment'></div>所读者何书？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206522_comment'></div>因书示及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206522_comment'></div>未涯良会，惟希力学慎爱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206522_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206523' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206523' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206523?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年5月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206523_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206523'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206523'>为别倏两年，穷居寡便邮置，安否之问，彼此旷绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206523_comment'></div>倾念之至，每形梦寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206523_comment'></div>迩日不审起居何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206523_comment'></div>某到官逾月矣，人事稍息，过此渐可追寻旧学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206523_comment'></div>汝阳亦不至多事，想不废读书，因风愿以所得来告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206523_comment'></div>尚远高论，暑毒，切冀自重。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1206523_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　在徐州任。有书寄游酢。作品：与游定夫书 其一。与游定夫书 其二。<div id='poem_1206549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206549?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与游定夫书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206549")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206549'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206549'>春初至建安，曾托志宁附书，计尘听览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206549_comment'></div>为别滋久，瞻系之至，旦夜不能忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206549_comment'></div>夏热，不审起居何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206549_comment'></div>某自衢买舟渡江，沿淮入清河，过吕梁百步，凡五十有二日始达彭城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206549_comment'></div>东南风波之险，所历几尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206549_comment'></div>幸而举家幼累各安，差足为慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206549_comment'></div>彭城古郡僻寂，达官显人不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206549_comment'></div>其境颇无将迎之劳，而民事又简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206549_comment'></div>虽敝司有库务，兼局之多，然出纳有时，亦不至劳力，尤称养拙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206549_comment'></div>在鄙心为可悔恨者，特去亲远耳，其他无足念者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206549_comment'></div>所怀千万，临纸不能悉布，惟冀为道自重。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1206549_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206550' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206550?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206550_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206550'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206550'>某四月二日到官舍，初四日交承职事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206550_comment'></div>彭城风物质陋，与吾乡大异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206550_comment'></div>幸有鱼稻鹑雉之类，足以充食，故南人处之差为便耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206550_comment'></div>太守王大夫宽厚，颇有恺悌之风，属吏之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206550_comment'></div>某离家将半年，思亲之怀日甚一日，其情意若不可堪，不知愈久何以处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206550_comment'></div>定夫官期犹一年，思复时常相聚，讲学之乐何可量，但钦羡耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206550_comment'></div>志宁曾来相会否，企仰高论，无日忘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206550_comment'></div>惟数以书见教，庶足少慰鄙心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206550_comment'></div>暑毒，千万珍卫。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1206550_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年8月</a>　在徐州任。八月，校所著《庄子解》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　在徐州任。有与明道先生论《春秋》书。作品：与明道先生 其二。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　在徐州任。有书寄林志宁。作品：与林志宁书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　在徐州任。哀郭思道辞。<div id='poem_1206884' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206884' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206884?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郭思道哀辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206884")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206884_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206884'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206884'>吾友思道，讳某，姓郭氏，福唐人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206884_comment'></div>先世皆隐德不仕，其族系盖莫得而详焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206884_comment'></div>思道自少时尤喜黄老之术，以求卫生之经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206884_comment'></div>不利货财，不近声色，淡然自得，视天下之物若无足以赘其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206884_comment'></div>晚颇好浮图氏之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206884_comment'></div>其与人交，久而愈亲，与朋友言，必以忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206884_comment'></div>其辞气抗直，不能与物逶迤，以苟悦世俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206884_comment'></div>熙宁乙卯，同余游京师，余缀名秋官，思道失志，遂同入太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206884_comment'></div>今知制诰黄公见而悦之，用以为直学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206884_comment'></div>未几职小学教谕，其纯德懿行虽为当路者之所知，其自处慊然，亦未尝因之驰骋，以求见于世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206884_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206884_comment'></div>周道衰，为士者不孚于名实，而国论不出乡闾州党之间，盗名窃利之人，肆行机变以欺世罔上，贪得忘义，屈道徇物，以至昏冥颠踣而不悟，虽妾妇乞人之所悲羞而不受者，犹将泰然矜耀以自得，其辞受取舍尚何足诛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206884_comment'></div>君于是时也，超然远览，不以贫贱富贵撄拂其志，斯亦难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206884_comment'></div>其志行虽未能尽概于古人，其贤于众人也亦远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206884_comment'></div>余从之游且十年，得其所以治身养性之实非一二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206884_comment'></div>以余之所言，推余所不言，盖可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206884_comment'></div>享年三十有八，以疾终于京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206884_comment'></div>余闻之，为之悲恸不能自已，故为辞以泄其哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206884_comment'></div>辞曰：嗟乎思道，木讷而仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206884_comment'></div>内行纯懿，幽无责于鬼，明无非于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206884_comment'></div>宜得其禄，何颠沛于道路，而终死于贱贫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206884_comment'></div>宜享其寿，何弃世之遽，而天年不及于中身！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206884_comment'></div>死谁葬兮，暴骸骨于汴之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206884_comment'></div>魂无依兮，托厉鬼以为邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206884_comment'></div>自古圣贤兮，自有显荣富贵，腾声飞誉，振耀于无垠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206884_comment'></div>亦有湮沦汩没，终屈而不伸，死同腐骨兮，俱磨灭乎埃尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206884_comment'></div>寿夭穷通，子能自达，吾亦不足以伤神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206884_comment'></div>重以故人之情，追思感叹，不觉涕泪之沾巾。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1206884_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年3月18日</a>　在徐州司法任。三月十八日，次子迥生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年6月30日</a>　在徐州司法任。六月晦，闻明道先生之讣，设位恸哭于寝门，有哀辞。作品：哀明道先生。<div id='poem_1206882' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206882' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206882?labeling=true' target='_blank'>明道先生哀辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年6月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206882")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206882_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206882'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206882'>元丰八年夏六月既望，河南承议先生以疾终于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206882_comment'></div>是月晦，邸报至彭城，其门人杨某闻知，为位，恸哭于寝门，而以书讣诸尝同学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206882_comment'></div>呜呼，道之无传也久矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206882_comment'></div>孟子没千有馀岁，更汉历唐，士之名世扬雄氏而止耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206882_comment'></div>雄之自择所处，于义命犹有未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206882_comment'></div>自雄而下，其智足以窥圣学门墙者，盖不可一二数也，况足与语道而传之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206882_comment'></div>宋兴百年，士稍知师古，诸子百氏之籍与夫佛老荒唐谬悠之书，下迨战国纵横之论，幽人逸士浮誇诡异可喜之文章，皆杂出而并传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206882_comment'></div>世之任道者日夜惫精劳思，深探博取，可为勤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206882_comment'></div>然其支离蔓衍，不知慎择而约守之，故其用志益劳，而去道弥远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206882_comment'></div>使天下学者靡然趋之，如适诸夏而弃通衢大道，犯荆棘之墟，行苍崖之巅，眩然迷殆，而卒莫知自反者，其于世教何补哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206882_comment'></div>先生于是时乃独守遗经，合内外之道，默识而性成之，其学之渊源盖智者不能窥，而善言者所不能称说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206882_comment'></div>自周衰以来，天下之学其失如彼，则后之得圣人之道而传之者，于吾先生可不独任其责哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206882_comment'></div>呜呼，道之传亦难矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206882_comment'></div>夫由尧、舜而来，至于汤、文、孔子，率五百有馀岁而后得一人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206882_comment'></div>孔子没，其徒环天下，然独积百年而后孟子出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206882_comment'></div>由孟子而来，迄汉、唐千有馀岁，卒未有一人传之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206882_comment'></div>若孔、孟又皆穷老于衰世，其道方不得一施于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206882_comment'></div>夫圣贤之不世出，而时之难值也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206882_comment'></div>今幸而有其人，又且遭时清明，朝廷方登崇俊良，而先生未及用而死，则予之恸哭，岂特以师弟子之私恩而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206882_comment'></div>故为辞以泄其哀而自慰云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206882_comment'></div>余悲古人之不见兮，逢世德之险微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206882_comment'></div>析道真之纯美兮，肆全体而分刲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206882_comment'></div>驾异端而并逐兮，骈支毂乎多岐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206882_comment'></div>亘千岁其泯泯兮，去圣远而。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206882_comment'></div>卓彼先觉兮，惟德是仔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206882_comment'></div>展斯文之在兹兮，万世之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206882_comment'></div>锄榛棘之荒秽兮，辟正路之孔夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206882_comment'></div>伏圣贤之轨躅兮，背世辙而疾驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206882_comment'></div>带钩距而负绳兮，纷万变而莫窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206882_comment'></div>弛衔勒而弗厉兮，尚回旋其中规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206882_comment'></div>嗟命之县于天兮，匪予敢知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206882_comment'></div>畜溟渤而载华岳兮，曾有尘之弗施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206882_comment'></div>叹道之难行兮，孔孟穷老以栖栖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206882_comment'></div>伊时势则然兮，此云胡其若兹？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206882_comment'></div>通辟阖于一息兮，尸者其谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206882_comment'></div>斡天枢而自尔兮，欲执咎其焉归？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206882_comment'></div>齐死生于昼夜兮，天理之常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206882_comment'></div>匪往匪来兮，虽寿夭兮何伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206882_comment'></div>想德音其未远兮，俨若在傍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206882_comment'></div>固诚之不可掩兮，何有何亡？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206882_comment'></div>日月逝兮形魂藏，呜呼已矣兮斯亦难忘！</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1206882_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
赣州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cfe2aa767fb64df7a64c06d0ee14a3be_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cfe2aa767fb64df7a64c06d0ee14a3be");'><span id='cfe2aa767fb64df7a64c06d0ee14a3be_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1090')">1088-1090年</a>，36-38岁</div><div id='cfe2aa767fb64df7a64c06d0ee14a3be' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　赴调虔州司法，有惠政。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　在虔州。有诗。作品：送虔守楚大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1089')">1088-1089年</a>　在虔州。有文。作品：谢太守启。谢楚大夫启。代人谢解启。谢张朝散启。谢马通直启。祭楚守县君。上毛宪书。寄毛宪书。贺正旦表。张氏墓志铭。哀邹尧叟。贺坤成节表。贡物表。贺收河湟表。<div id='poem_1206627' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206627' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206627?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢太守启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206627")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206627_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206627'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206627'>仕禄养亲，素非求进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206627_comment'></div>分曹莅职，自愧无堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206627_comment'></div>方虞谴责之难逃，岂意褒称之偶及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206627_comment'></div>宠荣过分，循省若惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206627_comment'></div>窃以郡县王室之屏藩，而守令士民之师帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206627_comment'></div>尊卑虽异，任责则同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206627_comment'></div>一非其人，众受其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206627_comment'></div>顾兹百里之重寄，实惟万室之具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206627_comment'></div>军国调度之须，所取非一；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206627_comment'></div>兵民什一之会，其职匪轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206627_comment'></div>严之以法，则众离而不亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206627_comment'></div>抚之以宽，则事弛而不集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206627_comment'></div>苟非岂弟之君子，曷庇困穷之小民？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206627_comment'></div>古谓其难，今尤慎择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206627_comment'></div>矧夫极治之盛际，固多间出之英材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206627_comment'></div>刃发新硎，莫匪庖丁之手；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206627_comment'></div>人胥易使，率皆言偃之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206627_comment'></div>宜得异能，称此公举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206627_comment'></div>如某者驽骀下乘，樗栎散材，自惟衔辔之难驱，敢希匠石之或顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206627_comment'></div>徒守过庭之训，耻为趋世之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206627_comment'></div>一瓢屡空，方慕颜渊之好学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206627_comment'></div>三釜而乐，又怀曾子之及亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206627_comment'></div>虽未信辞仕，固贤者之宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206627_comment'></div>而公养为贫，亦圣人不免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206627_comment'></div>猥从科举，误玷缙绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206627_comment'></div>庶乎饩廪之微，足为晨夕之奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206627_comment'></div>伶仃一病，流落八年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206627_comment'></div>气形并衰，神志俱耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206627_comment'></div>身同野鹿，甘自屏于樵渔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206627_comment'></div>衣若悬鹑，复何意于轩冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206627_comment'></div>方将投蛙足于缺甃，寄鹪巢乎一枝，俯仰终身，优游卒岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206627_comment'></div>倘徉尘垢之外，游泳诗书之渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206627_comment'></div>与世相忘，脱桁杨之接摺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206627_comment'></div>放形自适，近鱼鸟之沉浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206627_comment'></div>奈何糟糠无以畜妻孥，甘旨不足事父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206627_comment'></div>年丰病乏，冬暖嗟寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206627_comment'></div>在人情难以恬安，于人子尤当隐恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206627_comment'></div>遂参选调，补吏掾曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206627_comment'></div>来游会府之英躔，辄去衡门之陋处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206627_comment'></div>惟思窃食，何路进身？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206627_comment'></div>欲为辙鲋之呼，逆知无济；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206627_comment'></div>忍效冶金之跃，自取不祥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206627_comment'></div>故虽幸馀光之可依，莫敢饰鄙辞而上黩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206627_comment'></div>岂图异宠，遽及非材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206627_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官扩大度以兼容，推至仁而博施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206627_comment'></div>智虽周物，能不病人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206627_comment'></div>未尝片善之或遗，致此甚愚而不弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206627_comment'></div>受恩有地，图报无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206627_comment'></div>敢不允蹈圣言，雅不忘于旧学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206627_comment'></div>益勤职守，庶无负于己知。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1206627_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206628' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206628' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206628?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢楚大夫启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206628")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206628_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206628'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206628'>右，某启：伏蒙知府大人先生保举某堪充职官任使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206628_comment'></div>仕禄养亲，素非求进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206628_comment'></div>分曹莅职，自愧无堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206628_comment'></div>方虞谴责之难逃，岂意荐论之偶及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206628_comment'></div>被恩优渥，抚己兢惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206628_comment'></div>窃闻以身徇道者，君子之格言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206628_comment'></div>事君以人者，上臣之明义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206628_comment'></div>怀瑾握瑜，欲有待也，虽鼓刀自溷，犹不为辱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206628_comment'></div>尊德乐义，欲有求也，虽忘势自竭，乃其当然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206628_comment'></div>永惟上下之相资，莫知贵贱之有间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206628_comment'></div>世道沦丧，风猷浸隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206628_comment'></div>居下者以难仕为迂谋，在上者以旁招为末事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206628_comment'></div>公论一废，私谒肆行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206628_comment'></div>待价而沽，顾连城而莫售；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206628_comment'></div>无因而至，虽照乘而难前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206628_comment'></div>苟非先容，孰匪弃物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206628_comment'></div>如某者赋材疏拙，禀性顽愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206628_comment'></div>徒闻师友之绪言，妄窥圣贤之遗学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206628_comment'></div>獐头鼠目之贱，何意求官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206628_comment'></div>牛溲马勃之污，宁堪待用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206628_comment'></div>已绝凌霄之望，方图祭灶之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206628_comment'></div>欲为辙鲋之呼，逆知无济；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206628_comment'></div>忍效冶金之跃，自取不祥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206628_comment'></div>岂谓未遑竿牍之修，遽玷齿牙之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206628_comment'></div>终怀直道，窃希东国之臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206628_comment'></div>已附青云，不作西陵之饿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206628_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官至公处己，内恕及人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206628_comment'></div>以教育英材为乐，而务在兼容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206628_comment'></div>以推毂士类为任，而常思博取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206628_comment'></div>致兹庸妄，亦与甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206628_comment'></div>敢不勉自激昂，仰怀知遇，无忘旧学，益励前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206628_comment'></div>驽乘何能，幸尝骖于骥尾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206628_comment'></div>天池可到，终有待于鹏风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206628_comment'></div>过此以还，未知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1206628_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206633' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206633' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206633?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代人谢解启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206633")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206633'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206633'>卞璧前陈，顾何求于燕石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206633_comment'></div>秦医并畜，俄有取于猪苓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206633_comment'></div>省分知荣，抚躬增愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206633_comment'></div>窃以难进者君子之义，易失者圣人之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206633_comment'></div>环辙载贽，将有行也，虽急仕犹不以为污；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206633_comment'></div>操筑鼓刀，将有待也，虽自溷或不以为辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206633_comment'></div>永惟出处之大致，固宜义命之两全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206633_comment'></div>贵乎中行，孰可已甚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206633_comment'></div>况值离明之两作，仍丁泰吉之大来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206633_comment'></div>设科目以振拔滞淹，举经行以网罗遗逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206633_comment'></div>朝以进贤为急务，士知不谷为可羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206633_comment'></div>故韬光晦迹者弃岩穴之居，而怀瑾握瑜者有廊庙之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206633_comment'></div>顾兹千载之兴运，是为希世之罕逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206633_comment'></div>凡有见闻，孰不奋励？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206633_comment'></div>如某者学惟为己，才不逮人，徒袭父兄之馀风，不坠箕裘之素业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206633_comment'></div>并驱夷路，自惭跛鳖之难前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206633_comment'></div>笃信所行，终类愚公而见笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206633_comment'></div>一窃乡荐，旋黜春闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206633_comment'></div>分甘自屏于樵渔，意复何祈于轩冕？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206633_comment'></div>再攘之臂，忘搏虎之可虞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206633_comment'></div>屡北之兵，徒闻风而犹骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206633_comment'></div>孰谓已归之气，俄伸久屈之中，退省厥由，所来有自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206633_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官至公处己，内恕及人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206633_comment'></div>以教育英材为乐，而务在兼容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206633_comment'></div>以推毂士类为任，而常思博取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206633_comment'></div>致兹庸妄，亦与甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206633_comment'></div>敢不勉自激昂，仰怀知遇，益勤素学，愈砺前锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206633_comment'></div>驽乘何能，幸尝骖于骥尾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206633_comment'></div>天池可到，终有待于鹏风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206633_comment'></div>过此以还，未知所措。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1206633'></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1206633_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206629' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206629' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206629?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢张朝散启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206629")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206629_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206629'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206629'>显膺宸命，荣领郡符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206629_comment'></div>方怀庆问之未遑，岂意缄封之先辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206629_comment'></div>恭惟某官，赋材忠实，禀器纯深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206629_comment'></div>更贰正于名藩，蔼休声于舆论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206629_comment'></div>果兹遴柬，付以承宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206629_comment'></div>云翼怒飞，匪泠风之能负：霜蹄一跃，骋千里以诚宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206629_comment'></div>敢希得士之名，姑逭蔽贤之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206629_comment'></div>过蒙归德，益用愧怀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206629_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206630?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢马通直启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206630")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206630'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206630'>显奉纶言，荣升朝籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206630_comment'></div>恭惟某官懿文外炳，硕德中纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206630_comment'></div>芝草之灵，人皆知其美瑞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206630_comment'></div>圭璋之质，初无事于先容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206630_comment'></div>未遑竿牍之修，遽辱缄题之及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206630_comment'></div>褒荣过分，悚愧无涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206630_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206630_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206885' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206885' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206885?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭楚守县君文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206885")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206885_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206885'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206885'>于惟夫人，伊洛右族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206885_comment'></div>归嫔雎汭，懿柔静淑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206885_comment'></div>功施于内，隐行弗彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206885_comment'></div>中外式孚，允也其臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206885_comment'></div>雍雍和鸣，袒衣编饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206885_comment'></div>大邑之封，视夫之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206885_comment'></div>谓宜百年，黄发偕老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206885_comment'></div>天胡不相，中道而夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206885_comment'></div>归旐翩翩，江流㳽㳽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206885_comment'></div>魂兮何之，与水俱逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206885_comment'></div>酒殽既馨，用祖其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206885_comment'></div>荐以斯文，以寓哀诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206885_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206885_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206543' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206543' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206543?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上毛宪书<span class='inlineComment2'>（名渐字正仲）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206543")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206543_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206543'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206543'>某愚无似，家世业儒，而名不隶于农工商贾之籍，惟是专笃于文学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206543_comment'></div>以天资顽鄙，不能雕绘组织，著为文辞，以取名当世，独好观古人大节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206543_comment'></div>自三代以来风声气俗、兴衰治乱，与士之遭时遇变、出处语默，窃尝窥较其一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206543_comment'></div>而谓当先王之盛，礼义之泽渐磨浸灌，天下亹亹向风承德，敦厚而成俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206543_comment'></div>于斯时也，士游乎胶庠术序之间，揽六艺之英华，而充饫乎道德之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206543_comment'></div>凡耳目之所习闻者，皆足以迪己而励行，优游自得，不见异物而迁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206543_comment'></div>此三代之士所以彬彬多全德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206543_comment'></div>夷陵至于战国，暴君污吏各逞其私欲，磨牙摇毒相吞噬者，天下相环也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206543_comment'></div>机会之变，间不容发，故从人合之以效其谋，衡人离之以攻其后，掉三寸之舌，斗天下之诸侯，歛为己功，由是靡靡日入于乱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206543_comment'></div>汉兴，袭秦遗俗，而高皇帝起于布衣户伍之中，一呼而有天下，慢而侮人，尤不喜儒士，故一时贪利顽钝无耻者多归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206543_comment'></div>虽秉国钧衡为一代宗臣者，犹且囚拘缧绁而不知去，况其馀人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206543_comment'></div>光武中兴，尤旌节义之士，而依违附逆之徒多见戮辱，故宏儒远志、累行高举、激扬风流者方轨而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206543_comment'></div>及其衰也，怀济时之志，则以触权而撄祸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206543_comment'></div>谢事丘壑，则以党锢而陷刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206543_comment'></div>虽舆败辐脱，犹不忍改辙，一犯清议，则蹈鈇伏锧而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206543_comment'></div>终汉之社稷，仅如垂发而不绝者，亦众君子之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206543_comment'></div>东晋之兴，士惩前轨，皆遗世绝俗，视天下治乱恝然如秦人视越人之肥瘠也，而晋从而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206543_comment'></div>此气俗之不同，然亦兴衰治乱之所系也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206543_comment'></div>故战国之士务奇谋而不徇正道，西汉之士喜功名而不务奇节，东汉之士贵节义而不通时变，东晋之士乐恬旷而不孚实用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206543_comment'></div>是皆为世变所移，而昧乎中行者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206543_comment'></div>惟古之圣贤则不然，不以世治而坚其操，世乱而败其度，虽变故日更，而吾之所守自若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206543_comment'></div>某窃观仁宗皇帝承祖宗遗烈，纲纪法度一循旧典，四十二年之间，天下熙然咏仁而蹈德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206543_comment'></div>上自朝廷，下至乎郡县，皆习为宽大；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206543_comment'></div>而其卒也，纵弛而不振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206543_comment'></div>迨夫神宗皇帝，励精为治，综核名实，而奉承之吏多失其旨，类皆以苛察为明，裒歛为功，其极也惨覈少恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206543_comment'></div>主上即位，尽蠲前弊，而昔之惨覈者往往变其旧习，勉为宽厚以自媚于上者，不可胜计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206543_comment'></div>恭惟阁下以清名重德，简在二圣，世方惨覈，不矫激以赴功，俗尚宽厚，不矜饰以干誉，挺然中立，不为世变所移，是真常德君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206543_comment'></div>非夫蕴道藏器复古圣贤之轨躅者，其何能尔？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206543_comment'></div>某闽海之鄙人，窃承下风之日久矣，今兹使旆按临，某也实为部吏，幸得抠衣歛板，朝夕进趋于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206543_comment'></div>自惟碌碌无可称者，而遽辱一言之知，在愚贱疏逖之分，其何以当此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206543_comment'></div>非中行之士不狃于势利者，殆无以及此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206543_comment'></div>故辄详列古人之大节与夫平昔景慕之意，以为请见之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206543_comment'></div>进之退之，俯伏俟命，不胜战悚之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1206543_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206544' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206544' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206544?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄毛宪书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206544")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206544_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206544'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206544'>始闻湖北溪洞寇边，将臣失于制御，或恐使旆当有湖北之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206544_comment'></div>一方小警固不足烦经略，然公之威德素为边民信畏，旌驭一行，使朝廷无南顾之忧，亦非小补也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206544_comment'></div>某尝谓边事之兴多出于饕功幸利之人，媟武玩寇，不以朝廷大计为念，视生灵荼毒若非己事，恬不以为戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206544_comment'></div>夫蛮獠猖獗，自古然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206544_comment'></div>缓之则豺噬狶勇，干纪而不受命，急之则鸟惊鱼散，依险以自匿，盖其常态也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206544_comment'></div>不务抚驯之，使恩威两行，乃欲幸其有事，草薙而兽狝之，以求有功，一有失律，则败衄不支，上贻朝廷忧，此边吏之大弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206544_comment'></div>某愚无知，不能晓时事，然自少游四方，窃观当世公卿贤士大夫为不少矣，然未见忧国如家，视民如赤子有如公者，此正朝廷今日寄委之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206544_comment'></div>然溪洞之民，恃险为奸非一日也，必欲加兵尽诛之，则正犹驰韩卢搏蹇兔于穴中，虽有疾足，无所骋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206544_comment'></div>更愿縻以岁月，无急近功，要足以安驯服之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206544_comment'></div>夫致人而不致于人，为主而不为客，亦兵家常胜之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206544_comment'></div>识浅智昏，暗于事机，何足以上裨高明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206544_comment'></div>然自以为辱大君子之知，而意之所欲言者，不敢不自尽耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206544_comment'></div>浼渎清视，惟仁明矜察，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206544_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206487' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206487' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206487?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺正旦表<span class='inlineComment2'>（代虔守作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206487")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206487_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206487'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206487'>陈辂鸣銮，揭示汉仪之盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206487_comment'></div>献琛效职，允怀舜德之敷<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206487_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下圣敬日新，勇智天锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206487_comment'></div>大明继照，御六气以乘乾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206487_comment'></div>百辟在庭，共众星而环极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206487_comment'></div>修礼文之广备，表圣日之光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206487_comment'></div>顾惟履地而戴天，孰不咏仁而蹈德？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206487_comment'></div>臣叨兹眷命，附以名藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206487_comment'></div>玉陛称觞，莫厕鸾鹥之侣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206487_comment'></div>虎城向日，但倾葵藿之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206487_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1206487_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206849' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206849' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206849?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐四年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206849")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206849_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206849'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206849'>殿直杨君一日诣予而告曰：「安持之皇祖考，有高世之行，得无生忍法于善知识者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206849_comment'></div>其事有礼部侍郎李公常、朝奉郎刘公谊之铭文可考，不诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206849_comment'></div>二公皆当时显人，而一言之出，足以信后世，则虽没不朽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206849_comment'></div>独念吾母氏之贤，配先君无违德，而其没也，不克铭以葬，使闺门隐行湮灭而无闻，将无以昭示后世子孙，用是为大惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206849_comment'></div>欲以铭累公，不识可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206849_comment'></div>予得二公铭文读之，窃叹杨氏世为江西右族，赀累钜万，而其父子不以一毫入其胸次，饭蔬饮水，与遗世绝俗之士游，卒能坐亡立逝，无怛于死生之变，则其所养可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206849_comment'></div>而夫人事其舅以为贤妇，配其夫以为贤室，是宜铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206849_comment'></div>乃叙而铭之，使归而揭之墓上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206849_comment'></div>夫人姓张氏，南康军建昌人，居士讳某之室也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206849_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，父讳某，皆隐德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206849_comment'></div>夫人资静淑，尤谨于事佛，乐善好施，姻族内外贫窭者必归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206849_comment'></div>元祐戊辰六月二十四日以疾终于家，越明年正月二十日葬于洪源之南，享年四十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206849_comment'></div>生男八人，女四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206849_comment'></div>长曰安道，安世、安止、安行、安时，皆业儒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206849_comment'></div>曰正真，为浮屠氏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206849_comment'></div>曰安持，绍圣中以材武得官，今为左班殿直、监杭州馀杭县浣坎镇，乃其次子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206849_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1206849'>蠢兹世人，徇物丧己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206849_comment'></div>骄吝日滋，富不期侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206849_comment'></div>于惟杨氏，己物两亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206849_comment'></div>家累万金，视犹秕糠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206849_comment'></div>允矣夫人，其德克配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206849_comment'></div>刻铭墓傍，以诏来裔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1206849_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206883' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206883' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206883?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邹尧叟哀辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1089年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206883")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206883_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206883'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206883'>宋有君子姓邹，名某，字尧叟，邵武泰宁人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206883_comment'></div>先生自少有文名，尤工辞赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206883_comment'></div>比壮，游四方，始从中山刘公彝为学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206883_comment'></div>镌磨浸灌，六经之旨、百氏之书，无不该洽，旁穿曲贯，各得其宗，不为异端迁惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206883_comment'></div>汪洋大肆，发为词章，遂以名称于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206883_comment'></div>嘉祐中登进士第，其莅官虽冗职，必尽其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206883_comment'></div>凡决狱听讼，钩考簿书，赴期会，他人视若不胜其烦，先生处之日未尝废书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206883_comment'></div>其用志益深，后之所自得者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206883_comment'></div>余自垂髫诵先生之文，及长闻其名籍甚，益歆慕之，尚恨未及见，叩其馀论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206883_comment'></div>元丰初，余弃官家居，先生适丁家难，寄余里中，始获从之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206883_comment'></div>先生不予弃，进而友之殆一年，未尝一日相舍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206883_comment'></div>其后先生官于闽，余适东徐，差池南北，遂不复相值，今其已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206883_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206883_comment'></div>先生学充其志，而用不究其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206883_comment'></div>其平昔朋友共学者，往往登显仕，居要津，视其颠沛，忍不一引手提掖之，卒以穷死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206883_comment'></div>噫，命矣，其谁尤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206883_comment'></div>余独恨相去之远，不凭棺一恸，吊其遗孤，以尽其师友之情，故为辞以泄其哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206883_comment'></div>其辞曰：有美一人，众之郭郛兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206883_comment'></div>邦国之祯，应时须兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206883_comment'></div>纯明笃实，允式孚兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206883_comment'></div>胸中之藏，罗琼琚兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206883_comment'></div>位卑德尊，惨莫舒兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206883_comment'></div>汗血龙驹，絷芳岖兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206883_comment'></div>云帆蔽天，胶沮洳兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206883_comment'></div>天地吸嘘，鼓洪炉兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206883_comment'></div>铸物范形，曾莫图兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206883_comment'></div>自尔遭之，末所如兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206883_comment'></div>既实尔德，孰云癯兮？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206883_comment'></div>胡啬尔寿，忽闻徂兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206883_comment'></div>嗟余与子，阻修途兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206883_comment'></div>不得凭棺，吊遗孤兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206883_comment'></div>饮恨于怀，曷由除兮？</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1206883_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206488' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206488?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺坤成节表<span class='inlineComment2'>（代作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1089年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206488")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206488_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206488'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206488'>唐兴帝业，天开润石之祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206488_comment'></div>周兆王基，诗咏《生民》之什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206488_comment'></div>斯人神之协应，罄夷夏以交欣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206488_comment'></div>恭惟太皇太后坤德含洪，离明旁烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206488_comment'></div>正始有光于京室，代终益裕于孙谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206488_comment'></div>万国承规，普被《关雎》之化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206488_comment'></div>群黎遍德，一趋《麟趾》之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206488_comment'></div>臣备位藩臣，驰心魏阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206488_comment'></div>一人有庆，均涵天地之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206488_comment'></div>万寿无疆，愿效岗陵之祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206488_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1206488_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206489' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206489' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206489?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贡物表<span class='inlineComment2'>（代作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1089年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206489")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206489_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206489'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206489'>分职任民，不遗于嫔妇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206489_comment'></div>因土制贡，敢废于玄纤<span class='inlineComment2'>（前件）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206489_comment'></div>经纬有常，质文中理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206489_comment'></div>用参庭实，愧非前列之宝龟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206489_comment'></div>庶广至仁，推作万夫之衣被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206489_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1206489_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　在虔州。有诗。作品：感怀寄乡友。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　在虔州。有文。作品：代太守贺苏左丞启。代虔守谢李运使启。代虔守荐杨孝本奏状。<div id='poem_1206634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206634?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代虔守谢李运使启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1090年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206634")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206634'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206634'>被命吴东，幸叨联属；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206634_comment'></div>领麾江左，获庇恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206634_comment'></div>顾惟无堪，曷称公举？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206634_comment'></div>伏念某蚤膺圣眷，屡握使符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206634_comment'></div>才不适时，愧无实用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206634_comment'></div>学虽笃志，徒守空文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206634_comment'></div>误蒙彊敏之称，复玷该通之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206634_comment'></div>荣踰所望，愧溢于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206634_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官大德并容，至仁博施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206634_comment'></div>不忘敬故，益敦末俗之偷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206634_comment'></div>于以包荒，或副中行之尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206634_comment'></div>致兹庸陋，特与甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206634_comment'></div>敢不誓竭孤忠，永坚素守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206634_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1206634_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206475' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206475' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206475?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代虔守荐杨孝本状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1090年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206475")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206475_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206475'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206475'>右，臣猥以非才，谬当郡寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206475_comment'></div>窃惟事君之义，莫尚以人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206475_comment'></div>而不祥之实，蔽贤为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206475_comment'></div>苟有所知，臣敢不勉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206475_comment'></div>伏见虔州进士杨孝本，学富行纯，为舆论信服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206475_comment'></div>曩游京师，一时忠义之士多从之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206475_comment'></div>短褐不完，饭疏饮水，而束修之馈悉以市书，捆载而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206475_comment'></div>自晦岩穴，不求仕进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206475_comment'></div>乡闾故旧怜其贫，协力周之，非其义不受也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206475_comment'></div>此虽古人操履，无以过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206475_comment'></div>当路柄臣亦尝论荐，然久未蒙旌擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206475_comment'></div>伏望圣慈不以臣言之轻，特加收采，锡之一命，以称朝廷尊德励善之实。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1206475_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　在虔州。待太守望及同僚公平有守。<br /></div>
-----end

宜春
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='01a9a75fb6d74cbe95d5412885eee8ee_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("01a9a75fb6d74cbe95d5412885eee8ee");'><span id='01a9a75fb6d74cbe95d5412885eee8ee_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>，42岁</div><div id='01a9a75fb6d74cbe95d5412885eee8ee' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过宜春，有诗。作品：宜春溪上。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在宜春？过春波亭，有诗。作品：春波亭上。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>宜春道上，有诗。<br /></div>
