-----title
浏阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f4d5eab830d640d4975fedaab8c3065c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f4d5eab830d640d4975fedaab8c3065c");'><span id='f4d5eab830d640d4975fedaab8c3065c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1098')">1094-1098年</a>，42-46岁</div><div id='f4d5eab830d640d4975fedaab8c3065c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　在浏阳，有文。作品：寄俞仲宽书（其一）寄俞仲宽书（其二）寄俞仲宽书（其三）与俞彦修书。寄翁好德书 其一。寄翁好德书 其二。<div id='poem_1206529' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206529' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206529?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄俞仲宽别纸<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206529")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206529_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206529'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206529'>闽之八州，惟建、剑、汀、邵武之民多计产育子，习之成风，虽士人间亦为之，恬不知怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206529_comment'></div>某尝窃悼之，恨世未有诚意，足以感格流俗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206529_comment'></div>与之广谕曲譬，使少变其习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206529_comment'></div>近得吉甫解惑，读之隐然有得于吾心，然尚恨其说似犹以利害告之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206529_comment'></div>若以利言，则「多男多忧」，盖古语有之，非特今日也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206529_comment'></div>孰若以理谕之，使民晓然知有不可为之义，则庶乎其惑可解矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206529_comment'></div>吾郡吾邑此风唯顺昌独甚，富民之家不过二男一女，中下之家大率一男而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206529_comment'></div>小人暴殄天理，侮悖人义，至身陷大恶而不知省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206529_comment'></div>且为父而杀其子，虽豺虎犹不忍为，孰谓人而为之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206529_comment'></div>某比乘舟过境，见有赤子暴尸洲渚间，为乌鹰食者，恻然感之，有泚吾颡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206529_comment'></div>窃惟仲宽仁民爱物出于诚心，计未有以此言闻于左右者，故辄及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206529_comment'></div>莅事间有衣冠之士，傥或相接，愿以至言谕之，使少变一二，莫大之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206529_comment'></div>狂瞽之言，何足仰裨高明万一，徒用增愧耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206529_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206530' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206530?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206530_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206530'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206530'>某软懦不立，迷方之学无以趋今，而望古益远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206530_comment'></div>常惧自画，为士君子鄙弃，每思得朋游共学，前引后驱，以进其不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206530_comment'></div>而所寓乃在乎小州下邑僻陋之邦，贤士大夫罕至其境，乡党之与居，旦暮之与游，不过田夫野老与夫后生晚学章句之儒，辩折声病，为科举之文耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206530_comment'></div>以是而求道，几何不见笑于大方之家？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206530_comment'></div>比因经由，得接教论，若将引至于道者，使驽钝之质增激懦心，慨然知圣人之可窥，而忘其力之不足也，幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206530_comment'></div>迫于之官，不得款奉，徒深歉然耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206530_comment'></div>因风幸时见教，乃所愿望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206530_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206531' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206531' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206531?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206531_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206531'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206531'>顺昌之学久不正师席，得长者留意，学者幸幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206531_comment'></div>好德云何，有意相从否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206531_comment'></div>邑令帅诸生诣门，严师之礼，自近年以来未有如此者，固有道者之不宜辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206531_comment'></div>某亦有书勉之矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206531_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206535' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206535' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206535?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与俞彦修书<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　名袤，仲宽子。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206535")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206535_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206535'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206535'>某昏蔽之久，无以自发，幸蒙君子不见鄙外，曲加奖引，猥赐示问，过自损抑，若将有求者，某何以当之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206535_comment'></div>所谕方寸之间暗浪时时间作，此病岂独公耶，盖学者通患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206535_comment'></div>从心不踰矩，孔子至七十而后能，况馀人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206535_comment'></div>苟未至七十，则犹须操而后存也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206535_comment'></div>故孟子论不动心之道，亦曰「持其志，无暴其气」，曰持之，曰无暴，则是虽孟子，犹不敢任其能尔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206535_comment'></div>虽然，忘之不可也，助长又不可也，其用力固有在矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206535_comment'></div>循是充之，使吾胸中浩然，则暗浪岂不自息欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206535_comment'></div>浼渎高明，非敢谓足以资足下之所须，姑欲取正其是非耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206535_comment'></div>言之是耶，固愿与朋友共之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206535_comment'></div>或未中理，幸明告我，庶警未悟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1206535_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206536' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206536' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206536?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与俞彦修书<span class='inlineComment2'>（二）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206536")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206536_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206536'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206536'>某愚无似，无过人器识，又学未优而仕，为世累羁缠，坚白未能万一于古人，而磨涅不已，几何而不至于淄磷欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206536_comment'></div>从游之徒又无箴规磨切之益，恐遂至于目盲齿豁，老死于无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206536_comment'></div>故每逢学士真儒，则愧汗惕息发于颜面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206536_comment'></div>岂意足下收怜，犹以君子望之，幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206536_comment'></div>敢不刻意自勉，庶几不负所期耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206536_comment'></div>未涯良晤，驰想何已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1206536_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206533' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206533' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206533?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄翁好德书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206533")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206533_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206533'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206533'>前日公皂还仓卒，奉问不谨，深用惶愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206533_comment'></div>为别踰月，不审孝履何如，伏惟万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206533_comment'></div>某愚无似，加以齿少，视公为前辈，每辱眷遇，进之为执友之游，顾何足当？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206533_comment'></div>自惟直谅多闻之益，所得于长者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206533_comment'></div>然至于古人为学之大方，则语未尝及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206533_comment'></div>今兹经由，因得奉晤语，慨然乃自进于圣人之学，非笃信好古，其何能尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206533_comment'></div>益使昏懦之心思自奋励，锐然知圣域之可到，而不知愚鄙之不可彊也，幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206533_comment'></div>方且进己之有，挹公之馀，以相扶助，属之官有期，遽然西归，不得从容以尽讲习之乐，至今犹以为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206533_comment'></div>然尝谓君子之学求仁而已，伯夷之清，伊尹之任，柳下惠之和，皆圣人也，其道不同而趋向则同者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206533_comment'></div>曰仁而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206533_comment'></div>故古之君子虽相去千里，相望异世，或出或处，或默或语，未尝同及，考其所归，若合符契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206533_comment'></div>然则吾徒所学，又奚必朝闻而暮讲之欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206533_comment'></div>要同归于仁而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206533_comment'></div>苟知此，则前日之遽然犹不足恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206533_comment'></div>夫求仁之方，孔子盖言之详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206533_comment'></div>然而亲炙之徒，其说犹有未闻者，岂孔子有隐于彼欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206533_comment'></div>犹之大匠能诲人以规矩，不能与之巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206533_comment'></div>故言之在我，闻不闻者在彼，虽圣人亦不能进其不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206533_comment'></div>后世之士未尝精思力究，妄以肤见臆度，求尽圣人之微言，分文析字，寸量铢较，自谓得之，而不知去本益远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206533_comment'></div>夫至道之归，固非笔舌能尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206533_comment'></div>要以身体之、心验之，雍容自尽于燕闲静一之中，默而识之，兼忘于书言意象之表，则庶乎其至矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206533_comment'></div>反是，皆口耳诵数之学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206533_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206533_comment'></div>道无传久矣，举天下皆溺于末习，不有豪杰之士，孰能自拔流俗，以追圣学？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206533_comment'></div>若某之不肖，岂敢自谓能尔！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206533_comment'></div>幸尝侧闻先生长者之馀论，窃有志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206533_comment'></div>尚赖朋游共学，左右提掖，相进于此道，每得一人焉，则通夕不寐，喜见颜面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206533_comment'></div>今又得吾好德，益知朋友之足望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206533_comment'></div>区区临纸不能尽万一，未间，惟力学慎爱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1206533_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206534' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206534' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206534?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206534_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206534'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206534'>明道行状计已读之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206534_comment'></div>惟吾先生道学行义足以泽世垂后，进不得行其志，退未及明之书而死，使其道将遂泯灭而无传，则学者不忍焉，此行状叙述所以作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206534_comment'></div>道废千年，士不知所止，故物我异观，天人殊归，而高明中庸之学析为二，致天下泯然莫以为非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206534_comment'></div>故行状之末，深论吾先生之趋，以明世学之失，庶几志道之士有闻风而起者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206534_comment'></div>则行状之传，盖将以明道，非如长者所疑也，幸亮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206534_comment'></div>某向亦尝作哀辞一篇，谩录去，试一观之如何耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206534_comment'></div>好德闲居，与学者相聚，势未能免，仲宽礼意勤厚，不必辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206534_comment'></div>若于僧寺中得十数人而止，如公前日之言固善矣，但恐同邑之士翕然从之，则公亦不得而拒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206534_comment'></div>使县庠一空，则于邑中事有所未顺，公更思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206534_comment'></div>尝许见过，尚能如言否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206534_comment'></div>非敢望也，乃所愿耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1206534_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　在浏阳，有惠政。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　在浏阳，在四牌楼坊题“龟山遗爱”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　在浏阳，有文。作品：谢程漕书。上提举书。<div id='poem_1206539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206539' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206539?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢程漕书<span class='inlineComment2'>（博文）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206539")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206539_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206539'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206539'>某闽陬鄙人也，在昔执事出守乡邦，某方窃居下邑，尝误辱一言之誉，欲召寘学校，自惟荒薄，不敢承命，以取忝冒无实之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206539_comment'></div>比来湖湘，始得从部吏之末，瞻望舄履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206539_comment'></div>碌碌无适时才用，方愧惧踧踖不宁，恐明知之下，无以自逭瘝旷，故不敢辄恃昔日眷遇之私，妄进一言，上浼高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206539_comment'></div>岂虞过听，远示教翰，见索鄙文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206539_comment'></div>奉命惊惶，荣愧交集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206539_comment'></div>夫荆湖望高地重，譬之据九达之衢、舟车之会，四方百物盖衔尾结辙而至，明玑翡翠、夜光之璧、照乘之珍为不乏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206539_comment'></div>有人于此，持千金之资，坐市区，售奇货，宜无不获也，而搜罗掇拾，犹下及于三家之市，非务欲兼收尽取，不遗一物，其何尔乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206539_comment'></div>长沙盖南北冲会之市区也，执事以清名重德，简在君相，馀论所及，天下以为轻重，而士之荣辱系焉，则所持之资，非特千金也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206539_comment'></div>部属之吏负超卓瑰异之才，抱其器欲贾于左右者岂一二哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206539_comment'></div>往往以疏逖，无先为容者，不能自达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206539_comment'></div>顾某何人，乃独以经术取之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206539_comment'></div>非执事敦大兼容，欲尽取三家之市，何以得此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206539_comment'></div>惠出非望，刻铭肺腑，不敢忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206539_comment'></div>某自少尝从事于学，六经微言虽未能究观尽识，然尝侧闻缙绅先生绪论，窃有意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206539_comment'></div>夫《易》于六经尤难知，自汉魏以来，以《易》名家者殆数十百人，观其用力之勤，盖自谓能窥天人之奥，著为成书，足以师后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206539_comment'></div>然其书具在，不为士大夫议评讪笑用覆酱瓿者无几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206539_comment'></div>然则《易》其可易言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206539_comment'></div>以孔子之圣，犹曰「加我数年，五十以学《易》」，其玩味之久，至于韦编三绝，况其下者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206539_comment'></div>某用是于《易》虽欲自进一辞，而不能措笔于其间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206539_comment'></div>虽然，学《易》者贵有得于象意之表而已，区区于章句之末，又安能免于讥评讪笑乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206539_comment'></div>故承命以来，无以上副所知，愧汗惕息，若无所容措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206539_comment'></div>蒙索他文，谨录古律诗、序、记合一编冒献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206539_comment'></div>玷浼清视，不胜惶惧战慄之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1206539_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206545' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206545' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206545?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上提举书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206545")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206545_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206545'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206545'>某闻之，在下位不获乎上，民不可得而治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206545_comment'></div>获乎上有道，其本在于明善诚身而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206545_comment'></div>某愚无似，虽未能明善诚身，窃有志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206545_comment'></div>不幸迫于穷空，故未及信而仕，徒苟升合之禄以自活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206545_comment'></div>然一邑之中，有民有社，休戚系焉，又不得如古之抱关击柝者之无责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206545_comment'></div>其自视欿然，惧终无以取获乎上，方罪戾是忧，尚何望治民之效哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206545_comment'></div>恭惟阁下以清德重望，为时显人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206545_comment'></div>当朝廷更法造令之初，遴简贤才，出将使指，而阁下首被其选，则明天子所以眷倚之意何如哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206545_comment'></div>下车之初，某幸得从部吏之末，瞻望舄履，与闻謦欬之馀论，高明之见，洞照幽隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206545_comment'></div>而不以贤贵自挟，询谋博访，务尽下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206545_comment'></div>凡所以丁宁教戒者，无非以民为念，非笃厚仁人以天下之重自任，其何能尔哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206545_comment'></div>某退而私自喜幸曰：「阁下之盛德兼容如此，某虽愚无似，不足以取获乎上，亦庶乎有赖以自全也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206545_comment'></div>既而寮吏相与言曰，阁下之务尽下情如此，法令有疑而未安者，可不自尽哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206545_comment'></div>疑而匿情，非所以事大君子之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206545_comment'></div>某私窃识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206545_comment'></div>近承州符，录准使命，应旧系代名人役未满而募充者，例不支钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206545_comment'></div>此于法有疑而未安者，故不敢不自尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206545_comment'></div>某不能周知十邑之利害，宁乡之请如此，是必宁乡可行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206545_comment'></div>浏阳之民未罢役以前，而雇人代充者，皆月计其直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206545_comment'></div>然每有踰期不偿而至于理诉者，时时有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206545_comment'></div>官既罢役矣，而彼自愿充，则又安肯复与之直？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206545_comment'></div>推之人情，万无此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206545_comment'></div>夫募役者亦岂有他意哉，为利而来耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206545_comment'></div>既不与之直，则谁复愿者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206545_comment'></div>若令取诸旧役者，则官既罢其役矣，而又使之出其直，则是昔之放罢皆罔之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206545_comment'></div>使代名者不愿而求去，则如之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206545_comment'></div>势须彊之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206545_comment'></div>彊之虽从，而匮乏者无资以自给，则势不能久也，而遂至于逃亡，则如之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206545_comment'></div>必以刑加之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206545_comment'></div>如是，得无骇民乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206545_comment'></div>然朝旨自有明文，特为乡差未满者设耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206545_comment'></div>代名之人，法所不载，不惟于理势未安，于前后敕旨亦自有妨，幸加明察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206545_comment'></div>如宁乡可行则行之，他邑使各陈其可否，然后徐审处之，莫大之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206545_comment'></div>如郴州议保正长不支钱，此固元丰旧法，行之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206545_comment'></div>然什伍之法，盖兆于治古之时，而元丰保正之役其实三大户也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206545_comment'></div>既使之输钱，又使之充役，则免役之名浮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206545_comment'></div>元祐之间，果于罢去而不疑者，特藉此为说耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206545_comment'></div>故朝廷更法之初，指言不得用保正长者，盖亦惩此说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206545_comment'></div>今又议不支钱，恐非朝廷始意，且不能使元祐议法者无辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206545_comment'></div>某窃谓不若计其岁雇之直，蠲减所出役钱为善耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206545_comment'></div>夫建议不支钱者，其意不过欲寡取于民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206545_comment'></div>某不能周知一路，以长沙一郡计之，所敷之数比元丰旧额固已十蠲其六七矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206545_comment'></div>元祐差役，自二百五十亩以上充弓手，大抵十年两役也，计其雇直，则十年所出无虑二百千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206545_comment'></div>以今法言之，有田二百五十亩，十年所输才五十馀千耳，其为法岂不优哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206545_comment'></div>方之元丰，所蠲如此，较之元祐，其利又如此，虽取之何伤也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206545_comment'></div>又奚必铢铢计其多寡哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206545_comment'></div>某愚不自量，妄以狂瞽之言闻于左右，是即蓍龟之神以自取渎耳，何足以上裨高明万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206545_comment'></div>然惓惓之情不敢不自尽者，盖以为事大君子之道，义当如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206545_comment'></div>惟仁明察其愚诚，不加妄言之诛，则幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206545_comment'></div>冒犯威严，俯伏俟命，不胜战慄之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1206545_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　在浏阳，有诗。作品：寄湘乡令张世贤。县斋书事寄湘乡令张世贤。县斋书事。县斋书事三首（其一）县斋书事三首（其二）县斋书事三首（其三）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　在浏阳，蔡安礼以宏词见勉，公寄诗。作品：安礼以宏词见勉奉寄。安礼以宏词见勉因成绝句奉寄。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　在浏阳，有诗。作品：和潭卒张朝请行县言怀。又用前韵和早梅二首（其一）又用前韵和早梅二首（其二）和张倅行县。假山。检田。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　在浏阳，于县圃建飞鷃亭并题额。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年5月5日</a>　在浏阳，建归鸿阁，作记。作品：归鸿阁记。<div id='poem_1206836' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206836' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206836?labeling=true' target='_blank'>归鸿阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年5月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206836")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206836_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206836'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206836'>县宇西北墉之隅有废址焉，久茀不治，畜豕之所游，鼯狌狸鼠之所家，荒堙芜没，蔚为秽墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206836_comment'></div>予一日曳杖蹑履，徜徉乎其下，周览左右，洒然异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206836_comment'></div>披蓁薙蔓，而嘉木茂卉连山穷谷，挺芳含媚，隐然四出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206836_comment'></div>乃取县庑之弃材为阁于其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206836_comment'></div>既成，肃宾而落之，相与扬眉拭目而望，微云洞开，一目千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206836_comment'></div>于是以「归鸿」名之，盖取昔人所谓目送归鸿之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206836_comment'></div>客有曰：「异乎哉，子之名阁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206836_comment'></div>始子以飞鴳名其亭，殆将有志乎蓬蒿之间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206836_comment'></div>今又以归鸿名其阁，尔之中无乃觳觫而受变于物欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206836_comment'></div>予謷然不答，隐几而卧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206836_comment'></div>俄而曰：「噫嘻，居，吾语汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206836_comment'></div>今人履步仞之丘，居环堵之室，虽有离朱之明，视不过寻常，踰阈之外，则不能瞩及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206836_comment'></div>夫登泰山之崖，游昆崙之墟，下临虞渊，观日之出入，则六合为小矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206836_comment'></div>夫阁非有加损也，而所寓不同，见亦随异焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206836_comment'></div>其所以见者，虽晋朦不亡也，物亦恶能变哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206836_comment'></div>且鸿之冥冥，乘飞云，御泠风，上窥青天，子其以是为高乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206836_comment'></div>鴳之腾跃而上，不过数仞而下，子其以是为卑乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206836_comment'></div>是未知各适其适也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206836_comment'></div>物各适其适，则天地之滨犹蓬蒿也，恶睹其异哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206836_comment'></div>盖天地之间一气而万形，一息而成古今，达观之士会物于一己，通昼夜而知，则虽死生之变无怛矣，又况其凡乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206836_comment'></div>惟世之人舞智自私，而其明不足以窥天人之蕴，故物我异观，而肝胆之间楚越矣，又恶足与语天理哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206836_comment'></div>子方疑我之觳觫而受变，予亦陋子之自梏于见闻也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206836_comment'></div>客于是规规然自失，忘其所以异，唯唯而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206836_comment'></div>予顾谓二三子，志之，镵诸石。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1206836_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　在浏阳，有诗题飞鷃亭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　在浏阳，有诗题归鸿阁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年5月18日</a>　在浏阳，三子遹生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　在浏阳，有诗。作品：浏阳五咏（洄渊浩荡白鸥飞）浏阳五咏（帘卷晴空独倚栏）浏阳五咏（芙蓉雕尽蕙兰芳）浏阳五咏（柔条䟱蔓绿交加）浏阳五咏（圣童去后水云门）荷花。偶成（天远何须问）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　在浏阳，著史论十篇寄程颐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　在浏阳，有书寄程颐论西铭。作品：寄伊川先生书。答伊川先生书。<div id='poem_1206514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄伊川先生书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206514")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206514'>某窃谓道之不明，智者过之，《西铭》之书，其几于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206514_comment'></div>昔之问仁于孔子者多矣，虽颜渊、仲弓之徒，所以告之者，不过求仁之方耳，至于仁之体未尝言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206514_comment'></div>孟子曰：「仁，人心也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206514_comment'></div>义，人路也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206514_comment'></div>言仁之尽最亲，无如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206514_comment'></div>然本体用兼举两言之，未闻如《西铭》之说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206514_comment'></div>孔孟岂有隐哉，盖不敢过之，以起后学之弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206514_comment'></div>且墨氏兼爱，固仁者之事也，其流卒至于无父，岂墨子之罪耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206514_comment'></div>孟子力攻之，必归罪于墨子者，正其本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206514_comment'></div>故君子言必虑其所终，行必稽其所弊，正谓此耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206514_comment'></div>《西铭》之书发明圣人微意至深，然而言体而不及用，恐其流遂至于兼爱，则后世有圣贤者出，推本而论之，未免归罪于横渠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206514_comment'></div>某窃意此书盖西人共守而谨行之者也，愿得一言推明其用，与之并行，庶乎学者体用兼明，而不至于流荡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206514_comment'></div>横渠之学造极天人之蕴，非后学所能窥测，然所疑如此，故辄言之，先生以为如何？</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206514_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答伊川先生书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206515")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206515'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206515'>示论《西铭》微旨，晓然具悉，如侍几席，亲承训诱也，幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206515_comment'></div>某昔从明道，即授以《西铭》使读之，寻绎累日乃若有得，始知为学之大方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206515_comment'></div>是将终身佩服，岂敢妄疑其失，比同于墨氏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206515_comment'></div>前书所论，谓《西铭》之书以民为同胞，长其长，幼其幼，以鳏寡孤独为兄弟之无告者，所谓明理一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206515_comment'></div>然其弊无亲亲之杀，非明者默识于言意之表，乌知所谓理一而分殊哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206515_comment'></div>故切恐其流遂至于兼爱，非谓《西铭》之书为兼爱而发，与墨氏同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206515_comment'></div>古之人所以大过人者无他，善推其所为而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206515_comment'></div>「老吾老，以及人之老，幼吾幼，以及人之幼」，所谓推之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206515_comment'></div>孔子曰「老者安之，少者怀之」，则无事乎推矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206515_comment'></div>无事乎推者，理一故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206515_comment'></div>理一而分殊，故圣人称物而平施之，兹所以为仁之至、义之尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206515_comment'></div>何谓称物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206515_comment'></div>亲疏远近各当其分，所谓称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206515_comment'></div>何谓平施？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206515_comment'></div>所以施之，其心一焉，所谓平也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206515_comment'></div>某昔者窃意《西铭》之书有平施之方，无称物之义，故曰「言体而不及用」，盖指仁义为说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206515_comment'></div>故仁之过，其蔽无分，无分则妨义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206515_comment'></div>义之过，其流自私，自私则害仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206515_comment'></div>害仁则杨氏之为我也，妨义则墨氏之兼爱也，二者其失虽殊，其所以得罪于圣人则均矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206515_comment'></div>《西铭》之旨隐奥难知，固前圣所未发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206515_comment'></div>前书所论窃谓过之者，特疑其辞有未达耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206515_comment'></div>今得先生开论，丁宁传之，学者自当释然无惑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206515_comment'></div>相去阻修，未缘趋侍以请毕馀教，兹为恨耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1206515_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　在浏阳，寄伊川所著《史论》十篇。有孝思堂记。<div id='poem_1206835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孝思堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206835")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206835'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206835'>绍圣元年，龙图谢公以疾薨于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206835_comment'></div>越明年，其子以柩归葬于建安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206835_comment'></div>又明年襄事，乃作孝思之堂，属予为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206835_comment'></div>予为之言曰：孝之德，其可谓至德也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206835_comment'></div>虽小夫贱隶、荛童牧叟，下逮穷发荒蜒无知之民，皆知其为美称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206835_comment'></div>一被之以不孝之名，则心踧踖而颜忸怩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206835_comment'></div>若夫夷考其实，则学士大夫诵六艺之文，讲先生仁义之说，有病其难者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206835_comment'></div>然则孝之德，其可谓至德矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206835_comment'></div>古之仁人孝子，岂他求哉，亦不过乎物而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206835_comment'></div>所谓物者，凡受于吾亲者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206835_comment'></div>故身者亲之枝，亲者身之本，其体一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206835_comment'></div>流僻涤滥之音，奇邪慢戏之物，日亵于耳目，而视听言动一失其则焉，皆过乎物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206835_comment'></div>过乎物，是不敬其身也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206835_comment'></div>不敬其身，是不敬其亲也，可不慎欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206835_comment'></div>故君子居处必庄，事君必忠，莅官必敬，朋友必信，战阵必勇，而后足以成亲之名，反是皆忘亲者也，又恶得为孝乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206835_comment'></div>惟公以布衣起闽陬数千里之外，隐然为世名臣，其殊功异德，足以励世范俗，铭鼎彝而镂金石，为邦家之光，况其所以训迪子孙者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206835_comment'></div>今其子乃不忘乎孝思，是能承公之训，将有志乎古之所谓孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206835_comment'></div>吾是以知谢氏之后能不坠其先烈，又光大之，其有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206835_comment'></div>故余承命不辞，而喜为天下道也，于是乎书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1206835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　在浏阳，安抚使张公舜民以客礼待之。有书与州牧乞求赈饥。作品：与州牧书乞求赈饥。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　在浏阳，有诗寄长沙孙照远。作品：寄长沙簿孙昭远。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　在浏阳，令旅居本县穷饿者可申请获寺舍饮食，终因去官而未及施行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年1月18日</a>　在浏阳，长子迪生孙云。<br /></div>
-----end

武夷山

-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4ca5ee585fd04cb8af5c67207b74118c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4ca5ee585fd04cb8af5c67207b74118c");'><span id='4ca5ee585fd04cb8af5c67207b74118c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>，46岁</div><div id='4ca5ee585fd04cb8af5c67207b74118c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　至杭州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='be68e4d2deb845d8a3faf1c5280edb79_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("be68e4d2deb845d8a3faf1c5280edb79");'><span id='be68e4d2deb845d8a3faf1c5280edb79_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>，47岁</div><div id='be68e4d2deb845d8a3faf1c5280edb79' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年10月8日</a>　初八日，至杭州，谒府公丰相之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　在钱塘江上，有诗。作品：梭山候潮。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　在杭州观潮。作品：过钱塘江迎潮。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b1f0438f962c4173ab7088ebb8268798_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b1f0438f962c4173ab7088ebb8268798");'><span id='b1f0438f962c4173ab7088ebb8268798_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>，55岁</div><div id='b1f0438f962c4173ab7088ebb8268798' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年3月19日</a>　到余杭任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　在余杭，有惠政。时蔡京母坟在余杭，欲浚湖潴水为形势便利，为公所沮。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　在余杭。有语录记丁亥三月间事。作品：余杭所闻一。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年7月5日</a>　在余杭。五子造生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年8月26日</a>　在余杭，有诗。作品：跋横渠先生书及康节先生人贵有精神诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　在余杭，有文。作品：陳居士傳。田曹吴公文集序。邹尧叟墓志铭。吴国华墓志铭。<div id='poem_1206847' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206847' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206847?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈居士传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年11月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206847")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206847_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206847'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206847'>陈选，南剑州将乐人，世以豪赀为乡闾大姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206847_comment'></div>其为人忠信愿悫，不妄与人交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206847_comment'></div>晨兴正冠修容坐堂上，夫妇相对如宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206847_comment'></div>非庆吊未尝出门，虽连墙有经时不见其面者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206847_comment'></div>间有所之，必筮而后往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206847_comment'></div>家人俟其归，其迹可数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206847_comment'></div>平居恂恂，人莫见其喜怒，闺门之内雍如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206847_comment'></div>其遇人无长幼必尽诚敬，虽横逆有恶声至，如弗闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206847_comment'></div>视其容貌泊然，若无足芥蒂者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206847_comment'></div>以故人亦信之，后虽有喜侵暴者，不敢犯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206847_comment'></div>卒年四十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206847_comment'></div>龟山杨某曰：予尝读沈公《笔谈》，见其所载杜生事，沈公自谓时方有军事，至夜半未卧，罢甚，僚属有谈杜生者，闻之不觉肃然忘其劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206847_comment'></div>考公之所为，于杜生几可无悔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206847_comment'></div>非其中有所养，讵能若是哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206847_comment'></div>惜公之亡，予尚幼，未能究知其所有，故不得而备论之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206847_comment'></div>当是时，陋郊小邑无缙绅先生明道德之归，以觉斯人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206847_comment'></div>又无高世之士含德隐耀，相与薰陶浸灌，辅成其美，此予所以深嗟而屡叹之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206847_comment'></div>然观其襟度夷旷，不可污挠，盖有非学之所能至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206847_comment'></div>世之薄夫浅子，一有戾己，仅如毛发，则悻悻然见于颜面，必反之而后已，其视公为如何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206847_comment'></div>故特为之论著，以示其子孙，使知先世所以遗己者在此不在彼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206847_comment'></div>公少时有故人将亡，子尚幼，以白金数镒委之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206847_comment'></div>比其子壮，公召与之，其人矍然谢之，初弗知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206847_comment'></div>盖其信义足以托孤如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206847_comment'></div>然此在公为不足书者，而邑人以是多公，故并述之，附于其末。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1206847_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206652' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206652' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206652?labeling=true' target='_blank'>田曹吴公文集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206652")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206652_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206652'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206652'>吾郡审律先生集录其先君遗文数百篇，以书属予为序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206652_comment'></div>田曹吾不及见其人，因得诵其诗，论其世，稽其行事，得其所以修之身、刑之家、施诸有政者为详焉，而后益知嘉祐、治平之间泽之入人深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206652_comment'></div>当是时，学士大夫达而位乎朝，则著之事业，光明硕大，追配前哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206652_comment'></div>其不显而在下，则载之空文，犹足以私淑诸人，如公之徒是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206652_comment'></div>孟子曰：「王者之迹熄而诗亡，诗亡然后《春秋》作」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206652_comment'></div>诗之存亡关时之盛衰，岂不信矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206652_comment'></div>公之仕不充其志，而用不究其才，故未老而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206652_comment'></div>其平居暇日有动于中而形诸外者，一见于诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206652_comment'></div>其偶俪应用之文，亦皆有典则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206652_comment'></div>其辞直而文，质而不俚，优游自适，有高人逸士之气，故其流风馀韵，足以遗其子孙，化其乡人，皆可见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206652_comment'></div>今其子弟之贤者多隐德不求闻达，而足以文行知名朝廷者二人焉，审律其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206652_comment'></div>审律名仪，去年以遗逸被召，相君说之，除大成府，审验音律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206652_comment'></div>已而非其好也，浩然有归志，盖有公之遗风也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206652_comment'></div>公之诗文足以自表于世，无待于余言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206652_comment'></div>至其所以遗子孙者，世或未之知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206652_comment'></div>故详著之，使夫乐道人之善者与闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206652_comment'></div>公姓吴，讳辅，字鼎臣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1206652_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206853' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206853' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206853?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邹尧叟墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观元年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206853")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206853_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206853'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206853'>先生讳某，字尧叟，姓邹氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206853_comment'></div>其先出于鲁国之邾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206853_comment'></div>唐季之乱，避地闽中，故今为邵武军泰宁人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206853_comment'></div>曾祖某，祖某，父某，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206853_comment'></div>先生自少有文名，尤工词赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206853_comment'></div>比壮游四方，始从中山刘公先生彝为学，六经之旨、百氏之书，无不该洽，旁穿曲贯，各得其宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206853_comment'></div>汪洋大肆，发为文章，遂以名闻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206853_comment'></div>嘉祐中登进士第，调淮阳军司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206853_comment'></div>丁父忧，服除，再调南剑州剑浦县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206853_comment'></div>监建州买纳茶场，移福州闽清县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206853_comment'></div>用荐者改宣德郎、知宣州宣城县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206853_comment'></div>元祐四年二月十八日以疾卒于官舍之正寝，享年五十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206853_comment'></div>先生为人重厚寡言，虽家人未尝见其喜愠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206853_comment'></div>貌温而气和，遇事坚正，不可以非义回屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206853_comment'></div>初在淮阳，卒有受杖不服而肆言，守怒，欲斩之，议不决，以其事付先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206853_comment'></div>已而复欲遂前议，先生不受令，守益怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206853_comment'></div>先生以为事在有司，则有常法，执之不移，士论韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206853_comment'></div>其莅官临民，虽冗职必尽力，故所至有风绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206853_comment'></div>其决狱听讼，钩考簿书，赴期会，他人观之若不胜其烦，先生处之裕如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206853_comment'></div>手未尝释卷也，故其用志益深，学之所造者远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206853_comment'></div>先生既没，子尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206853_comment'></div>大观元年十二月十五日始克葬于常州宜兴县善奉乡横山村黄宗坞之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206853_comment'></div>娶刘氏，先生彝之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206853_comment'></div>子男若干，曰某，曰某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206853_comment'></div>呜呼，先生学充其志，而用不究其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206853_comment'></div>一时朋游共学者登显仕，居要津，视其颠仆，忍不一引手提掖之，卒以穷死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206853_comment'></div>噫，命矣，其尚谁尤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206853_comment'></div>故叙而铭之，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1206853'>有美斯人，君子儒兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206853_comment'></div>纯明笃实，允式孚兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206853_comment'></div>胸中之藏，罗琼琚兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206853_comment'></div>位卑德尊，惨莫舒兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206853_comment'></div>汗血龙驹，絷荒岖兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206853_comment'></div>云帆蔽天，胶沮洳兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206853_comment'></div>天地吸嘘，鼓洪炉兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206853_comment'></div>铸物范形，曾莫图兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206853_comment'></div>自尔遭之，人莫如兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206853_comment'></div>既厚尔德，孰云癯兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206853_comment'></div>黄宗之原，安此居兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206853_comment'></div>镂石纪辞，永不渝兮！</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1206853_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206854' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206854' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206854?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴国华墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206854")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206854_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206854'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206854'>延平据闽之要津，号称多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206854_comment'></div>而以学行著闻乡闾者，吴氏有三人焉：曰某，字及之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206854_comment'></div>曰某，字季明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206854_comment'></div>而审律先生，其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206854_comment'></div>当嘉祐、治平之间，士方以声律偶俪之文争名于时，而三人者独相与切磋，以穷经学古为务，不事科举，退老于家，若将终身焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206854_comment'></div>其能自拔，贤于流俗远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206854_comment'></div>其后季明以经行被召，不赴，授某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206854_comment'></div>而审律先生晚亦出仕，独及之卒于布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206854_comment'></div>予视三人者为前辈，而少得从审律游最厚，先生不予鄙，进而友之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206854_comment'></div>今其亡也，以铭属予，何可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206854_comment'></div>乃序焉，铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206854_comment'></div>先生讳仪，字国华，世为延平人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206854_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，赠某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206854_comment'></div>父讳某，历任某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206854_comment'></div>先生为人刚毅笃实，洞见城府，而善善恶恶无所容贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206854_comment'></div>其事亲以孝显，交朋友以信义著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206854_comment'></div>自少笃志彊学，老益不懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206854_comment'></div>六经百代之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206854_comment'></div>盖无所不究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206854_comment'></div>穷探博取，自信不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206854_comment'></div>尤深于《诗》、《易》，皆有成说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206854_comment'></div>晚益玩心于象数音律之学，自为一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206854_comment'></div>有文集若干卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206854_comment'></div>崇宁五年诏求天下遗逸，部使者以先生应诏，辞不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206854_comment'></div>已而敦迫之，乃乘驿就道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206854_comment'></div>今相太师公见而说之，授将仕郎、大晟府审验音律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206854_comment'></div>未几府罢，先生亦浩然而归，不复出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206854_comment'></div>大观元年某月某日以疾卒于家，享年若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206854_comment'></div>某月某日葬于某所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206854_comment'></div>先生娶陈氏，某人之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206854_comment'></div>无子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206854_comment'></div>有女三人：长适某，次某，皆先卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206854_comment'></div>次适某官杨某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206854_comment'></div>呜呼，吾闻有德者必有后，而先生乃无子以奉其祀，是尤可哀也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206854_comment'></div>故为铭诗以慰诸幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206854_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1206854'>人孰无宗，世久则迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206854_comment'></div>惟德与名，万世之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206854_comment'></div>德名之孚，先生有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206854_comment'></div>不亡者存，夫又何悲！</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1206854_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　在余杭，有罗从彦所录见闻录。作品：余杭所闻二。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　在余杭，有陈渊录见闻录。作品：余杭所闻三。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　在余杭。问两浙路提学郑季常治《诗》一。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d8c65b421fb74f5c9ca5075ccba1b51a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d8c65b421fb74f5c9ca5075ccba1b51a");'><span id='d8c65b421fb74f5c9ca5075ccba1b51a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>，56岁</div><div id='d8c65b421fb74f5c9ca5075ccba1b51a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年3月</a>　是年三月，以八宝恩转奉议郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年9月28日</a>　在余杭。迁应天府敦宗院宗子博士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年10月1日</a>　交割县事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　在余杭。有文。作品：吴子正墓志铭。<div id='poem_1206855' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206855' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206855?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴子正墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206855")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206855_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206855'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206855'>君讳思，字子正，姓吴氏，邵武人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206855_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，祖讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206855_comment'></div>父讳某，累赠宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206855_comment'></div>母朱氏，封蓬莱、福昌二县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206855_comment'></div>君之皇考以上，世有隐德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206855_comment'></div>至君始以进士起家，中元丰三年第，授蕲州黄梅县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206855_comment'></div>再调处州右司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206855_comment'></div>俗犷悍，喜讼斗，吏明习法令，挟以为奸，故狱事视他郡为难治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206855_comment'></div>君敏达彊济，吏不能欺，事至迎刃辄解，无留狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206855_comment'></div>会昌民有诬告毒死者，县狱具，君为直其冤，得不死者五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206855_comment'></div>令狠愎，讼君不已，弥年不敢决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206855_comment'></div>其后更二狱，卒如君所直也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206855_comment'></div>君之全活五人，法当迁秩，任事者不以闻，而君亦置不问也，曰：「吾为理官，狱求生，蕲尽吾职而已，无他觊也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206855_comment'></div>闻者以君为长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206855_comment'></div>就移和州防御推官，知吉州吉水县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206855_comment'></div>有老吏舞智玩法，为邑巨蠹，君得其状，系治之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206855_comment'></div>吏穷迫，欲以事污君，缓其狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206855_comment'></div>阚君之亡，谬为家问，置金其中，嘱小吏内之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206855_comment'></div>君夫人黄氏得书觉重，疑之，却不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206855_comment'></div>君适自外至，发书得金，诘其所自，为诬者情得，咸伏其辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206855_comment'></div>故缙绅皆知黄氏之贤，而益奇君绳家有法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206855_comment'></div>用是当路交荐之，改宣义郎、知池州建德县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206855_comment'></div>君始至，大兴学校，劝农桑，教民力本，岁馀邑大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206855_comment'></div>迄去，狱无系囚，民到于今颂之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206855_comment'></div>以年劳改宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206855_comment'></div>上即位，覃恩迁奉议郎，赐绯衣银鱼，辟福建路转运司管勾文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206855_comment'></div>明年丁太夫人忧，服除，监江州广临监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206855_comment'></div>会更钱法，日夜鸠工赴期会，旁视若不可堪，而君独裕如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206855_comment'></div>未几以课最闻，再迁承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206855_comment'></div>还阙，除监大观库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206855_comment'></div>遂以疾卒于京师，大观元年某月某日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206855_comment'></div>享年五十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206855_comment'></div>君娶黄氏，左中散大夫某之女，封寿安县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206855_comment'></div>有贤行，配君无违德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206855_comment'></div>男一人曰伟明，擢崇宁五年进士第，秀州崇德县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206855_comment'></div>女二人：长适某，次适某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206855_comment'></div>君为人乐易，不事表襮，居家奉亲无违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206855_comment'></div>兄亡，事寡嫂尽敬，畜其孤如己子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206855_comment'></div>家素贫，清约自克，而赒恤族党无吝色，内外姻睦，人无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206855_comment'></div>初与侍御邹公某、管城尉游君某友善，二人皆蚤世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206855_comment'></div>君教育其子，恤其家，卒克有立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206855_comment'></div>古之朋友视兄弟，斯道废久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206855_comment'></div>观公所为，足以激颓俗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206855_comment'></div>性嗜学，自六经百氏、古今传记，盖无所不读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206855_comment'></div>下逮山经地志、阴阳卜筮星历之书，浮屠道家之说，亦无所不究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206855_comment'></div>旁穿曲贯，各得其宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206855_comment'></div>为文长于论议，尤工于诗，辞义清远，有作者风气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206855_comment'></div>莅官临政务近民，不为进趋计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206855_comment'></div>明达吏治，所至有称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206855_comment'></div>士论每以用不极其材为恨，而君处筦库恬然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206855_comment'></div>其自守不回盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206855_comment'></div>有文集五十卷，《契丹西夏录》十卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206855_comment'></div>疾且革，为治命数百言，惟以孝弟诏其子孙，不及其他，非守死善道，何以有此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206855_comment'></div>君既没之明年，其孤奉君之柩归，将以某年某月某日葬君于某所，道过钱塘，以尚书户部黄公之状来乞铭，曰：「先君之友，惟公为最厚，宜得铭以葬」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206855_comment'></div>予虽不能铭，义不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206855_comment'></div>乃论次其平生历官行治之大节而铭之，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1206855'>允矣吴侯，猎德在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206855_comment'></div>閟弗大施，而卒于穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206855_comment'></div>其施惟何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206855_comment'></div>二邑之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206855_comment'></div>泽卑不流，乃止于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206855_comment'></div>其存不朽，有晔其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206855_comment'></div>铭昭于幽，以诏后人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_61_1206855_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年12月14日</a>　十二月十四日赴宗博任。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d81816f8a89f4427923bc1192b88df18_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d81816f8a89f4427923bc1192b88df18");'><span id='d81816f8a89f4427923bc1192b88df18_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: -----end

id='poem_sentence_2_130280_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_130281' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_130281' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/130281?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_130282'>过檐赫日昼如燔，睡转庭阴始一反。<div id='poem_sentence_0_130282_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_130282'>纵有诸人来问疾，毗耶居士已忘言。<div id='poem_sentence_1_130282_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_130282'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_130282_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　在应天府。有书答瓘书。作品：答陈莹中  其六。答陈莹中  其七。答陈莹中  其八。<div id='poem_1206562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答陈莹中书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206562")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206562'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206562'>《孟子》之书，世儒未尝深考之，故尊之者或过其实，疑之者或损其真，非灼知圣贤之心，未易以私意论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206562_comment'></div>世之尊孟子者多失其传，非孟子过也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206562_comment'></div>而遂疑之，亦过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206562_comment'></div>近见一书，力诋孟子之非，恐非有所授，难遽以口舌争也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206562_comment'></div>无由展奉，一尽区区。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1206562_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206563' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206563' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206563?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206563_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206563'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206563'>德齿之说，前书尽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206563_comment'></div>重蒙以《师说》见谕，三复来贶，益用惭惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206563_comment'></div>古之人，其道足以师世范俗，惟孔孟足以当之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206563_comment'></div>东汉而下，师道益严，然稽其所知所行，皆不足以胜其任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206563_comment'></div>唐之韩愈固尝欲以师道自居矣，其视李翱、张籍辈皆谓「从吾游」，今翱、籍之文具在，考其言，未尝以弟子自列，则师果可好为乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206563_comment'></div>苟其道未足以达材成德，则虽欲为之，而人不与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206563_comment'></div>愈且如是，况其下者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206563_comment'></div>某愚陋，齿发已衰矣，而未有闻焉，盖孔子所谓不足畏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206563_comment'></div>方且拘縻升斗之禄，未能从黑发之士以承教左右，而反以见谓，是岂当然乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206563_comment'></div>非公乐与人为善，务欲搜扬隐伏，何以有此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206563_comment'></div>将使清和之士，不终为西山之饿夫、东国之黜臣，盖古圣贤之用心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206563_comment'></div>第恐说之不当，徒有累于高明耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206563_comment'></div>幸亮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206563_comment'></div>临纸愧汗，言不能究。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1206563_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206564' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206564' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206564?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206564_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206564'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206564'>《先天图》得太极所生自然数，非人私智所能为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206564_comment'></div>昔未尝见，幸得一观，此非尧夫不能知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206564_comment'></div>蒙示《法养观》，与相见乎离，辞异旨同，开发蔽陋多矣，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206564_comment'></div>世之昧者妄以狂瞽无稽之言眩瞀学者，方自以为得，恶足与论此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206564_comment'></div>然杜顺集此，不涉《华严》一字，束以二门，谓足以贯六经之旨，可谓能说约矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206564_comment'></div>然不知二门者于经何施也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206564_comment'></div>愿更开示，以警未悟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206564_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年3月</a>　在应天府。磨勘转承议郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年3月19日</a>　在应天府。罢宗子博士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　在应天府。有文。作品：陈君玉墓志铭。<div id='poem_1206856' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206856' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206856?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈君玉墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206856")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206856_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206856'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206856'>大观三年岁在己丑二月乙酉，居士陈君卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206856_comment'></div>越明年，其嗣孤经德不远数千里状其行，走仆来睢阳，乞铭于予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206856_comment'></div>予虽未尝知君也，而与其二子游厚善，今不远数千里来请铭，义何可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206856_comment'></div>乃为之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206856_comment'></div>君讳某，字君玉，温州平阳人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206856_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，祖讳某，以好学笃行称于州里，父讳某，皆隐德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206856_comment'></div>君为人刚果有远志，迪诸子以学，资其费不吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206856_comment'></div>其遇人乐易，无疏戚之间，宾至必为具尽欢乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206856_comment'></div>人有善，虽小伎，称之若不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206856_comment'></div>周人之急，不责报，务尽其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206856_comment'></div>虽轑橐扫庾，不为后日计留也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206856_comment'></div>里俗尚鬼而信巫，有以疠疫死者，必累月乃敢发丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206856_comment'></div>君之母夫人亡，举族献疑，欲从俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206856_comment'></div>君独曰：「吾宁死耳，奚忍为是耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206856_comment'></div>其至诚不惑，盖天性也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206856_comment'></div>疾已革，召诸子而戒之曰：「汝等慎无析居，为鄙俗常态」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206856_comment'></div>义方之训，死犹不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206856_comment'></div>非笃于为善，何以臻此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206856_comment'></div>君喜佛学，而不为求福田利益事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206856_comment'></div>将属纩，所亲有为浮屠氏者，泣涕问所欲，对曰：「庭前柏树子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206856_comment'></div>复问，乃曰：「已在言前」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206856_comment'></div>则君于死生之际，可谓安矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206856_comment'></div>享年五十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206856_comment'></div>娶缪氏，先君十四年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206856_comment'></div>子男四人，经德、经邦、经辨，皆业儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206856_comment'></div>女四人：长适缪氏，次适季氏，次适张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206856_comment'></div>其季皆早夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206856_comment'></div>某月某日，葬君于乐溪大岭之原，与其室缪氏同穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206856_comment'></div>君既没，而经邦始以上舍赐第，人皆以君不及见为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206856_comment'></div>而君于死生之际，犹不累其心，况其他乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206856_comment'></div>然积善之报，其后也必大，可不占而知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206856_comment'></div>故系之诗曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1206856'>天之于人不可求，服田力穑乃有秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206856_comment'></div>君乎有子皆珍璆，韫匮待价千金酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206856_comment'></div>乐溪之原蔚松楸，君其无憾安此丘！</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1206856_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年4月5日</a>　往开封。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='57826055fd1d4a42b158c89516b27931_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("57826055fd1d4a42b158c89516b27931");'><span id='57826055fd1d4a42b158c89516b27931_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>，60岁</div><div id='57826055fd1d4a42b158c89516b27931' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年2月3日</a>　到应天府。见刘安世。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年2月4日</a>　在应天府。刘安世见访。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年2月8日</a>　在应天府。赴器之饭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年2月9日</a>　在应天府。别器之。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ecd682cc324f426d86d777d8fb41a4c2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ecd682cc324f426d86d777d8fb41a4c2");'><span id='ecd682cc324f426d86d777d8fb41a4c2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>，75岁</div><div id='ecd682cc324f426d86d777d8fb41a4c2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年7月15日</a>　令赴行在。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年7月21日</a>　在应天府。以疾辞免，不允。作品：辞免召赴行在奏状。<div id='poem_1206464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免召赴行在状</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎元年七月二十一日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206464")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206464'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206464'>右，臣准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，令臣乘递马疾速发来赴行在者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206464_comment'></div>切念臣昨蒙渊圣皇帝误恩，自谏省迁给事中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206464_comment'></div>臣以衰老，久患腰膝，乘骑不便，累表恳辞补外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206464_comment'></div>蒙恩得请除待制、提举嵩山崇福宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206464_comment'></div>未及一年，伏遇皇帝陛下嗣登宝位，在臣子之分，义当入觐，况蒙促召，敢不奔走奉命？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206464_comment'></div>缘臣实以痼疾如旧，乘骑未得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206464_comment'></div>伏望圣慈矜察，许臣免赴行在，臣见已乘舡起发前去楚泗间，听候指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206464_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年7月25日</a>　在应天府。有奏状。作品：申省状。<div id='poem_1206465' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206465' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206465?labeling=true' target='_blank'>〔附〕申省状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年7月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206465")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206465_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206465'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206465'>右，某先于七月十五日准尚书省劄子，令乘骑赴行在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206465_comment'></div>某昨蒙渊圣皇帝误恩除给事中，某以久患腰膝，乘骑不便，累表恳辞得请，除待制、提举西京嵩山崇福宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206465_comment'></div>主上即位，复蒙睿旨召赴行在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206465_comment'></div>某为旧疾未安，寻具前项因依，七月二十一日自常州附递奏闻辞免，不敢居家，坐待朝旨，仍一面乘船自去楚、泗州听候指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206465_comment'></div>今已到楚州日久，未蒙指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206465_comment'></div>切念某犬马之齿七十有五，加以痼疾间作，拜履俱艰，不任朝谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206465_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省，伏乞检会前奏施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206465_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e140e29e0da5409d867bc5c5336c31eb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e140e29e0da5409d867bc5c5336c31eb");'><span id='e140e29e0da5409d867bc5c5336c31eb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>，47岁</div><div id='e140e29e0da5409d867bc5c5336c31eb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年10月3日</a>　十月三日，至苏州，谒李思和。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='abab298f7ad1457ba22a61a577f25a95_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("abab298f7ad1457ba22a61a577f25a95");'><span id='abab298f7ad1457ba22a61a577f25a95_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1115')">1114-1115年</a>，62-63岁</div><div id='abab298f7ad1457ba22a61a577f25a95' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年11月6日</a>　由余杭徙居毗陵（江苏常州），过吴江，有跋文。作品：跋贺方回鉴湖集。<div id='poem_1206662' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206662' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206662?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋贺方回鉴湖集</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年11月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206662")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206662_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206662'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206662'>元丰末年，予始筮仕，与方回俱在彭城为同僚友，自彭城一别，声迹不相闻，盖三十年馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206662_comment'></div>政和甲午秋八月，予还自京师，过平江，谒方回，披腹道旧，相视惘然，如昨梦耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206662_comment'></div>方回之诗，予见之旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206662_comment'></div>复出《鉴湖集》示予，其托物引类，辞义清远，不见雕绘之迹，浑然天成，殆非前日诗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206662_comment'></div>方回自少有奇才，若仪、秦之辩，良平之画，皆其胸中餍饫者，意谓其功名可必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206662_comment'></div>世变屡更，流落州郡不少振，岂诗真能穷人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206662_comment'></div>然方回诗益工，名日益高，足以传不朽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206662_comment'></div>与世之酣豢富贵与草木同腐者，岂可同日议哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206662_comment'></div>以此易彼，亦可自释也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206662_comment'></div>是年冬十有一月癸未，自馀杭徙居毗陵，道过吴江，舟中书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1206662_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年12月</a>　在毗陵，作《中庸序》作品：中庸义序。<div id='poem_1206646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中庸义序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206646")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206646'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206646'>伊川先生有言曰：「不偏之谓中，不易之谓庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206646_comment'></div>中者天下之正道，庸者天下之定理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206646_comment'></div>《中庸》之书，盖圣学之渊源，入德之大方也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206646_comment'></div>孔子殁，群弟子离散，分处诸侯之国，虽各以其所闻授弟子，然得其传者盖寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206646_comment'></div>故子贡之后有田子方，子方之后为庄周，则其去本浸远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206646_comment'></div>独曾子之后，子思、孟子之传得其宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206646_comment'></div>子思之学，《中庸》是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206646_comment'></div>孟子之书，其源盖出于此，则道学之传，有是书而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206646_comment'></div>世儒之尊孟氏，而于《中庸》之书未有能尽心者，则其源流可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206646_comment'></div>予昔在元丰中，尝受学明道先生之门，得其绪言一二，未及卒业而先生殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206646_comment'></div>继又从伊川先生，未几先生复以罪流窜涪陵，其立言垂训，为世大禁，学者胶口无敢复道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206646_comment'></div>政和四年夏六月，予得请祠馆，退居馀杭，杜门却扫，因得温寻旧学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206646_comment'></div>悼斯文之将坠，于是追述先生之遗训，著为此书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206646_comment'></div>以其所闻，推其所未闻者，虽未足尽传先生之奥，亦妄意其庶几焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206646_comment'></div>学者因吾言而求之于圣学之门墙，庶乎可窥而入也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206646_comment'></div>《杨龟山先生集》卷二五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206646_comment'></div>又见《国朝二百家名贤文粹》卷一五一，《经义考》卷一五一。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1206646_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在毗陵，作《校正伊川易传后序》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在毗陵。是年有文。作品：问邹侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年3月8日</a>　在毗陵。三月初八，孙云生曾孙礼。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8ee4e774cfd84d338d2dd97ba7edb198_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8ee4e774cfd84d338d2dd97ba7edb198");'><span id='8ee4e774cfd84d338d2dd97ba7edb198_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1122')">1115-1122年</a>，63-70岁</div><div id='8ee4e774cfd84d338d2dd97ba7edb198' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年11月</a>　还毗陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　在毗陵，作文。作品：许德占墓志铭。校正伊川易传后序。<div id='poem_1206858' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206858' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206858?labeling=true' target='_blank'>许德占墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206858")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206858_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206858'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206858'>政和五年春二月戊辰，居士许君卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206858_comment'></div>越三月癸酉，葬于晋陵万安西乡之原，与其先夫人同域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206858_comment'></div>是时予方归省松楸，其子知微不远数千里以书来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206858_comment'></div>岁十一月，予至自延平，知微复踵门而告曰：「先君潜德隐行，足以贻范后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206858_comment'></div>诸孤奉承，罔敢失坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206858_comment'></div>惟是幽堂之铭，所以撰德纪善，发扬幽光，而无词以刻，大惧泯没无称，以为亲羞，重诸孤之罪，敢以是请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206858_comment'></div>予来居毗陵久，窃谓君一乡必有一乡之善士，访求之，得君之行治为详，又与其子知微游，其何可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206858_comment'></div>君讳𪻑，字德占。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206858_comment'></div>生而有至性纯行，未十岁丧其怙恃，哀毁如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206858_comment'></div>家素丰美，而君独澹然，不以一毫置其胸中，其所取仅足而已，不为多寡计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206858_comment'></div>约于自奉，而急人之急，不翅如在己者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206858_comment'></div>虽里巷疏逖之人，昏丧之不能具，疾病之无医，必悉力周之，至倒廪倾囷不吝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206858_comment'></div>娶李氏，有贤行，作配无违德，先二十三年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206858_comment'></div>生子四人：长曰知微，处州缙云县丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206858_comment'></div>次曰知彰，太学内舍生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206858_comment'></div>曰知柔，早夭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206858_comment'></div>季曰知刚，处州贡士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206858_comment'></div>三女：长适进士李敦复，次适承奉郎、应天府宋城县丞晏躬行，次蚤卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206858_comment'></div>孙男三人：曰秝，曰𥟱，曰栎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206858_comment'></div>女三人皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206858_comment'></div>平居励诸子以学，曰：「士知为己而已，须以发策决科以誇耀流俗，非吾志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206858_comment'></div>初丧其夫人，年尚壮，即屏居于外，不复以世累撄拂其心，日味佛老之书以自颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206858_comment'></div>萧然一室，虽家人有经日不见其面者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206858_comment'></div>非静定，讵能尔乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206858_comment'></div>自缙云得疾，其子沿檄奉君以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206858_comment'></div>已而疾少瘳，忽一夜向晨，顾谓侍子曰：「今何时」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206858_comment'></div>曰「鸡鸣矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206858_comment'></div>遂命扶起，正其四体，反席而没，享年五十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206858_comment'></div>君为人貌温而气和，喜怒未尝形于色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206858_comment'></div>清慎寡欲，恂恂惟谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206858_comment'></div>辑睦中外，必尽诚意，故其存也无间言，其没也吊哭尽哀焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206858_comment'></div>惟许氏之先曰坚者，有卓行，浮沉庐阜、九华之间，初不知其何许人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206858_comment'></div>至君之高祖正显，始自江宁徙居常州之晋陵，故今为晋陵人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206858_comment'></div>结庐东山之阿，与孙氏比居友善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206858_comment'></div>未几夫妇俱亡，而君之曾大父怀素尚幼，孙氏收鞠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206858_comment'></div>其后族人自江宁来访坚之后者，携而往，孙氏匿不以告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206858_comment'></div>比其长，以其子妻之，且告之曰：「高人之后宜蕃衍，必有大其门者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206858_comment'></div>并其资付之而去，卒莫知所之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206858_comment'></div>孙氏亡其名，殆坚之徒欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206858_comment'></div>怀素生延福，延福生亿，君其季子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206858_comment'></div>唐亡，更五季之乱，衣冠旧族流离散徙，虽名卿大夫有不知其所从出者，况坚之与世相忘乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206858_comment'></div>自坚至正显，谱系中绝，其世次莫可考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206858_comment'></div>然邦人至今以君之居为许坚家云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206858_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1206858'>坚有卓行，其存不亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206858_comment'></div>展矣斯人，于坚有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206858_comment'></div>无坠前修，必大其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206858_comment'></div>德人之言，以诏后昆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1206858_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>校正伊川易传后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206647")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206647'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206647'>伊川先生著《易传》，方草具，未及成书，而先生得疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206647_comment'></div>将启手足，以其书授门人张绎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206647_comment'></div>未几而绎卒，故其书散亡，学者所传无善本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206647_comment'></div>政和之初，予友谢显道得其书于京师示予，而错乱重复，几不可读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206647_comment'></div>东归待次毗陵，乃始校定，去其重复，逾年而始完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206647_comment'></div>先生道学足为世师，而于《易》尤尽心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206647_comment'></div>其微辞妙旨，盖有书不能传者，恨得其书晚，不及亲受旨训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206647_comment'></div>其谬误有疑而未达者，姑存之，以俟知者，不敢辄加损也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206647_comment'></div>然学者读其书，得其意，忘言可也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1206647_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　在毗陵。作文。作品：孙先生春秋传序。答吕居仁（其一)答吕居仁（其二 )答吕居仁（其三)答吕居仁（其四)跋蔡襄自书诗帖。<div id='poem_1206648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206648?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙先生春秋传序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206648")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206648_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206648'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206648'>孟子曰：「王者之迹熄而《诗》亡，《诗》亡然后《春秋》作」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206648_comment'></div>春秋之时，《诗》非尽亡也，《黍离》降而为《国风》，则王者之诗亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206648_comment'></div>王者之诗亡，则《雅》不作，而天下无政矣，《春秋》所为作也，故曰《春秋》天子之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206648_comment'></div>孔子没，更秦燔书，微言中绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206648_comment'></div>汉兴，诸儒守专门之学，互相疵病，至父子有异同之论，况馀人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206648_comment'></div>然自昔通儒达识，未有不由此而学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206648_comment'></div>熙宁之初，崇儒尊经，训迪多士，以谓三《传》异同，无所考正，于六经尤为难知，故《春秋》不列于学官，非废而不用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206648_comment'></div>而士方急于科举之习，遂阙而不讲，可胜惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206648_comment'></div>高邮中丞孙公先生以其餍馀，尽发圣人之蕴，著为成书，以传后学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206648_comment'></div>其微辞妙旨，多先儒之所未言者，启其关键，使学者以稽其门，叩其户，以窥堂奥，岂曰小补之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206648_comment'></div>余得而伏读之，不能释手，闻所未闻多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206648_comment'></div>而其孙广伯乃以其书属余为序，以予之浅陋，使得挂名经端，自托不腐，岂不幸矣哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206648_comment'></div>然承命以来，于兹有年矣，而不敢措笔于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206648_comment'></div>窃谓先生以宗工钜儒，世所师仰，虽片言寸简皆足以垂世传后，况其成书耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206648_comment'></div>晚学后进，妄以芜辞污镘之，非惟不足以为重，乃退之所谓言之适有累于高明也，故绝意不敢为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206648_comment'></div>而广伯之请益至，乃勉为之书其后，庶乎如古之附骥尾者，后之览者矜其意而勿诮焉可也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1206648_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206591' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206591' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206591?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答吕居仁书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206591")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206591_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206591'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206591'>承示《问学》一篇，博究先儒异同之论，益知好学之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206591_comment'></div>然其间与鄙意不合者，敢不以告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206591_comment'></div>扬子湍水之说，荀子杞柳之说也，其论极善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206591_comment'></div>孟子七篇之书，其要道性善而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206591_comment'></div>湍水之说，孟子固尝辨之，不可与性善混为一说明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206591_comment'></div>而论者欲一之，皆未究其所以也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206591_comment'></div>孔子曰「性相近也，习相远也」，「惟上智与下愚不移」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206591_comment'></div>言相近，则不可谓一，孟子论白羽之白与白雪之白是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206591_comment'></div>惟相近，故以习而相远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206591_comment'></div>若叔鱼之生，其母视之，知其必以贿死，若此类，是生而恶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206591_comment'></div>文王在母也，母不忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206591_comment'></div>既生也，傅不勤；<div class='inline'
