id='poem_sentence_11_1206591_comment'></div>既学也，师不烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206591_comment'></div>若此类，是生而善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206591_comment'></div>韩子不究其所以然，遂列为三品，则失之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206591_comment'></div>是数说，要之皆原于性善，然后为得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206591_comment'></div>横渠曰：「形而后有气质之性善；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206591_comment'></div>反之，则天地之性存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206591_comment'></div>故气质之性，君子有弗性者焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206591_comment'></div>又曰：「德不胜气，性命于气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206591_comment'></div>德胜其气，性命于德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206591_comment'></div>斯言尽之，更当深考之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206591_comment'></div>《中庸》曰：「反身不诚，不顺乎亲矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206591_comment'></div>诚身有道，不明乎善，不诚乎身矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206591_comment'></div>《大学》曰：「欲诚其意，先致其知，致知在格物」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206591_comment'></div>盖致知乃能明善，不致其知而能明善，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206591_comment'></div>此不须分为二说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206591_comment'></div>孔子曰：「学而不思则罔，思而不学则殆」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206591_comment'></div>孔子论学与思如此，既曰「学以成行」，又曰「学也者，受之性而发于文字言语者也」，斯言似不相应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206591_comment'></div>世儒之病，正在以言语文字为学，不可不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206591_comment'></div>浅陋妄意如此，高明试一思之如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206591_comment'></div>两日大暑，去人候书，挥汗作此，辞不逮意，幸亮之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1206591_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206592' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206592' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206592?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年2月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206592_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206592'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206592'>辱问所疑，皆非浅陋所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206592_comment'></div>然厚意不可虚辱，辄试言之，请自择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206592_comment'></div>夫守一之谓敬，无适之谓一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206592_comment'></div>敬足以直内而已，发之于外，则未能时措之宜也，故必有义以方外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206592_comment'></div>毋我者，不任我也，若舜舍己从人之类是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206592_comment'></div>四者各有所施，故兼言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206592_comment'></div>道固与我为一也，非至于从心所欲不踰矩者，不足以与此，言志于道、依于仁，固无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206592_comment'></div>《中庸》曰：「道不远人，人之为道而远人，不可以为道」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206592_comment'></div>道固不可为也，然不示之以入德之方，则是以圣人望人，不容进学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206592_comment'></div>故卒曰：「忠恕违道不远，施诸己而不愿，亦勿施于人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206592_comment'></div>勿施于人，忠恕之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206592_comment'></div>由是而求之，道不远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206592_comment'></div>孔子曰：「若圣与仁，则吾岂敢」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206592_comment'></div>然非圣人则不足以尽仁，而仁特未化而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206592_comment'></div>管仲之仁，盖称其功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206592_comment'></div>利贞者，言《乾》之性情也，《易传》可以究观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206592_comment'></div>夫在心为志，发言为诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206592_comment'></div>诗特发于言者，故于动天地，感鬼神，言近而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206592_comment'></div>来人立候书，匆匆作此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1206592_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206593?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年2月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206593'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206593'>承问格物，向答李君书尝道其略矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206593_comment'></div>六经之微言，天下之至赜存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206593_comment'></div>古人多识鸟兽草木之名，岂徒识其名哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206593_comment'></div>深探而力求之，皆格物之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206593_comment'></div>夫学者必以孔孟为师，学而不求诸孔孟之言，则末矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206593_comment'></div>《易》曰：「君子多识前言往行，以畜其德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206593_comment'></div>孟子曰：「博学而详说之，将以反说约也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206593_comment'></div>世之学者欲以彫绘组织为工，誇多斗靡，以资见闻而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206593_comment'></div>故摭其华不茹其实，未尝畜德而反约也，彼亦焉用学为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206593_comment'></div>某老矣，虽有志焉，而力不逮，区区有望于左右者，正在此而不在彼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206593_comment'></div>勉之勉之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1206593_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206685' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206685' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206685?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋蔡襄自书诗帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206685")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206685_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206685'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206685'>端明蔡公诗稿，云此一篇极有古人风格者，欧阳文忠公所题也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206685_comment'></div>二公齐名一时，其文章皆足以垂世传后，端明又以翰墨擅天下，片言寸简落笔，人争藏之以为宝玩，况盈轴之多，而兼有二公之手泽乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206685_comment'></div>览之弥日，不能释手，因书于其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206685_comment'></div>政和丙申夏四月癸未，延平杨时书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206685_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年2月</a>　在毗陵。除提点成都府国宁观。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　在毗陵。作文。作品：跋邹道乡所书女诫。张牧之子名。<div id='poem_1206663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋邹道乡所书女诫</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206663")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206663'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206663'>古者大夫以上，子生，立三母，必求其宽裕慈惠、温良恭慎而寡言者为之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206663_comment'></div>女子十年不出，教之婉娩听从，执<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1206663", 1206663, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>麻枲</span>，治丝茧，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1206663", 1206663, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>织纴</span>组紃，学女事，以共衣服；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206663_comment'></div>观于祭祀，纳酒浆、笾豆、菹醢，礼相助奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206663_comment'></div>闺门之内，朝夕之所习闻者，惟是而已，不见异物而迁焉，故德言容功不待异禀而能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206663_comment'></div>礼废千有馀年，士且不知师，而况于女子乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206663_comment'></div>故膏粱之族，酣豢逸放于幽閒之中，而涂歌巷语、淫亵不可读者日积于耳目，其不沦胥而散者幸而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206663_comment'></div>毗陵张氏世有显人，其子孙皆高才远识，绝出伦辈，今见其人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206663_comment'></div>牧之间出道乡所书《女诫》示予，极称其稚子之贤，益知张氏之刑家贻后者其流未艾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206663_comment'></div>以圭璋之质，又得良工切磨之，其成岂易量哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206663_comment'></div>道乡盛德之士也，言动足以经世范俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206663_comment'></div>其所书不特有补于张氏而已，后必有因斯文以兴起者，其于世教岂小补哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1206663_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206823' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206823' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206823?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张牧之子名</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206823")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206823_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206823'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206823'>张氏世有清德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206823_comment'></div>由圣得子，求名于侍讲吕公原明，而名之曰清孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206823_comment'></div>夫伯夷，圣之清者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206823_comment'></div>推恶恶之心，思与乡人立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206823_comment'></div>其冠不正，望望然而去之，若将浼焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206823_comment'></div>故其流风之弊，容德不足，而至于隘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206823_comment'></div>今牧之得子而求名于予，请名曰容孙，盖将以济其世德也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206823_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　在毗陵。罗从彦从学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　在毗陵。作文。作品：养浩堂记。<div id='poem_1206841' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206841?labeling=true' target='_blank'>养浩堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206841")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206841_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206841'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206841'>建城之东有寺曰开元，负山之阿，下临清流之渊，林壑茂密，望之隐然若鳌戴而出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206841_comment'></div>吾友翁行简昔尝燕休其中，而以「养浩」名其所居之堂，属予为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206841_comment'></div>予尝论养气之道，以谓体、心、气、神，人之所同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206841_comment'></div>四者合于无，则天地与我其一乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206841_comment'></div>夫天地，其体也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206841_comment'></div>气，体之充也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206841_comment'></div>养而无害，则塞乎天地之间，理固然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206841_comment'></div>古之人负耒鼓刀而不为污，任天下之重而不为泰，临之以斧钺而不吾惴，岂其心独有异于人乎哉，所养素定故耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206841_comment'></div>行简自少知名于时，而流落场屋，晚而后中第，人固意其颓堕而不自振也，而其行益修，气益完，文日益工，莅官临政无细大，迎刃立解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206841_comment'></div>此其所养，岂易量哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206841_comment'></div>吾知其才必为世用也，今见其兆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206841_comment'></div>异时推其所养而羽仪于朝，必有可观者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206841_comment'></div>故予承命不辞，而喜为之道也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206841_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年6月</a>　在毗陵。磨勘转朝散郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年10月</a>　在毗陵。作文。作品：杨氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1206859' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206859' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206859?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和元年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206859")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206859_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206859'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206859'>陈涛子通将葬其母夫人，不远千里以书属予铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206859_comment'></div>子通，予之外兄弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206859_comment'></div>吾母与其父京，皆居士讳选之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206859_comment'></div>居士，予昔为之传者，盖隐德君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206859_comment'></div>其夫妇俱蚤世，吾母与其兄少孤，友爱异甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206859_comment'></div>其为人严恭俨恪，不妄嬉笑，静慎有父风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206859_comment'></div>夫人尊事之，每顺适其意，无少忤者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206859_comment'></div>比其亡，而予尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206859_comment'></div>夫人抚存之，视犹子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206859_comment'></div>今欲志其墓，舍予其谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206859_comment'></div>宜乃叙而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206859_comment'></div>夫人杨氏，将乐人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206859_comment'></div>祖讳思，父讳苗，世为田家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206859_comment'></div>夫人年十六归于陈氏，其事舅姑以孝闻，事其夫尽妇顺，晨昏奉甘旨，必身亲之，不少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206859_comment'></div>辑睦中外，无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206859_comment'></div>夫亡，励其子以学，卒克有立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206859_comment'></div>宣和元年六月十七日以疾终于正寝，享年八十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206859_comment'></div>子男二人：长曰渤，次曰涛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206859_comment'></div>女二人：长适进士黄宁，与长子皆先夫人卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206859_comment'></div>次适进士孙升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206859_comment'></div>孙三人：曰致柔，曰致虚，曰宗虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206859_comment'></div>女孙一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206859_comment'></div>以是年十月九日葬于城南阳坑之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206859_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1206859'>富而寿，福所先兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206859_comment'></div>攸好德，力足贤兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206859_comment'></div>志诸幽，永弗谖兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1206859_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　在毗陵，提点国宁观。作文。作品：沈夫人墓志铭。梁明道墓志铭。范君墓碣。<div id='poem_1206880' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206880' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206880?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沈夫人墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和二年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206880")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206880_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206880'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206880'>夫人沈氏，其先尝仕吴越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206880_comment'></div>父充，将作监主簿，母费氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206880_comment'></div>夫人生有淑质，及笄明慧绝人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206880_comment'></div>时邹公随父官历阳，遂以归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206880_comment'></div>公历官维扬、襄、颍间，士有不远千里鼓箧而至者，蹐门问道无虚席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206880_comment'></div>公辟馆居之，膳馐之事，取具于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206880_comment'></div>夫人区处之不少懈，病则躬为之粥药，故士得悉意于肄业，而忘其旅琐者，夫人之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206880_comment'></div>公以长育人才为己任，而夫人相之如此，非夫妇一德，能如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206880_comment'></div>元符中，以言事谪岭南，夫人侍其姑安康归毗陵，左右顺事之，无一不适其意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206880_comment'></div>迨建中初，公召还，登禁从，复以前事窜零陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206880_comment'></div>夫人欲留侍，安康谓曰：「前者儿远谪，汝不行，吾身则安矣，而心未尝宁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206880_comment'></div>今汝行，则吾无忧，是乃所以安吾心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206880_comment'></div>至零陵，席未及温，而公徙昭平，以夫人与两儿留零陵而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206880_comment'></div>远寄异土，门廷肃如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206880_comment'></div>夫人两经患难，其留也使其夫无将母之念，其行也安其姑无南顾之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206880_comment'></div>非躬尽妇道，畴克尔哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206880_comment'></div>公之亡，乡人赙之甚厚，其子柄欲归之，谓无以累先德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206880_comment'></div>夫人曰：「非汝所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206880_comment'></div>尔诸父皆贫空，受而推与之，使阖门无号寒啼饥之声闻于安康，不亦善乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206880_comment'></div>且赙赗，礼也，而吾无与焉，庸何伤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206880_comment'></div>故其子柄卒从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206880_comment'></div>昔司徒旅归四布，孔子可之而未善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206880_comment'></div>子硕既葬其母，欲以赙布之馀具祭器，子柳曰：「吾闻之也，君子不家于丧，请颁诸兄弟之贫者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206880_comment'></div>著在礼经，以为万世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206880_comment'></div>夫人之是举也，其合矣乎，非远识，庸有是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206880_comment'></div>宣和元年七月二十五日以疾卒，享年五十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206880_comment'></div>庚子年二月二十五日祔于公之墓右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206880_comment'></div>始以公恩封崇德县君，再封蓬莱县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206880_comment'></div>男二人，曰柄、曰栩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206880_comment'></div>柄以布衣召对，除承务郎、枢密院编脩，栩未仕，皆以学行世其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206880_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1206880'>幼施于内，维妇之常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206880_comment'></div>中外有闻，妇道之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206880_comment'></div>作配君子，一德靡悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206880_comment'></div>铭无溢辞，其永不坠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1206880_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206860' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206860' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206860?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梁明道墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和二年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206860")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206860_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206860'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206860'>政和八年七月戊戌，梁侯卒于其子昆山令之官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206860_comment'></div>越明年，其孤欲扶柩归于其乡，以宣和二年八月十六日葬于蛟湖山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206860_comment'></div>前期，自青龙走毗陵乞予铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206860_comment'></div>予，梁侯同邑也，虽未之识，而闻诸乡评得其行熟矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206860_comment'></div>今其子又请之勤，若是，义何可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206860_comment'></div>乃为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206860_comment'></div>梁侯讳伯臣，字明道，南剑州将乐人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206860_comment'></div>曾祖龚，祖筠，父世广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206860_comment'></div>明道资孝友，事其亲能尽力，抚诸弟无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206860_comment'></div>母夫人得末疾馀三十年，未尝斯须去其侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206860_comment'></div>晨兴奉盥馈，侍汤剂，必躬服其劳，终其身不懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206860_comment'></div>亲亡，哀毁几不胜丧，逾年乃能襄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206860_comment'></div>其遇人无疏戚，必尽诚意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206860_comment'></div>岁饥，有告急者，虽扫庾赈之不吝，后虽自窭，弗顾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206860_comment'></div>人有称贷，或负之弗偿，悉焚券不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206860_comment'></div>其胸中洞然无纤毫芥蒂，皆此类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206860_comment'></div>其姻家官于岭外，而夫妇俱丧，子尚幼，五女未有归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206860_comment'></div>明道曰：「吾可坐视之乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206860_comment'></div>乃命其子迎致之别馆，为办奁具，以次择士族归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206860_comment'></div>呜呼，末俗日益偷，虽天属之亲，迫穷祸患，盖有不相收者，况外姻乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206860_comment'></div>闻其风，可以少激矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206860_comment'></div>梁氏世有隐德，至明道始励子弟以学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206860_comment'></div>而其子泽民遂中上舍第，昆山之政有惠爱，明道阴相之力为多，故邑人欣戴之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206860_comment'></div>其病也，为之祈禳，几月无虚日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206860_comment'></div>其没也，哭之无不尽哀焉，其得人心盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206860_comment'></div>晚留心释氏，疾且革，问棺敛之具已备，遂安寝而逝，享年五十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206860_comment'></div>娶萧氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206860_comment'></div>有子男二人：长曰泽民，宣义郎，即昆山令也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206860_comment'></div>次曰俊民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206860_comment'></div>女一人，先五年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206860_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1206860'>积善之报，于后必蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206860_comment'></div>蛟湖之丘，其归永安。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1206860'></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1206860_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206879?labeling=true' target='_blank'>范君墓碣</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206879")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206879'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206879'>君讳某，字济美，姓范氏，建州建阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206879_comment'></div>曾祖某，祖某，父某，皆晦迹不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206879_comment'></div>君生而有异禀，自为提孩，识虑已有过人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206879_comment'></div>闽中地瘠而人贫，俗俭陋，常以不足为忧，多计产育子，虽士人不免者，浸而成风，恬不以为怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206879_comment'></div>君时五岁，闻之恻然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206879_comment'></div>适诸母有妊者，乃谓之曰：「他日所生，无问儿女，愿勿弃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206879_comment'></div>生子而弗举，人理不可为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206879_comment'></div>我长立，当鞠养之，不须以贫窭为念」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206879_comment'></div>其慈惠盖天性也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206879_comment'></div>六岁即读书，书过目辄成诵，日记数千言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206879_comment'></div>未成童，从师友肄业于郡庠，敝衣菲食，与贵游子弟居，不少屈以苟合，视膏粱文绣澹如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206879_comment'></div>厥父闻之喜曰：「吾有子矣，夫复何患」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206879_comment'></div>既冠，入太学，与之方轨并驰者皆一时豪士，然未能先之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206879_comment'></div>政和五年登进士第，授将仕郎，调河南府新安县尉，就除宿州教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206879_comment'></div>官制行，改迪功郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206879_comment'></div>君在学声名籍甚，宿之士人向风久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206879_comment'></div>既莅职，学者造门授经，朝暮踵相蹑，皆虚往而实归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206879_comment'></div>秩满，士争请留，不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206879_comment'></div>用荐者改从事郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206879_comment'></div>初，右丞薛公某常自负学有师承，为世儒宗，闻君名，以礼币延置门下，命诸子从游，间与之辨析疑义，虽逢其族，皆迎刃而解，由是薛公加敬畏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206879_comment'></div>自符离罢还，会薛公被旨编集荆公遗文，辟为检讨官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206879_comment'></div>仅逾月，以疾终于京师甘泉坊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206879_comment'></div>时宣和二年三月二十六日也，享年六十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206879_comment'></div>君为人夷易，不事表襮，胸中洞然无城府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206879_comment'></div>其事亲无违，交朋友有信，遇人无贤愚一以诚意，故中外无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206879_comment'></div>博闻彊记，诸子百氏之书无所不究，而歉然常自以为不足，虽晚暮而志学不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206879_comment'></div>初娶胡氏，故赠朝请大夫某之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206879_comment'></div>生二男：长曰某，从事郎、武安军节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206879_comment'></div>次某<span class='inlineComment2'>（缺）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1206879_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在毗陵。作文。作品：孙龙图墓志铭。<div id='poem_1206871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙龙图墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206871")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206871'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206871'>公讳谔，字正臣，邵武人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206871_comment'></div>崇宁中有旨改名，遂以字行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206871_comment'></div>曾祖讳昌龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206871_comment'></div>祖讳文准，左宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206871_comment'></div>父讳迪，太常博士，同提举两浙市易司，累赠通议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206871_comment'></div>公幼敏慧，读书数过辄成诵不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206871_comment'></div>既冠，登进士第，授池州司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206871_comment'></div>通议以公素谨厚，静默寡言笑，恐其不更事，而司法民命所属，不可忽，故令就学律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206871_comment'></div>明年试大法，中第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206871_comment'></div>是时舒王用事，中书置五房检正，遴柬天下贤才以济，公方筮仕，而以材名在选中，除监制敕库，制敕库用士人自公始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206871_comment'></div>未几除吏房习学公事，同编修中书条例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206871_comment'></div>同列皆极一时之选，其后列侍从、居要津者相属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206871_comment'></div>习学例一考即真，公未阅岁，丁通议忧去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206871_comment'></div>复除，会罢习学官，再监制敕库，仍多摄五房职事，因议司农法，驳其不当者，大臣力主之，公犹反覆论不已，忤其意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206871_comment'></div>又尝叱堂吏，语有所侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206871_comment'></div>大臣闻而疾之，造为讪上语以闻，赖神宗仁圣，察其无根，得不坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206871_comment'></div>会库吏编进条目漏常程劄子三道，公已自陈再进矣，大臣交诋之，出为睦州司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206871_comment'></div>公两为宰属，尝与国论矣，盖今尚书都司之任，侍臣之资也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206871_comment'></div>一旦屈于偏州下吏，人意其不事事，而亲吏牍，钩狱情，委曲周尽，略不见迁谪容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206871_comment'></div>烂卢酒户之仆乘醉督逋，殴欠者至死，引其主为之唱，主诬服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206871_comment'></div>邑上其狱为重辟首，公阅牍得其情，曰：「殴之日，主适外未还，安得有唱」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206871_comment'></div>即日释之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206871_comment'></div>青溪民有诉匿镪者，词已伏，而容色若有冤者，诘之，则曰：「托者饮我，出书云，已使人置镪于舟底。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206871_comment'></div>酒酣醉归卧舟中，比及城登岸，犹未醒，其家执书以索，而舟已出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206871_comment'></div>僦舟非有素，莫识为谁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206871_comment'></div>公为缓其狱，物色之，求僦舟者甚急，而舟人负镪来告，曰：「且我闻孙检正治狱不可欺，故以自归也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206871_comment'></div>睦人至画像祠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206871_comment'></div>元丰五年，复召为重修编敕所删定官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206871_comment'></div>书成论赏，就循一资，充详定省曹寺监条贯删定官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206871_comment'></div>三年改宣议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206871_comment'></div>元祐四年，监在京都进奏院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206871_comment'></div>六年迁左宣德郎，除太学博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206871_comment'></div>以大父母春秋高，乞就吏部，调通判建昌军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206871_comment'></div>将行，除太常博士，乃谒告归省而后就职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206871_comment'></div>王文公赐谥有定，一博士有欲为其文，极言推尊，自结于用事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206871_comment'></div>公当笔，辄推其次，盖事有近于追逐时好，以取世资，终不屑为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206871_comment'></div>绍圣元年，迁秘书省正字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206871_comment'></div>二年，权发遣梓州路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206871_comment'></div>八路差遣，例多狃袭拘碍，注拟不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206871_comment'></div>熙宁、元丰间许在任官前期一年射阙，每一官阙，则遍问属郡应入之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206871_comment'></div>其后前期射阙之法废，须罢任以到铨为先后之次，则人人身在铨所矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206871_comment'></div>而遍问之法犹存，往复待报，有弥年者，公私病之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206871_comment'></div>公建明季阙榜十日，非次及过满见阙五日，限满，如吏部法定差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206871_comment'></div>朝廷善之，仍颁其法，七路行焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206871_comment'></div>先是，泸南罗始党八姓生夷，自元丰中收服，团结为义军三千一营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206871_comment'></div>岁月浸久，其数著籍者皆名存而实不足，骤覈之必至于变故生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206871_comment'></div>公为建言朝廷，初以罗始党八姓依七姓、十九姓熟夷团结者，止欲羁縻远蕃，渐令习汉化耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206871_comment'></div>今夷情已安，则八姓前阙义军之数，可置勿问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206871_comment'></div>今而后遇有阙，因犒设夷首，使转相译问，以本族愿补者充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206871_comment'></div>从之，至今为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206871_comment'></div>三年迁承议郎，四年移成都府路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206871_comment'></div>成都为蜀剧郡，公裁处暇裕，而事细大毕集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206871_comment'></div>相度开兴助正盐井，建明差选职令条制，人情惬当，所奏皆可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206871_comment'></div>至于增置武宁诸军，般买眉戎岁米，皆长久之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206871_comment'></div>召为尚书刑部员外郎，辞不拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206871_comment'></div>改吏部员外郎，复恳辞，前后章六七，不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206871_comment'></div>既就职，赐对从容，请儒臣讨论官制而补完之，以成一代之典，追配《周官》，有旨条具以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206871_comment'></div>会言者擿公元祐辨诉，论罢职，出知南剑州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206871_comment'></div>未赴，遇上皇登极恩，迁朝奉郎，赐绯鱼袋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206871_comment'></div>召为司勋员外郎，迁朝散郎，除右司员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206871_comment'></div>靖国初，差点检皇太后园陵文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206871_comment'></div>还朝，除秘书少监，国子祭酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206871_comment'></div>崇宁改元，兼权秘书监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206871_comment'></div>中外期公朝夕且进用，而抗章力请补外，除直龙图阁、权发遣江淮荆浙等路制置发运副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206871_comment'></div>初，蔡太师京一见公奇之，为户部尚书，荐以自代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206871_comment'></div>及与政，欲以公为刑部侍郎，辞免曰：「某昔尝免刑部郎，今为侍郎，非所安」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206871_comment'></div>曰：「以为他曹何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206871_comment'></div>又辞曰：「异时闻从官阙，大臣有以某名进者，上未以为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206871_comment'></div>公秉政，宜慎所引，毋以不肖累君也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206871_comment'></div>太师意未已，会有传公趣与新政异者，遂罢发运，知润州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206871_comment'></div>未几得管勾杭州洞霄宫，公曰：「吾志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206871_comment'></div>大观元年迁朝请郎，二年以八宝恩迁朝奉大夫，洞霄再任恩，复请差提举舒州灵仙观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206871_comment'></div>一日盥栉更衣，谓家人曰：「生死去来，无足深悲，惟念佛不忘，是真吾眷属」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206871_comment'></div>言讫而瞑，实三年己丑七月二十一日也，享年五十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206871_comment'></div>是年十二月二十六日葬于兴化县善应乡颜村青龙冈之原，从治命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206871_comment'></div>母黄氏，再适游氏，封同安县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206871_comment'></div>公欲便亲闱，故卜居高邮，尽斥先世资产与诸弟，而俸馀稍稍买田筑室，为伏腊计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206871_comment'></div>多病早衰，常欲谢事，自屏物外，恐伤慈怀，故不果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206871_comment'></div>公天资夷旷，貌如其心，平居恂恂似不能言，一旦坐官府，胥吏纷纷持牒互进，公各使尽其意，徐以片言折之，群吏帖耳结舌，不敢出息，退而相语曰：「公神明也，不可欺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206871_comment'></div>乐善急义，重然诺，荐士每先寒素，不可干以私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206871_comment'></div>识虑精敏，多人意所未到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1206871_comment'></div>闲居七年，未尝以一字至公门，兀兀自守，泊如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1206871_comment'></div>妙洞心法，于佛书无所不观，手录要义皆成诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1206871_comment'></div>其屏声色，黜滋味，盖笃信而然，非彊绝之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1206871_comment'></div>常有疾，得异方，须鸲鹆，公素不杀，而厉物以卫生，不忍为也，故药久不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1206871_comment'></div>忽有鸷禽击死者堕庭中，公得而饵之，疾随愈，此殆神相，非人力可致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1206871_comment'></div>公于刑书中悉详尽，世之名知法者皆叹莫及，而朝廷欲以刑官处之，弗居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1206871_comment'></div>于阴阳星历之学皆精到，而未尝一言及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1206871_comment'></div>异时尝苦天官历火、木二星及蚀时刻多不合，与姚舜辅所撰历互有疏密，委官考详，前后有异，秘书不能决，有旨命公校之，其说遂定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1206871_comment'></div>九宫贵神坛位失次，悉釐正之，皆因事而见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1206871_comment'></div>盖公以儒学自将，该洽有文，而以法家术数名世，非其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1206871_comment'></div>有奏议、解经、杂著、文集四十卷藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1206871_comment'></div>前娶刘氏，追封真定县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1206871_comment'></div>今夫人刘氏，赠太中大夫处约之女，孝谨冲淡，克配君子，封靖安县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1206871_comment'></div>男二人：长曰钜，假将仕郎，蚤卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1206871_comment'></div>次曰镇，修职郎，今为池州司兵曹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1206871_comment'></div>女一人，适文林郎、洪州司兵曹事游撝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1206871_comment'></div>靖国郊祀当任子，引旧比荐其弟诫，有司持元丰法不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1206871_comment'></div>后六年宗祀，卒以诫为请，今为奉议郎、知庐州慎县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1206871_comment'></div>公既没十有三年，其弟诫始以游公状来请铭，乃为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_99_1206871'>一德不回，践更三世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1206871_comment'></div>不附于时，其节靡悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1206871_comment'></div>不杀之诫，诚通于幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1206871_comment'></div>有陨其庭，疾已随瘳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1206871_comment'></div>刑名星历，详尽精到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1206871_comment'></div>法家者流，非志所好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1206871_comment'></div>公之神明，其德可钦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1206871_comment'></div>百世不朽，勒歌于珉。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_106_1206871'></div><div id='poem_sentence_106_1206871_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在毗陵。胡铨来见，杨时劝其勤学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在毗陵，任秘书郎。作文。作品：李修撰墓志铭。令人吴氏墓志铭。祭陈莹中。<div id='poem_1206862' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206862' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206862?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李修撰墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206862")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206862_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206862'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206862'>宣和三年闰五月二十有七日，中大夫、右文殿修撰、陇西县开国男、食邑三百户李公以疾终于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206862_comment'></div>岁八月二十有八日，葬于常州无锡县开元乡湛岘之原，与其夫人吴氏同穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206862_comment'></div>越明年，其孤以晋陵邹柄状来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206862_comment'></div>余与公俱闽人，又尝同为诸生，肄业于上庠，挟策考疑，时相从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206862_comment'></div>俯仰四十馀年，一时朋游凋丧略尽，与公有平生之旧，而知公之详，盖无遗矣，宜其有请于余也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206862_comment'></div>余虽不能铭，其何可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206862_comment'></div>公讳夔，字斯和，其先江南人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206862_comment'></div>唐末避乱，徙家邵武，故今为邵武人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206862_comment'></div>曾祖讳待，仕闽以武力显，闽亡，退处田野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206862_comment'></div>祖讳僧护，考讳赓，皆隐德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206862_comment'></div>考以公贵，累赠正议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206862_comment'></div>妣黄氏，资政殿大学士履之姊，累赠高平郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206862_comment'></div>继妣饶氏，累赠广平郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206862_comment'></div>皆改赠太硕人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206862_comment'></div>公幼孤，鞠于外家，成童犹未知书，而颖悟绝人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206862_comment'></div>舅氏大资政黄公擢第归，一见器之，使赋诗，有惊人语，因授以书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206862_comment'></div>凡耳濡目染，过即成诵，至日数千言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206862_comment'></div>自是于六经诸子百氏之书，下至毛郑笺传，期年之间，无所不窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206862_comment'></div>学日进，文日益有名，从黄公游者，咸推先焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206862_comment'></div>是时朝廷方以经术造士，公声闻籍甚，所至学者景从，赢粮重趼，越百舍而至者，常相蹑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206862_comment'></div>逮居上庠，所交皆一时知名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206862_comment'></div>初补监生，洎选内舍，皆第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206862_comment'></div>龚公原得其文读之，叹曰：「此必山林幽栖笃学之士所为，今之学者莫能为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206862_comment'></div>其后预天府荐，及试南省，皆第二，遂中元丰三年进士第，释褐调秀州华亭尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206862_comment'></div>邑令所为多不法，公每规正之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206862_comment'></div>部使者欲有所按治，声言行邑，公迓之境上，则以温言慰荐，且询令所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206862_comment'></div>公力庇之，不以言，部使者不悦，正色复询之丞簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206862_comment'></div>丞簿与令素不协，则互讦所短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206862_comment'></div>而令初不知公庇之也，亦言公尝以私故不过厅，于是部使者以公为长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206862_comment'></div>已而考覈之，三人者皆以罪去，而公独无累，人以是知公之器度为未易量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206862_comment'></div>丁继母饶氏太硕人忧，服除，调建州松溪县尉兼主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206862_comment'></div>秩满，移池州军事推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206862_comment'></div>太守罗公彦辅性彊愎，行事或失中，公必面折之，初虽不悦，而后卒相知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206862_comment'></div>民有乙与甲争塘水，而殴甲至死者，狱具，刑官欲寘之极典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206862_comment'></div>公当书断，建议以为事有所因，法不至死，争之，得减等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206862_comment'></div>公犹不已，太守怒甚，至以语诋公，公不为屈，争之愈力，于是命他官书断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206862_comment'></div>其后大理详谳，以甲准盗论，乙乃止当杖，审刑书断官以失入抵罪，众始愧服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206862_comment'></div>然公犹坐尝签书及用荐者改官，降次等，授宣义郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206862_comment'></div>人多劝公直其事，公卒不自明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206862_comment'></div>差知无为军庐江县，改福州怀安县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206862_comment'></div>未赴，从故龙图阁直学士陈公轩辟知杭州钱塘县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206862_comment'></div>有兄弟争财而讼者，累政不能决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206862_comment'></div>公至，取案牍焚之，谕以同气至情，财不足言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206862_comment'></div>兄弟感泣，拜于庭而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206862_comment'></div>异日公复过钱塘，二人犹求见公以谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206862_comment'></div>故观文殿大学士吕公惠卿帅鄜延，辟充经略安抚司勾当公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206862_comment'></div>初，公之尉松溪，吕公谪居建州，得公之文奇之，一见如故，以是首辟公置幕下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206862_comment'></div>至延安未逾月，适夏人倾国入寇，号百万，人心危慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206862_comment'></div>公徐为吕公陈方略，一路赖以完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206862_comment'></div>及米脂之役，工未毕，谍言贼兵十馀万且至，诸将弃城而遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206862_comment'></div>公曰：「彼众我寡，去将安之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206862_comment'></div>是速死尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206862_comment'></div>不若按兵勿动，城虽未完，冒以楼橹，彼将以我为有备，必不敢进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206862_comment'></div>兵法所以使敌人疑者，正谓此也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206862_comment'></div>诸将然之，卒如所料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206862_comment'></div>凡筑殄羌、威羌等十馀城，未尝不在其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206862_comment'></div>其后奉进筑图至阙下，因上五议，欲使诸路乘虚互出，以伐其并兵之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206862_comment'></div>进取横山，断其右臂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206862_comment'></div>参用汉唐实边转输之术；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206862_comment'></div>申命州郡，广招置之法，为足食足兵之计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206862_comment'></div>惩二寇辅车相依之势，以备不虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206862_comment'></div>识者以为切中边事之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206862_comment'></div>累赏转奉议郎，除江淮荆浙等路制置发运司勾当公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206862_comment'></div>未赴，改授签书平江军节度判官厅公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206862_comment'></div>尝摄郡事，适当累政因循之后，狱系甚众，公命数吏分条其所犯，不日皆决遣之，遂以无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206862_comment'></div>今上即位，覃恩转承议郎，勋武骑尉，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206862_comment'></div>以太学博士召，道除太常博士，转朝奉郎，迁知大宗正丞事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206862_comment'></div>因职事奏疏上四事，大略以谓缌麻亲宜有荫孙之法，非袒免以下小宗，有未食禄者，宜广流泽，特官之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206862_comment'></div>宗室虽得以科举进，尚宜许之入学，以养成其材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206862_comment'></div>且罢刺史以上公使，以恤非袒免无官之孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206862_comment'></div>皆当时所宜行者，有旨送讲议司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206862_comment'></div>除屯田员外郎，以论鄜延进筑功，特迁两官，转朝请郎，勋云骑尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206862_comment'></div>久之迁礼部员外郎，天子视学，公以为盛德事，献《视学颂》，有旨第其文高等，迁朝奉大夫，勋飞骑尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206862_comment'></div>时朝廷议礼考文，礼官视他部为重，非通知古今之学不足以当其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206862_comment'></div>公傅经稽史，无留事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206862_comment'></div>两以考课被赏，改司封员外郎，长贰相与举留之，复还礼部，转朝散大夫，勋骁骑尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206862_comment'></div>然公雅意欲就閒旷，力请外补，除知蔡州，朝廷惜其去，留为宗正少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206862_comment'></div>训辞有曰「非清德老儒，曷任兹选」，士论荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206862_comment'></div>转朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206862_comment'></div>天子受八宝，覃恩特迁左朝议大夫，兼学制局参详官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206862_comment'></div>移太常少卿，时故相刘公正夫在政府，刘公，大资政黄公婿也，以公联姻娅，亟请避嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1206862_comment'></div>上曰：「此真太常也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1206862_comment'></div>因批其奏曰：「公议所在，何嫌之有」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1206862_comment'></div>公遂就职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1206862_comment'></div>官制行，换中奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1206862_comment'></div>未几，复慨然语所亲曰：「吾平生为礼学，方布衣时已预修衣冠制度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1206862_comment'></div>今备位卿寺，得司天子礼文，于吾足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1206862_comment'></div>士当知止，岂可冒进不已」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1206862_comment'></div>遂坚求退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1206862_comment'></div>或者勉公曰：「奉常清切，于禁从才一间，盍少留乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1206862_comment'></div>公笑谢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1206862_comment'></div>朝廷度其不可复挽，则除公集贤殿修撰、知邓州、兼西南路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1206862_comment'></div>陛辞，天子劳问优渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1206862_comment'></div>公建言：「先帝尝命官修《中书备对录》，以知官吏流品、户口钱谷之数，以知礼法文为、军兵名额之数，以知刑罚赦宥、工事夫役之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1206862_comment'></div>盖体《周官》岁终受会之意，而所以周知天下之务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1206862_comment'></div>方今内外事物之要，盈虚繁简之实，欲有所稽考，盍命左右司略仿前制，为一书上之，以资观览」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1206862_comment'></div>天子深然之，有旨如公所请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1206862_comment'></div>公之意，盖非苟然而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1206862_comment'></div>南阳大藩，为帅者多务大体，不亲事，吏得舞文为奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1206862_comment'></div>公下车尽革前弊，纲纪大整。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1206862_comment'></div>与部使者议事，有所不合，公独请于朝，事卒见听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1206862_comment'></div>当路滋不悦，公弗顾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1206862_comment'></div>然自是若有不释然者，遂以疾请宫祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1206862_comment'></div>朝廷意公惮安抚一路之劳，除知颍州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1206862_comment'></div>章再上，祈恳愈力，除提举杭州洞霄宫，勋骑都尉，赐爵陇西县开国男、食邑三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1206862_comment'></div>公东归，居于梁溪锡山之傍，日以文字为娱，澹如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1206862_comment'></div>子纲为镇江教官，就养子舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1206862_comment'></div>与宾客过从，尽登临之适，优游自得，不复以世事介意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1206862_comment'></div>尝有贵公素知公者，被召与公相遇于途，询以所欲，公从容诵少陵「江汉垂纶」之句以答之，贵公咨美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1206862_comment'></div>还朝，每称于诸公间，以为不可及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1206862_comment'></div>及纲为尚书郎，丐迎养京师，除公提举醴泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1206862_comment'></div>转中大夫，改右文殿修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1206862_comment'></div>顷之，以足疾不任朝谒，请复洞霄，凡为宫祠者逾十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1206862_comment'></div>纲自左史论事得罪方远谪，公诲之曰：「进退出处，士夫之常，汝勉自爱，毋以吾老为念也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1206862_comment'></div>父子之懿，闻者仰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1206862_comment'></div>及归，公喜见颜间，曰：「汝罪大谪轻，谪未久而归，上恩厚矣，何以论报」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1206862_comment'></div>时公方避寇海陵，盛夏遽促归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1206862_comment'></div>既还，以微疾上章告老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1206862_comment'></div>命未及下，而公疾已革，顾诸子曰：「汝等皆在吾左右，吾何忧」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1206862_comment'></div>因不复语，怡然而逝，享年七十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1206862_comment'></div>公天资纯孝，继母饶氏性严肃，公事之尽子道，得其欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1206862_comment'></div>于兄弟间友爱尤笃，既除饶氏丧，尽以资产推与之，独与季弟曼出居浙右，廪入之馀，一以付之，置不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1206862_comment'></div>其后禋祀，许及期亲，即以与其子纬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1206862_comment'></div>其教子以孝弟忠信为本，闻人一善，于父子兄弟间誉之不容口，退而未尝不以训诸子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1206862_comment'></div>自为小官，喜周人之急，禄虽微，不为有无计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1206862_comment'></div>亲族之贫不能家者，均养之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1206862_comment'></div>妹侄甥女无资以遣者，必择配归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1206862_comment'></div>故乡里语风义，以公为称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1206862_comment'></div>其交朋友尽信义，与人接洞然无城府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1206862_comment'></div>尤喜提奖后进，孜孜不倦，门人之跻膴仕者相望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1206862_comment'></div>其在朝廷，每有贡举，公未尝不为考官，其所取多一时名士，人服其鉴裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1206862_comment'></div>平生唯嗜书，无他好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1206862_comment'></div>幼学尝苦无书，既仕，节衣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_132_1206862", 1206862, "Clauses/429/Comments/0")'>贬食</span>，而积书之富，至与巨室名家埒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1206862_comment'></div>初，黄公以名儒有重望，自熙宁以来，累践大官，被遇泰陵，进位承辖，士之出其门者，众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1206862_comment'></div>公为儿童时，甥舅自为知己，而退然官州县垂二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1206862_comment'></div>逮今上纂极，黄公已均逸于外，乃始以学官召擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1206862_comment'></div>盖黄公所以期公者远，而公亦安于义命，不汲汲于进也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1206862_comment'></div>晚位通显，而恬于进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1206862_comment'></div>又率常数考一迁，至一日有归意，则慨然决去不可留，其难进勇退如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1206862_comment'></div>公貌怡而气和，襮顺而中劲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1206862_comment'></div>少有大志，而深自韬养，不以所长自见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1206862_comment'></div>至其謇然持议，无所回隐，不为世变所移，则有人所不能者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1206862_comment'></div>建中靖国初，丞相范忠宣公薨，太常议行易名，公为博士，定其议曰：「公任台谏，当朝廷清明，民物阜安之时，而公正色立朝，力陈安危治乱之几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1206862_comment'></div>至于法度之废兴，典章之施设，大臣之去留，人材之用舍，一有不当其心，则抗章论列，无所顾避，至有不得其言而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1206862_comment'></div>其列侍从，居宥密，位台辅，益行所知，从容进见，有责难之恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1206862_comment'></div>朝廷有大利害，与同列辨论上前，各以理胜，如罢大河东注之议，寝鬼章款塞之质，下宽大之诏以安群心，释朋党之疑以全善类，皆自公发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1206862_comment'></div>然公处心积虑，务在体国，持论平允，不以好憎易情，不以同异介意，惟其是之从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1206862_comment'></div>故邓绾移扬，公置绾前日论己之憾，而言今日指摘绾事之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1206862_comment'></div>元祐纷更，公置熙宁论议不同之念，而言今日法度尽变之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1206862_comment'></div>非公诚心慷慨，不为利回，不为义疚，孰能然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1206862_comment'></div>若夫救蔡确新州之贬，而忘高位厚禄之为可怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1206862_comment'></div>论吕大防等宜从宽宥之叙，而不知疏远嫌疑之为可避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1206862_comment'></div>此人之所尤难，而公优为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1206862_comment'></div>盖公以谓大臣之于国，有股肱心膂之托，而乃心王室，曾无内外之间，安往而不任其责耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1206862_comment'></div>方是时，范公名在罪籍，虽门生故吏往往讳言之，而公之议挺挺不挠如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1206862_comment'></div>呜呼，斯可以观公之心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1206862_comment'></div>故余备载其辞，以是铭之，庶其流风犹足以立懦敦薄云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1206862_comment'></div>公娶吴氏，奉议郎桓之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1206862_comment'></div>初封仁和县君，先公二十一年卒，累赠濮阳郡君，改赠令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1206862_comment'></div>子男四人：曰纲，起居郎兼国史编修官，以论事谪监南剑州沙县税务，得旨复本等差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1206862_comment'></div>曰维，承事郎，前监在京诸司粮料院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1206862_comment'></div>曰经，通仕郎，试补太学上舍生，未赴殿试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1206862_comment'></div>曰纶，通仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1206862_comment'></div>女三人：长蚤卒，次适奉议郎、杭州司仪曹事张端礼，次适迪功郎、衢州司工曹事周琳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1206862_comment'></div>孙男六人：仪之、宗之、集之、琳之、文之、麟之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1206862_comment'></div>女三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1206862_comment'></div>有文集二十卷、《礼记义》十卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1206862_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_167_1206862'>目无全牛，奏刀砉然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1206862_comment'></div>不逢其族，孰知其难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1206862_comment'></div>亡故屡更，鲜不畔援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1206862_comment'></div>秉义弗渝，其节乃见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1206862_comment'></div>公于建中，士方纷如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1206862_comment'></div>不倚不流，介然中居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1206862_comment'></div>哲人之萎，谗波稽天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1206862_comment'></div>鲠议直辞，如防在川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1206862_comment'></div>群言不孚，咸底于罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1206862_comment'></div>皇明烛幽，公独无悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1206862_comment'></div>易名之美，自公发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1206862_comment'></div>世济之荣，公与有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1206862_comment'></div>我作铭诗，以示万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1206862_comment'></div>庶其流风，闻者兴起。</div><div id='poem_sentence_180_1206862_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206863?labeling=true' target='_blank'>令人吴氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206863")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206863'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206863'>中大夫、右文殿脩撰李公讳夔之夫人吴氏，其先越州山阴人，仕唐为谏大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206863_comment'></div>董昌之乱，义不屈，遁居括州，故今为括苍剑川人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206863_comment'></div>曾祖崇避哲宗讳，赠大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206863_comment'></div>祖彀赠承事郎，父桓故任奉议郎、知湖州长兴县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206863_comment'></div>母鲍氏，金华县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206863_comment'></div>夫人资孝谨，事父母能尽其力，饮食起居未尝斯须去侧，省定温凊，各适其节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206863_comment'></div>言德功容，人鲜俪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206863_comment'></div>父母贤之，谓必得名士乃可以为配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206863_comment'></div>是时，李公以诸生与修衣冠制度，名闻朝廷，继而擢高科，遂以妻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206863_comment'></div>惟吴氏世为望族，夫人生大家，而李公起寒素，夫人事之尽妇顺，能以清约自将，无骄矜气，柔明端静，人不见其喜愠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206863_comment'></div>治家有常法，遇妾媵有恩意，闺门之内雍如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206863_comment'></div>方李公筮仕之初，官卑禄微，喜过从，赒人之急如不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206863_comment'></div>甥侄孤女未有家者，必择对归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206863_comment'></div>夫人躬治殽馔，必致其精旨，罄奁具资遣之，无吝容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206863_comment'></div>人以为难，而夫人安为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206863_comment'></div>故乡闾笃风义者，必以李公为称首，夫人之力为多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206863_comment'></div>李公从辟鄜延，夫人挈诸子归宁，而金华尚无恙，夫人事之益至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206863_comment'></div>吴氏族大，间有不相能者，必迎致其家，听其言，视其容色，而鄙倍必消矣，其懿范感人盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206863_comment'></div>建中靖国元年，李公自签书平江军节度判官厅公事被召为太学博士，既登舟而夫人感疾，遂不起，实正月七日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206863_comment'></div>以其年三月十八日葬于常州无锡县开元乡历村湛岘山之原，享年四十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206863_comment'></div>初封仁和、仁寿二县君，李公之舅右丞黄公以夫人之贤奏赐冠帔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206863_comment'></div>既没，累赠永嘉濮阳郡君，改赠令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206863_comment'></div>男四人：曰纲，起居郎，国史编修官，坐言事谪监南剑州沙县税务，有言牵复未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206863_comment'></div>曰维，承事郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206863_comment'></div>曰经，曰纶，皆通仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206863_comment'></div>女三人：长蚤卒，次适奉议郎、杭州司议曹事张端礼，次适迪功郎、衢州司功曹事周琳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206863_comment'></div>宣和四年，余过锡山，以其舅从政郎爽侯彦申之状属余铭，且谓余曰：「吾母之亡，先子方趋朝，而诸孤皆稚弱，不克铭以葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206863_comment'></div>夫铭所以论撰先美，而明著之后世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206863_comment'></div>无美而称之，是诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206863_comment'></div>有而弗知，不明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206863_comment'></div>知而弗传，不仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206863_comment'></div>三者有一焉，人子之罪大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206863_comment'></div>今吾母之德善可考不诬如此，而积二十有馀年，幽堂无辞以纪，诸孤不仁之罪宜无以自逭，愿得铭以补前过，庶几发扬幽光，为存没之慰」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206863_comment'></div>余感其言，故不辞而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206863_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1206863'>内职之修，閟而弗彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206863_comment'></div>有子之贤，其传乃光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206863_comment'></div>贻尔后人，视此铭章<span class='inlineComment2'>（《杨龟山先生集》卷三二。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206863_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1206863'>「以其舅」上缺主语，疑有脱字。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1206863_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206888' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206888' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206888?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭陈莹中文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206888")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206888_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206888'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206888'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206888_comment'></div>天生我公，为时元龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206888_comment'></div>精贯白日，而无以自表；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206888_comment'></div>气包宇宙，而不容于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206888_comment'></div>止或尼之，非人能为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206888_comment'></div>嗟一跌而不振，卒困死于流离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206888_comment'></div>赖遗言之未泯，导原委而东之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206888_comment'></div>念生死之永诀，怅南北之差池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206888_comment'></div>徒反袂以长号，泪淋浪而沾衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206888_comment'></div>公乎不亡，其知我悲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1206888_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c8ff4f632c1546718872a7cc3e1b4327_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c8ff4f632c1546718872a7cc3e1b4327");'><span id='c8ff4f632c1546718872a7cc3e1b4327_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1124')">1123-1124年</a>，71-72岁</div><div id='c8ff4f632c1546718872a7cc3e1b4327' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　还毗陵。转朝请郎，不赴。在道南书院讲道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1124')">1123-1124年</a>　在毗陵。有文。作品：与吴国华书。莫中奉墓志铭。祭游定夫。翁行简墓志铭。与许少尹左丞（其一）与许少尹左丞（其二）与许少尹左丞（其三）与许少尹左丞（其四）跋张元干集先祖手泽。<div id='poem_1206866' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206866' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206866?labeling=true' target='_blank'>莫中奉墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和五年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206866")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206866_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206866'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206866'>公讳表深，字智行，邵武人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206866_comment'></div>曾祖扆，仕为三班奉职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206866_comment'></div>祖及，不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206866_comment'></div>父说，当景祐、宝元间，士方以声律决科，而君独以穷经为务，自闽陬数千里外赢粮趼足至京师，从泰山孙明复、徂徕石守道先生游，讲明道术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206866_comment'></div>还家杜门，不复求仕进，以公恩累赠至通议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206866_comment'></div>公自幼闻过庭之训，问学有家法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206866_comment'></div>是时安定先生居霅上，为世儒宗，公往师焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206866_comment'></div>一见奇之，谓公有器识，异日所至，未易量也，自是浸以名闻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206866_comment'></div>元丰二年登进士第，调洪州丰城尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206866_comment'></div>未赴，丁通议公忧，服除，再调建州建阳县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206866_comment'></div>秩满，用荐者移抚州宜黄令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206866_comment'></div>适丁母硕人忧，不赴，终丧，授凤翔府好畤县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206866_comment'></div>好畤在陇右为剧邑，号难治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206866_comment'></div>公至，明约信令，而人化服，终三年无一人犯重辟者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206866_comment'></div>仇齐路险绝，车舆不通，邑人病之久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206866_comment'></div>公谕父老鸠徒计工，治为坦途，往来便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206866_comment'></div>侍郎张公舜民领漕事，见而谓人曰：「莫侯可谓知为政矣，其为利非济人溱洧之比也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206866_comment'></div>率同列交荐之，改宣德郎、知泗州昭信县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206866_comment'></div>宪司有系囚，事联省曹，吏以枝辞蔓其狱，六更推治不能决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206866_comment'></div>命公往治之，一问而情得，人服其明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206866_comment'></div>民有持牒弃妻屏子者，公诘其所由，曰：「以病而贫，力不足以相收，故及此，非得已也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206866_comment'></div>公恻然悯之，曰：「吾为长民之吏，使人父子夫妇不相保，当任其咎者，其谁欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206866_comment'></div>于是出私钱赈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206866_comment'></div>里巷编氓感公之义，皆协力以周其匮急，故其室家复安如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206866_comment'></div>比公之行，是人与其妻拿攀号于道，见者咸嗟叹之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206866_comment'></div>公惠政及人，有以厚风俗，多此类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206866_comment'></div>上皇即位，覃恩迁奉议郎，赐绯衣银鱼，除真定府路都总管司勾当公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206866_comment'></div>会中山之安抚朱公绂以公兼领帅事，赖公颇多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206866_comment'></div>秩满，通判新安，除御史台主行，用中司不召，赴都堂审察，除光禄寺丞，未上，迁开封府司工曹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206866_comment'></div>朝廷更钱法，命夜下，公适直宿，阴为处画，人无知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206866_comment'></div>黎明揭示，大悉详下，吏不得摇手为奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206866_comment'></div>尹陛对被奖谕，遂以公之名闻于上，睿旨亲除左司录事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206866_comment'></div>中都不治，吏习以为常，黠胥舞知玩上，文移钳纸尾以进，官署唯唯惟谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206866_comment'></div>公察其尤无良者治其一二，一府屏息，无敢习故为傲慢者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206866_comment'></div>并僚恃权倖，虽没一悉趋之，公为折其短，独未尝少屈，乃讽言章，政和三年出公为广济军司录事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206866_comment'></div>士论惜之，而公处之恬如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206866_comment'></div>久之，朝廷察其非辜，起知睦州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206866_comment'></div>公曰：「文正范公、清献赵公尝守是邦，其遗范未远也，循而守之，则无馀事矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206866_comment'></div>已而郡大治，民至今思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206866_comment'></div>过朝除知饶州，东归待次毗陵，爱其土风，欲营菟裘，为归休计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206866_comment'></div>于是力请宫祠，除提举西京嵩山崇福宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206866_comment'></div>未几告老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206866_comment'></div>宣和五年六月丁未，以疾终于常州私第之正寝，享年七十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206866_comment'></div>是年十一月壬申葬于宜兴县清泉乡之梅林原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206866_comment'></div>公为人端劲有守，孝于亲，友于兄弟，人不间其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206866_comment'></div>畜幼孤如己子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206866_comment'></div>莅官临政，严而不苛，宽而有制，故吏畏其威，民怀其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206866_comment'></div>决滞讼，去民瘼，洞然幽隐，虽逢其族，迎刃立解，世之名能吏者，皆自以为莫及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206866_comment'></div>公自奉议郎或以年劳，或以恩典，九迁至中奉大夫，赐三品服，封文安县开国男，食邑三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206866_comment'></div>娶方氏，太常少卿、赠金紫光禄大夫讳峤之女，有贤行，能宜其家，累封至令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206866_comment'></div>男二人：曰多闻，通直郎、监镇江府排岸司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206866_comment'></div>曰多见，迪功郎、明州慈溪县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206866_comment'></div>女二人：长适宣教郎、知袭庆府邹县事朱缶，次适迪功郎、信州州学教授江文中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206866_comment'></div>孙男三人：曰革，曰萃，皆登仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206866_comment'></div>曰蒙，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206866_comment'></div>孙女二人尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206866_comment'></div>晚自号如如居士，有文集十五卷，曰《如如集》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206866_comment'></div>既葬，其孤请铭于予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206866_comment'></div>予与公有平生之旧，知公为详，义不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206866_comment'></div>乃为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1206866'>猎德之勤，积之在身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206866_comment'></div>府寺践更，蔚乎有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206866_comment'></div>出蕃于外，惠施于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206866_comment'></div>去思不忘，久而弥新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206866_comment'></div>百世之传，视此铭文。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1206866'></div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1206866_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206889' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206889' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206889?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭游定夫文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206889")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206889_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206889'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206889'>呜呼定夫，学通天人，而时不用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206889_comment'></div>道足济天下，而泽不加乎民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206889_comment'></div>今其已矣，夫复何云！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206889_comment'></div>怅百年之永诀，犹想见其音尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206889_comment'></div>念昔从师，同志三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206889_comment'></div>今皆沦亡，眇余独存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206889_comment'></div>虽未即死，而头童齿豁，茕然孤立而谁怜！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206889_comment'></div>嗟吾先生，微言未泯，而学者所记，多失其真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206889_comment'></div>赖公相与参订，去其讹谬，以传后学，书往未复，而讣之及门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206889_comment'></div>呜呼悲夫，宜任其责者复谁欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206889_comment'></div>斯文将泯灭而无传欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206889_comment'></div>抱遗编而求之，悼此志之不伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206889_comment'></div>重念南北相望，不得凭棺一恸，徒陨涕而驰神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206889_comment'></div>余言之悲，闻乎不闻？</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1206889_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206864' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206864' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206864?labeling=true' target='_blank'>翁行简墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206864")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206864_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206864'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206864'>公讳彦约，字行简，其先京兆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206864_comment'></div>唐末避地，子孙散居七闽，公之六世祖徙家建州之崇安白水乡，故今为崇安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206864_comment'></div>曾祖伯珍，不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206864_comment'></div>祖元方，以其子恩赐朝奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206864_comment'></div>父仲通，以文行为东南儒宗，学者咸师尊之，仕至朝奉郎，累赠银青光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206864_comment'></div>有子三人，公其长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206864_comment'></div>公天资颖悟绝人，自幼学已能属文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206864_comment'></div>既冠，博总经传，尤深于礼学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206864_comment'></div>元丰末游上庠，声闻籍甚，一时知名士皆慕与之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206864_comment'></div>元祐二年与国学荐，以祖母寿昌君之丧未赴礼部试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206864_comment'></div>银青外除造朝，欲候公策名而后告老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206864_comment'></div>公以谓用是缓吾亲归休计，非便也，请以世禄之恩授中第，银青不许，力请而后从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206864_comment'></div>已而兄弟更相推逊，闻于朝，事虽不行，缙绅义之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206864_comment'></div>公既不第，益自奋励，术业益加进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206864_comment'></div>建之举进士者，无虑五六十辈，公再举皆中首选，从而受业者常数十百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206864_comment'></div>元符二年上即位，以日食下诏求言，时公与计偕，奏《格言》二十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206864_comment'></div>上篇自祗命、原化、典学、崇俭以至审治，言所以立德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206864_comment'></div>下篇自择术、因任、兼听、务和以至审势，言所以立政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206864_comment'></div>皆陈古义以砭今非，言近而不迫，直而不忤，识者重焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206864_comment'></div>政和三年擢进士第，调汝州龙兴尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206864_comment'></div>丞相何公素知公，谓所亲曰：「翁生纵未能用，不宜辱之捶楚间也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206864_comment'></div>改常州司刑曹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206864_comment'></div>公莅事精敏，郡治赖之为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206864_comment'></div>恶吏屏息，有遁逃，讫公在幕府不敢出者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206864_comment'></div>居二年，江淮荆浙制置发运使以奏计对，上问所部人材，使者与公初无雅故，以清议所在，首以公对，驿召为详定《九域图志》编修官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206864_comment'></div>政和七年改宣教郎，除太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206864_comment'></div>以与修《因革礼》，迁奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206864_comment'></div>岁馀乞补外，除提举河北西路学事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206864_comment'></div>及陛对，建言：「朝廷更八行法，使俱试于有司，以革奔竞浮滥之弊，固善矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206864_comment'></div>然八行初非以文辞选也，今限以等第，有中程而不官者，与初立法异甚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206864_comment'></div>谓凡入等无问高下，俱与廷对，以示详行实、略文华之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206864_comment'></div>时浙寇犯衢、处，公之弟中丞公由御史府得请乡郡，公亟以书属之曰：「贼方炽，势必侵轶吾郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206864_comment'></div>自衢、信抵浦城、崇安，险阨易守，不可犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206864_comment'></div>惟处之龙泉至松溪、浦城，皆荡野无捍蔽，龙泉破则建危矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206864_comment'></div>龙泉之士有叶植者，其人迈往有智略，因之使拒守，宜可倚办」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206864_comment'></div>中丞公然之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206864_comment'></div>比至镇，植已率众拒贼，即出兵益给粮械助之，卒如公所料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206864_comment'></div>朔方士大夫闻之，谓公料贼于数千里外如指诸掌，非智虑精审过人，能如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206864_comment'></div>公在朔部尤以人材为意，有所荐拔，必择行能卓然者先之，如解习之徒是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206864_comment'></div>学政于民事初无与焉，公所至必诹访民间利病，与夫实边制胜之术，日与将士讲画，意谓异时以使事归报面陈之，为朝廷经远之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206864_comment'></div>既罢使事，不复对，除权发遣黄州，转承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206864_comment'></div>宣和四年夏之官，道改高邮军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206864_comment'></div>高邮当江淮孔道，商旅所出入类多以贸易茶盐为业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206864_comment'></div>奸民讦圭撮铢两之私，连逮抵罪者不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206864_comment'></div>公下车，有告言者，随决之无留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206864_comment'></div>吏犹习故常白于公，欲以枝辞蔓其狱，公曰：「两狱充斥，若等尚恨其少耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206864_comment'></div>吏愕眙失对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206864_comment'></div>于是一郡相庆，知公以民为念，吏不得倚法为奸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206864_comment'></div>岁大旱，公以祷祠疲甚，既而公得疾，所亲以是尤公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206864_comment'></div>公曰：「民苏而吾病，无憾矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206864_comment'></div>病浸亟，遂乞致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206864_comment'></div>章未报，以八月丁亥卒于军治之正寝，享年六十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206864_comment'></div>公性孝友，事亲尽子道，于兄弟怡怡如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206864_comment'></div>敦睦姻族，人无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206864_comment'></div>遇人无贤否，一以诚意，人人自以为亲厚，而与之同趣盖鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206864_comment'></div>延平陈公晚居淮南，见公喜，语人曰：「翁奉常静恪有谋，使得志，殆能济务」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206864_comment'></div>其为名流推重如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206864_comment'></div>公为高邮，视事才数日，属疾，民或未识公面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206864_comment'></div>及公之丧，行道之人皆出涕曰：「失吾贤守也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206864_comment'></div>盖诚之感人，未有不动者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206864_comment'></div>娶吴氏，奉议郎桓之女，封孺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206864_comment'></div>子男二人：曰挺，迪功郎、充两浙转运司管勾文字；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206864_comment'></div>抗，未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206864_comment'></div>女一人，适承事郎李维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206864_comment'></div>内外孙男女十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206864_comment'></div>有文集十卷，其文精致润缛，得作者之体，尤长于诗，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206864_comment'></div>昔公在太常，二弟俱持节还朝，列侍从，居要官，公复出使于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206864_comment'></div>建虽多士为东南最，而兄弟俱被荣宠，未有前比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206864_comment'></div>意公晚仕，积厚而源深，其发必远，遽尔沦丧，士论惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206864_comment'></div>其孤将以明年六月丁酉葬公于白水之源，属余铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206864_comment'></div>余于公有朋友之义，不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206864_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_1206864'>猎德之勤，名则随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206864_comment'></div>名实既孚，君子之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206864_comment'></div>滀深有源，渭流未施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206864_comment'></div>百世之传，视此铭诗。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1206864_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋张元干集先祖手泽</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206684")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206684'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206684'>仲宗诸父，皆特进公继室林夫人之子，俱非刘氏出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206684_comment'></div>其子孙声容，盖未尝相接，观公付委陈氏之意，所以望其子孙，其责亦轻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206684_comment'></div>仲宗得其手泽，乃访寻于丘荒蓁莽之间，割牲洒酒以致其诚意，又为文刻石以表识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206684_comment'></div>其于尊祖追远之义尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206684_comment'></div>吾将见其流风所被，使乡邦民德归厚，必自兹始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206684_comment'></div>宣和甲辰四月辛亥，龟山杨时书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1206684_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年9月</a>　在毗陵。授秘书郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　在毗陵。有文。作品：御史游公墓志铭。与陈公晦书。<div id='poem_1206865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206865?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御史游公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和六年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206865")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206865_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206865'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206865'>吾友定夫既没之明年，其子某自历阳涉大江，诣予而告曰：「先君之友惟公为最厚，今既葬，而幽堂之铭无辞以刻，恐遂堙没无传焉，敢以是请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206865_comment'></div>予告之曰：「知先公之名德皎如日星，虽奴隶之贱皆知之，其流风馀韵足以师世范俗，岂待予言而传乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206865_comment'></div>然昔在元丰中俱受业于明道先生兄弟之门，有友二人焉，谢良佐显道，公其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206865_comment'></div>三年之间，二公相继沦亡，存者独予而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206865_comment'></div>追念平生，触事无一不可悲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206865_comment'></div>今吾子以铭见属，舍予其奚之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206865_comment'></div>公讳酢，定夫其字也，建州建阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206865_comment'></div>初与其兄醇俱以文行知名于时，所交皆天下豪英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206865_comment'></div>公虽少，而一时老师宿儒咸推先之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206865_comment'></div>伊川先生以事至京师，一见谓其资可与适道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206865_comment'></div>是时明道先生兄弟方以倡明道学为己任，设庠序，聚邑人子弟教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206865_comment'></div>召公来职学事，公欣然往从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206865_comment'></div>得其微言，于是尽弃其学而学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206865_comment'></div>其后得邑清河，予往见之，伊川谓予曰：「游君德气粹然，问学日进，政事亦绝人远甚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206865_comment'></div>其在师门见称如此，则所造可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206865_comment'></div>公于元丰六年登进士第，调越州萧山尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206865_comment'></div>用侍臣荐，召为太学录，改宣德郎，除博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206865_comment'></div>公以食贫待次，奉亲不便，就拟知河南府清河县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206865_comment'></div>忠宣范公判河南，待以国士，事有疑议，必与之参订。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206865_comment'></div>移守颍昌，辟公自随，为府学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206865_comment'></div>未几还朝，复秉国政，即除公太学博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206865_comment'></div>已而忠宣罢政，公亦请外矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206865_comment'></div>除齐州签书判官厅公事，用年劳改奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206865_comment'></div>丁太中公忧，服除，再调泉州签判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206865_comment'></div>上皇即位，覃恩改承议郎，赐绯衣、银鱼袋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206865_comment'></div>还，召为监察御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206865_comment'></div>磨勘转朝奉郎，出知和州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206865_comment'></div>岁馀管勾南京鸿庆宫，居太平州，两乞再任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206865_comment'></div>以八宝恩转朝散郎，磨勘转朝请郎、知汉阳军，磨勘转朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206865_comment'></div>以亲老再乞宫祠，除提点成都府长生观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206865_comment'></div>丁太硕人忧，服除，除知舒州，移知濠州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206865_comment'></div>不数月，会从官谪守冲罢归，寓历阳，因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206865_comment'></div>宣和五年五月乙亥，以疾终于正寝，享年七十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206865_comment'></div>是年十二月丙午，与夫人合葬于和州含山县升城乡车辕岭之原，用治命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206865_comment'></div>公自幼不群，读书一过目辄成诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206865_comment'></div>比壮，益自力，心传目到，不为世儒之习，诚于中，形诸外，仪容辞令粲然有文，望之知其为成德君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206865_comment'></div>其事亲无伪，交朋友有信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206865_comment'></div>莅官遇僚吏有恩意，虽人乐于自尽，而无敢慢其令者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206865_comment'></div>惠政在民，戴之如父母，故去则见思，愈久而不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206865_comment'></div>筮仕之初，未更事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206865_comment'></div>县有疑狱，馀年不能决，公摄邑事，一问得其情而释之，精练如素官者，人服其明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206865_comment'></div>比年以来，编民困于征敛，而脩奉祠馆，市材调夫无虚月，所至骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206865_comment'></div>公历守四郡，处之裕如，虽时有兴造，民初不知而事集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206865_comment'></div>此在公特其秕糠耳，无足道者，故不复缕载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206865_comment'></div>若其道学足以觉斯人，馀润足以泽天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206865_comment'></div>遭时清明，不及用而死，此士论共惜之，非予一己之私言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206865_comment'></div>曾祖尚，祖礼之，不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206865_comment'></div>父潜，赠太中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206865_comment'></div>娶吕氏，封宜人，有贤行，事舅姑以孝闻，友姊姒，睦姻族，人无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206865_comment'></div>公素贫，不治生产，夫人攻苦食淡，能宜其家，其内助多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206865_comment'></div>先公三年卒，享年六十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206865_comment'></div>子男七人：撝，文林郎、洪州司兵曹事，卒于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206865_comment'></div>拟、救、握，皆蚤世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206865_comment'></div>损，迪功郎，前授归州司兵曹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206865_comment'></div>掞，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206865_comment'></div>拂，未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206865_comment'></div>皆业儒世其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206865_comment'></div>女一人，归时之子遹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206865_comment'></div>孙男三人，女五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206865_comment'></div>有《中庸义》一卷，《诗二南义》一卷，《论语》《孟子》杂解各一卷，文集十卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206865_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_1206865'>呜呼天乎，故不慭遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206865_comment'></div>方时清明，哲人其萎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206865_comment'></div>道虽不行，斯文未亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206865_comment'></div>百世而下，其传有光。</div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1206865_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206625' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206625' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206625?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与陈公晦书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206625")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206625_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206625'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206625'>自公之东，无由通问，惟是倾念，未尝忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206625_comment'></div>春寒，伏惟孝履支福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206625_comment'></div>正远披晤，伏冀节哀慎卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206625_comment'></div>某辱尊公眷知最厚，义虽朋友，情实兄弟。<div class='inline'
