id='poem_sentence_3_1206625_comment'></div>自其弃世，每一念之，肝腑摧裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206625_comment'></div>共惟至性，万里生还，不及一见，终天之恨，何以堪处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206625_comment'></div>道路阻修，无由驰慰，临纸悲哽，区区不能悉布。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206625_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206626' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206626' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206626?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206626_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206626'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206626'>去岁数月之间，定夫、民表相继沦亡，朋友殆尽，无复存者，衰老殊不能堪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206626_comment'></div>念公乍还，家事能不费力否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206626_comment'></div>通川僻郡，士人稀小，赖存诸任，可以往还也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206626_comment'></div>寒阴未解，惟加爱是望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206626_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='815d70b7640645659560b7c104e27311_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("815d70b7640645659560b7c104e27311");'><span id='815d70b7640645659560b7c104e27311_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>，75岁</div><div id='815d70b7640645659560b7c104e27311' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年5月1日</a>　在毗陵。高宗皇帝登位，大赦改元，有贺表。作品：贺皇帝即位表。<div id='poem_1206480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206480?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺皇帝即位表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206480")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206480_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206480'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206480'>寇氛逆天，痛二圣之播越；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206480_comment'></div>民心戴后，幸九庙之再安<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206480_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下体舜聪明，躬汤勇智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206480_comment'></div>忧勤孚于内外，孝弟通乎神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206480_comment'></div>践宝位于艰难之中，安神器于倾侧之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206480_comment'></div>臣叨尘法从，莫效微劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206480_comment'></div>愿思高祖之好谋，仍奋文皇之英武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206480_comment'></div>两宫返国，徐当责效于侯公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206480_comment'></div>巨丑成擒，终见收功于李靖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206480_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1206480_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8a6988950bf44e67b430c055750d2ddc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8a6988950bf44e67b430c055750d2ddc");'><span id='8a6988950bf44e67b430c055750d2ddc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>，76岁</div><div id='8a6988950bf44e67b430c055750d2ddc' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>自扬州还，复寓毗陵。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在毗陵，有文。作品：章端叔墓志铭。<div id='poem_1206872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206872?labeling=true' target='_blank'>章端叔墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206872")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206872_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206872'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206872'>公讳某，字端叔，姓章氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206872_comment'></div>八世祖及为康州刺史，自南康徙居建州之浦城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206872_comment'></div>其孙仔钧仕王氏，官至太傅，仔钊为泉州团练副使，兄弟俱有功于闽，故号仔钊为小太傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206872_comment'></div>仔钧之后居西村，仔钊之后居珠林，自是分为二族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206872_comment'></div>宋兴几二百年，西族世有显人，珠林久不振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206872_comment'></div>至景德中，公之大王父始以进士中甲科，而位秘书丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206872_comment'></div>公于熙宁三年继登科，而后珠林之族浸显矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206872_comment'></div>公资颖悟，方幼学已能属文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206872_comment'></div>年十四即辞亲求师友，薄游江淮间殆十年，能自力，卒以名闻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206872_comment'></div>初调抚州临川尉，盗有劫行商杀人者，吏以支辞蔓其狱，连逮者以十数，累日情不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206872_comment'></div>公呼囚令环坐，以事验之，俄引三人出曰：「汝实为盗」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206872_comment'></div>馀悉纵之使去，三人者卒伏其辜，无异辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206872_comment'></div>其遇事巧发奇中类如此，人莫能测也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206872_comment'></div>就移寿州寿春令，大臣有以公《孟子义》进者，诏付秘书省，除应天府国子监教授，用举者改著作佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206872_comment'></div>官制行，换宣德郎，知越州山阴县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206872_comment'></div>山阴号繁剧，讼牒日纷至，公处之裕如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206872_comment'></div>巨猾陆璋辈窜易户名，以避征役，公阅籍具得其奸状，坐流配者数人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206872_comment'></div>老奸宿赃屏迹听命，无敢复为欺者，邑大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206872_comment'></div>境内有海塘潴水溉民田，岁久堙塞不治，为旱患，公鸠徒浚之，仍为经画，为久计，民至今赖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206872_comment'></div>秩满转奉议郎，监左藏北库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206872_comment'></div>哲宗即位，转承议郎，通判宿州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206872_comment'></div>先是，南京押纲侍禁史士宗侵耗官米数百石，反讼仓官交纳不公，狱久不决，朝廷以委公，至即片言折之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206872_comment'></div>士宗虽坐流窜，而自以为不冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206872_comment'></div>又两迁为朝散郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206872_comment'></div>继丁亲忧，去丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206872_comment'></div>久之，除太府寺丞，转朝请郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206872_comment'></div>召对称旨，除府界提举常平等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206872_comment'></div>鄢陵旧有双泊河，数溢为民害，二县以开浚为请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206872_comment'></div>公为亲行堤上，得旧河经始之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206872_comment'></div>本欲杀惠民河水流而归之蔡河，稍加开浚，则惠民之注流益悍，而蔡河不足以吞纳，则为害滋甚，不若增浚河外故道，双泊虽溢，可恃以无患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206872_comment'></div>是岁河朔饥民流而入畿甸者不可以数计，公召而廪给之，因以用其力，故堤成，民不告病，而饥者得以全活，公私之利盖两得之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206872_comment'></div>上皇即位，转朝奉大夫，未几除知虔州，为江西剧郡，俗健讼，公下车，痛治妄诉者一人，迄公去，无或干政犯令者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206872_comment'></div>是时承平日久，屡丰年，天下讳言灾伤，无以民病告者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206872_comment'></div>公还朝，首言淮甸岁凶，宜加赈恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206872_comment'></div>大臣初虽不悦，而公诚意恳恻，故卒从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206872_comment'></div>翌日遣使大发仓廪，而民赖以济，公之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206872_comment'></div>崇宁初，党论复兴，义士胶口无敢窃议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206872_comment'></div>公除郎官，得旨陛对，抗言：「元祐臣僚削秩投荒皆缘国事，陛下即位，稍令内徙，道路交庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206872_comment'></div>今复刻名著籍，禁锢其子孙，恐非陛下本意，臣窃惑焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206872_comment'></div>上虽优容之，然亦由是与时论不合矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206872_comment'></div>会宰相曾公布得罪，言者因以微文诋公，从坐降一官，罢，寻知泰州，遂挂冠退居吴门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206872_comment'></div>未几，上记其姓名，特旨落致仕，复知泰州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206872_comment'></div>之官数月，即乞宫祠，得提举舒州灵仙观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206872_comment'></div>崇宁五年六月八日，以疾终于平江府之私第，享年六十二岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206872_comment'></div>以其年十二月十六日，葬于吴县长山乡仕墟道士坞之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206872_comment'></div>公庄重简默，而接人以和气，行己莅官，一本于诚，不表襮以自售。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206872_comment'></div>其论天下事不苟不随，期于当理而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206872_comment'></div>方元符末议役法，请循元丰为便，或疑其朋附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206872_comment'></div>及崇宁陛对，抗言党锢非是，闻者骇汗，乃知公之用心合天下至公，无彼时此时之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206872_comment'></div>公以是数忤权贵，竟以不遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206872_comment'></div>公仕于朝，兄弟请别籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206872_comment'></div>公尽以己所当得田业均之，且立券与之约，毋得辄典卖，而其后兄弟之子有破其产者，卒赖此以为生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206872_comment'></div>公之惇族，为之长虑，盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206872_comment'></div>公平生无女妓珍奇之好，独读书万卷，增校精至，手泽具在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206872_comment'></div>有文集二十卷，《孟子解义》十四卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206872_comment'></div>曾祖故任秘书丞，祖故不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206872_comment'></div>父故任通直郎，赠朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206872_comment'></div>娶沈氏，起居舍人讳季长之女也，封宜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206872_comment'></div>公襟度简远，未尝问生事，然奋羁旅起家，阖门千指，有宅以居，有田以食，夫人之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206872_comment'></div>其经理家事，无巨细皆有节法，丰而不侈，俭而不陋，正睦中外，雍如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206872_comment'></div>自政和以来，四方无虞，仕进者以攀附为荣，而夫人每戒其子曰：「宜安素分，远权门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206872_comment'></div>盗贼且起，无远官，以贻吾忧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206872_comment'></div>诸子仕者谨奉其戒，卒无患，闻者服其远识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206872_comment'></div>建炎二年八月二十五日，以疾终于正寝，享年七十有四，以是年十月二十二日祔葬于公之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206872_comment'></div>子男八人：长愿，宣教郎、知杭州临安县事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206872_comment'></div>次师中，早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206872_comment'></div>次悫，迪功郎、池州士曹掾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206872_comment'></div>次愈，迪功郎、福州士曹掾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206872_comment'></div>次惠，次宪，次懋，次悊，皆业儒，未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206872_comment'></div>女四人：长适宣教郎、知舒州宿松县事孙寔，次适朝散郎、直秘阁、广东路提举常平等事王舜举，次适奉议郎、主管亳州明道宫吕弸中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206872_comment'></div>孙男女二十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206872_comment'></div>建炎之初，其子宪不远数舍诣毗陵踵吾门而告曰：「先君之亡二十有馀年矣，而无幽堂之铭，其盛德中行，恐遂泯没无传焉，敢以是请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206872_comment'></div>久之，余未暇作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206872_comment'></div>又遭母夫人之丧，复以书抵余，而请之益至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206872_comment'></div>余虽不及见公，而公之子宪、悊从余游，义不得辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206872_comment'></div>乃为铭，使归而揭诸墓上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206872_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_1206872'>奋身羁穷，砥节不移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206872_comment'></div>遵义而行，不苟不随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206872_comment'></div>党籍之兴，公独有言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206872_comment'></div>为人不能，展也直贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206872_comment'></div>铭以昭之，庶永其传。</div><div id='poem_sentence_80_1206872_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
桐庐
-----detail

-----title
南平
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b2dc2bd2bd29428bb8c7834c58d512da_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b2dc2bd2bd29428bb8c7834c58d512da");'><span id='b2dc2bd2bd29428bb8c7834c58d512da_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>，47岁</div><div id='b2dc2bd2bd29428bb8c7834c58d512da' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在南平，有诗。作品：言溪早起。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在南平？有诗。作品：夜雨。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e52063733a0f42e2ad510da9c83410ff_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e52063733a0f42e2ad510da9c83410ff");'><span id='e52063733a0f42e2ad510da9c83410ff_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，49岁</div><div id='e52063733a0f42e2ad510da9c83410ff' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在建阳，任县丞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在建阳。张公舜民入长谏垣，荐公为教官，除荆南府学教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在建阳。又蒙张舜民辟为定州教官，不赴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年3月</a>　在建阳。沙阳陈公渊投书问学。公喜其识性明敏，遂妻以女。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在建阳。罗从彦从学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在建阳。有书与邹志完，劝进谏。作品：与邹志完书。<div id='poem_1206555' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206555' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206555?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与邹至完书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206555")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206555_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206555'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206555'>窃惟天子睿圣，方嗣位之始，未有左右便嬖近习之私迎意而取悦，未有奸邪谗佞欺负之徒投间而乱其聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206555_comment'></div>圣度虚明，忠言易入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206555_comment'></div>《书》曰：「为上为德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206555_comment'></div>孟子曰：「一正君而国定矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206555_comment'></div>此正其时，不可失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206555_comment'></div>宜迪之以先王道德之要言、为治之大方，参之以古今成败之明效，使圣智益明，则天下之利病、左右之忠邪自判矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206555_comment'></div>舍此宜无足为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206555_comment'></div>公之道学究极天人之蕴，某之所知，盖公之所厌馀者，安能上裨高明万一？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206555_comment'></div>然愚鄙尝辱一盼之私，故辄自竭，惟宽仁不罪其狂瞽，乃幸也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1206555_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长沙
-----detail

-----title
湖口
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b133f8b58851420ea7881bc053432032_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b133f8b58851420ea7881bc053432032");'><span id='b133f8b58851420ea7881bc053432032_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>，50岁</div><div id='b133f8b58851420ea7881bc053432032' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>入鄱阳湖，有诗。作品：鄱阳湖观打鱼。南康值雨。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在江州，有诗。作品：东林道上闲步三首（其一）东林道上闲步三首（其二）东林道上闲步三首（其三）东林道上闲步二首（其一）东林道上闲步二首（其二）<br /></div>

-----title
庐山
-----detail

-----title
星子
-----detail

-----title
武汉
-----detail

-----title
荆州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b1cb098cdbfb4dbb9f9d813338f76aba_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b1cb098cdbfb4dbb9f9d813338f76aba");'><span id='b1cb098cdbfb4dbb9f9d813338f76aba_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1104')">1102-1104年</a>，50-52岁</div><div id='b1cb098cdbfb4dbb9f9d813338f76aba' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年12月23日</a>　到荆南府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年12月26日</a>　在荆州。二十六日交割，交代胡安国。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年12月</a>　在荆州，有诗。作品：遇石首谒县官回作诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　在荆州。有文。作品：书义序。论语义序。孟子义序。<div id='poem_1206643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206643?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书义序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206643")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206643'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206643'>古者左史记言，右史记事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206643_comment'></div>《书》者，记言之史也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206643_comment'></div>上自唐虞，下迄于周，更千有馀年，圣贤之君继作，其流风善政，可传于后世者且载于百篇之《书》，今其存者五十有九篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206643_comment'></div>予窃以一言蔽之曰，中而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206643_comment'></div>尧之咨舜曰：「天之历数在尔躬，允执其中，四海困穷，天禄永终」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206643_comment'></div>舜亦以命禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206643_comment'></div>夫三圣相授，盖一道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206643_comment'></div>贵为天子而以天下与人，穷为匹夫而受人之天下，其相与授受之际，岂不重哉，而所言止此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206643_comment'></div>《仲虺之诰》称汤曰「建中于民」，箕子为武王陈洪范曰「皇建其有极」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206643_comment'></div>然则帝之所以为帝，王之所以为王，率此道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206643_comment'></div>予故以一言蔽之曰中而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206643_comment'></div>夫所谓中者，岂执一之谓哉，所贵乎时中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206643_comment'></div>时中者，当其可之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206643_comment'></div>尧授舜，舜授禹，受而不为泰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206643_comment'></div>汤放桀，武王伐纣，取而不为贪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206643_comment'></div>以至为臣而放其君，非篡也，为弟而诛其兄，非逆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206643_comment'></div>《书》之所载大伦大要不越是数者，以其事观之，岂不异哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206643_comment'></div>圣人安为之而不疑者，盖当其可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206643_comment'></div>是《尧典》之书为让舜而作，而其名谓之典，言大常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206643_comment'></div>盖苟当其可，虽以天下与人，犹为常而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206643_comment'></div>后世昧执中之权，而不知时措之宜，故徇名失实，流而为子哙之让，白公之争，自取绝灭者有之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206643_comment'></div>至或临之以兵而为忠，小不可忍而为仁，皆失是也，又乌足与论圣人之中道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206643_comment'></div>国家开设学校，建师儒之官，盖将讲明先王之道，以善天下，非徒为浮文以誇耀之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206643_comment'></div>以予之昏懦不肖，岂敢自谓足以充其任哉，姑诵所闻，以行其职耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206643_comment'></div>然圣言之奥，盖有言不能论而意不能致者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206643_comment'></div>诸君其慎思之，超然默会于言意之表，则庶乎有得矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1206643_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206644?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论语义序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206644")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206644'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206644'>学者之视圣人，其犹射之于正鹄乎，虽巧力所及，有远近中否之不齐，然未有不志乎正鹄而可以言射也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206644_comment'></div>士之去圣人或相倍蓰，或相什百，所造固不同，然未有不志乎圣人而可以言学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206644_comment'></div>道废千有馀年，百家之言盈天下，学者将安取正乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206644_comment'></div>质诸圣人而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206644_comment'></div>夫《论语》之书，孔子所以告其门人，群弟子所以学于孔子者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206644_comment'></div>圣学之传，其不在兹乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206644_comment'></div>然而其言近，其指远，世儒以其近也，易之以为童子之习而莫之究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206644_comment'></div>入德之途，背而去之，如在荒墟之中，曾无蘧庐以托宿焉，况能宅天下之广居乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206644_comment'></div>善夫伯乐之论马也，以为天下马不可以形容筋骨相，视其所视而遗其所不视，则马之绝尘弭辙者无遗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206644_comment'></div>余于是得为学之方焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206644_comment'></div>夫道之不可以言传也审矣，士欲窥圣学渊源，而区区于章句之末，是犹以形容筋骨而求天下马也，其可得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206644_comment'></div>余于是书也，于牝牡有不知者盖多矣，学者能视其所视而遗其所不视，则于余言其庶矣乎。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1206644_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206645?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孟子义序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206645")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206645_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206645'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206645'>道之不行久矣，自周衰以来，处士横议，儒墨异同之辩起，而是非相胜非一日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206645_comment'></div>孟子以睿知刚明之材，出于道学陵夷之后，非尧舜之道不陈于王前，非孔子之行不行于身，思以道援天下，绍复先王之令绪，其自任可谓至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206645_comment'></div>当是之时，人不知存亡之理，恃强威弱，挟众暴寡，以谓久安之势在此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206645_comment'></div>夫由其道，则七十里而兴，不由其道，虽天下而亡，古今之常理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206645_comment'></div>彼方恃强挟众，而骤以仁义之言诱之，动逆其所顺，则不悟其理，宜其迂阔而不足用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206645_comment'></div>故辙环于齐、鲁、晋、宋之郊，而道终不行，亦其势然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206645_comment'></div>虽膏泽不下于民，其志不施于事业，而世之赖其力亦岂鲜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206645_comment'></div>方世衰道微，使儒墨之辩息，而奸言诐行不得逞其志，无君无父之教不行于天下，而民免于禽兽，则其为功非小矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206645_comment'></div>古人谓孟子之功不在禹下，亦足为知言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206645_comment'></div>今其书具存，其要皆言行之迹而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206645_comment'></div>君子之言行无所不在道，肆诸笔舌以传后世，皆所以明道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206645_comment'></div>发诸身，措诸用舍，皆所以行道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206645_comment'></div>世之学者因言以求其理，由行以观其言，则圣人之庭户可渐而进矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206645_comment'></div>精思之，力行之，古之好学者皆然，而亦不肖之所望于诸君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206645_comment'></div>然圣道渊懿，非浅识所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206645_comment'></div>姑诵所闻，未知中否，诸君其择之，反以告焉，是亦朋友之义也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1206645_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　在荆州。有诗。作品：向和卿览余诗见赠次韵奉酬。江陵令张景常万卷堂。荆州书事二首（其一）荆州书事二首（其二）直舍书事。闲居书事（其一）闲居书事（其二）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　在荆州。有答胡康侯问学书。作品：答胡康侯（其一）答胡康侯（其二）<div id='poem_1206565' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206565' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206565?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答胡康侯书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206565")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206565_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206565'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206565'>辱疏示所疑，非公敦朋友之义，不以贤自挟，何能如是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206565_comment'></div>以能问于不能，以多问于寡，士无此风久矣，乃今得吾康侯也，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206565_comment'></div>以某之不肖，何足以知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206565_comment'></div>然不敢不尽所闻，以求切磋之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206565_comment'></div>言而是耶，固愿与朋友共之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206565_comment'></div>言而非耶，亦愿公见告，庶乎其有警也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206565_comment'></div>「致知格物」，盖言致知，当极尽物理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206565_comment'></div>理有不尽，则天下之物皆足以乱吾之知，思祈于意诚心正，远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206565_comment'></div>《书》云：「惟精惟一，允执厥中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206565_comment'></div>执中之道，精一是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206565_comment'></div>夫中者，不偏之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206565_comment'></div>一物不该焉，则偏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206565_comment'></div>《中庸》曰「喜怒哀乐之未发谓之中」，但于喜怒哀乐未发之时，以心验之时，中之义自见，非精一，乌能执之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206565_comment'></div>夫盈天地之间，孰非道乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206565_comment'></div>道而可离，则道有在矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206565_comment'></div>譬之四方有定位焉，适东则离乎西，适南则离乎北，斯可离也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206565_comment'></div>若夫无适而非道，则乌得而离耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206565_comment'></div>故寒而衣，饥而食，日出而作，晦而息，耳目之视听，手足之举履，无非道也，此百姓所以日用而不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206565_comment'></div>伊尹耕于有莘之野，以乐尧舜之道，夫尧舜之道，岂有物可玩而乐之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206565_comment'></div>即耕于有莘之野是已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206565_comment'></div>此农夫田父之所日用者，而伊尹之乐有在乎是，若伊尹，所谓知之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206565_comment'></div>夫精义入神乃所以致用，利用安身乃所以崇德，此合内外之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206565_comment'></div>天下之物，理一而分殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206565_comment'></div>知其理一，所以为仁，知其分殊，所以为义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206565_comment'></div>权其分之轻重，无铢分之差，则精矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206565_comment'></div>夫为仁由己尔，何力不足之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206565_comment'></div>颜渊之「克己复礼」，仲弓之「出门如见大宾，使民如承大祭」，若此，皆用力处也，但以身体之，当自知尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206565_comment'></div>夫通天下一气也，人受天地之中以生，其盈虚常与天地流通，宁非刚大乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206565_comment'></div>人惟自梏于形体，故不见其至大；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206565_comment'></div>不知集义所生，故不见其至刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206565_comment'></div>善养气者无加损焉，勿暴之而已，乃所谓直也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206565_comment'></div>用意以养之，皆揠苗者也，曲孰甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206565_comment'></div>某之鄙意如此，公试思之如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206565_comment'></div>适会同官黎君到，而来仆立候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206565_comment'></div>仓卒奉答，不逮意，幸亮之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1206565_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206566?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206566'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206566'>某辱示问，皆圣贤大致，某也何足以知，然试尝语其所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206566_comment'></div>孟子曰：「鸡鸣而起，孳孳为善，舜之徒也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206566_comment'></div>孳孳为利，蹠之徒也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206566_comment'></div>舜蹠之相去远矣，而其分乃在乎善利之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206566_comment'></div>故颜渊得一善则拳拳服膺而不敢失，其学为舜，亦曰「择善而固执之」而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206566_comment'></div>舜、文之圣，若合符节，则潜心乎文王者，亦岂外是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206566_comment'></div>《记》曰：「当其可之谓时」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206566_comment'></div>孔子圣之时，一当其可之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206566_comment'></div>故曰：「可以仕则仕，可以止则止，可以速则速，可以久则久」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206566_comment'></div>是皆天下之中道，非有甚高难行之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206566_comment'></div>故孟子曰「仲尼不为已甚者」，非真知之，乌能以是称孔子乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206566_comment'></div>然则所愿学者，亦求所谓当其可已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206566_comment'></div>夫参也鲁，疑非通敏之才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206566_comment'></div>然某切尝谓曾子竟以鲁得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206566_comment'></div>若夫便儇激厉，则其去道也远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206566_comment'></div>自孟子没，圣学失传，荀卿而下，皆未得其门而入者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206566_comment'></div>七篇之书具在，始终考之，不过道性善而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206566_comment'></div>知此，则天下之理得，而诸子之失其传皆可见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206566_comment'></div>夫学道者，舍先圣之书何求哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206566_comment'></div>譬之适九达之衢，未知所之，六经能指其攸趣而已，因其所指而之焉，则庶乎其有至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206566_comment'></div>徒敝精神于章句之间，则末矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206566_comment'></div>孔子固天纵之将圣也，其学宜不俟十年乃一进，盖圣人以其身为天下法，故言之序如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206566_comment'></div>颜渊未至乎从心，故未达者一间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206566_comment'></div>夫论伯夷之清，则圣人之清也，柳下惠之和，则圣人之和也，故孟子曰「皆古圣人也，未至乎大成，故孔子曰贤人而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206566_comment'></div>伊尹耕于有莘之野，汤三币聘之，乃幡然而改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206566_comment'></div>伯夷特不事非君尔，闻文作兴，则曰「盍归乎来」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206566_comment'></div>方伯夷居北海之滨，文王以三币聘之，伊尹居有莘之野，汤致之不以其道，二人者宜如何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206566_comment'></div>此未可论必进必退也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206566_comment'></div>伊尹利泽及天下，故孟子不言伊尹之风者，则后世又安得有弊乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206566_comment'></div>孔子之时去柳下惠亦未远矣，长沮、桀溺、荷蓧、楚狂之徒皆不进者也，柳下惠所以救其弊者，其效安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206566_comment'></div>孟子曰：「闻伯夷之风者，贪夫廉，懦夫有立志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206566_comment'></div>闻柳下惠之风者，鄙夫宽，薄夫敦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206566_comment'></div>第深考此言，则二人之风不为进退明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206566_comment'></div>然其风足以廉贪敦薄，故可为百世之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206566_comment'></div>论其学则必至于隘与不恭矣，此君子所以不由也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206566_comment'></div>田常为乱于齐，齐君盖弗胜也，宰予附田常，则谁得而杀之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206566_comment'></div>使其为齐君而死，则予何罪焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206566_comment'></div>当是时，有阚止字子我，死于田常之乱，是必传之者误而为宰我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206566_comment'></div>孔子谓「于予与何诛」，岂以予无质而遂弃之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206566_comment'></div>则人之有赖乎圣人者鲜矣，谓之不诛，乃所以切责之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206566_comment'></div>凡孔子之门人，皆未可以一言断其终身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206566_comment'></div>后之所进者多矣，与于四科，何足怪哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206566_comment'></div>管仲为政于齐，足以合诸侯而正天下，其功足录也，然学当为王者事，故仲尼之徒无道桓文者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206566_comment'></div>昔嬖奚与王良乘，王良曰：「吾为之范，我驰驱终日不获；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206566_comment'></div>一为之诡遇，一朝而获十」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206566_comment'></div>管仲之功，曾西未必能为之，然管仲之功诡遇也，诡遇而得禽兽，虽若丘陵弗为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206566_comment'></div>曾西羞比管仲，正类是欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206566_comment'></div>朋友道丧久矣，切磋之益，吾徒所当勉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206566_comment'></div>鄙意如此，恐未中理，愿以见告。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1206566_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1104')">1103-1104年</a>　在荆州。有诗。作品：送胡康候使湖南。诸宫观梅寄康侯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年5月4日</a>　在荆州。长子迪卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　在荆州。有诗。作品：送向和卿还京。天宁节。送赵循道赴都讲。直舍大风书事寄循道。荆州偶作。留别富宜德诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　在荆州。有答胡康侯问学书。作品：答胡康侯 其三。答胡康侯 其四。答胡康侯 其五。答胡康侯 其六。答胡康侯 其七。<div id='poem_1206567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答胡康侯书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206567")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206567'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206567'>示谕别后持五戒，益知进学之力也，欣慰欣慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206567_comment'></div>某窃谓古之善授戒者莫如孔子，善持戒者莫如颜渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206567_comment'></div>非礼勿视勿听，勿言勿动，持此，则士之所以修身慎行者无遗力矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206567_comment'></div>持之奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206567_comment'></div>曰礼而已，此一言足以蔽之，约而易守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206567_comment'></div>不窒其源而杜其末流，虽日省之，遇事辄发矣，不可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206567_comment'></div>《春秋义》探赜精到，恨不及见全书也，玩味钦叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206567_comment'></div>然《周官》有司盟之职，凡诅盟皆天子以吏治之，诸侯不得私相盟也，一有渝盟，则刑随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206567_comment'></div>春秋之时，诸侯不复听命于天子，故口血未乾，而报复之兵已至其境，失政刑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206567_comment'></div>凡书盟者，皆恶之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206567_comment'></div>《记》言「大道既隐，天下为家」，谓三代盛时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206567_comment'></div>商人作誓而民始畔，周人作会而民始疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206567_comment'></div>若《汤誓》、《秦誓》之类，盖汤武之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206567_comment'></div>此数者似非圣人之言，恐不足引以为證，更思之如何。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1206567_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206568?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206568'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206568'>《正蒙》之书，关中学者尊信之与《论语》等，其徒未尝轻以示人，盖恐未信者，不惟无益，徒增其鄙慢尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206568_comment'></div>如《西铭》一篇，伊川谓与孟子性善养气之论同功，皆前圣所未发也，详味之，乃见其用意之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206568_comment'></div>性命之说，虽扬雄犹未能造其藩篱，况他人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206568_comment'></div>而世儒易言之，多见其妄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206568_comment'></div>孔子曰：「五十而知天命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206568_comment'></div>以孔子之圣，犹待五十而后知，其所知盖有未易言者，非止如世儒之说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206568_comment'></div>学者当求之，圣人不当徒为空言而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206568_comment'></div>公之笃志好学，而每蒙谦虚，不见鄙外，故辄肆言之，而不自知其愚也，惟亮之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206568_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206569?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206569_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206569'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206569'>承示及《春秋事实》，鄙意犹有疑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206569_comment'></div>所论虞氏之史，直书其君之名而不避，载其父母昆弟之恶而不隐，某窃谓四岳称舜之父顽、母嚚、象傲，乃舜在侧微未登庸之时言之，宜若无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206569_comment'></div>周人虽以讳事神而有谥法，然且名之曰幽厉，孝子慈孙百世不能改，则虽有谥，其恶犹不隐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206569_comment'></div>《礼》曰「临文不讳」，故文王名昌，而《雍》之诗曰「克昌厥后」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206569_comment'></div>武王名发，而《小宛》之诗曰「明发不寐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206569_comment'></div>若此类，皆临文不讳也，虽周亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206569_comment'></div>庄公名同，而书「同盟」，僖公名申，而书「戊申」，不可谓从虞史之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206569_comment'></div>「将仲子」、「叔于田」皆刺庄公也，「清人」刺文公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206569_comment'></div>不胜其母而害其弟，诗人以刺庄公，而不及段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206569_comment'></div>使高克将兵久而不召，众散而归，诗人以刺文公而不及克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206569_comment'></div>以庄、文之罪著矣，不待《春秋》书之而后见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206569_comment'></div>鄙意如此，更思之如何。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1206569_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206570?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206570_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206570'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206570'>刘质夫受经于明道、伊川之门积有年矣，其论元年之义详甚，某故未敢轻议其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206570_comment'></div>蒙录示第一段，义非高明不见鄙外，何以得此，幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206570_comment'></div>公之用意精深，非浅陋所能窥其阃奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206570_comment'></div>然意有所疑，义不敢默，姑试言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206570_comment'></div>所谓元者，仁也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206570_comment'></div>仁者，心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206570_comment'></div>《春秋》深明其义，当自贵者始，故治国先正其心，其说似太支离矣，恐改元初无此意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206570_comment'></div>三代正朔如忠、质、文之尚，循环无端，不可增损也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206570_comment'></div>秦以亥为正，失其旨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206570_comment'></div>斗纲之端连贯营室，织女之纪指牵牛之初，以纪日月，故曰星纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206570_comment'></div>五星起其初，日月起其中，其时为冬至，其辰为丑，三代各据一统，明三统常合而迭为首，周环五行之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206570_comment'></div>周据天统，以时言也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206570_comment'></div>商据地统，以辰言也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206570_comment'></div>夏据人统，以人事言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206570_comment'></div>故三代之时，惟夏为正，谓春秋以周正纪事是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206570_comment'></div>正朔必自天子出，改正朔恐圣人不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206570_comment'></div>若谓以夏时冠月，如定公元年冬十月陨霜杀菽，若以夏时言之，则十月陨霜，乃其时也，不足为灾异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206570_comment'></div>周十月乃夏之八月，若以夏时冠月，当曰秋十月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206570_comment'></div>正朔如建子丑是也，虽用夏时月，不可谓改正朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206570_comment'></div>鄙意如此，公试思之如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206570_comment'></div>如未中理，更希疏示，以开未悟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1206570_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206571' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206571?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206571_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206571'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206571'>圣学不明，士志于道者往往汩于世习而不知，虽英才异禀，卒能自拔于流俗者无几也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206571_comment'></div>某尝私窃谓学者之视圣人，其犹射者之于正鹄乎，虽巧力所及，有远近中否之不齐，未有不至于正鹄而可以言射也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206571_comment'></div>士之去圣人或相倍蓰，或相什百，所造固不同，未有不同乎圣人而可以言学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206571_comment'></div>譬之升堂奥者，必得其门而入乃可至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206571_comment'></div>过其藩，望望然去之，则终身不能至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206571_comment'></div>然则至学非难，知所以学为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206571_comment'></div>某愚不自量力之不足也，妄有意焉，思得朋游共学，左右提掖，觊获一游其藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206571_comment'></div>乃今得康侯，盖知衰老之有望也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206571_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　在荆州。有答陈瓘书。陈瓘得答书及诗，深喜所方言中其病，乃复书，称以“先生”作品：答陈莹中  其一。答陈莹中  其二。答陈莹中  其三。答陈莹中  其四。答陈莹中  其五。答陈莹中  其六。<div id='poem_1206557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答陈莹中书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206557")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206557'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206557'>辱示《华严大旨》，辞义精奥，得所未闻，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206557_comment'></div>然此书昔尝读之，虽未尽解，要之大略可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206557_comment'></div>其论布施也，至于刳心剔髓而不吝，此其用心广矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206557_comment'></div>来书所谓其施也不欲狭，其济也不欲寡，岂不信然欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206557_comment'></div>然某每读孟子书，至其论墨子「苟利天下，虽摩顶放踵为之」，未尝不悯其为人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206557_comment'></div>原其心，岂有他哉，盖亦施不欲狭，济不欲寡而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206557_comment'></div>此与世之横目自营者，固不可同日议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206557_comment'></div>而孟子力攻之，至比禽兽，孟子岂责人已甚乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206557_comment'></div>盖君子所以施诸身，措之天下，各欲当其可而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206557_comment'></div>禹思天下之溺，犹己溺之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206557_comment'></div>稷思天下之饥，犹己饥之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206557_comment'></div>过门不入，弗子其子，至胼胝手足而不为病，君子不谓之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206557_comment'></div>颜渊在陋巷，饭蔬饮水，终日如愚人，然君子不谓之不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206557_comment'></div>盖禹、稷被发缨冠而往救之者也，颜渊闭户者也，故孟子曰「易地则皆然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206557_comment'></div>若颜渊、禹、稷不当其可，则是杨墨而已，君子不与也，此古人之样辙章章明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206557_comment'></div>今公卿大夫比肩在上，则天下有任其责者，自惟愚鄙无所用于世，虽闭户可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206557_comment'></div>故不敢出位冒天下之责而任之，以贻身忧，非忘天下也，循古样辙而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206557_comment'></div>若谓「不辞一身之有过，愿成来者之无过」，窃意贤知者过之，则道终不明不行矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206557_comment'></div>而欲来者之无过，或恐未能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206557_comment'></div>所谓「仲尼无言，颜子有言」，考之吾儒之书，不知所自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206557_comment'></div>荒芜之学，欲质于左右者非一二事，愿无惜见教，以开未悟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1206557_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206558' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206558' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206558?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206558_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206558'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206558'>康节先天之学不传于世，非妙契天地之心不足以知此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206558_comment'></div>某盖尝玩之，而陋识浅闻未及足以叩其关键。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206558_comment'></div>八卦有定位，而先天以《乾》、《巽》居南，《坤》、《震》居北，《离》、《兑》居东，《坎》、《艮》居西；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206558_comment'></div>又以十数分配八卦，独《艮》、《坎》同为三数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206558_comment'></div>此必有说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206558_comment'></div>以爻当期，其原出于《系辞》，而以星日气候分布诸爻，《易》未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206558_comment'></div>其说详于纬书，世传《稽览图》是也，扬子草《玄》盖用此耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206558_comment'></div>卦气起于《中孚》，冬至卦也，《太玄》以《中》准之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206558_comment'></div>其次《复》卦，《太玄》以《周》准之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206558_comment'></div>《升》，大寒卦也，《太玄》以《千》准之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206558_comment'></div>今之历书亦然，则自汉迄今同用此说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206558_comment'></div>而先天以《复》为冬至，《噬嗑》为大寒，又谓八卦与文王异，若此类，皆莫能晓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206558_comment'></div>康节之学究极天人之蕴，玩味之久，未能窥其端倪，况敢议其是非耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206558_comment'></div>以公之精识贯通古今，于先天必能洞见之矣，愿疏示一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206558_comment'></div>所论康节学伏羲，温公学仲尼，某亦不知其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206558_comment'></div>夫自八卦重而为六十四，《易》之大成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206558_comment'></div>孔子于《易》，赞之而已，窃谓无所加损焉，而分为二说，皆深所未谕也，并乞开示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206558_comment'></div>夫孔子之赞《易》，尤详于《乾》、《坤》二卦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206558_comment'></div>《系辞》中论释诸爻亦多矣，然未有及象数者，岂得意而忘象，真孔子之学耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206558_comment'></div>无由面承，东望徒增企仰耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1206558_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206559' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206559' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206559?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206559_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206559'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206559'>辱示法界三门大旨，引据精博，极儒佛之奥，使蔽陋者与闻焉，幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206559_comment'></div>然其间鄙意有疑者，敢不请？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206559_comment'></div>《系辞》曰：「爻有等，故曰物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206559_comment'></div>物相杂，故曰文」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206559_comment'></div>《贲》之《彖》曰：「柔来而文刚，分刚上而文柔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206559_comment'></div>刚柔相杂，贲之所以为文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206559_comment'></div>「白贲」，受色者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206559_comment'></div>「贲无色」，色色者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206559_comment'></div>惟有质为能受，惟无色为能贲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206559_comment'></div>爻之辞曰「白贲」，而卒乃曰「贲无色」，斯谓之普融可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206559_comment'></div>以文会友，以友辅仁，此学者之事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206559_comment'></div>谓之会色归空，吾儒之书或恐无此意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206559_comment'></div>孟子曰：「固哉，高叟之为诗也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206559_comment'></div>则为诗犹有得失焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206559_comment'></div>为之如高叟，是固而已，非知诗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206559_comment'></div>则为之一言，恐未足以蔽二《南》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206559_comment'></div>孔子曰：「诗三百，一言以蔽之曰思无邪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206559_comment'></div>则二《南》固在其中矣，恐不须他求也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206559_comment'></div>颜渊三月不违仁，非由仁者，盖有时而违也，然而其复不远矣，故以《复》之初爻当之，复之未远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206559_comment'></div>《坤》之初六曰「履霜坚冰至」，夫坤之初，阴始凝也，未至乎坚冰矣，而卒乎坚冰者理之必至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206559_comment'></div>辨之者不于始凝之时，而于坚冰而后辨，则鲜不及矣，若鲁昭公、高贵乡公是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206559_comment'></div>此二爻以禹、稷、颜渊出入往来之事当之，亦恐不相似也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206559_comment'></div>夫《乾》一变而为《姤》，五变而为《剥》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206559_comment'></div>《坤》一变而为《复》，五变而为《剥》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206559_comment'></div>《复》者阳之来，而《剥》者阴之极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206559_comment'></div>阳极生阴，阴极生阳，故剥穷而反，反而复阴极故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206559_comment'></div>窃意《剥》者，其《乾》之终乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206559_comment'></div>自古乱臣贼子，其初岂有意哉，驯致其道，以至于此耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206559_comment'></div>故《易》于小人几微之际每致意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206559_comment'></div>《姤》之辞曰：「女壮，勿用取女」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206559_comment'></div>《姤》之初，阴始生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206559_comment'></div>女也者，阴始生之象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206559_comment'></div>始生，未至于壮也，而有壮之道焉，犹《坤》所谓「履霜坚冰至」也，故曰「勿用取女」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206559_comment'></div>盖取之则引而与之齐，引而与之齐，则终末如之何也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206559_comment'></div>昔阳城之于唐，其任职非不久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206559_comment'></div>其初裴延龄未用也，不于未壮之时止之，至天子将用为相，乃欲取白麻裂之，而哭于庭，岂不晚乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206559_comment'></div>夫白麻，王言也，不可裂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206559_comment'></div>天子之庭，非哭所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206559_comment'></div>以是而处昏主乱相之间，其免也，幸而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206559_comment'></div>故《姤》之初六曰「系于金柅」，盖于其未壮而止之，使勿行也，与《坤》初六异矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206559_comment'></div>《坤》之《文言》曰：「履霜坚冰至，盖言顺也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206559_comment'></div>而其卒也，有疑阳之战，顺而无以止之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206559_comment'></div>自《姤》至于《剥》，阴之进极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206559_comment'></div>《坤》顺而《艮》止，《剥》之所以成象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206559_comment'></div>观《剥》之象，则知所以治剥矣，故曰：「顺而止之，观象也，君子尚消息盈虚，天行也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206559_comment'></div>消息盈虚，天且不能暴为之，而况于人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206559_comment'></div>然君子之尚消息盈虚，无时而不然，独于《剥》言之者，盖君子小人相为消长，至《剥》而极矣，此成败之机，而邦之兴丧系焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206559_comment'></div>虽动息语默之微，一失其机，不可复救矣，况施于事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206559_comment'></div>东汉之衰，君子欲以力胜之，引奸凶而授之柄，卒至乎俱伤两败，而国随以亡，不知此故也，后之治剥者可不监之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206559_comment'></div>至于《剥》，则阳之进极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206559_comment'></div>君子众而小人独，其夬之易矣，然疾之已甚，乱也，故苋陆夬夬，虽中行仅无咎而已，未光也，况过之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206559_comment'></div>当是时，若禹之班师可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206559_comment'></div>夫乱世不能无君子，治世不能无小人，特其消长异耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206559_comment'></div>此天地之义，阴阳之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206559_comment'></div>故治世能使小人不为恶而已，不能绝之使无也，此处夬之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206559_comment'></div>承示论《坤》、《复》之义，故辄及此、以取质左右，高明以为如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206559_comment'></div>或未中理，幸明教我。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1206559_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206560?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206560_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206560'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206560'>康节先生，某少尝闻其风矣，每恨不及见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206560_comment'></div>洛中诸尝从先生游者皆略识之，亦尝见其子，问之，俱莫能传其所学万一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206560_comment'></div>前书所疑，虽蒙谆诲，愚陋终未能晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206560_comment'></div>夫八卦有伏羲、文王之辨，于经无见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206560_comment'></div>天下之赜存焉，岂人私智能为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206560_comment'></div>康节之言必有稽也，索隐之士宜知其所以然者，恨未得亲叩之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206560_comment'></div>《乾》南而《坤》北，《离》上而《坎》下，位不同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206560_comment'></div>自《乾》左而至《震》，一二三四；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206560_comment'></div>自《坤》右而至《巽》，八七六五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206560_comment'></div>本宫之卦，《乾》一《兑》二，《离》三《震》四，《坤》一《艮》二，《坎》三《巽》四，数不同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206560_comment'></div>以为未尝同，默而识之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206560_comment'></div>位与数相为异同者明如此，安得无说乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206560_comment'></div>自羲、农以来，更六七圣人，所因习者八卦而已，六十四卦之名未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206560_comment'></div>其制器尚象乃有取于十三卦，则羲、农之世卦虽未重，而六十四卦之用已在炉锤之中矣，特其名未显也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206560_comment'></div>故曰：八卦成，列象在其中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206560_comment'></div>用是言之，文王之《易》固具于伏羲画卦之初，文王能因而用之，不能有所加损也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206560_comment'></div>《乾》、《坤》、《屯》、《蒙》之序，意必文王为之，孔子序卦，特释其义而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206560_comment'></div>《乾》、《履》、《大有》、《大壮》之序，于《易》不见其端倪，所谓文王阖其门而拒其出者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206560_comment'></div>「文王阖之，康节辟之」，其数其义，必有可玩而习者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206560_comment'></div>凡此，皆某所深疑而未谕也，愿略疏示，使得稽其门，叩其键而入，则为赐多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206560_comment'></div>《太玄》之书，昔尝读之，虽未竟其义，而其略可识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206560_comment'></div>子云覃思浑天，三摹而四分之，极于八十一首，旁则三摹九据，极之七百二十九赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206560_comment'></div>当期之日，又为踦嬴二赞，以尽馀分之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206560_comment'></div>其用自天元推一昼一夜，阴阳数度、星日之纪，与《泰初历》相应，其取数似与《易》异矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206560_comment'></div>其为书则欲自成一家，初无意于赞《易》也，考诸《解难》之文可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206560_comment'></div>夫《易》之六十四卦，八卦相错而成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206560_comment'></div>《玄》之有方、州、部、家，则各有分域矣，不可相错也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206560_comment'></div>故一而三之，自三而九，又三之为二十七，终于八十一，而《玄》之首毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206560_comment'></div>八十一家又离为三，以极三玄之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206560_comment'></div>方、州、部各三之为九，又三之为二十七家，此一玄之数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206560_comment'></div>以次比之，不可相易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206560_comment'></div>赞辞自一至九，配丽五行，而日星节候分布其间，皆有成数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206560_comment'></div>恐其书特《易》中之一事，与《易经》不尽相涉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206560_comment'></div>世之治历者守成法而已，非知历也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206560_comment'></div>自汉迄今，历法之更不知其几人，未有不知历理而能创法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206560_comment'></div>求《玄》于历理之内，亦恐未足以尽《玄》之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206560_comment'></div>更深考之，并以见教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206560_comment'></div>近得温公《太玄论》阅之，皆先儒所共知者，其隐赜不著之事，殆未可窥其蕴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206560_comment'></div>温公之学笃于自信，虽《论语》亦有未然者，非其深造自得，隐之于心而不疑，不轻以为信，真善学者，与世之耳濡目染遂以为得者有间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206560_comment'></div>然子云、温公之学与《语》、《孟子》书，其远近浅深必有能辨之者，不可诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206560_comment'></div>温公自孔子而下，独以扬雄为知道，雄之论孟子曰：「知言之要，知德之奥，非苟知之，亦允蹈之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206560_comment'></div>又曰：「诸子者，以其异于孔子也，孟子异乎，不异乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206560_comment'></div>雄之言以孟子不异于孔子，则其尊孟子也至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206560_comment'></div>温公于孟子乃疑之，则虽以雄为知道，而于雄书亦未尽信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206560_comment'></div>夫众言殽乱折诸圣，自汉田、焦、费氏之学兴，而三家之传不一，后虽名儒继出，而异说益滋，《易》之微言隐矣，学者将安折衷乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206560_comment'></div>折诸孔子而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206560_comment'></div>某尝用是学《易》，以谓孔子之已言者，当详说而谨守之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206560_comment'></div>其未言而不见其兆者，虽略之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206560_comment'></div>《皇极》之书，皆孔子之所未言者，然其论古今治乱成败之变，若合符节，故不敢略之，恨未得其门而入耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206560_comment'></div>至其论《易》、《诗》、《春秋》，配四时之府、生长收藏，与《易》之《诗》、《易》之《书》、《易》之《春秋》之类，窃恐圣人复起，未能不易其言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206560_comment'></div>譬之观奕，必以李、刘为信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206560_comment'></div>《法言》曰：「杨墨塞路，孟子辞而辟之，廓如也，后之塞路者有矣，窃自比于孟子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206560_comment'></div>夫孟、扬之自任重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206560_comment'></div>由汉而来，士以李、刘望之非一日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206560_comment'></div>今其书具在，疑而未信者如此，则后之视今，又焉知不犹今之视昔乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206560_comment'></div>学者审其是而已，于疑信尤当慎择也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206560_comment'></div>然某于雄，昔尝疑之，重蒙诲谕，继今当力求之以补前过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206560_comment'></div>末由展晤，一快蔽蒙，东望徒增惓耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1206560_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206561?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206561'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206561'>恶诗非敢自附于贤者之作，厚意不可虚辱，故勉强继之，重蒙称与过当，徒用增愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206561_comment'></div>「先生」，有德齿之称也，宜施于前辈，如某之不肖，徒有犬马之齿耳，辄以见称，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206561_comment'></div>恐闻者以为失言，使老拙者重为世所讪笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206561_comment'></div>继此幸削去，至恳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206561_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206562?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206562'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206562'>《孟子》之书，世儒未尝深考之，故尊之者或过其实，疑之者或损其真，非灼知圣贤之心，未易以私意论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206562_comment'></div>世之尊孟子者多失其传，非孟子过也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206562_comment'></div>而遂疑之，亦过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206562_comment'></div>近见一书，力诋孟子之非，恐非有所授，难遽以口舌争也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206562_comment'></div>无由展奉，一尽区区。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1206562_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　在荆州。有文。作品：请媒书。婚书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　在荆州。有和陈瓘诗。陈瓘得答书及诗，深喜所方言中其病，乃复书，称以“先生”作品：和陈莹中了斋自警六绝(画前有易方知易)和陈莹中了斋自警六绝(八荒同宇混车书)和陈莹中了斋自警六绝(行藏须信执中难)和陈莹中了斋自警六绝(造次欲安嗟孰是)和陈莹中了斋自警六绝(圣门事业学须强)和陈莹中了斋自警六绝(盈科日进几时休)<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　在荆州。有诗。作品：次韵何吉老游金銮寺。和席季成游金銮寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　有语录记甲申(1104年)四月至乙酉（1105年）十一月事。作品：荆州所闻。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='42bc6b981c2142629a57e3211ccb90b5_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年2月21日</a>　离荆州，如京师。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4b01eaa6fa44481883ebda875b4d74c8_label'><a href='javascript: -----title
鄂州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3c675e9c8d6c4710a4e4a06cb218d358_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3c675e9c8d6c4710a4e4a06cb218d358");'><span id='3c675e9c8d6c4710a4e4a06cb218d358_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>，53岁</div><div id='3c675e9c8d6c4710a4e4a06cb218d358' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年7月</a>　在荆州。如武昌为考试出题，有策问。作品：策问（1-11）<div id='poem_1206804' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206804' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206804?labeling=true' target='_blank'>策问<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206804")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206804_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206804'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206804'>书契之兴，至数千百岁，其间圣帝明王、公侯、贤士大夫、暴君污吏、梼杌嵬琐之人、贤妃淑女、艳妻嬖妾，与夫山林居穷处独之士，隐德潜耀，见于载籍，盖不可胜记焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206804_comment'></div>然历世绵远，编脱简去，其存而略可知者亦未易一二数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206804_comment'></div>班固表古今人，列为九等之序，究极经传，旁质诸子，驰骋数千岁之中，如度量权衡之较物，铢分不遗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206804_comment'></div>抑其书有所受欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206804_comment'></div>将亦奋私智而为之欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206804_comment'></div>何其说之详明也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206804_comment'></div>夫由千载而下，而上论千载之人，智愚贤否，俦列等降，若亲觌焉，斯亦难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206804_comment'></div>其是非得失，亦将必有在矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206804_comment'></div>诸君试考而折衷之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1206804_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206805' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206805' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206805?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206805_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206805'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206805'>孟子没，圣学失传，六经之旨晦蚀于异端，诸子之书名家而传后世者，非一人也，然而论不诡于圣人者无几焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206805_comment'></div>扬雄之《太玄》，王通之《续经》，皆拟圣人之作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206805_comment'></div>二人者亦以斯文为己任，其为书宜有异于诸子焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206805_comment'></div>然当时之论尚或以雄非圣人而作经，犹吴楚之君僭号而称王，盖贬绝之罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206805_comment'></div>后之论通者亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206805_comment'></div>予以谓为此论者，是特以名讥之，未究其实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206805_comment'></div>使其书不谬于圣人，而有补于六经，则二子也奚罪焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206805_comment'></div>学者审其是而已，又奚以名为然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206805_comment'></div>观雄之书，三摹、四分、九据，极八十首、七百二十九赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206805_comment'></div>其用自天元推一昼一夜，阴阳气候，星日度数，律历之纪，无不备具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206805_comment'></div>其闳意妙旨，驰骋乎有无之际，可谓至矣，其于《易》也何准焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206805_comment'></div>通之《续经》，其始终之义，四名五志，策命诰诏，赞议诫谏，断疑褒贬之法，具载于其书，可考而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206805_comment'></div>诸君试明其所以准《易》之旨，与夫《续经》之作，是非得失，详择而折衷之，以释论者之疑焉，毋或谓其僭拟而不足道也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206805_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206806' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206806' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206806?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206806_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206806'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206806'>古者士不患无名，而患实之不至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206806_comment'></div>不患无位，而患德之不孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206806_comment'></div>故公卿大夫士至于抱关击柝、乘田委吏之贱，皆因实与名，量能授位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206806_comment'></div>其养之有素，考之有渐，而贤愚善否，不容相淆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206806_comment'></div>此三代所以直道而行，而士亦无觊觎于其间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206806_comment'></div>周衰，教养选士之法废，而纵横之士始相与乘时射利，观时君之好，因其刚柔缓急、喜怒爱恶之变，阳开阴阖，以迁惑其志，摇吻动喙，卒取卿相者，无国无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206806_comment'></div>自是朝无常度，而士亦鲜克有廉耻之行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206806_comment'></div>汉初，刬除前弊，诏举贤良方正，州郡察孝廉，中兴以后，复增四行，以网罗遗逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206806_comment'></div>其规范虽未足方古，其犹庶几乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206806_comment'></div>唐以六科取士，至杨绾举词藻宏丽，又加诗赋，国家因之，专用声律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206806_comment'></div>熙宁更新法度，登延儒臣，讲明六经之旨，尽革雕虫之习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206806_comment'></div>未十馀年间，士之应科举者类皆剽掠补缀，迭相祖袭，有司眩于铨择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206806_comment'></div>识者患之，欲复加诗赋，而国论未一，诸君究观前世得失，试详明之，无或隐焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1206806_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206807' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206807' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206807?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206807_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206807'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206807'>宗庙之制尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206807_comment'></div>汉兴至本始间，凡祖宗庙与在郡国者合百六十七所，其岁时祠祀，与卫士、祝宰、乐人皆以钜万数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206807_comment'></div>至元帝时，贡禹始议罢郡国庙，定迭毁之礼，未及施行而禹卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206807_comment'></div>其后天子追用其议，然而通儒或非之，异论纷如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206807_comment'></div>而班固述父彪之言，则独称刘歆之论博而笃，其是非安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206807_comment'></div>幸详明之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1206807_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206808?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206808'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206808'>羿，天下之善射也，而弓拨矢钩，则虽羿不能取中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206808_comment'></div>造父，天下之善御者也，而舆脱马疲，则虽造父不能以致远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206808_comment'></div>人主，天下之利势也，而辅之以庸人小夫，则虽有利势，其能为治乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206808_comment'></div>予观虞、周之间，何其盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206808_comment'></div>以舜、武之为君，后稷、周、召之为臣，而相与共成帝王之业，岂不易欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206808_comment'></div>孔子称曰才难，则自古豪杰俊伟之人固不可多得，而后可以为治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206808_comment'></div>西汉之初，承暴秦残刻之馀，高惠之间，卒至太平，其佐命之臣，则若有萧、曹而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206808_comment'></div>孝宣中兴，丙、魏有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206808_comment'></div>兹四人者，皆卓然一代之良弼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206808_comment'></div>唐兴垂三百年，则亦前称房、杜，后称姚、宋而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206808_comment'></div>所谓豪杰俊伟之人自古不可多得者，岂不信然欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206808_comment'></div>然汉唐之治，号称近古，而文采足以表见于后世者，抑亦兹数人之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206808_comment'></div>其致治之方，所操之术，亦必有可言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206808_comment'></div>然卒不能追复舜、武之盛，以自附于伊、周、禹、稷之列者，其故何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206808_comment'></div>岂所操之术有未尽欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206808_comment'></div>然是数人者之器业远近优劣，亦可以概见，诸君其悉著于篇，以观所学。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1206808_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206809' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206809' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206809?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206809_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206809'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206809'>《传》曰「财用足故百志成，百志成故礼乐兴」，自古帝王不易之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206809_comment'></div>熙宁更新百度，无非以理财为务，其知此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206809_comment'></div>故谓之青苗以宽民之财，免役以宽民之力，立市易以权货贿之与通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206809_comment'></div>使兼并无所侵渔，而穷乏者安其生，农得尽力于耕，而游惰兼有所事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206809_comment'></div>其施设之意厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206809_comment'></div>然未十有年间，羡馀之息充溢府库，而民反有受其弊者，其故何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206809_comment'></div>是岂立法之方未尽与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206809_comment'></div>主上锐意于为治，凡法有害于民者，一切蠲除之，可谓善矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206809_comment'></div>然抑兼并，振穷乏，宽民力，役游惰，其可无术乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206809_comment'></div>将欲数者之利，而无其害，学者宜知其说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206809_comment'></div>幸悉陈之，以俟采择焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1206809_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206810' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206810' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206810?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206810_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206810'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206810'>光武不以功臣任职，议者多非之，史氏谓深图远算，将有以焉，其说安在？</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1206810_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206811' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206811' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206811?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206811_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206811'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206811'>周德衰，圣王不作，寇攘争取之祸起，而名实不加于天下久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206811_comment'></div>孔子惧而作《春秋》，以明先王之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206811_comment'></div>纲条大小，罔不毕举，善善恶恶，因实称情，而轻重长短，各中权度，无锱铢分毫之差，振幽显微，而乱臣贼子知惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206811_comment'></div>孔子没，更战国至秦，遂焚书坑学，微言中绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206811_comment'></div>汉兴，六艺残缺，盖久而后完，而《春秋》之学列为三家，虽异端竞起，然自通才博识，未有不由此而学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206811_comment'></div>国家崇尚经术，以训释之，造极其精微，而于《春秋》独废而不讲，是何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206811_comment'></div>议者欲置博士，与诸经比，或者其可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206811_comment'></div>幸明言之，将以告于有司。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206811_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206812' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206812' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206812?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206812_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206812'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206812'>三代之政亡，而暴君污吏慢其经界，天下无常产，自战国以来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206812_comment'></div>民无常产则无常心，乘之以饥馑，则老弱者操瓢囊，转乎沟壑，壮者则聚而为盗，此其常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206812_comment'></div>国家兴利脩废，务以保民为心，独能无意于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206812_comment'></div>然乘千载之弊，将欲追复三代之政，使天下之人各有常产，宜何施而可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206812_comment'></div>幸明言之，抑亦观诸君之所蕴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1206812_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206813' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206813' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206813?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206813_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206813'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206813'>三代教学废，而礼义之泽竭，士无中行，非特今日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206813_comment'></div>熙宁之初，天子尤锐意于辟雍成均之法，以作新人材为务，其有不在于兹乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206813_comment'></div>然士虽无卑近之习，而忠信之道微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206813_comment'></div>革雕虫之弊，而浮诞诡异之风炽，薄廉耻而敦进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206813_comment'></div>则士之失又不特无中行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206813_comment'></div>今将欲追三代教学之法，以渐磨士类，使无过行，宜何施而可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206813_comment'></div>博古之君子，幸详言之毋隐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206813_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206814?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年7月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206814'>荆江合蜀，众水所委，源高而流下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206814_comment'></div>自夷陵以东，地多沮洳陂泽，无高山大陵以为阻固，所恃以御水者，堤防而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206814_comment'></div>人力一不至，则靡溃千里，潴为平流，不见涯涘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206814_comment'></div>昔人有支为九河以疏瀹之者，而后水之为患消，荆人利之，非一日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206814_comment'></div>濒河之民，玩习久安，乃始盗河为田，而河之故道湮没无复存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206814_comment'></div>比年以来，水患浸剧，而今岁为尤甚，意者其职此之由乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206814_comment'></div>国家修明百度，置丞以贰令，正以变移水陆为先务，苟可以除民患者，亦无不举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206814_comment'></div>诸君亲被其害者，知其所自矣，愿详言之，将以告于有司。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206814_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
