-----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bb009372ff2d4df2b08ee93a14a49f62_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bb009372ff2d4df2b08ee93a14a49f62");'><span id='bb009372ff2d4df2b08ee93a14a49f62_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>，56岁</div><div id='bb009372ff2d4df2b08ee93a14a49f62' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年1月</a>　在余杭。正月，差出越州为考试出题。作品：策问（12-17）<div id='poem_1206815' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206815' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206815?labeling=true' target='_blank'>策问<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206815")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206815_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206815'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206815'>孔子曰：「足食足兵，民信之矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206815_comment'></div>于斯三者，不得已而去之，则先兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206815_comment'></div>又不得已而去之，则先食，而信不可去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206815_comment'></div>夫圣人恃民之信如此其重也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206815_comment'></div>国家遴选儒臣镇抚兹土，师出有名，士以义奋，投甲徒扬，以趋敌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206815_comment'></div>鴃舌之酋，系颈束手，为地千里，绍成先志，可谓盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206815_comment'></div>议者犹患兵食之不足，而有戍役转输之劳，不可以持久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206815_comment'></div>诸君境地相邻，宜习知其利害，而承学之久，孔子所谓去兵去食而恃民之信，亦必有说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206815_comment'></div>幸详言之毋隐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1206815_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206816' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206816' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206816?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206816_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206816'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206816'>孟子没，圣人之道不传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206816_comment'></div>六经微言晦蚀于异论，士不知所以学，非一日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206816_comment'></div>自熙宁以来，训明经术，以风多士，所以迪之，可谓至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206816_comment'></div>然大学之道，必先知所止，知所止然后能定，能定然后能应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206816_comment'></div>不知所止而欲应酬曲当，是犹射者未知正鹄之所在而欲取中也，其可得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206816_comment'></div>诸君承学之久，宜知所止矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206816_comment'></div>异时施于有政，将必有道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206816_comment'></div>愿试言之，以观攸趋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206816_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206817' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206817' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206817?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206817_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206817'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206817'>孟子言：「禹、稷、颜回同道」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206817_comment'></div>夫回之在陋巷，饭蔬饮水，终日如愚人，然邈乎其若无意于世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206817_comment'></div>禹思天下之溺者犹己溺之也，稷思天下之饥者犹己之饥也，其以身任天下之责，可谓重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206817_comment'></div>则三人者，疑若内外之不相及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206817_comment'></div>而孟子曰「易地则皆然」，则古之人所以修身善世之道，盖一而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206817_comment'></div>后世道学不明，士大夫穷而善其身，则进无以经世之务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206817_comment'></div>汲汲于事功，则退无以处箪瓢捽茹之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206817_comment'></div>自汉唐以来，往往皆是也，其失果安在哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206817_comment'></div>国家比诏有司，推原熙、丰三舍之令，播告之修，所以迪士者至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206817_comment'></div>盖将养天下之成材，而望之以禹、稷之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206817_comment'></div>承学之士，宜知古人所以修身善世之道，与夫后世之失，躬蹈而力行之，以副朝廷出长入治之选，请试言之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1206817_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206818' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206818' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206818?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206818_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206818'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206818'>三代之政亡，暴君污吏慢其经界，天下无常产，自战国以来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206818_comment'></div>民无常产则无常心，乘之以饥馑，则流亡转徙救死之不赡，欲驱而之善，尚可得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206818_comment'></div>国家修明百度，凛凛乎成周之际矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206818_comment'></div>议者欲为限田之法，渐复古制，此三代甚盛之举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206818_comment'></div>然豪宗大族富连阡陌，一旦夺其有馀以与不足，得无纷纷乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206818_comment'></div>此当今之要务，施设之方，学者宜知其说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206818_comment'></div>幸详言之，将以献于有司。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206818_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206819' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206819' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206819?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206819_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206819'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206819'>无君子莫治野人，无野人莫养君子，此天下之常分，古今之通义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206819_comment'></div>先王度地以居民，分田以制禄，五家之寡，则以一下士长之，其治野人可谓详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206819_comment'></div>自比长而上至于乡老大夫，皆养于野人者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206819_comment'></div>一乡之广，又二千五百家而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206819_comment'></div>以今较之，犹非赤望县之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206819_comment'></div>而卿大夫士列于其间，无虑数千人，岂不冗且多乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206819_comment'></div>先王未尝以饩廪为忧，而野人之养君子者亦不以为厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206819_comment'></div>今之郡县官有常员，宜其易禄矣，而议者每以冗官为患，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206819_comment'></div>国家修饰治具，将复三代之制，致治之原，有在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206819_comment'></div>学者宜知其说也，幸著于篇。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1206819_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206820?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206820'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206820'>太极函三为一，一而三之，历十二辰，而五数备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206820_comment'></div>阴阳合德，气钟于子，而黄钟之实全焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206820_comment'></div>其长为度，其籥为量，其重为权，其实一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206820_comment'></div>三者立，斯民不约而信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206820_comment'></div>故曰律为万事根本，而舜所以同律度量衡，而天下治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206820_comment'></div>周衰更秦，反古是今，变乱先王之制，无复存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206820_comment'></div>魏晋而下，因陋袭弊，律尺不同，而诸儒纷纷，无复稽正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206820_comment'></div>权衡度量，至或家自为之，莫能相一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206820_comment'></div>上无以考其数度，下无以立民信，而礼乐亦或几乎熄矣，可胜悼哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206820_comment'></div>国家审法度，修废官，凡先王为治之具，盖无不举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206820_comment'></div>而舜之所以同律度量衡，与孔子所谓谨权量者或未备也，独何欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206820_comment'></div>岂本末先后固有序欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206820_comment'></div>诸君讲明经世之务详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206820_comment'></div>愿悉陈之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1206820_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='cd5440e860df4a73ae356c80dc591cf6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cd5440e860df4a73ae356c80dc591cf6");'><span id='cd5440e860df4a73ae356c80dc591cf6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1113')">1112-1113年</a>，60-61岁</div><div id='cd5440e860df4a73ae356c80dc591cf6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年4月</a>　赴萧山知县。公劝民浚治湘湖，溉田数千顷，是岁大熟，邑民感德，为公立祠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年7月</a>　在萧山。有文。作品：跋司马温公与明道先生帖。<div id='poem_1206675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋司马温公与明道先生帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206675")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206675'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206675'>横渠先生既没，其门人欲谥为明诚，中子以谥议质诸明道先生，先生与温公参订之，故有是书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206675_comment'></div>其辞义典奥而引据精密，足以是正先儒之谬，故宝藏之以传后学。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1206675_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在萧山。罗从彦仲素来学，从游之士肩摩袂属。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年8月</a>　在萧山。是年，有语录记五月至八月事。作品：萧山所闻。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　在萧山任。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
常州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='79c52f1127b74064b1eff0391332117a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("79c52f1127b74064b1eff0391332117a");'><span id='79c52f1127b74064b1eff0391332117a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>，60岁</div><div id='79c52f1127b74064b1eff0391332117a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年3月4日</a>　到常州，寓居龟窠巷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年3月6日</a>　在常州。谒邹浩问时事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在常州。有语录记七月至十月事。作品：毗陵所闻。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年9月3日</a>　在常州。有答李杭问学书。作品：答李杭书。<div id='poem_1206541' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206541' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206541?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答李杭书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年9月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206541")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206541_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206541'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206541'>良佐足下：某愚不知力学，未足以窥古人大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206541_comment'></div>凡平居毫聚铢积，而仅有之者，皆陈腐熟烂，无以誇示流俗，故胶口自绝，不敢辄出一语，与时相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206541_comment'></div>犬马之齿已衰矣，而碌碌犹无闻焉，盖孔子所谓不足畏者，宜士大夫之所悯笑，背而去之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206541_comment'></div>足下乃过自贬损，若有求于不肖者，其所称道，语皆过情，虽名世有不敢当者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206541_comment'></div>僬侥之童，付之以千钧之重，非其任也，故捧读愧汗，踧踖不宁者累日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206541_comment'></div>虽然，某则陋矣，而厚意不可以虚辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206541_comment'></div>昔尝侧闻先生长者之馀论，试一言之，足下自择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206541_comment'></div>夫今人与古人之学异，来书论之悉矣，此不复道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206541_comment'></div>孟子曰：「鸡鸣而起，孳孳为善者，舜之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206541_comment'></div>鸡鸣而起，孳孳为利者，蹠之徒也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206541_comment'></div>舜、蹠之相去远矣，而其分乃在乎善利之间，则为尧舜者，亦力于为善而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206541_comment'></div>颜子曰：「舜何人也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206541_comment'></div>有为者亦若是」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206541_comment'></div>论颜子之学，则曰：「得一善则拳拳服膺而弗失之矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206541_comment'></div>此古之人用力，可考而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206541_comment'></div>夫圣人，人伦之至也，岂有异于人乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206541_comment'></div>尧舜之道曰孝弟，不过行止疾徐而已，皆人所日用而昧者不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206541_comment'></div>夏葛而冬裘，渴饮而饥食，日出而作，晦而息，无非道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206541_comment'></div>譬之莫不饮食，而知味者鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206541_comment'></div>推是而求之，则尧舜与人同，其可知也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206541_comment'></div>然而为是道者，必先乎明善，然后知所以为善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206541_comment'></div>明善在致知，致知在格物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206541_comment'></div>号物之多至于万，则物盖有不可胜穷者，反身而诚，则举天下之物在我矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206541_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「天生烝民，有物有则」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206541_comment'></div>凡形色具于吾身者，无非物也，而各有则焉，反而求之，则天下之理得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206541_comment'></div>由是而通天下之志，类万物之情，参天地之化，其则不远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206541_comment'></div>夫入德之门有宜先传者，有后倦者，其序不可诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206541_comment'></div>若洒扫应对，则门人小子所宜先传者，苟于成人而复使为之，则或倦矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206541_comment'></div>然圣人所谓性与天道者，亦岂尝离夫洒扫应对之间哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206541_comment'></div>其始也，即此而为学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206541_comment'></div>其卒也，非离此以为道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206541_comment'></div>后倦焉者，皆由之而不知者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206541_comment'></div>故曰：「有始有卒者，其惟圣人乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206541_comment'></div>某之所闻如此，足下试思之如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206541_comment'></div>老倦艰于执笔，辞不逮意，幸亮之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1206541_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在常州。有文。作品：答吴敦智书。与刘器之书。邹公挽辞二首（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（邹公，即邹至完。）</span>邹公挽辞二首（其二）复古编后序。祭邹侍郎。李子约墓志铭(李撰)书李从政墓志。跋了翁祭邓南夫文。<div id='poem_1206542' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206542' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206542?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答吴敦智书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206542")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206542_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206542'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206542'>某尝谓舜、蹠之分在善利而已，使世无科举足以取荣利，则父不以诏其子，而士不以学也，如是而不为蹠之徒也几希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206542_comment'></div>足下乃独切切然以明善为急，其度越世人远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206542_comment'></div>勉而卒之，无怠而止焉，则其终为舜之徒也必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206542_comment'></div>所示问，其旨已具李君书，此不复言，取而观之可也，幸照亮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206542_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206556' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206556' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206556?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与刘器之书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206556")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206556_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206556'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206556'>向承垂示许丞《易义》，其用意精深，自成一家之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206556_comment'></div>伏读之久，开发多矣，然鄙意犹有疑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206556_comment'></div>《复卦义》曰：「怒，恶之使也，东方之情也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206556_comment'></div>元，善之长也，东方之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206556_comment'></div>善恶之分，吉凶始焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206556_comment'></div>《中庸》曰：「喜怒哀乐之未发谓之中，发而皆中节谓之和」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206556_comment'></div>四者一本于中，则怒不可独谓恶之使也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206556_comment'></div>怒而中节，是谓达道，而遂以元怒为善恶之分，亦恐未可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206556_comment'></div>又曰：「文王一怒而安天下之民，武王亦一怒而安天下之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206556_comment'></div>所谓出怒不怒，盖以救世，非修身之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206556_comment'></div>修身则致虚守静，不可以动，动则有怒，有怒，与仁违矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206556_comment'></div>某以谓诚者合内外之道，成己乃所以成物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206556_comment'></div>谓不可以修身而可以救世，恐无是理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206556_comment'></div>修身不可与仁违，治天下独可与仁违乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206556_comment'></div>颜子不迁怒，非无怒也，不迁而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206556_comment'></div>是谓中节，此颜子所以修身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206556_comment'></div>而孟子以禹、稷之事与之，谓之易地则皆然，盖救世修身本无二道故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206556_comment'></div>《大学》论治天下国家必始于正心诚意，孟子则曰「天下之本在国，国之本在家，家之本在身」，皆是意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206556_comment'></div>夫物我易观，不能通天下为一，正今日学者之失，此弊尤当救之，不可畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206556_comment'></div>又曰：「孟子四十不动心，颜子之年未至也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206556_comment'></div>是未以不动心与颜子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206556_comment'></div>又曰：「颜子复礼以存心，故其静也仁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206556_comment'></div>是以仁与之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206556_comment'></div>公孙丑问不动心，孟子曰：「是不难，告子先我不动心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206556_comment'></div>孔子曰：「若圣与仁，则吾岂敢」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206556_comment'></div>夫仁，孔子不敢居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206556_comment'></div>不动心，告子之所易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206556_comment'></div>以孔子不敢居者与之，而不与告子之所易者，恐似不伦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206556_comment'></div>又曰：「孟子之言不动心也，曰『我知言，我善养吾浩然之气』，此方以不动涉动者也，不动则专气致柔，复以自知而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206556_comment'></div>动则养气以为马，知言以为途也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206556_comment'></div>孟子论知言养气，乃不动心之道所以异告子者，恐非专为涉动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206556_comment'></div>又曰：「颜子之所养夜气也，孟子之所养旦气也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206556_comment'></div>夜气不存，则于旦气乎何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206556_comment'></div>旦昼之所为，有以梏亡之，则夜气亦不存矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206556_comment'></div>但深考孟子之言，则其义可见，恐所养不须离而为二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206556_comment'></div>古之好学者，必就有道而正焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206556_comment'></div>某不敢自谓好学，至于就有道而正焉，心不敢忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206556_comment'></div>故辄布所闻，取正于左右，如未中理，愿详见教。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1206556_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206642?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复古编后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206642")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206642'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206642'>孔子曰：「河出图，洛出书，圣人则之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206642_comment'></div>则图书之文，天实兆之，非人私智所能为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206642_comment'></div>秦人以吏为师，严是古之禁，尽灭先王之籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206642_comment'></div>汉兴，去秦未远也，科斗书世已无能知者，况泯泯数千载之后乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206642_comment'></div>扬子曰：「言，心声也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206642_comment'></div>书，心画也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206642_comment'></div>世传小篆，盖李斯、赵高之徒以反古逆乱之心为之，其渊源可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206642_comment'></div>三家之学，与古文奇字缪虫之书并行于时，虽去古浸远，而六书仅存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206642_comment'></div>先王之时，书必同文，故建官以达之，所以一道德之归，立民信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206642_comment'></div>汉初犹有六体课试之科、有司举劾之令，以同天下之习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206642_comment'></div>时变事异，法亦随废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206642_comment'></div>故事作无正，而人用其私，古书几亡矣，可胜惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206642_comment'></div>吴兴张友谦中用意兹学，著《复古编》，三十年馀矣，而其书始成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206642_comment'></div>形声近似，而用也不同，盖眇忽之间耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206642_comment'></div>其辨析釐正，皆有稽据，后之有志于古者，必有取于斯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206642_comment'></div>政和之初，余居毗陵，谦中以其书示余，求文以为序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206642_comment'></div>余嘉其用力之勤，而有补于字书也，故为之说，以附于其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206642_comment'></div>谦中善篆，用笔有古意，当与李阳冰、徐常侍并驱争先云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1206642_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206891' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206891' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206891?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭邹侍郎文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206891")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206891_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206891'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206891'>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206891_comment'></div>天爵之尊，天宜啬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206891_comment'></div>奚为于公，独厚锡之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206891_comment'></div>大钧赋物，实劳以生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206891_comment'></div>胡反吝兹，而弗与龄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206891_comment'></div>锡予之柄，尸之其谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206891_comment'></div>杳冥茫昧，理莫可推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206891_comment'></div>公昔在庭，朝阳凤鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206891_comment'></div>谗波弗溺，惟帝之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206891_comment'></div>建中之初，来自南荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206891_comment'></div>人争睹之，景星煌煌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206891_comment'></div>秉义不回，屹如乔岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206891_comment'></div>黄陂万顷，莫能清浊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206891_comment'></div>至言硕画，百未一施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206891_comment'></div>流离困厄，天实为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206891_comment'></div>公之云亡，梁木其坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206891_comment'></div>世亡仁贤，人将焉赖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206891_comment'></div>生荣死哀，身诎道信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206891_comment'></div>公则无憾，实哀斯人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206891_comment'></div>嗟予与公，声气相求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206891_comment'></div>话言之出，其同不谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206891_comment'></div>顷来视公，公疾已困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206891_comment'></div>匪疾之忧，国事是问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206891_comment'></div>精贯白日，神其听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206891_comment'></div>云胡不淑，而不憖遗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206891_comment'></div>死而可赎，人百其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206891_comment'></div>旻天高高，邈乎不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206891_comment'></div>道之穷矣，恸非以私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206891_comment'></div>公乎不忘，其知我悲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1206891_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206857' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206857' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206857?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李子约墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和元年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206857")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206857_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206857'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206857'>公讳撰，字子约，姓李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206857_comment'></div>本唐诸王苗裔，其先恭王明，以太宗子国于曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206857_comment'></div>有子五人，俊、杰、价、备、偲，遭武氏之祸，屡更封，传五王而绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206857_comment'></div>价生济国公臻，无嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206857_comment'></div>独其季偲，官止左武卫大将军，子孙蕃延，与唐始终，迄今班班可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206857_comment'></div>世居陈留，至公之七世祖澄为温州永嘉令，始迁福州之连江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206857_comment'></div>国初三从祖亚笋，以进士高第起家至三司盐铁判官，任公之祖为应天府法曹掾，稍迁至县令、郡守，所至有能称，最后以国子博士守毗陵，卒于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206857_comment'></div>柩将行，州人不忍其去，共挽留之，葬横山，泣送者填道，又图其像，岁时祠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206857_comment'></div>至今人有疾，取坟土服之辄愈，其威惠在人久而不忘盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206857_comment'></div>国博君生五子，公之皇考，其冢嗣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206857_comment'></div>娶范氏，司封员外郎亢之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206857_comment'></div>国博之丧，诸孤无所归，范为营室于苏，故今为苏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206857_comment'></div>公九岁而孤，执丧奉亲如礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206857_comment'></div>既冠，丁母夫人忧，寠甚，家徒四壁，惟闭门自守，虽廪食不继，澹如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206857_comment'></div>亲故高之，争持薪米以饷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206857_comment'></div>服除，游太学，闻南丰曾公巩以文名天下，公往受业其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206857_comment'></div>刻意励行，务多识以畜德，不为进取计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206857_comment'></div>南丰器其材，谓当为世用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206857_comment'></div>会熙宁五年，诏郡国贡士，乃作《湖水碧》诗以勉其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206857_comment'></div>六年，遂登进士第，调越州馀姚县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206857_comment'></div>用举者监扬州高邮县酒税，移江州彭泽县令，迁镇安军节度推官，知河南密县事，除澶州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206857_comment'></div>考满，荐书应格，改左宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206857_comment'></div>曾鲁公布帅青社，辟置公幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206857_comment'></div>公少从南丰游，南丰兄弟三人皆登显仕，有重望，而公尤为翰林公所知，及从青社辟，其兄弟至以书相贺，谓幕府得忠信之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206857_comment'></div>碍吏部格不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206857_comment'></div>青社移河间，再辟公州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206857_comment'></div>岁满，除太仆寺主簿，转奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206857_comment'></div>坐乘骑误过钦圣太后仪卫，贬饶州德兴县监酒税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206857_comment'></div>上即位，覃恩转承议郎，加武骑尉，赐绯衣银鱼，通判莫州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206857_comment'></div>转朝奉郎，加云骑尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206857_comment'></div>堂除人例不赴吏部选，公罢选，即自陈归部，授通判永静军，转朝散郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206857_comment'></div>未赴，以堂除人衔罢，改授签书泰宁军节度判官厅公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206857_comment'></div>八宝赦，转朝请郎，用年劳转朝奉大夫，加骁骑尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206857_comment'></div>任满，以恩例就差通判袁州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206857_comment'></div>自永静改授及罢泰宁任，或劝公诣朝廷申理，公曰：「吾每以士人老不知退为鉴，今固躬蹈之耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1206857_comment'></div>竟不往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1206857_comment'></div>执政大臣贤公行，就除通判保州，将引用，遽以疾终于正寝，实大观三年七月二十日也，享年六十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1206857_comment'></div>公初在馀姚时，有茶商夜行，遇海舶钲鼓偕鸣，更相疑为盗，持短兵格斗，杀伤十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1206857_comment'></div>系萧山狱，吏求正名不得，连年不能决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1206857_comment'></div>清献赵公守越，闻公名，檄公摄县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1206857_comment'></div>公至，吏前负案盈积，公一视之，即得其情，曰：「犯时不知，在律勿论」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1206857_comment'></div>具闻于州，杖遣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1206857_comment'></div>馀悉迎刃族解无留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1206857_comment'></div>未几，邑大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1206857_comment'></div>清献益知公能，荐公可任县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1206857_comment'></div>彭泽县频江，俗穷陋喜讼，尚鬼而信巫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1206857_comment'></div>公一以信义道之，晨兴视事，亲为决曲直，吏簪笔立庭下，屏气惕息，受成命行文，无敢出一语者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1206857_comment'></div>久而民化服，讼日益稀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1206857_comment'></div>使者按行，见之，疑公不事事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1206857_comment'></div>既而勾稽帐簿，皆精致，无毫发疵戾可指摘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1206857_comment'></div>引囚诘吏，吏以素不深与，不能对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1206857_comment'></div>公徐进，具道所以，曲折详尽，卒大喜出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1206857_comment'></div>朝廷下括田令，转运使倚法务苛扰，欲多得匿户羡田为功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1206857_comment'></div>公争以为不可，使者怒，欲劾公留令，又沮格无得申复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1206857_comment'></div>翌旦且行，公抱牍径造卧内，使者惊问，公曰：「彭泽令以公事白，愿起视之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1206857_comment'></div>面抗论移时，且请就劾，并解印绶去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1206857_comment'></div>使者度不可屈，卒从之，然怒犹不置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1206857_comment'></div>是时王公安礼为部刺史，使者还金陵，盛言公抗对状，阴激怒之，觊共置公罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1206857_comment'></div>刺史反壮公所为，曰：「县令乃敢与部使者争衡，此必介特有守士也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1206857_comment'></div>亟呼书吏对使前草奏荐公，使者意沮，犹数阴伺短失，卒无一事可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1206857_comment'></div>巫觋有前期唱言某日某所灾者，已而果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1206857_comment'></div>暴桀因缘为奸，转以相恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1206857_comment'></div>公召群巫于庭，问以火将起状、期日、处所，令将诣伺，有不信，抵罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1206857_comment'></div>又卜于城隍神祠，如所问巫言，有不然者，毁庙，皆曰无有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1206857_comment'></div>乃下令，敢有复假鬼神造言惑众者，坐之，人心悉安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1206857_comment'></div>朔方士鲜知学，公为二州教授，始得名儒为师，士向风，翕然一变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1206857_comment'></div>将门子弟至褫跗注、衣缝掖为诸生者，不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1206857_comment'></div>澶渊濒大河，自元丰初决小吴，河流不复由故道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1206857_comment'></div>元祐三年，始议遣使修复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1206857_comment'></div>公作《复河赋》二篇赞明禹功，究当时利害甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1206857_comment'></div>上之，不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1206857_comment'></div>大抵言河不可复，后卒如公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1206857_comment'></div>又广孟子说，著《养气论》三篇传学者，其言深切著明，皆可考而行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1206857_comment'></div>莫当北使道，公至，谓宜先示以文教，乃增辟学舍，益市书，日亲为讲说，士皆诵其言，化其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1206857_comment'></div>初岁才五六人，未期至十倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1206857_comment'></div>崇宁诏天下兴学，莫遂为边郡第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1206857_comment'></div>其在泰宁，事无小大，悉赖公为理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1206857_comment'></div>虽守将屡易，幕府号为省事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1206857_comment'></div>岁水灾，首议赈救，民不知有饥，公之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1206857_comment'></div>公性刚直，不泊于私欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1206857_comment'></div>居家友顺，遇妻子以礼，闺门之内雍如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1206857_comment'></div>收养孀稚，均其所有，中外无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1206857_comment'></div>不事生产，约于自奉，而周人之急惟恐不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1206857_comment'></div>交朋友尤笃于信义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1206857_comment'></div>莅官临事，以理自将，澹乎若无意于仕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1206857_comment'></div>至其遇事立断，有不便于民，虽要权必争，不少回屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1206857_comment'></div>率意尽诚，亦不为矫激之行，徼名于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1206857_comment'></div>虽仕筦库必尽力，故所至人安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1206857_comment'></div>既去，而久益思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1206857_comment'></div>流落州县三十年，位不称德，士论惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1206857_comment'></div>而公与家人言，未尝有滞淹之叹，其视得丧无足介其胸中者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1206857_comment'></div>故天下识与不识，皆知其为钜人长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1206857_comment'></div>及其亡，亦莫不咨嗟叹惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1206857_comment'></div>公晚尤深佛学，前数月尚无恙，居静室燕坐终日，对家人未尝辄语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1206857_comment'></div>屏绝情累，若预有知者，间惟焚香诵佛书而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1206857_comment'></div>家人私窃怪之，莫敢问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1206857_comment'></div>手书寒山诗一首，意若示诸子者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1206857_comment'></div>大抵以攻人之恶，伐己之善为戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1206857_comment'></div>疾革，犹怡怡自若，卒无一言及后事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1206857_comment'></div>公于死生之际，安之若此，则其素所养可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1206857_comment'></div>曾祖讳慕玢，故任秘书省著作佐郎，赠尚书二部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1206857_comment'></div>国博君讳馀庆，赠屯田郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1206857_comment'></div>考讳处常，故任忠武军节度推官，赠朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1206857_comment'></div>公娶柳氏，括苍人，朝散郎珣之女，有贤行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1206857_comment'></div>生子男六人：弥性、弥伦、弥大、弥逊、弥中、弥正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1206857_comment'></div>女二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1206857_comment'></div>弥伦以公遗奏，补假将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1206857_comment'></div>弥大、弥逊，崇宁、大观间连举登进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1206857_comment'></div>弥大登仕郎，兴仁府宛亭县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1206857_comment'></div>弥逊单州司户参军，馀皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1206857_comment'></div>长女适进士张延之，次适从仕郎、庐州舒城县尉陈温舒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1206857_comment'></div>孙男一人，女一人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1206857_comment'></div>公喜著述，文辞简古，有理趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1206857_comment'></div>作《毛诗训解》二十卷、《孟子讲义》十四卷、文集五十卷、史赞论五卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1206857_comment'></div>其孤将以政和元年二月二十四日葬公于横山祖茔之西，状公之行与其族系世次来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1206857_comment'></div>予虽未尝知公，而与其子弥大游，考公之行与其历官行事始终之大节，皆足以垂世传后，是宜铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1206857_comment'></div>乃叙而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1206857_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_117_1206857'>李本嬴姓，爰自高阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1206857_comment'></div>天祚神尧，兴于有唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1206857_comment'></div>本支十三，明国于曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1206857_comment'></div>或绝或封，惟时之遭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1206857_comment'></div>偲实其季，为卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1206857_comment'></div>位虽不充，蕃蕃子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1206857_comment'></div>世载其德，著于毗陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1206857_comment'></div>疾谁与瘳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1206857_comment'></div>邦君之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1206857_comment'></div>公蕴大器，增光于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1206857_comment'></div>匪斲匪雕，矩方规圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1206857_comment'></div>问学有原，左右之逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1206857_comment'></div>士得其师，靡然向风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1206857_comment'></div>有社有民，庇之以身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1206857_comment'></div>义在必争，力回千钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1206857_comment'></div>畜大不施，其行则踬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1206857_comment'></div>寄之去来，视犹一蜕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1206857_comment'></div>善无不报，不于其躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1206857_comment'></div>力穑之勤，后穫必丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1206857_comment'></div>矧公多子，惟公是似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1206857_comment'></div>责报于天，如执右契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1206857_comment'></div>横山之阴，有坟其墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1206857_comment'></div>公则无憾，永安此居。</div><div id='poem_sentence_139_1206857_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206676' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206676' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206676?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书李从政墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206676")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206676_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206676'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206676'>公少时过钱塘，东平吕公惠卿得公之文，以示翰林沈公文通，二公奇其文，引为忘年之交，谓人曰：「毗陵素多士，未有如李公者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206676_comment'></div>于是文日益有名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206676_comment'></div>公于书无不读，其心传目到之学，盖非浅者所能窥较也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206676_comment'></div>晚在彭城，方计司议法兴利之时，百役毛起，公处之裕如，手未尝废卷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206676_comment'></div>利国监有中贵人，阴以事中其同僚者，部使者付公治之甚急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206676_comment'></div>已而事连中贵人，公请并治之，中贵人惧甚，部使者又欲两释之，公曰：「事未暴白，治不治在公而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206676_comment'></div>付之有司，则有法守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206676_comment'></div>狱已具，不可易也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206676_comment'></div>使者不悦，度公不可以势夺，卒移他司释之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206676_comment'></div>是时，颜复长道居里中，闻之，谓予曰：「奄宦恃嬖昵之私，胁持上下，虽当路要官无敢辄忤其意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206676_comment'></div>李君一以法绳之，不少贷，非秉义不可回屈，不能为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206676_comment'></div>郡守高邮孙公觉尤深器之，事无大小惟公听也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206676_comment'></div>萧县有剧贼竹军者，土兵力不支，被重伤，亡其主将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206676_comment'></div>通守李陶行县，闻流言，谓土兵不战而北，凡二十有五人，欲置之极典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206676_comment'></div>公曰：「有司讯治曲折详尽，犹恐不得其情，今以道路之言置人于死地，非审克之道也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206676_comment'></div>持之月馀不能决，后卒如公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206676_comment'></div>微公争之力，几为淫刑滥诛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206676_comment'></div>公之治狱平反类如此，其小者不能悉数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206676_comment'></div>政和之初，予待次毗陵，公之子殊以公志铭示予，读之蹙然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206676_comment'></div>追念平昔，悼斯人之不复见也，惜其遗事可传于后，又皆予所亲见者，故序次之，以补志文之阙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1206676_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋了翁祭邓南夫文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206679")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206679'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206679'>余闻南夫平居，家人不见其喜怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206679_comment'></div>一日因事怒甚，已而悔之，自恨其养之未至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206679_comment'></div>充是心以往，可谓知好学矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206679_comment'></div>了翁友之，其厚如此，不问可知其贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206679_comment'></div>余幸与之同乡，未及识而南夫已逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206679_comment'></div>悲夫，不复见斯人也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206679_comment'></div>因读了翁之文，怅然久之，故姑书其所闻附于后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206679_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
无锡
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b7f8b990be7746d7986888ab94f366f9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b7f8b990be7746d7986888ab94f366f9");'><span id='b7f8b990be7746d7986888ab94f366f9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>，60岁</div><div id='b7f8b990be7746d7986888ab94f366f9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在无锡。建东林书院，前后于此讲学达十八年。<br /></div>

-----title
金华
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d2da45a501154874bc00d66afb88d38d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d2da45a501154874bc00d66afb88d38d");'><span id='d2da45a501154874bc00d66afb88d38d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1123')">1122-1123年</a>，70-71岁</div><div id='d2da45a501154874bc00d66afb88d38d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　是年，公如婺州，权教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在婺州。权通判。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在婺州。权通判。有文。作品：跋了翁与韦深道书。<div id='poem_1206665' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206665' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206665?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋了翁与韦深道书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206665")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206665_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206665'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206665'>道同则相望异世，其合有若符节者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206665_comment'></div>气禀有异，虽一身之内，肝胆楚越矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206665_comment'></div>三山在弱水之外，舟舆不通，居之者形影自相吊耳，深道乃眷然念之，非声气相求，神交于万里之外，宁有是夫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206665_comment'></div>了翁天下士也，世以其言为轻重，而相与如此，余虽未尝知深道，而信其贤也无疑矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206665_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年4月</a>　在婺州。除监常州市易务。作文。作品：张进之墓志铭。<div id='poem_1206861' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206861' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206861?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张进之墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206861")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206861_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206861'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206861'>张氏讳序，字进之，常州晋陵人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206861_comment'></div>曾祖庭赞，祖延祚，不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206861_comment'></div>父霖，以其子恩赠通直郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206861_comment'></div>进之兄弟七人，长曰巨，次曰与，俱登进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206861_comment'></div>巨虽位不至通显，而以学行为欧阳文忠公所知，其所交皆一时名流，如右丞修简胡公，枢密蒋公是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206861_comment'></div>故张氏遂为毗陵著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206861_comment'></div>进之幼孤，能自力，其为人谨信原悫，与人有诚意，虽喜怒遇事辄发，无所容隐，过即夷然，未尝宿怨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206861_comment'></div>轻财乐施，无疏戚之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206861_comment'></div>视其缓急贷与无所吝，虽时有见负，折券不问也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206861_comment'></div>亲戚之贫者月廪食之有常数，行之十有馀年不少替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206861_comment'></div>暴雨雪，乡邻艰食，则给薪米以赈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206861_comment'></div>市材治棺，以待贫无周身者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206861_comment'></div>每千人为一录，曰「冥惠」，饭千僧以荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206861_comment'></div>岁饥，殍死被原野，进之敛其遗骸藏之，殆不可以数计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206861_comment'></div>俚俗信禨巫，宗人得疠疾，阖户无敢往来者，进之日往省之，无难色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206861_comment'></div>比其亡也，所遗一孤女尔，进之力为经纪之，事无巨细，皆纤悉详尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206861_comment'></div>又育其女，为置奁具，择良士归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206861_comment'></div>郡寮有雅相善者，贫甚，而抱疾久不愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206861_comment'></div>进之往抚其家，亲为调剂，周之无不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206861_comment'></div>将属纩，以后事付之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206861_comment'></div>又有闽士自京都还，暴卒于逆旅，茕然一小僮守之，无与语者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206861_comment'></div>进之任其托，哀其无告，为之棺敛，凡附于身者，咸使无悔焉，悉力赙之，资其柩以归，二家存没得以无憾，闻者义之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206861_comment'></div>宣和四年二月初二日卒于正寝，享年五十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206861_comment'></div>前一日澡浴更衣，若将远适，然家人初莫之省也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206861_comment'></div>越日，盥栉坐堂上，有亲宾与之笑语如常时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206861_comment'></div>坐顷，忽瞑目，起视，屹然已亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206861_comment'></div>其于死生之际，与世之所谓善知识者庸有异乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206861_comment'></div>盖其平生于佛事未尝斯须忘于心，虽在尘劳中而能自拨，乐与方外之士游，得其一言之善，则终身佩服而不敢失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206861_comment'></div>其诚著于中，而自信其所得，故能安逝若此，为善之效，其至矣夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206861_comment'></div>初娶李氏，再娶孙氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206861_comment'></div>男二人：曰茹，曰蔚，皆有文行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206861_comment'></div>女一人，适凌仲皋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1206861_comment'></div>孙二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1206861_comment'></div>其孤将以是年四月二十一日葬于武进县怀德南乡巢野之原，以朝奉郎高元修之状来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1206861_comment'></div>乃为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1206861'>积德以润身，施惠以及物，庆覃后昆，其永无极。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1206861_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年2月</a>　在婺州。作文。作品：婺州新城记。<div id='poem_1206842' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206842' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206842?labeling=true' target='_blank'>婺州新城记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206842")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206842_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206842'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206842'>宣和三年盗发帮原，蹂数州之地，皆狼顾失守，而婺女罹害尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206842_comment'></div>天子恻然念之，遴简儒臣镇抚兹土，河南范公实被其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206842_comment'></div>公至之日，残孽未殄，四境之内钲鼓之声相闻，环寇之师殆且数万，而转输馈饷取具焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206842_comment'></div>夷伤之馀，窜伏山谷，还定安集，无一不得其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206842_comment'></div>越岁杪寇平，百废具兴，顽凶革心，屏息听命，无敢复出为恶者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206842_comment'></div>政成治定，乃顾谓僚属曰：「国家承五季之乱，海内分裂，擅彊兵负固而不服者，地相属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206842_comment'></div>独钱氏据有全吴，首效臣顺，为国屏翰垂二百年，无东顾之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206842_comment'></div>故城郭不修，士卒不练，一夫跳梁而六州为之暴骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206842_comment'></div>盖承平之久，吏惰而不知戒故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206842_comment'></div>则城郭之不完，其可忽诸」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206842_comment'></div>于是因其旧而新之，周十里，基三丈，面广三之一，而高倍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206842_comment'></div>浚隍而为池，陶甓以为堞，募七邑之夫，倍其庸直，因以济其艰食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206842_comment'></div>其费无虑数百万，而一毫不取于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206842_comment'></div>又载食与醪，时往劳之，故人乐于趋事而忘其勤焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206842_comment'></div>以工计之六万一千七百有奇，经始于九月甲戌，告成于十有二月丁酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206842_comment'></div>望之屹然山立，不可陵犯，民吏欢忻鼓舞，相与诣余而告曰：「昔之垝垣废址践为通衢，故关无讥，宵行者无禁，草窃奸宄得以自肆，而人受其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206842_comment'></div>今吾民奠枕而居，无异时之患，宁可不知其所自耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206842_comment'></div>愿纪成绩，以昭示于后」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206842_comment'></div>余尝读《易》，至《坎》之《彖》曰：「天险不可升也，地险山川丘陵也，王公设险以守其国」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206842_comment'></div>而后知先王为城郭沟池之固，盖本诸天地义理之不可无者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206842_comment'></div>故文武以《天保》以上治内，《采薇》以下治外，卒命南仲往城朔方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206842_comment'></div>以《六月》之诗考之，文武所以治内外者，其本末先后废一不可也，故出车废则功力缺矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206842_comment'></div>今婺女之政，纲条纪律，纤悉备具，而又完其郭郛，为邦人无穷之赖，芳猷伟绩，追配南仲，是宜有纪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206842_comment'></div>使后之人知本末先后之序，无废前修，岂曰小补之哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1206842_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='096ef230eb2340cc95ccb19624bf8c23_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("096ef230eb2340cc95ccb19624bf8c23");'><span id='096ef230eb2340cc95ccb19624bf8c23_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年12月</a>　至扬州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年12月26日</a>　在扬州。除工部侍郎，有辞状。作品：辞免工部侍郎奏状。<div id='poem_1206466' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206466' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206466?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免工部侍郎状<span class='inlineComment2'>（十二月二十六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年12月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206466")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206466_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206466'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206466'>右，臣今月二十五日准尚书省吏房帖子，三省同奉圣旨，除臣工部侍郎，日下供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206466_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206466_comment'></div>伏念臣犬马之齿七十有五，衰病，筋力不支，不足以任职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206466_comment'></div>伏望圣慈追还成命，除臣一在外宫观差遣，庶沾薄禄，毕此馀生，不胜幸愿之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206466_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1128')">1127-1128年</a>　在扬州，有文。作品：与杨仲远书。谢除工部侍郎表。谢赐诏乞出不允表。举曾统自代奏状。<div id='poem_1206482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206482' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206482?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除工部侍郎表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206482")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206482'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206482'>臣某言：准告除臣试尚书工部侍郎，仍赐对衣金带者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206482_comment'></div>赐环荐至，方力疾以造朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206482_comment'></div>出綍遽膺，敢辞难于就职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206482_comment'></div>甄收甚渥，刻厉无穷<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206482_comment'></div>伏念臣智不竞时，学惟泥古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206482_comment'></div>素行贫贱，付忧患之薰心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206482_comment'></div>备历险艰，见盛衰之反掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206482_comment'></div>岂图迟暮，获预选抡？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206482_comment'></div>荷二圣之深知，当一时之大变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206482_comment'></div>擢繇学省，置在谏垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206482_comment'></div>念当效命之秋，何暇多言之恤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206482_comment'></div>乞身去国，凝睇围城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206482_comment'></div>空怀天地之恩，无从报塞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206482_comment'></div>已迫桑榆之景，徒极殒伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206482_comment'></div>赖神圣之有临，致邦家之再造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206482_comment'></div>眷惟销患，无竞得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206482_comment'></div>招徕下及于衰残，奔赴莫先于艰厄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206482_comment'></div>属有负薪之疾，阻于叱驭之驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206482_comment'></div>仰被宽隆，载加超越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1206482_comment'></div>未及瞻光于黼陛，已令贰事于官曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1206482_comment'></div>虽主忧臣辱之时，不求营缮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1206482_comment'></div>而内修外攘之际，专赖谋猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1206482_comment'></div>弗许牢辞，曷胜重拜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1206482_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下忧劳图治，刚健继明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1206482_comment'></div>深怀播越之勤，克笃孝恭之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1206482_comment'></div>凡侧身而修行，皆应天而顺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1206482_comment'></div>期瞻见于两宫，庶肃清于四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1206482_comment'></div>广收群策，用翊丕基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1206482_comment'></div>有如疲曳之馀，亦在简求之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1206482_comment'></div>臣敢不追惟旧学，佩服至仁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1206482_comment'></div>持橐奉身，益尽论思之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1206482_comment'></div>枕戈励志，更输忧愤之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1206482_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206483' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206483' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206483?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐诏乞出不允表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206483")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206483_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206483'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206483'>臣某言：伏蒙圣慈以臣乞除一在外宫官，赐诏不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206483_comment'></div>纶言俯及，朽质生光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206483_comment'></div>祗荷宠灵，惟深感涕<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206483_comment'></div>伏念臣亲逢圣旦，叨被误恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206483_comment'></div>耄无能为，寖隳职业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206483_comment'></div>老不知止，有腼面颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206483_comment'></div>以居有食指之繁，而退无周身之策，尚资薄禄，以毕馀生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206483_comment'></div>恃君父之眷知，披腹心而上渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206483_comment'></div>愚衷已竭，天听未俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206483_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下端一德以当天，奉三无而抚世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206483_comment'></div>神威不怒，圣武布昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206483_comment'></div>扩大度以并容，耻一夫而不获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206483_comment'></div>致兹庸妄，亦未弃捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206483_comment'></div>荷天地之至仁，宜思论报；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206483_comment'></div>迫桑榆之晚景，徒积兢惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206483_comment'></div>敢不勉服训辞，益坚素守？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206483_comment'></div>庶几晚节，无忝前修。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1206483_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206467' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206467' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206467?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举曾统自代状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206467")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206467_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206467'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206467'>右，臣伏见奉议郎、守尚书工部员外郎曾统，名臣之后，能世其家，举以代臣，实允公议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1206467_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年2月</a>　在扬州，转朝散大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年2月15日</a>　在扬州，有文。作品：乞宫祠奏状（其一）<div id='poem_1206468' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206468' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206468?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞宫祠状<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　建炎二年二月十五日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年2月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206468")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206468_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206468'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206468'>右，臣以凡庸之材，叨被误恩，擢寘贰卿之列，顾虽糜捐，不足报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206468_comment'></div>重念臣行年七十有六，素有足疾，拜履俱艰，日虞颠仆，触事昏忘，难以任职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206468_comment'></div>欲望圣慈矜恤，除臣一在外宫观差遣，任便居住。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1206468_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　在扬州，陛对，论自古贤圣之君应以典学为务。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年3月2日</a>　在扬州，有文。作品：乞宫祠奏状（其二）<div id='poem_1206469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞宫祠状<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　三月二日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年3月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206469")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206469'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206469'>右，臣伏蒙陛下以臣乞宫观差遣，任便居住，赐诏不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206469_comment'></div>伏念臣自熙宁中叨窃科第，五十馀年，晚始蒙渊圣皇帝误知，擢居禁从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206469_comment'></div>銮舆北狩，臣以老病在外，无以自效，偷生忍死，负罪宜无所逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206469_comment'></div>陛下嗣位，特蒙矜贷，召寘贰卿之列，受恩逾分，虽糜捐未足以报称万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206469_comment'></div>臣虽至愚，岂敢饰辞避事，以求便安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206469_comment'></div>重念臣犬马之齿七十有六，筋骸衰瘁，心志眊昏，两胫痹挛，日虞颠仆，故不避烦渎之诛，再干天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206469_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣诚恳，除臣一宫观差遣，任便居住，庶沾薄禄，使垂尽之年，不至失所。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206469_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年3月</a>　在扬州，除兼侍讲，有文。作品：谢除侍讲表。乞宫祠奏状（其三）<div id='poem_1206484' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206484' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206484?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除侍讲表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206484")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206484_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206484'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206484'>臣某言：准告除臣兼侍讲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206484_comment'></div>叨奉宸纶，进陪经幄，宠荣过分，愧惧交并<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206484_comment'></div>伏念臣以垂尽之年，适多艰之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206484_comment'></div>滥窃不虞之誉，初非有用之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206484_comment'></div>疾病交攻，神志俱耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206484_comment'></div>日怀丘首之念，亟图曳尾之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206484_comment'></div>自命奇穷，已绝荣望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206484_comment'></div>眷恩俯逮，奚殊罔象之得珠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206484_comment'></div>天禄坐糜，几类支离而受粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206484_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下舜聪四达，汤德日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206484_comment'></div>虽大明之升，容光必照；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206484_comment'></div>而清问所及，下民不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206484_comment'></div>致兹妄庸，亦与抡选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206484_comment'></div>涓流何有，无裨溟渤之深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206484_comment'></div>老马已疲，终冀敝帷之赐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1206484_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1206470' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206470' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206470?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞宫祠状<span class='inlineComment2'>（三　辞免兼侍讲）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206470")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206470_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206470'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206470'>右，臣以老病上干天听，乞一宫祠差遣，未赐俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206470_comment'></div>方欲再具陈情，伏蒙圣恩除臣兼侍讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206470_comment'></div>闻命惊惶，无所容措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206470_comment'></div>伏念臣逮事渊圣皇帝，复侍经席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206470_comment'></div>臣以衰病，目昏不能远视，足弱不能久立，辞免职任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206470_comment'></div>蒙渊圣皇帝矜悯，除臣提举西京嵩山崇福宫，任便居住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206470_comment'></div>今已逾三年，精神昏眊，手足挛痹，又甚于前日，岂敢冒贪宠荣，复居此职？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206470_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣诚恳，追还成命，除臣一宫观差遣，以安愚分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1206470_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年4月6日</a>　在扬州，乞宫祠，未允。作品：乞宫祠奏状（其四）<div id='poem_1206471' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206471' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206471?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞宫祠状<span class='inlineComment2'>（四　四月六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年4月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206471")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206471_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206471'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206471'>右，臣伏蒙陛下擢寘贰卿，仍侍经幄，皆一时高选，岂惟陋学浅闻不足以任职，而臣犬马之齿七十有六，衰病日增，虽欲贪荣冒居，精力不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206471_comment'></div>伏望圣慈矜察，除臣一宫观差遣，任便居住，庶沾薄禄，毕此馀生。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1206471_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年4月15日</a>　在扬州，再乞宫祠，遂罢工部侍郎兼侍讲。作品：乞宫祠奏状（其五）<div id='poem_1206472' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206472' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206472?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞宫祠状<span class='inlineComment2'>（五　十五日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年4月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206472")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206472_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206472'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206472'>右，臣今月十三日准尚书省劄子，以臣乞宫观差遣，奉圣旨不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206472_comment'></div>臣以凡庸之才，误蒙睿恩，擢侍经幄，遂获日近清光，臣非土木，岂不知幸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206472_comment'></div>重念臣年龄迟暮，精力衰残，旧学荒芜，十忘八九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206472_comment'></div>仰见圣德日跻，非陋识浅闻足以上裨万一，惧旁招人言，自贻悔咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206472_comment'></div>加之目视昏花，两胫痹弱，晨趋殿陛，每虞颠仆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206472_comment'></div>徒以食贫指众，仰禄为生，未能引年辞仕，冒宠侥求，负罪多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206472_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下天度并容，无物不覆，察臣诚恳，除臣一宫观差遣，任便居住，庶沾厚禄，以尽馀年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1206472_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年4月19日</a>　在扬州，除龙图阁直学士，提举洞霄宫。作品：辞免龙图阁直学士奏状。<div id='poem_1206473' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206473' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206473?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免龙图阁直学士状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年4月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206473")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206473_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206473'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206473'>右，臣伏准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，除臣龙图阁直学士、提举杭州洞霄宫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206473_comment'></div>叨被误恩，荣愧交集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206473_comment'></div>所有直学士之职，朝廷清选，如臣衰朽，岂敢冒居？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206473_comment'></div>伏望圣慈追还成命，庶安愚分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1206473_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年4月19日</a>　在扬州，有文。作品：谢除龙图阁学士表。<div id='poem_1206485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除龙图阁直学士表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年4月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27995, "宋", "杨时", "poem_title_1206485")'>杨时</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206485'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206485'>臣某言：伏奉告命，除臣龙图阁直学士，依前朝散大夫、提举杭州洞霄宫，仍赐对衣金带者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206485_comment'></div>纶言下逮，朽质生光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206485_comment'></div>误膺华衮之褒，滥厕昔贤之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206485_comment'></div>宠恩逾厚，荣惧交并<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206485_comment'></div>伏念臣才不适时，学惟泥古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206485_comment'></div>投身世网，流落半生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206485_comment'></div>擢寘经帷，历侍三圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206485_comment'></div>顾桑榆之已晚，惊岁月之屡迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1206485_comment'></div>神志俱昏，筋骸难彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1206485_comment'></div>罄愚衷而上诉，荷天听之俯从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1206485_comment'></div>冒延阁之清资，窃琳宫之荣禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1206485_comment'></div>锡之显服，束以精镠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1206485_comment'></div>夫何妄庸，有此遭遇？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1206485_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下体乾坤之博施，推日月之至明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1206485_comment'></div>成物不遗，均涵动植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1206485_comment'></div>容光必照，无间隐微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1206485_comment'></div>致兹衰残，亦未捐弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1206485_comment'></div>敢不益坚晚节，上副深仁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1206485_comment'></div>虽馀龄无路以效勤，而图报尚期于结草。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1206485_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　在扬州，请朝廷恩准八闽山无米地无租，圣旨即准。<br /></div>
